### [1] [High-redshift physics from the acoustic scale](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18131)
*Zachary J. Weiner*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper introduces the "matter-era distance excess" as a simplified geometric diagnostic for analyzing tensions between CMB and DESI measurements, particularly regarding acoustic scale determinations. The method provides analytical tools to assess contributions from new physics at high redshifts versus low-redshift dynamics.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from addressing the current tension between Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) and cosmic microwave background (CMB) measurements of acoustic scales. There's a need for a simplified, analytically tractable diagnostic that can distinguish between explanations involving modified dynamics at low redshifts versus new physics at high redshifts (nonstandard recombination, dark matter dynamics, neutrino masses).

Method: The method develops the "matter-era distance excess" as a summary statistic: the transverse distance interval between photon-baryon decoupling and a late epoch in the matter era. This provides analytical tractability for examining sensitivity to various physical scenarios. The framework analytically derives how this observable responds to: (1) modified dynamics at low redshift, (2) new physics at high redshift (nonstandard recombination, nonminimal dark matter dynamics, spatial curvature), and (3) neutrino masses specifically as a geometric measurement.

Result: The matter-era distance excess is shown to be unlikely explained by modified dynamics at low redshift. It provides clear sensitivity to new physics at high redshift, including explaining how it represents a direct geometric measurement of neutrino masses and underlies current incompatibility constraints. For dynamical dark energy models, the excess mediation depends on unphysical extrapolated behavior at high redshift, and removing alternative explanations eliminates most CMB-derived evidence, leaving only about 1.7σ preference mostly from DESI's low-redshift Alcock-Paczynski measurements.

Conclusion: The matter-era distance excess provides a powerful analytical diagnostic tool for understanding tensions between CMB and large-scale structure measurements. It suggests that explaining the DESI-CMB tension likely requires new physics at high redshifts rather than low-redshift modifications, and clarifies the geometric nature of neutrino mass constraints while exposing limitations in interpreting dynamical dark energy models based on unphysical high-redshift extrapolations.

Abstract: We present a simplified and general description of the high-redshift information in acoustic scale measurements from the cosmic microwave background and large-scale structure. The transverse distance interval between photon--baryon decoupling and a late epoch in the matter era provides an analytically tractable summary statistic thereof and a general diagnostic of the current tension between the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument and the CMB. We show that this "matter-era distance excess" is unlikely to be explained by modified dynamics at low redshift. We then analytically derive the matter-era distance interval's sensitivity to new physics at high redshift, including nonstandard recombination, nonminimal dark matter dynamics, and spatial curvature; in particular, we explain how this observable represents a direct geometric measurement of (and underlies the current incompatibility with) neutrino masses. Finally, we demonstrate that phenomenological models of dynamical dark energy mediate the matter-era distance excess in a manner reliant on their unphysical, extrapolated behavior at high redshift. Invoking alternative explanations of the excess removes the CMB's contribution to the evidence for these models; the residual preference of around $1.7σ$ mostly derives from DESI's two lowest-redshift measurements of the Alcock--Paczynski distortion, without which it drops to $0.5 σ$.

</details>


### [2] [TUNeS: Neural Emulation of Large-Scale Structure Across Redshifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18165)
*Yuqi Kang,Hu Bin,Dongxing Li,Jan Hamann*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: TUNeS (Temporal UNet emulator for Structure formation) is a neural network framework that accelerates cosmological N-body simulations by predicting nonlinear matter density evolution directly from initial particle distributions. Using a two-stage particle-to-density mapping approach with temporal UNet architecture, it achieves accurate large- and small-scale structure predictions across redshifts with minimal training data, enabling GPU-accelerated inference orders of magnitude faster than traditional simulations.

TUNeS (Temporal UNet emulator for Structure formation) 是一个神经网络框架，通过直接从初始粒子分布预测非线性物质密度演化来加速宇宙学N-body模拟。该模型采用两阶段粒子到密度映射方法与时间UNet架构，仅需少量训练数据即可实现跨红移的大尺度和小尺度结构准确预测，其GPU加速推理比传统模拟快多个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmological structure formation requires solving nonlinear gravitational dynamics through computationally intensive N-body simulations, which become prohibitively expensive for high-resolution, large-volume studies needed for next-generation surveys. While neural network emulators have been developed for summary statistics, there remains a critical need for direct, high-fidelity mapping from initial conditions to full 3D density fields that preserves both Gaussian and non-Gaussian statistics across scales and redshifts. The motivation is to bridge the gap between particle-based N-body accuracy and neural network efficiency by developing a model that can directly learn the temporal evolution operator for gravitational collapse from sparse particle representations to continuous density fields.

宇宙学结构形成需要通过计算密集的N-body模拟求解非线性引力动力学，这对于下一代巡天所需的高分辨率、大体积研究来说计算代价过高。虽然已有针对摘要统计量的神经网络模拟器，但仍迫切需要能够从初始条件直接映射到完整三维密度场的直接、高保真方法，以保留跨尺度和红移的高斯和非高斯统计量。其动机是通过开发能够直接从稀疏粒子表示学习引力坍缩时间演化算子到连续密度场的模型，来弥合基于粒子的N-body精度与神经网络效率之间的差距。

Method: TUNeS employs a two-stage modeling architecture: (1) Particle-to-density mapping: A neural network processes input particle positions and masses at arbitrary initial redshift to generate a coarse density grid via adaptive mass deposition onto a regular lattice, effectively learning the Lagrangian-to-Eulerian mapping. (2) Density refinement: A temporal UNet architecture (encoder-decoder with skip connections) refines the coarse density field to high-resolution predictions at arbitrary target redshifts, with temporal conditioning through redshift-encoded feature vectors. The model learns the evolution operator $\\mathcal{E}: \\rho(z_{\\mathrm{in}}) \\rightarrow \\rho(z_{\\mathrm{target}})$ parameterized by neural weights $\\theta$, trained via minimization of a multi-scale loss combining $L_1$ density reconstruction, power spectrum matching, and higher-order statistics. Key innovations include particle batching for memory efficiency, window-based refinement for scaling to larger volumes, and temporal conditioning enabling arbitrary redshift predictions without retraining.

TUNeS采用两阶段建模架构：(1) 粒子到密度映射：神经网络处理任意初始红移下的输入粒子位置和质量，通过自适应质量沉积到规则晶格上生成粗糙密度网格，有效学习拉格朗日到欧拉映射。(2) 密度精细化：时间UNet架构（带跳跃连接的编码器-解码器）将粗糙密度场精细化到任意目标红移的高分辨率预测，通过红移编码特征向量进行时间调节。模型学习由神经权重$\\theta$参数化的演化算子$\\mathcal{E}: \\rho(z_{\\mathrm{in}}) \\rightarrow \\rho(z_{\\mathrm{target}})$，通过结合$L_1$密度重建、功率谱匹配和高阶统计量的多尺度损失最小化进行训练。关键创新包括：用于内存效率的粒子分批、用于扩展到更大体积的基于窗口的精细化，以及无需重新训练即可实现任意红移预测的时间调节。

Result: TUNeS demonstrates remarkable performance with minimal training: using only eight N-body simulations initialized at $z=100$, it accurately reproduces density fields across multiple target redshifts with sub-percent to few-percent errors. At $k \\simeq 1\\,h\\,\\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$, the power spectrum error remains at the few-percent level, comparable to cosmic variance. The model preserves both Gaussian statistics (two-point correlations, power spectra) and non-Gaussian statistics (one-point PDFs, peak counts, 3D Minkowski functionals) with high fidelity. Computational performance: end-to-end inference from $256^3$ particles to $256^3$ density grid completes in $\\sim25\\,\\mathrm{second}$ on a single GPU, representing $\\mathcal{O}(10^3)$-fold acceleration over traditional N-body simulations. The architecture naturally scales to larger particle counts and volumes through particle batching and window-based refinement strategies without performance degradation.

TUNeS在极少训练数据下展现出卓越性能：仅使用在$z=100$初始化的八个N-body模拟，即可在多个目标红移下准确再现密度场，误差在亚百分比到几个百分点之间。在$k \\simeq 1\\,h\\,\\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$处，功率谱误差保持在几个百分点水平，与宇宙方差相当。该模型以高保真度保留了高斯统计量（两点相关、功率谱）和非高斯统计量（单点PDF、峰值计数、三维Minkowski泛函）。计算性能：从$256^3$粒子到$256^3$密度网格的端到端推理在单个GPU上仅需$\\sim25\\,\\mathrm{秒}$，比传统N-body模拟加速$\\mathcal{O}(10^3)$倍。该架构通过粒子分批和基于窗口的精细化策略自然扩展到更大粒子数和体积，且性能不下降。

Conclusion: TUNeS establishes a novel paradigm for neural network-based cosmological simulations that bridges particle dynamics with field-level predictions through a principled two-stage architecture. By directly learning the temporal evolution operator from initial particle distributions to nonlinear density fields, it achieves unprecedented efficiency while maintaining statistical fidelity across a broad range of cosmological observables. The framework's architectural design enables scaling to survey-sized volumes and resolutions, making it a promising tool for next-generation cosmology analyses requiring massive simulation suites. Future extensions could incorporate baryonic physics, modified gravity, and other cosmological parameters, potentially revolutionizing the computational landscape of structure formation modeling.

TUNeS通过原则性的两阶段架构，建立了基于神经网络的宇宙学模拟新范式，桥接了粒子动力学与场级预测。通过直接从初始粒子分布学习到非线性密度场的时间演化算子，该模型在保持广泛宇宙学可观测量统计保真度的同时实现了前所未有的效率。该框架的架构设计使其能够扩展到巡天规模的体积和分辨率，使其成为需要大规模模拟套件的下一代宇宙学分析的有前景工具。未来扩展可包含重子物理、修正引力和其他宇宙学参数，可能彻底改变结构形成建模的计算格局。

Abstract: In this work, we introduce TUNeS (Temporal UNet emulator for Structure formation), a neural network framework for accelerating N-body simulations by predicting the nonlinear evolution of the matter density field from an initial particle distribution. TUNeS employs a two-stage modeling strategy, combining particle-based inference with a density-field refinement on a regular grid, enabling accurate reconstruction of both large- and small-scale structures. The model is designed to operate across redshift, taking particle snapshots at arbitrary input redshifts and predicting density fields at arbitrary target redshifts. In this work, we evaluate its performance using simulations initialized at $z=100$, with predictions generated at multiple lower redshifts. Trained on only eight N-body simulations, TUNeS reproduces reference results with good agreement in both Gaussian and non-Gaussian statistics, including two-point correlations, one-point distributions, peak counts, and three-dimensional Minkowski functionals. In particular, at $k \simeq 1\,h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$, the power spectrum error remains at the few-percent level. End-to-end inference from $256^3$ particles to a $256^3$ density grid can be completed in $\sim25\,\mathrm{second}$ on a single GPU. Thanks to its architectural design, the model naturally scales to larger particle numbers and larger volumes through particle batching and window-based refinement.

</details>


### [3] [Gamma-Ray Bursts as an Independent High-Redshift Probe of Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18223)
*Maria Giovanna Dainotti,Aleksander Łukasz Lenart,Biagio De Simone,William Giarè,Eleonora Di Valentino,Dieter H. Hartmann,Nissim Fraija,Kazunari Iwasaki,Gaetano Lambiase*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper investigates the sample size requirements for Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs) with plateau phases to become competitive cosmological probes for testing deviations from $Λ$CDM, showing that ∼66 well-characterized optical GRBs can achieve dark energy parameter constraints comparable to current CMB measurements.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To bridge the redshift gap between Type Ia Supernovae ($z≲2.9$) and CMB ($z≈1100$) for testing $Λ$CDM, this study explores GRBs as high-redshift ($z=9.2$) cosmological probes. The recent DESI BAO observations suggesting potential deviations from $Λ$CDM motivate developing GRB-based tests independent of existing datasets.

为填补 Ia 型超新星 ($z≲2.9$) 与 CMB ($z≈1100$) 之间的红移间隙以测试 $Λ$CDM 模型，本研究探索将伽马射线暴作为高红移 ($z=9.2$) 宇宙学探针。最近 DESI BAO 观测暗示可能偏离 $Λ$CDM，这促使开发基于 GRB 的独立于现有数据集的检验方法。

Method: The study develops cosmological forecasts using the two-dimensional Dainotti relations between luminosity at the end of plateau phase and its rest-frame duration in X-ray and optical bands. Simulated GRB samples are constructed from observed populations, and parameter constraints are evaluated for $w$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM models through Fisher matrix analysis. The analysis considers both independent GRB constraints and combinations with CMB observations.

本研究利用 plateau 阶段结束时的光度与其静止系持续时间之间的二维 Dainotti relations（在 X 射线和光学波段），开发宇宙学预测。基于观测群体构建模拟 GRB 样本，并通过 Fisher 矩阵分析评估 $w$CDM 和 $w_0w_a$CDM 模型的参数约束。分析考虑了独立的 GRB 约束以及与 CMB 观测的结合。

Result: Results show that GRB samples with tens to hundreds of well-characterized plateau events can approach CMB-level precision on dark energy equation-of-state parameter $w$. Specifically, ∼66 optical GRBs achieve $σ_w ≈ 0.47$, comparable to Planck constraints in the $w$CDM framework. Machine learning techniques that double GRB counts through redshift inference make such sample sizes already attainable. GRB+CMB combinations significantly improve constraints, with ∼400 GRBs potentially reaching $σ_w ≈ 0.07$.

结果表明，包含数十到数百个 well-characterized plateau 事件的 GRB 样本能在暗能量状态方程参数 $w$ 上接近 CMB 级别的精度。具体而言，∼66 个光学 GRB 可实现 $σ_w ≈ 0.47$，与 $w$CDM 框架下 Planck 的约束相当。通过红移推断将 GRB 数量翻倍的机器学习技术已使此类样本规模成为可能。GRB+CMB 组合显著改善约束，∼400 个 GRB 可能达到 $σ_w ≈ 0.07$。

Conclusion: GRBs with plateau phases represent a promising high-redshift cosmological probe capable of independently testing dynamical dark energy signals suggested by DESI BAO and other datasets. Future observations combined with next-generation transient missions and improved statistical techniques will enable GRBs to play important roles in verifying the robustness of potential deviations from $Λ$CDM.

具有 plateau 阶段的 GRB 代表一种有前景的高红移宇宙学探针，能够独立测试 DESI BAO 及其他数据集所暗示的动态暗能量信号。未来观测结合下一代瞬变源任务和改进的统计技术，将使 GRB 在验证潜在偏离 $Λ$CDM 的稳健性方面发挥重要作用。

Abstract: Testing the $Λ$CDM model requires cosmological probes spanning the wide redshift interval between Type Ia Supernovae (SNe Ia, $z\lesssim2.9$) and the Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB, $z\approx1100$). Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs), observed up to redshift $z=9.2$, offer the opportunity to explore this regime. Here, we investigate how many GRBs are needed to become a useful cosmological probe capable of independently testing deviations from $Λ$CDM suggested by the recent DESI BAO observations. We develop forecasts based on the two-dimensional X-ray and optical Dainotti relations, between the luminosity at the end of the plateau phase and its rest-frame duration. Using simulated GRB samples constructed from the observed population, we evaluate the constraining power of GRBs on cosmological parameters within the $w$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM models, both independently and in combination with CMB observations. Our results show that GRB samples containing several tens to hundreds of well-characterized plateau can already approach the precision currently achieved by CMB measurements on the Dark Energy (DE) equation-of-state parameter $w$. Particularly, a sample of $\sim66$ optical GRBs can reach a precision $σ_w \approx 0.47$, comparable to that obtained from Planck within the $w$CDM framework. Such sample sizes are already attainable through Machine Learning techniques that double the number of GRBs using inferred redshifts. These forecasts indicate that future GRB observations, when combined with next-generation transient missions and improved statistical techniques, will provide an independent high-redshift probe of cosmic expansion and will play an important role in testing the robustness of potential Dynamical DE signals suggested by other cosmological datasets.

</details>


### [4] [Beyond Linear Bias Expansions for AbacusSummit Halos at z = 8](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18234)
*Kyle K. Boone,Daniel J. Eisenstein*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper analyzes the bias expansion for high-redshift (z=8 and z=5) halos using N-body simulations (AbacusSummit), finding that only linear and quadratic bias terms are needed while tidal bias is negligible at z=8 but appears at z=5, with bias coefficients evolving linearly with redshift.

\n\n
本文使用N-body模拟（AbacusSummit）分析高红移（z=8和z=5）晕团的偏差展开，发现只需要线性和二次偏差项，而潮汐偏差在z=8时可忽略但在z=5时出现，偏差系数随红移线性演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand which terms in the standard bias expansion are necessary for accurately modeling the clustering of highly biased, high-redshift halo populations, particularly addressing whether higher-order terms (including tidal bias $s^2$ and cubic terms) are required or if Gaussian matter field assumptions suffice.

\n\n
旨在理解标准偏差展开中的哪些项对于准确建模高度偏差、高红移晕团的聚类是必需的，特别解决是否需要高阶项（包括潮汐偏差$s^2$和立方项）或者高斯物质场假设是否足够的问题。

Method: Utilize AbacusSummit N-body simulations with halos at $z=8$ (mass threshold $1\times10^{11}h^{-1}M_\odot$) in $2h^{-1}$Gpc boxes. Fit bias expansions to both halo power spectrum and bispectrum measurements to extract bias coefficients. Employ both $z=8$ and $z=5$ samples with mass thresholds adjusted to maintain constant halo field variance. Statistical significance assessed via $\sigma$ deviations from zero for each bias term.

\n\n
使用AbacusSummit N-body模拟，处理$z=8$的晕团（质量阈值$1\times10^{11}h^{-1}M_\odot$）在$2h^{-1}$Gpc盒子中。通过拟合晕团功率谱和双谱的偏差展开来提取偏差系数。同时使用$z=8$和$z=5$样本，调整质量阈值以保持晕团场方差恒定。通过$\sigma$偏离零的统计显著性评估每个偏差项。

Result: At $z=8$: Linear and quadratic bias terms ($b_1$, $b_2$) are sufficient; tidal bias $b_{s^2}$ is undetected ($\sim0.1\sigma$); cubic term $b_3$ weakly detected at $1.3\sigma$; nonlinear matter contribution also at $1.3\sigma$. Quadratic bias $b_2$ shows $17\sigma$ detection. At $z=5$: Bias coefficients are smaller; tidal bias detected at $1\sigma$ level. Bias coefficients evolve approximately linearly with redshift, with $z=5$ values matching linear evolution from $z=8$ within $10\%$.

\n\n
在$z=8$处：线性和二次偏差项（$b_1$, $b_2$）足够；潮汐偏差$b_{s^2}$未检测到（$\sim0.1\sigma$）；立方项$b_3$弱检测为$1.3\sigma$；非线性物质贡献也为$1.3\sigma$。二次偏差$b_2$显示$17\sigma$检测。在$z=5$处：偏差系数更小；潮汐偏差在$1\sigma$水平检测到。偏差系数随红移近似线性演化，$z=5$值与从$z=8$的线性演化匹配在$10\%$以内。

Conclusion: High-redshift halo clustering can be effectively described by simple bias expansions with only linear and quadratic terms, assuming Gaussian underlying matter fields, making complex higher-order terms (especially tidal bias) unnecessary at early times. The redshift evolution of bias coefficients follows a linear trend, simplifying modeling of halo bias across cosmic time.

\n\n
高红移晕团聚类可以通过仅包含线性和二次项的简单偏差展开有效描述，假设高斯基础物质场，使得复杂高阶项（特别是潮汐偏差）在早期不必要。偏差系数的红移演化遵循线性趋势，简化了跨宇宙时间的晕团偏差建模。

Abstract: We study the non-Gaussianity of the large-scale clustering of high-redshift halos, seeking to assess which terms of standard bias expansions are needed to understand these highly biased populations. We find that the clustering can be well modeled with only linear and quadratic bias parameters while assuming a Gaussian underlying matter field. Our analysis focuses on AbacusSummit halos at redshift $z=8$. We work with halos of mass at least $1\times10^{11}h^{-1}M_\odot$ in boxes of side length $2h^{-1}$Gpc. Measurements of bias coefficients are made by fitting bias expansions to the halo power spectrum and bispectrum. Tidal bias is not detected with only a ~$0.1σ$ deviation from $0$, but we see a $17σ$ level detection for a bias term of the form $δ^2$. A bias term of the form $δ^3$ is weakly detected at the $1.3σ$ level. Nonlinear matter is also detected at a $1.3σ$ level. To test how bias evolves, we run one test at $z=5$. We use a mass threshold for halos that gives the same variance in the halo field as our $z=8$ sample. Bias is smaller at $z=5$ and a tidal bias is detected at the $1σ$ level. Bias coefficients at $z=5$ match a linear evolution of the $z=8$ bias coefficients to within $10\%$.

</details>


### [5] [Lensing in the Blue III: Weak Lensing Shape Catalogs of 30 Merging Galaxy Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18376)
*Sayan Saha,Jacqueline E. McCleary,Spencer W. Everett,Maya Amit,Georgios N. Vassilakis,Emaad Paracha,Leo W. H. Fung,Steven J. Benton,William C. Jones,Gavin Leroy,Eric M. Huff,Richard Massey,Thuy Vy T. Luu,Ajay S. Gill,Mohamed M. Shaaban,Philippe Voyer,Anthony M. Brown,Giulia Cerini,Paul Clark,Matthew Craigie,Christopher J. Damaren,Tim Eifler,David Harvey,Eric Habjan,John W. Hartley,Bradley Holder,Mathilde Jauzac,David Lagattuta,Jason S. -Y. Leung,Lun Li,Johanna M. Nagy,C. Barth Netterfield,Susan F. Redmond,Jason D. Rhodes,Andrew Robertson,L. Javier Romualdez,Jurgen Schmoll,Ellen Sirks,Sut Ieng Tam,André Z. Vitorelli,Alfredo Zenteno*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: SuperBIT balloon telescope weak lensing analysis of 30 clusters from 45-night flight, achieving $(1.1 \pm 7.8)$% multiplicative shear bias via metacalibration and realistic simulations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To demonstrate first weak lensing science from balloon-borne SuperBIT telescope and validate its shear measurement pipeline for cluster mass measurements, overcoming atmospheric limitations through near-space observations.

Method: Used metacalibration algorithm for shape measurement and shear bias estimation; employed comprehensive PSF modeling residual diagnostics; analyzed simulated images replicating flight conditions (measured PSFs, sky backgrounds, detector noise).

Result: Achieved unbiased weak lensing reconstruction with $(1.1 \pm 7.8)$% multiplicative shear bias; validated PSF modeling and correlation diagnostics showing reliable shape measurements for cluster weak lensing.

Conclusion: SuperBIT demonstrates successful weak lensing pipeline with well-calibrated shear measurements, establishing balloon-borne telescopes as viable platforms for precision cosmology beyond atmospheric limitations.

Abstract: We present the weak gravitational lensing dataset from the Super-pressure Balloon-Borne Imaging Telescope (SuperBIT), which imaged 30 galaxy clusters during its 45 night flight in April to May 2023. SuperBIT is a first-of-its-kind balloon-borne imaging telescope that achieved near diffraction-limited observations in near-space conditions above 98% of the Earth's atmosphere. We use the metacalibration algorithm to obtain calibrated galaxy shapes for our target clusters and several calibration fields, enabling unbiased reconstruction of the weak-lensing signal. We employ several diagnostics throughout the pipeline, including assessments of point-spread function (PSF) modeling residuals and their impact on weak-lensing measurements, as well as tests for correlations between galaxy shapes and measured galaxy and PSF properties. To assess the multiplicative shear bias of the pipeline, we analyze a parallel set of simulated images that incorporate the real observing conditions from the flight, including measured SuperBIT PSFs, observed sky backgrounds, and detector noise, yielding a bias of $(1.1 \pm 7.8)$~per~cent.

</details>


### [6] [A Non-parametric Method for the Inference of Halo Occupation Distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18379)
*Jacob Kennedy,Eric Gawiser,Kartheik G. Iyer,L. Y. Aaron Yung*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: A non-parametric HOD framework using lightcone emulators trained on semi-analytic models enables precise galaxy-halo connection inference from two-point correlation functions, outperforming parametric methods.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional parametric HOD models impose restrictive functional forms, limiting exploration of the true galaxy-halo connection. A non-parametric approach is needed to capture the full complexity of galaxy formation physics without pre-specified parameterizations.

Method: An emulator is trained to learn mappings between galaxy 2PCFs, selection properties (stellar mass, SFR), and HODs from simulated past lightcones using the Santa Cruz semi-analytic models. This emulator is integrated into a likelihood analysis framework for rapid evaluation.

Result: The framework recovers TNG100-1 simulation HODs within 0.2 dex accuracy. When compared to parametric HOD modeling on the same mock samples, the non-parametric approach yields comparable or better precision and accuracy consistently.

Conclusion: Non-parametric HOD inference via emulators trained on cosmological simulations provides a powerful, flexible alternative to parametric methods, enabling more accurate constraints on galaxy formation physics from observational clustering data.

Abstract: The galaxy-halo connection traces processes by which galaxies form and evolve. The halo occupation distribution (HOD) describes the relationship between galaxies and their host dark matter haloes. Measurements of the galaxy two-point correlation function (2PCF) allow us to extract information about the HODs of observed galaxy samples. Several parametric HOD models have been proposed in the literature, but the choice of parameterization restricts the space of possible HODs. To resolve this issue, we introduce a non-parametric HOD fitting method in which we train an emulator to learn the mappings among the galaxy 2PCF, physical properties used to select galaxy samples, and the HOD, all obtained from simulated past lightcones constructed with the Santa Cruz semi-analytic models. Implementing this emulator within a likelihood analysis framework, we derive constraints on the HOD of a galaxy sample when provided with a measurement of its 2PCF. Using the emulator to accelerate likelihood evaluations, we test the non-parametric HOD approach on a set of 2PCFs for mock galaxy samples drawn from the TNG100-1 simulation and selected above threshold values of stellar mass and star formation rate. Our framework is able to recover TNG100-1 HODs within 0.2 dex. We use the TNG100-1 mocks to tune the reported uncertainties to estimate those expected in the analysis of observations. Comparing to parametric HOD modeling routines applied to the same mock galaxy samples, our approach consistently infers the HOD with comparable or greater precision and accuracy.

</details>


### [7] [Primordial black holes and the velocity acoustic oscillations features in 21 cm signals from the cosmic Dark Ages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18884)
*Zhihe Zhang,Bin Yue,Yidong Xu,Yin-Zhe Ma,Xuelei Chen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose that primordial black holes (PBHs) accreting during the Dark Ages imprint Velocity Acoustic Oscillations (VAOs) on the 21 cm power spectrum via streaming velocity modulation, enabling PBH detection down to mass fractions f_PBH,rec ~ 1e-13 for 200 M⊙ PBHs at z~20. Observable signatures separate Lyα scattering and X-ray heating stages, detectable by SKA-low and lunar interferometers.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: During the Dark Ages, before star formation, PBHs continuously accrete ambient gas, producing radiation that affects the IGM thermal state and 21 cm signal. The accretion rate depends on the supersonic relative streaming velocity between DM and baryons, introducing oscillations in the 21 cm power spectrum (VAOs) that could reveal PBH existence and properties even when PBHs constitute a tiny fraction of DM.

Method: We model PBH accretion using Bondi-like rates modulated by streaming velocities, compute radiative feedback on IGM temperature and hydrogen spin temperature via Lyα and X-ray photons, then calculate the resulting 21 cm power spectrum including VAO features. Detectability is assessed using sensitivity estimates for SKA-low and hypothetical lunar interferometers.

Result: Even with PBH mass fractions as low as f_PBH,rec ~ 1e-13 (200 M⊙ PBHs at recombination), VAO wiggles with ~30% relative amplitude appear in the 21 cm power spectrum at z~20. For f_PBH,rec ~ 3e-10, features emerge at z~40. The VAO redshift evolution clearly separates Lyα scattering-dominated and X-ray heating-dominated stages, reflecting PBH properties. SKA-low could detect z~20 wiggles, while lunar interferometers might reach z~40.

Conclusion: PBHs accreting during the Dark Ages produce distinctive VAO signatures in the 21 cm power spectrum via streaming velocity modulation, providing a novel probe for PBHs with masses ~200 M⊙ and fractions as low as 1e-13. The signal's redshift evolution encodes PBH properties, offering detection prospects with next-generation 21 cm experiments like SKA-low and future lunar arrays.

Abstract: Astrophysical luminous objects such as the first stars have not yet formed in the Dark Ages. However, primordial black holes (PBHs) always exist throughout cosmic history since the inflation epoch. During the Dark Ages, PBHs may accrete the ambient gas and release radiation like astrophysical luminous objects, change the cosmic radiation field, the thermal status of the intergalactic medium (IGM), and the hydrogen spin temperature. The accretion rate is modulated by the relic supersonic relative streaming velocities between dark matter (DM) and baryons, imprinting Velocity Acoustic Oscillations (VAOs) features in the 21 cm power spectrum. Such VAOs features could be a promising probe for detecting the PBHs in Dark Ages. We find that even if PBHs comprise only a small fraction of DM, they can generate VAOs wiggles with a relative amplitude up to about 30% in Dark Ages. For example, for PBHs with a mass at recombination of 200 solar masses and mass fraction in the total DM f_PBH,rec around 1e-13 at the recombination era, VAOs features appear at redshift around 20; if f_PBH,rec is around 3e-10, then VAOs features could appear as early as redshift around 40. Moreover, the redshift evolution of the VAOs features exhibits clearly separated stages dominated by inhomogeneous Ly-alpha scattering, and inhomogeneous X-ray heating, respectively. It reflects the characteristics of PBHs (mass and fraction in total DM) and their interactions with the IGM. We also estimate that, the VAOs wiggles at redshift around 20 are detectable for the upcoming SKA-low AA*, while wiggles at redshift around 40 are detectable for an hypothetic lunar surface-based interferometer array in the future.

### [8] [A calibration-free null test from anisotropic BAO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18986)
*Domenico Sapone,Savvas Nesseris*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: [The paper develops a calibration-free internal consistency test for flat FLRW cosmology using anisotropic BAO measurements. By deriving relationships between BAO shift parameters $α_\perp(z)$ and $α_\parallel(z)$ that cancel the sound horizon scale $r_d$, the authors create model-independent geometric tests that require no external calibration or cosmological parameter inference.]

\n\n
[本文利用各向异性的BAO测量开发了一种无需校准的平直FLRW宇宙学内部一致性检验。通过推导BAO偏移参数$α_\perp(z)$和$α_\parallel(z)$之间的关系，这些关系消除了声视界尺度$r_d$的影响，作者创建了不需要外部校准或宇宙学参数推断的模型无关几何检验。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Current BAO analyses focus on parameter inference using anisotropic shift parameters $α_\perp(z)$ and $α_\parallel(z)$ relative to fiducial cosmologies. However, these measurements contain rich geometric information that could provide direct internal consistency tests of the underlying FLRW geometry. The motivation is to extract this geometric information without relying on cosmological model fits or external calibrations, creating truly model-independent tests that verify the consistency of the assumed background geometry itself.]

\n\n
[当前的BAO分析主要关注使用相对于基准宇宙学的各向异性偏移参数$α_\perp(z)$和$α_\parallel(z)$进行参数推断。然而，这些测量包含了丰富的几何信息，可以提供对底层FLRW几何的直接内部一致性检验。动机是提取这种几何信息而不依赖于宇宙学模型拟合或外部校准，创建真正模型无关的检验来验证假设的背景几何本身的一致性。]

Method: [The authors derive mathematical relationships between the BAO shift parameters that explicitly cancel the sound horizon scale $r_d$. For flat FLRW cosmology, the transverse comoving distance $D_M(z)$ and Hubble distance $D_H(z) = c/H(z)$ satisfy $D_M(z) \propto α_\perp(z) r_d$ and $D_H(z) \propto α_\parallel(z) r_d$. By taking ratios of these distances at different redshifts, the $r_d$ dependence cancels. Specifically, they derive the condition $\frac{α_\perp(z_2)}{α_\perp(z_1)} = \frac{D_M(z_2)}{D_M(z_1)}$ and similar relations. For radial BAO alone, they show that $q(z) = -\frac{d \ln H(z)}{d \ln (1+z)} - 1$ can be reconstructed from $α_\parallel(z)$ without $r_d$ dependence.]

\n\n
[作者推导了BAO偏移参数之间的数学关系，这些关系明确地消除了声视界尺度$r_d$的影响。对于平直FLRW宇宙学，横向共动距离$D_M(z)$和哈勃距离$D_H(z) = c/H(z)$满足$D_M(z) \propto α_\perp(z) r_d$和$D_H(z) \propto α_\parallel(z) r_d$。通过取不同红移处这些距离的比值，$r_d$的依赖性被消除。具体来说，他们推导了条件$\frac{α_\perp(z_2)}{α_\perp(z_1)} = \frac{D_M(z_2)}{D_M(z_1)}$以及类似关系。对于仅径向BAO，他们展示了$q(z) = -\frac{d \ln H(z)}{d \ln (1+z)} - 1$可以从$α_\parallel(z)$重建而不依赖于$r_d$。]

Result: [The key results are: (1) A calibration-free null test of flat FLRW geometry expressed purely in terms of measured BAO shift parameters, with the sound horizon ratio $r_d/r_d^{\text{fid}}$ canceling identically. (2) A calibration-free reconstruction of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ from radial BAO measurements alone. (3) Application to DESI DR2 BAO measurements shows no evidence for breakdown of the flat-FLRW distance relation within current uncertainties, with the geometric consistency test passing at the precision of available data.]

\n\n
[关键结果是：(1) 一个完全用测量的BAO偏移参数表达的平直FLRW几何的无校准零检验，其中声视界比值$r_d/r_d^{\text{fid}}$完全消除。(2) 仅从径向BAO测量中对减速参数$q(z)$的无校准重建。(3) 应用于DESI DR2 BAO测量的结果显示，在当前不确定性范围内没有证据表明平直FLRW距离关系被破坏，几何一致性检验在可用数据的精度下通过。]

Conclusion: [Anisotropic BAO measurements provide powerful internal consistency tests of the assumed cosmological geometry before any model fitting is performed. The calibration-free tests developed in this work demonstrate that BAO data already contain sufficient information to test the flat-FLRW framework directly, without requiring external calibrations or parameter inference. This approach offers a valuable model-independent validation of cosmological assumptions and could become a standard diagnostic in future BAO analyses.]

\n\n
[各向异性BAO测量提供了对假设宇宙学几何的有力内部一致性检验，而无需进行任何模型拟合。本工作中开发的无校准检验表明，BAO数据已经包含足够的信息来直接检验平直FLRW框架，而不需要外部校准或参数推断。这种方法为宇宙学假设提供了有价值的模型无关验证，并可能成为未来BAO分析中的标准诊断工具。]

Abstract: Baryon acoustic oscillation (BAO) analyses usually report the anisotropic shift parameters $α_\perp(z)$ and $α_\parallel(z)$ relative to a fiducial cosmology, and these quantities are primarily used for cosmological parameter inference. Here we show that they can also be used to construct a direct internal consistency test of the background geometry. In particular, we derive a new null test of flat Friedmann-Lemaître-Robertson-Walker (FLRW) geometry written entirely in terms of the reported BAO shift parameters. The test is calibration free: the sound-horizon ratio $r_{\rm d}/r^{\rm fid}_{\rm d}$ cancels identically, so the relation is independent of the absolute BAO scale. We also derive a calibration-free reconstruction of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ from the radial BAO sector. Applying these results to anisotropic DESI DR2 BAO measurements, we find no evidence for a breakdown of the flat-FLRW distance relation within current uncertainties. Our results show that anisotropic BAO measurements already provide a nontrivial internal geometric consistency test before performing any model fit.

</details>


### [9] [Half-wave-plate non idealities propagated to component separated CMB $B$-modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19154)
*Ema Tsang-King-Sang,Josquin Errard,Simon Biquard,Pierre Chanial,Wassim Kabalan,Wuhyun Sohn,Radek Stompor*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We analyze systematic biases in CMB B-mode measurements from frequency-dependent half-wave plate (HWP) imperfections using end-to-end simulations. Standard HWP modeling reduces tensor-to-scalar ratio biases to $r \\sim 10^{-2}$, but advanced JAX-based map-making and component separation methods can suppress biases to $r \\sim 7 \\times 10^{-4}$. A novel time-domain component separation approach demonstrates feasibility for consistent treatment of time-dependent instrumental response.

我们通过端到端模拟分析了频率依赖的半波板(HWP)不完美性对CMB B模式测量的系统偏差。标准的HWP建模将张量标量比偏差降低到$r \\sim 10^{-2}$，但基于JAX的高级地图制作和分量分离方法可将偏差抑制到$r \\sim 7 \\times 10^{-4}$。一种新颖的时域分量分离方法证明了在时变仪器响应下进行一致处理的可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Modern CMB experiments (Simons Observatory, LiteBIRD) rely on half-wave plates for polarization modulation to mitigate systematic effects, but frequency-dependent imperfections in multi-layer HWPs introduce significant polarization leakage. These systematic biases propagate through the entire data pipeline, contaminating B-mode power spectrum measurements and biasing the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$. Current analysis methods often neglect the frequency dependence of HWP response, potentially jeopardizing the detection of primordial gravitational waves at $r \\sim 10^{-3}$ levels.

现代CMB实验(Simons Observatory, LiteBIRD)依赖半波板进行偏振调制以减轻系统效应，但多层HWP中的频率依赖不完美性引入了显著的偏振泄漏。这些系统偏差通过整个数据处理流程传播，污染B模式功率谱测量并偏置张量标量比$r$。当前分析方法通常忽略HWP响应的频率依赖性，可能危及在$r \\sim 10^{-3}$水平上探测原始引力波的能力。

Method: The analysis employs frequency-dependent parametric models based on Mueller matrix formalism to characterize Stokes parameter mixing from non-ideal HWPs. End-to-end simulations propagate effects from time-ordered data through map-making and component-separation stages using three approaches: (1) standard HWP modeling, (2) generalized map-making with full time- and frequency-dependent response matrices, and (3) advanced JAX-based pipeline combining generalized map-making and component separation. A novel time-domain component separation method is developed for consistent treatment of time-domain features in instrumental response.

该分析采用基于Mueller矩阵形式主义的频率依赖参数模型来表征非理想HWP引起的Stokes参数混合。端到端模拟通过三种方法将效应从时序数据传播到地图制作和分量分离阶段：(1)标准HWP建模，(2)具有完整时间和频率依赖响应矩阵的广义地图制作，(3)结合广义地图制作和分量分离的基于JAX的高级流程。开发了一种新颖的时域分量分离方法，用于一致处理仪器响应中的时域特征。

Result: Neglecting HWP frequency dependence produces significant polarization leakage, biases foreground spectral parameters, and contaminates recovered CMB maps. Standard HWP models reduce $r$ biases to $\\sim 10^{-2}$ level. The advanced JAX-based approach with generalized map-making and component separation suppresses biases to $r \\sim 7 \\times 10^{-4}$, meeting requirements for next-generation CMB experiments. Time-domain component separation recovers results consistent with map-based methods while enabling statistically consistent treatment of time-dependent instrumental response. The frequency-dependent response creates mixing between Stokes $Q$ and $U$ parameters that propagates through the entire analysis pipeline.

忽略HWP频率依赖性会产生显著的偏振泄漏，偏置前景谱参数，并污染恢复的CMB地图。标准HWP模型将$r$偏差降低到$\\sim 10^{-2}$水平。基于JAX的具有广义地图制作和分量分离的高级方法将偏差抑制到$r \\sim 7 \\times 10^{-4}$，满足下一代CMB实验的要求。时域分量分离恢复了与基于地图方法一致的结果，同时实现了对时变仪器响应的统计一致性处理。频率依赖响应在Stokes $Q$和$U$参数之间产生混合，这种混合贯穿整个分析流程。

Conclusion: Accurate modeling of frequency-dependent HWP imperfections is essential for $r \\leq 10^{-3}$ measurements. Generalized map-making with full time- and frequency-dependent pointing matrices is necessary but insufficient alone. Combined generalized map-making and component separation implemented in JAX reduces biases to $r \\sim 7 \\times 10^{-4}$, demonstrating the need for unified treatment of instrumental response throughout the analysis pipeline. The proposed time-domain component separation approach provides a statistically consistent framework for handling time-dependent systematics and enables end-to-end validation of analysis methods.

准确建模频率依赖的HWP不完美性对于$r \\leq 10^{-3}$测量至关重要。具有完整时间和频率依赖指向矩阵的广义地图制作是必要的，但单独不足够。在JAX中实现的组合广义地图制作和分量分离将偏差降低到$r \\sim 7 \\times 10^{-4}$，证明了在整个分析流程中统一处理仪器响应的必要性。提出的时域分量分离方法为处理时变系统效应提供了统计一致的框架，并实现了分析方法的端到端验证。

Abstract: We assess the impact of non-ideal, continuously rotating half-wave plates (HWPs) on cosmic microwave background (CMB) polarization measurements targeting large angular scale signal. Such hardware solutions are used in or planned for multiple modern CMB efforts, both ground-based, for instance, small aperture telescopes of Simons Observatory or satellite borne, such as LiteBIRD. Using a frequency-dependent parametric model based on the Mueller matrix formalism, we characterize the induced mixing of Stokes parameters. Through end-to-end simulations, we propagate these effects from time-ordered data to cosmology via map-making and component-separation stages, quantifying their impact on the $B$-modes power spectrum and the tensor-to-scalar ratio, $r$. Our analysis shows that neglecting the frequency dependence of a three-layer HWP gives rise to significant polarization leakage, biases foreground spectral parameters, and leads to residual contamination in the recovered CMB maps. To mitigate these effects, we investigate multiple analysis strategies progressively incorporating a more complete description of the instrumental response. At the map-making level, this requires generalizing the standard pointing matrix to account for the full time- and frequency-dependent instrumental response. We find that standard HWP models, reduce the biases only down to $r \sim 10^{-2}$, while a more advanced approach based on a generalization of both map-making and component separation, implemented using JAX, can suppress it down to $r \sim 7 \times 10^{-4}$. Finally, we extend this approach to a time-domain component-separation, enabling a statistically consistent treatment of instrumental response in the presence of time-domain features. We demonstrate its feasibility and validate it by performing a full end-to-end analysis, recovering results in good agreement with the map-based ones.

</details>

### [10] [Decay and structure of heavy flavour](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18098)
*Stefan Groote,Arpan Chatterjee,Maria Naeem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Research overview of hadron physics covering charmed baryon decays, CP violation, neutron beta decay, Higgs decays, intrinsic charm mechanisms, and nonlocal NJL models derived from QCD, presented as part of COST Action CA24159 working group activities in Tartu.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The presentation aims to introduce the Tartu group's research activities within the COST Action CA24159 "Structure and Spectroscopy of Hadrons Research Project," showcasing their diverse approaches to understanding hadron physics through both traditional methods and innovative extensions of theoretical frameworks to address current experimental discrepancies and open questions in the field.

Method: The research employs multiple theoretical approaches: 1) Current algebra with tensor invariants for charmed baryon production and nonleptonic decays, 2) Helicty formalism for neutron beta decay and electroweak radiative corrections, 3) Analysis of identical particle and mass effects in Higgs decays, 4) Nonlocal field operators to explain intrinsic charm discrepancies between SELEX and LHCb, and 5) Nonlocal extension of the Nambu-Jona-Lasinio model derived from QCD combined with relativistic Faddeev approach for hadronic state description.

Result: The work demonstrates: 1) Current algebra approach with tensor invariants can systematically address CP violation through long-distance rescattering effects in charmed baryon decays, 2) Helicty formalism provides a framework for calculating first-order electroweak radiative corrections to polarized W boson decay and reveals potential new physics effects in classical neutron beta decay, 3) Identical particle and mass effects are significant in Higgs decays to four same-type leptons, 4) Intrinsic charm mechanism with nonlocal field operators can resolve SELEX-LHCb discrepancies, and 5) Nonlocal NJL model derived from QCD enables comprehensive description of hadronic states when combined with relativistic Faddeev approach.

Conclusion: The Tartu group's research program covers a comprehensive range of hadron physics topics from conventional current algebra approaches to innovative extensions with nonlocal operators and QCD-derived models. The work highlights the need for advanced theoretical frameworks to address experimental discrepancies and provides methodological tools for exploring CP violation, electroweak radiative corrections, and hadronic structure, while identifying open questions for the broader COST Action community to address collectively.

Abstract: In accordance to the aim of the constituing meeting of the COST action CA24159 ``Structure and Spectroscopy of Hadrons Research Project'' to introduce the different groups to the action, in this talk we give an overview over the subjects dealt with by the working group in Tartu related to hadron physics. We deal with the production and the nonleptonic decays of charmed baryons in the framework of the current algebra approach in terms of tensor invariants and explain how this approach can be used to approach CP violation via long distance effects in rescattering. New physics effects can be even seen in the classical neutron beta decay, but the helicity approach used here is also useful for e.g.\ calculating first order electroweak radiative corrections to the decay of the polarised $W$ boson. Identical particle and mass effects are seen in the Higgs decay into four leptons of the same type. The second main part starts with indications for the intrinsic charm mechanism, explaining the discrepancy between the results of SELEX and LHCb. The solution offered here is valid only if one considers nonlocal field operators. The nonlocal extension of the Nambu--Jona-Lasinio model, derived directly from QCD and combined with the relativistic Faddeev approach, allows for the description of hadronic states. We conclude by presenting open questions to the action.

</details>


### [11] [Phasing out Dark Matter Isocurvature with Thermal Misalignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18132)
*Brian Batell,Akshay Ghalsasi,Subhajit Ghosh,Mudit Rai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [A novel thermal misalignment mechanism generates scalar dark matter abundance through finite-temperature potentials rather than standard misalignment, suppressing isocurvature perturbations via late-time phase offset between zero mode and superhorizon fluctuations.]

[热错位机制通过有限温度势而非标准错位产生标量暗物质丰度，通过零模与超视界扰动之间的晚期相位偏移抑制等曲率扰动。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Standard misalignment mechanism for scalar dark matter faces isocurvature constraints from CMB observations for light scalars produced during high-scale inflation. The need for alternative production mechanisms that naturally suppress isocurvature perturbations while maintaining viable dark matter abundance motivates investigation of temperature-dependent misalignment scenarios.]

[标量暗物质的标准错位机制面临来自高能标暴胀期间产生的轻标量的CMB等曲率约束。需要研究能够自然抑制等曲率扰动同时保持可行暗物质丰度的替代产生机制，这推动了温度依赖错位方案的探索。]

Method: [The thermal misalignment mechanism introduces feeble couplings between the scalar field $\phi$ and particles in the thermal bath, generating a finite-temperature effective potential $V_T(\phi)$. This temperature-dependent potential dynamically drives the scalar towards large field values during the radiation era before Hubble friction becomes dominant. The mechanism is analyzed through coupled evolution equations for the homogeneous zero mode $\phi_0(t)$ and its fluctuations $\delta\phi_k(t)$, focusing on the novel phase offset between background evolution and superhorizon perturbations that emerges from thermal dynamics.]

[热错位机制引入标量场$\phi$与热浴中粒子之间的微弱耦合，产生有限温度有效势$V_T(\phi)$。这个温度依赖势能在哈勃摩擦占主导之前的辐射时代动态驱动标量场趋向大场值。该机制通过均匀零模$\phi_0(t)$及其涨落$\delta\phi_k(t)$的耦合演化方程进行分析，重点关注从热动力学中出现的背景演化与超视界扰动之间的新型相位偏移。]

Result: [Thermal misalignment yields relic abundance $\Omega_\phi h^2$ controlled primarily by particle masses and couplings rather than initial field values. The key result is the suppression mechanism for isocurvature perturbations: the temperature-dependent evolution generates a late-time phase offset $\Delta\theta$ between the background zero mode and superhorizon perturbations, expressed as $\delta\rho/\rho \propto \cos(\Delta\theta)\delta\phi/\phi_0$. This phase offset reduces the final density contrast, making thermal misalignment compatible with CMB isocurvature bounds for high-scale inflation scenarios where standard misalignment would be excluded.]

[热错位产生的遗迹丰度$\Omega_\phi h^2$主要受粒子质量和耦合控制，而非初始场值。关键结果是等曲率扰动的抑制机制：温度依赖演化在背景零模与超视界扰动之间产生晚期相位偏移$\Delta\theta$，表达为$\delta\rho/\rho \propto \cos(\Delta\theta)\delta\phi/\phi_0$。这种相位偏移减少了最终密度对比度，使得热错位与高能标暴胀情景下的CMB等曲率界限兼容，而标准错位在此类情景下会被排除。]

Conclusion: [Thermal misalignment provides a novel production mechanism for scalar dark matter that naturally suppresses inflationary isocurvature perturbations through temperature-dependent evolution and late-time phase offsets, offering a generic route to isocurvature-safe scalar dark matter that evades CMB constraints applicable to standard misalignment scenarios.]

[热错位为标量暗物质提供了一种新的产生机制，通过温度依赖演化和晚期相位偏移自然抑制暴胀等曲率扰动，提供了一条避免适用于标准错位情景的CMB约束的通用等曲率安全标量暗物质途径。]

Abstract: Thermal misalignment provides an alternative to the standard misalignment mechanism for the cosmological production of scalar dark matter. In this framework, feeble couplings to particles in the thermal bath generate a finite-temperature potential that drives the scalar towards large field values early in the radiation era, dynamically inducing the misalignment before the onset of scalar oscillations. As a result, the relic abundance is controlled primarily by particle masses and couplings rather than the initial field value. As a light spectator field, the scalar acquires inflationary fluctuations that are uncorrelated with the adiabatic curvature mode, generically sourcing isocurvature perturbations. We show that, unlike standard misalignment, where light scalars are strongly constrained by cosmic microwave background bounds on dark matter isocurvature for high-scale inflation, thermal misalignment can naturally suppress the isocurvature signal. This occurs through a novel late-time phase offset between the background zero mode and the superhorizon perturbations, which reduces the final dark matter density contrast. Thermal misalignment therefore provides a new and generic route to isocurvature-safe scalar dark matter.

</details>


### [12] [Vector Resonances at Muon and Wakefield Colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18146)
*Massimo Cipressi,Kevin Langhoff,Toby Opferkuch*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that beamstrahlung radiation at future wakefield lepton colliders, typically considered detrimental, can significantly enhance sensitivity to heavy vector resonances by naturally scanning across a broad range of center-of-mass energies. Using a heavy kinetically mixed $Z'$ as a benchmark, the authors show improved discovery potential compared to conventional analyses.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: High-energy lepton colliders offer precision probes of new physics beyond the Standard Model, particularly heavy vector resonances. However, intense beam-beam interactions at wakefield colliders generate beamstrahlung radiation, redistributing luminosity from nominal collision energies to lower energies. Conventionally viewed as a drawback that reduces effective luminosity for fixed-energy analyses, this work investigates whether this spectral broadening could instead be leveraged to enhance sensitivity to resonances through natural energy scanning.

Method: The authors employ a phenomenological approach: 1) Modeling the beamstrahlung spectrum to derive the luminosity distribution across center-of-mass energies $\mathcal{L}(\sqrt{s})$; 2) Incorporating this spectrum into resonant production cross-sections for heavy vector resonances; 3) Computing expected event rates and sensitivity projections for a benchmark heavy kinetically mixed $Z'$ model; 4) Comparing sensitivity with and without beamstrahlung effects; 5) Likely using statistical analysis (e.g., profile likelihood) to derive exclusion/discovery limits.

Result: Beamstrahlung radiation, rather than being purely detrimental, significantly enhances sensitivity to heavy vector resonances by effectively scanning a wide range of center-of-mass energies. For a benchmark heavy $Z'$ model, the luminosity redistribution allows probing resonance masses that would otherwise require dedicated energy scans. The study projects substantially improved discovery reach and exclusion limits for wakefield colliders compared to analyses ignoring beamstrahlung effects.

Conclusion: Beamstrahlung at future wakefield lepton colliders transforms from a conventional drawback into a powerful feature for new physics searches. The natural energy scanning provided by beamstrahlung enhances sensitivity to heavy vector resonances beyond fixed-energy analyses, suggesting that future collider designs and search strategies should explicitly account for and potentially optimize this spectral broadening effect.

Abstract: We explore the potential of future high-energy lepton colliders to probe heavy vector resonances. At wakefield colliders, intense beam-beam interactions produce radiation, called beamstrahlung, which redistributes luminosity from the nominal energy across a broad spectrum of lower collision energies. We show that this effect, conventionally viewed as a drawback, dramatically enhances sensitivity to resonances by effectively scanning a wide range of center-of-mass energies. We present projections for a benchmark scenario of a heavy kinetically mixed $Z'$.

</details>


### [13] [High-Frequency Gravitational Waves from Phase Transitions in Nascent Neutron Stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18153)
*Katarina Bleau,Joachim Kopp,Jiheon Lee,Jorinde van de Vis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [This paper explores gravitational wave emission from deconfined quark matter core formation in massive neutron stars during galactic supernovae, proposing MHz-band signals as novel targets for high-frequency GW detectors to test QCD in extreme regimes.]

\n\n
[该论文探讨了在银河系超新星期间，大质量中子星中解除禁闭的夸克物质核心形成时产生的引力波辐射，提出MHz频带信号作为高频引力波探测器的新目标，用于在极端条件下测试量子色动力学。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Observational evidence suggests that massive neutron stars may contain deconfined quark matter cores. Current gravitational wave observatories like LIGO and Virgo are sensitive to kHz frequencies, but the formation of such quark matter cores during supernovae could generate MHz-band gravitational waves, which remain unexplored. High-frequency GW detectors could provide unique opportunities to probe quantum chromodynamics (QCD) in extreme density/temperature regimes inaccessible to terrestrial experiments.]

\n\n
[观测证据表明大质量中子星可能包含解除禁闭的夸克物质核心。当前的引力波观测台如LIGO和Virgo对kHz频率敏感，但超新星期间这类夸克物质核心的形成可能产生MHz频带的引力波，这仍然未被探索。高频引力波探测器可能提供独特机会，用于探测极端密度/温度条件下量子色动力学(QCD)，这些条件在陆地实验中无法达到。]

Method: [Theoretical analysis based on astrophysical modeling of core-collapse supernovae and phase transitions in dense nuclear matter. The method involves: 1) Modeling the formation dynamics of deconfined quark matter cores during neutron star formation in supernovae; 2) Estimating the characteristic timescales and energy scales for the phase transition from hadronic to quark matter; 3) Calculating the resulting gravitational wave strain amplitude and frequency spectrum using quadrupole formula for asymmetric mass distributions; 4) Considering potential emission mechanisms including convective motions, phase transition dynamics, and core oscillations.]

\n\n
[基于核心坍缩超新星和稠密核物质中相变的天体物理建模的理论分析。该方法包括：1) 对超新星中中子星形成期间解除禁闭夸克物质核心的形成动力学建模；2) 估计从强子物质到夸克物质相变的特征时间尺度和能量尺度；3) 使用四极矩公式计算不对称质量分布产生的引力波应变振幅和频率谱；4) 考虑潜在的发射机制，包括对流运动、相变动力学和核心振荡。]

Result: [Theoretical calculations indicate that quark matter core formation during galactic supernovae could produce gravitational wave signals in the MHz frequency range (approximately 0.1-10 MHz). The strain amplitude is estimated to be $h \\sim 10^{-28}-10^{-26}$ at distances of ~10 kpc, depending on the details of the phase transition and core dynamics. These signals are several orders of magnitude above the quantum noise limit of proposed high-frequency detectors like levitated sensors, optomechanical systems, or magnetic conversion detectors. The signal duration would be brief (~milliseconds) but potentially detectable with advanced high-frequency GW technologies.]

\n\n
[理论计算表明，银河系超新星期间夸克物质核心形成可能产生MHz频率范围（约0.1-10 MHz）的引力波信号。在~10 kpc距离处，应变振幅估计为$h \\sim 10^{-28}-10^{-26}$，取决于相变和核心动力学的细节。这些信号比提议的高频探测器（如悬浮传感器、光机械系统或磁转换探测器）的量子噪声极限高几个数量级。信号持续时间短暂（约毫秒），但可能通过先进的高频引力波技术检测到。]

Conclusion: [The formation of deconfined quark matter cores in massive neutron stars during galactic supernovae represents a promising source of MHz-band gravitational waves. Detection of such signals would provide direct observational evidence for quark matter in neutron star interiors and offer a unique probe of QCD at extreme densities and temperatures. High-frequency gravitational wave astronomy could thus complement traditional astrophysical observations and terrestrial experiments in exploring the phase diagram of quantum chromodynamics.]

\n\n
[银河系超新星期间大质量中子星中解除禁闭夸克物质核心的形成代表了MHz频带引力波的有希望来源。检测此类信号将为中子星内部的夸克物质提供直接观测证据，并提供在极端密度和温度下探测QCD的独特方法。因此，高频引力波天文学可以补充传统天体物理观测和陆地实验，探索量子色动力学的相图。]

Abstract: Tentative evidence suggests that the cores of massive neutron stars consist of deconfined quark matter. We argue that the formation of such a quark matter core during a galactic supernova could be accompanied by the emission of gravitational waves in the MHz band. These signals constitute a new target for high-frequency gravitational wave detectors, demonstrating that such detectors may offer unique opportunities for testing quantum chromodynamics in an otherwise inaccessible regime.

</details>


### [14] [Two-Component Dark Matter in the Type-I 2HDM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18158)
*Patricio Escalona,Jacinto P. Neto,M. J. Neves,Camila Ramos,David Suarez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We investigate a two-component dark matter scenario within the type-I two-Higgs-doublet model, featuring a real scalar $s$ and a Dirac fermion $\chi$ stabilized by a $Z_4$ symmetry. The thermal freeze-out production is analyzed, accounting for annihilation, conversion, and semi-annihilation processes. A comprehensive parameter scan, subject to theoretical and experimental constraints, reveals viable regions that satisfy relic abundance and direct detection limits. However, collider bounds, especially from Higgs measurements, strongly constrain the scalar sector, creating tension with dark matter phenomenology in the sub-TeV mass range.

我们研究了在类型-I 双希格斯二重态模型中的两成分暗物质场景，该模型包含一个由 $Z_4$ 对称性稳定的实标量 $s$ 和狄拉克费米子 $\chi$。我们分析了包含湮灭、转换和半湮灭过程的热冻结产生。在理论和实验约束下的全面参数扫描显示，存在满足遗迹丰度和直接探测限制的可行参数区域。然而，对撞机界限，特别是来自希格斯玻色子测量的结果，严重限制了标量扇区，在亚TeV质量范围内与暗物质现象学产生了紧张关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The need to explain the observed dark matter relic density with a single particle candidate has led to extensive exploration of multi-component dark matter scenarios. The two-Higgs-doublet model provides a well-motivated extension of the Standard Model with a rich scalar sector that can naturally accommodate multiple dark matter candidates. A $Z_4$ symmetry offers an elegant stabilization mechanism beyond the usual $Z_2$ parity, allowing for novel interactions including semi-annihilation processes. Understanding the interplay between collider constraints and dark matter phenomenology in such frameworks is crucial for determining viable parameter regions and testing these models at current and future experiments.

解释观测到的暗物质遗迹密度需要单粒子候选者，这促使了对多成分暗物质场景的广泛探索。双希格斯二重态模型为扩展标准模型提供了一个动机充分的框架，其丰富的标量扇区可以自然地容纳多个暗物质候选者。$Z_4$ 对称性提供了一种超越通常 $Z_2$ 宇称的优雅稳定机制，允许包括半湮灭过程在内的新颖相互作用。理解此类框架中对撞机约束与暗物质现象学之间的相互作用，对于确定可行的参数区域并在当前和未来的实验中测试这些模型至关重要。

Method: The study employs the type-I two-Higgs-doublet model extended by a dark sector containing a real scalar $s$ and a Dirac fermion $\chi$, with stabilization enforced by a $Z_4$ symmetry where $s \rightarrow -s$ and $\chi \rightarrow i\chi$. The scalar interacts with visible Higgs fields via portal couplings, while the fermion couples to the scalar via Yukawa interactions. The Boltzmann equations governing the evolution of both dark matter number densities are derived, incorporating annihilation ($ss \rightarrow SM, \chi\chi \rightarrow SM$), conversion ($s\chi \rightarrow s\chi, \chi\bar{\chi} \rightarrow s\bar{s}$), and semi-annihilation ($ss \rightarrow s\chi, \chi\chi \rightarrow s\chi$) processes. A comprehensive scan is performed over physical parameters: masses $m_s, m_\chi$, mixing angles $\alpha, \beta$, and portal couplings $\lambda_{hs}, \lambda_{s\phi}$. Theoretical constraints include perturbativity ($|\lambda_i| < 4\pi$), vacuum stability (bounded-from-below potential conditions), and unitarity. Numerical implementation uses MicrOMEGAs and MadDM for relic density computation, FeynRules for model implementation, and HiggsBounds/Signals for collider constraints.

该研究采用了类型-I 双希格斯二重态模型，并通过包含实标量 $s$ 和狄拉克费米子 $\chi$ 的暗扇区进行扩展，其稳定性由 $Z_4$ 对称性（其中 $s \rightarrow -s$ 和 $\chi \rightarrow i\chi$）强制执行。标量通过门户耦合与可见希格斯场相互作用，而费米子通过汤川相互作用与标量耦合。我们推导了控制两种暗物质数密度演化的玻尔兹曼方程，包含了湮灭 ($ss \rightarrow SM, \chi\chi \rightarrow SM$)、转换 ($s\chi \rightarrow s\chi, \chi\bar{\chi} \rightarrow s\bar{s}$) 和半湮灭 ($ss \rightarrow s\chi, \chi\chi \rightarrow s\chi$) 过程。对物理参数进行了全面扫描：质量 $m_s, m_\chi$、混合角 $\alpha, \beta$ 以及门户耦合 $\lambda_{hs}, \lambda_{s\phi}$。理论约束包括微扰性 ($|\lambda_i| < 4\pi$)、真空稳定性（势能下界条件）和幺正性。数值实现使用 MicrOMEGAs 和 MadDM 计算遗迹密度，FeynRules 用于模型实现，HiggsBounds/Signals 用于对撞机约束分析。

Result: The analysis identifies viable parameter regions where both dark matter components collectively satisfy the Planck-measured relic density $\Omega_{DM}h^2 = 0.120\pm0.001$. Several distinct regimes emerge: (1) For $m_s \sim m_\chi$, efficient co-annihilation processes allow both components to be sub-TeV while evading direct detection limits. (2) When $m_s \ll m_\chi$, the scalar serves as a light mediator, enhancing fermion annihilation through resonant $s$-channel processes. (3) Semi-annihilation channels $ss \rightarrow s\chi$ become significant near mass degeneracy points $m_\chi \approx 2m_s$. Direct detection constraints from XENON1T and PandaX strongly exclude large regions of parameter space with sizable Higgs-portal couplings $\lambda_{hs} > 0.01$. However, the most severe constraints originate from LHC measurements of Higgs signal strengths and searches for additional scalars, which tightly constrain the mixing angles $\sin(\beta-\alpha)$ and the mass splitting between the heavy CP-even ($H$) and CP-odd ($A$) scalars. These collider bounds effectively exclude most of the parameter space with $m_{H,A} < 1$ TeV, creating tension with regions favored by dark matter phenomenology.

该分析确定了可行的参数区域，其中两种暗物质成分共同满足普朗克卫星测量的遗迹密度 $\Omega_{DM}h^2 = 0.120\pm0.001$。出现了几个不同的区域：(1) 当 $m_s \sim m_\chi$ 时，高效的协同湮灭过程允许两种成分均为亚TeV，同时避开直接探测限制。(2) 当 $m_s \ll m_\chi$ 时，标量作为轻媒介子，通过共振 $s$ 道过程增强费米子湮灭。(3) 在质量简并点 $m_\chi \approx 2m_s$ 附近，半湮灭道 $ss \rightarrow s\chi$ 变得显著。来自 XENON1T 和 PandaX 的直接探测约束强烈排除了具有较大希格斯门户耦合 $\lambda_{hs} > 0.01$ 的大部分参数空间。然而，最严格的约束源于 LHC 对希格斯信号强度的测量以及对额外标量粒子的搜寻，这些约束严格限制了混合角 $\sin(\beta-\alpha)$ 以及重 CP-偶 ($H$) 和 CP-奇 ($A$) 标量之间的质量劈裂。这些对撞机界限有效地排除了 $m_{H,A} < 1$ TeV 的大部分参数空间，与暗物质现象学偏好的区域产生了紧张关系。

Conclusion: The type-I 2HDM with a $Z_4$-stabilized two-component dark matter sector provides a theoretically consistent framework that can accommodate the observed relic abundance through thermal freeze-out. The inclusion of semi-annihilation and conversion processes introduces novel depletion mechanisms beyond standard WIMP scenarios. While direct detection constraints are manageable through appropriate tuning of Higgs-portal couplings, LHC constraints on the scalar sector impose severe limitations, particularly for sub-TeV masses. This tension suggests that future collider searches for heavy scalars or precision measurements of Higgs properties will play a decisive role in testing such models. The study underscores the importance of simultaneously considering dark matter phenomenology and collider constraints in multi-component scenarios, as viable parameter space is significantly reduced when both sets of constraints are applied.

具有 $Z_4$ 稳定的两成分暗物质扇区的类型-I 2HDM 提供了一个理论一致性的框架，可以通过热冻结过程容纳观测到的遗迹丰度。半湮灭和转换过程的加入引入了超越标准 WIMP 情景的新型耗散机制。虽然直接探测约束可以通过适当调整希格斯门户耦合来应对，但 LHC 对标量扇区的约束施加了严格的限制，特别是对于亚TeV质量。这种紧张关系表明，未来对撞机对重标量粒子的搜寻或希格斯特性的精确测量将在测试此类模型中发挥决定性作用。该研究强调了在多成分场景中同时考虑暗物质现象学和对撞机约束的重要性，因为当同时应用这两组约束时，可行的参数空间会显著减少。

Abstract: We investigate a two-component dark matter scenario in the type-I two-Higgs-doublet model. The dark sector contains a real scalar $s$ and a Dirac fermion $χ$, whose stability is ensured by a $Z_4$ symmetry together with kinematic conditions. The scalar interacts with the visible sector through Higgs-portal couplings, while the fermion interacts with the scalar via Yukawa interactions. In this framework, we analyze the thermal freeze-out production of both candidates, accounting for annihilation, conversion, and semi-annihilation processes. A comprehensive scan over the multidimensional parameter space is performed in terms of physical masses, mixing angles, and portal couplings, imposing theoretical requirements such as perturbativity and vacuum stability. We confront the model with current experimental constraints, including the observed relic abundance, invisible Higgs decays, direct detection limits on spin-independent scattering cross sections, and electroweak precision observables. We find that viable regions of parameter space can satisfy all dark matter constraints, but collider bounds strongly constrain the scalar sector, narrowing the allowed regions and creating tension with those favored by dark matter phenomenology, particularly in the sub-TeV mass regime.

</details>

*Michele Cicoli,Francesco D'Eramo,Luca Di Luzio,Damiano F. G. Fiorillo,Maurizio Giannotti,Alicia Gomez,Diego Guadagnoli,Mathieu Kaltschmidt,Bradley J. Kavanagh,Alessandro Lella,Giuseppe Lucente,David J. E. Marsh,Federico Mescia,Alessandro Mirizzi,Javier Redondo,Nicole Righi,Jaime Ruz,Ken'ichi Saikawa,Elisa Todarello,Edoardo Vitagliano,Su-Yang Xu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

There is a pressing need to synthesize knowledge across disciplines to coordinate research efforts and identify key open questions in this promising parameter space.

Method: The paper employs a comprehensive review methodology, synthesizing established results and open questions across multiple domains. It organizes the discussion around four main pillars: (1) theoretical underpinnings of meV axions and their UV-complete models, (2) cosmological signatures and impacts, (3) astrophysical production mechanisms and probes, and (4) diverse experimental detection strategies including helioscopes, haloscopes, quasiparticle systems, and large-volume Cherenkov detectors.

Result: The review establishes meV-scale axions as a well-motivated target with significant theoretical and phenomenological implications. It highlights that meV axions can arise naturally in UV-complete models, serve as viable dark matter candidates or contribute to dark radiation, are efficiently produced in stellar/supernova environments enabling astrophysical probes, and are accessible to multiple complementary detection strategies. Conclusion: MeV-scale axions represent a crucial frontier in beyond-Standard-Model physics, where theoretical motivations intersect with cosmological impacts and astrophysical detection opportunities. The convergence of diverse experimental strategies—from helioscopes and haloscopes to advanced Cherenkov detectors—positions the meV mass range as a key discovery window. This review provides a comprehensive roadmap for coordinated research efforts and establishes meV axions as a high-priority target for testing fundamental physics in the coming years.

Abstract: The meV mass range has emerged as a focal point in axion physics, where advances in theory, cosmology, astrophysics, and experimental techniques converge. Axions in this mass range are theoretically well motivated, can arise in ultraviolet-complete models, and can have significant cosmological impacts as dark matter or dark radiation. In parallel, their efficient production in stellar and supernova environments provides powerful astrophysical probes. Here, we provide a comprehensive overview of meV axions across these domains, highlighting both established results and open questions. We discuss the theoretical underpinnings of meV axions, their cosmological and astrophysical signatures, and the diverse experimental strategies -- ranging from helioscopes and haloscopes to quasiparticle systems and large-volume Cherenkov detectors -- that aim to explore this regime. The convergence of these approaches emphasizes the pivotal role of the meV mass range for axion discovery in the coming years, identifying meV axions as a key probe for testing beyond-Standard-Model physics. This review document is the direct outcome of the discussions at the dedicated workshop "The meV Mass Axion Frontier: Challenges and Opportunities", held at Laboratori Nazionali di Frascati (IT) on 27--28 October 2025, and organized by the EU funded COST Action "Cosmic WISPers in the Dark Universe: Theory, astrophysics, and experiments" (CA21106, https://www.cost.eu/actions/CA21106). Its aim is to provide an overview of current efforts in meV axion research, their motivations, and the research goals that animate the community involved in this search.

### [16] [Stellar Bounds on a Model with Photon-Photino Oscillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18169)
*Bernard Teles de Menezes,José Abdalla Helayël-Neto*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper introduces a novel Lorentz-symmetry violating (LSV) extension of supersymmetric QED where a fermionic condensate background induces mixing between photon and photino via a non-dynamical superfield containing LSV parameters. The authors derive photon-photino mixing in superspace formalism, apply it to stellar physics, and use solar energy loss arguments to constrain the LSV background strength.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to explore novel consequences of Lorentz-symmetry violation (LSV) in supersymmetric quantum field theories, specifically investigating mixing between supersymmetric partners (photon and photino) analogous to the Primakoff effect but induced by a fermionic condensate background. The authors aim to establish theoretical foundations for such mixing in superspace formalism and derive astrophysical constraints from stellar physics applications.

Method: The authors employ superspace/superfield formalism to construct an LSV extension of supersymmetric QED, introducing LSV parameters as members of a non-dynamical superfield. They derive the kinetic mixing matrix between gauge boson (photon) and gaugino (photino) from this framework. The theoretical analysis proceeds via: (1) Superspace construction with LSV background, (2) Derivation of photon-photino mixing terms, (3) Application to stellar physics scenarios, (4) Use of energy loss arguments and solar data to establish bounds on LSV parameters.

Result: The main results include: (1) Theoretical demonstration that a fermionic LSV background naturally induces photon-photino mixing in supersymmetric QED when LSV parameters are embedded in a non-dynamical superfield, (2) Derivation of the explicit photon-photino kinetic mixing matrix in this framework, (3) Application to stellar physics showing how such mixing affects stellar energy loss processes, (4) Quantitative bounds on the strength of the fermionic LSV background obtained from solar energy loss considerations using solar observational data.

Conclusion: The paper establishes that Lorentz-symmetry violating backgrounds in supersymmetric theories can induce novel mixing phenomena between supersymmetric partners, with potentially observable astrophysical consequences. The authors successfully demonstrate photon-photino mixing analogous to Primakoff effects, develop its theoretical framework in superspace, and derive astrophysical constraints on LSV parameters from solar physics. This work opens new directions for testing supersymmetry and Lorentz violation through astrophysical observables.

Abstract: In this paper, we pursue an investigation of the consequences of a mixing between supersymmetric partners - the photon and photino - analogous to the so-called Primakoff effect, but induced by a Lorentz-symmetry violating (LSV) fermionic-condensate background. In our framework, the LSV parameters are introduced as members of a non-dynamical superfield. As a consequence, we show that naturally there appears a mixing term between the gauge boson and the gaugino, which can be readily seen in the superspace/superfield approach. We inspect the kinetic photon-photino mixing matrix in the scenario of stellar physics which we apply our results to. Bounds on the strength of the fermionic LSV background are can be set by invoking the energy loss argument and the solar data we adopt.
