### [17] [Nuclear transverse momentum dependent gluon density at low $x$ and inclusive soft hadron production in proton-lead collisions at LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18312)
*A. V. Lipatov,G. I. Lykasov,M. A. Malyshev*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper develops a modified quark-gluon string model extended to proton-nucleus collisions by incorporating nuclear modifications of TMD gluon densities based on geometric scaling from nucleons to nuclei, enabling improved description of soft hadron production at low transverse momentum in LHC proton-lead collisions.

本文通过结合基于从核子到核的几何标度的TMD胶子密度的核修正，发展了一种扩展至质子-核碰撞的修正夸克-胶子弦模型，从而能够更好地描述LHC质子-铅碰撞中低横向动量的软强子产生。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to provide a consistent theoretical framework for describing inclusive soft hadron production in proton-nucleus collisions at LHC energies, particularly in the low-$p_T$ region where traditional perturbative QCD approaches face challenges. The authors seek to extend their previously successful quark-gluon string model, which provided simultaneous description of HERA and LHC data for $pp$, $ep$, and $\gamma p$ processes, to $pA$ collisions by incorporating nuclear modifications of TMD gluon densities.

动机是为LHC能量下质子-核碰撞中的包含性软强子产生提供一个一致的理论框架，特别是在传统微扰QCD方法面临挑战的低$p_T$区域。作者寻求将他们先前成功的夸克-胶子弦模型扩展到$pA$碰撞中，该模型通过结合TMD胶子密度的核修正，能够同时描述HERA和LHC的$pp$、$ep$和$\gamma p$过程数据。

Method: The methodology extends the modified quark-gluon string model (QGSM) to proton-nucleus interactions by incorporating nuclear modifications of transverse momentum dependent (TMD) gluon densities in a proton. The nuclear modification is based on the well-established property of geometric scaling from nucleons to nuclei. The approach focuses on the small-$x$ and low-scale region relevant for soft hadron production. Theoretical calculations are performed for transverse momentum spectra of pions and kaons at $p_T \leq 1$ GeV in proton-lead collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 5.02$ TeV.

该方法通过结合质子中横向动量依赖(TMD)胶子密度的核修正，将修正夸克-胶子弦模型(QGSM)扩展至质子-核相互作用。核修正基于从核子到核的几何标度这一成熟特性。该方法专注于与软强子产生相关的小$x$和低标度区域。理论计算针对$\sqrt{s} = 5.02$ TeV的质子-铅碰撞中$p_T \leq 1$ GeV的π介子和K介子的横向动量谱进行。

Result: The calculations predict transverse momentum spectra of pions and kaons in proton-lead collisions at $\sqrt{s} = 5.02$ TeV for $p_T \leq 1$ GeV. These predictions are compared with experimental data from CMS, ATLAS, and ALICE collaborations. The key finding is that the developed approach provides a better description of low-$p_T$ data compared to predictions from other theoretical groups. The framework successfully reproduces the nuclear modification effects observed in $pA$ collisions using the geometric scaling ansatz for TMD gluon densities.

计算结果预测了$\sqrt{s} = 5.02$ TeV的质子-铅碰撞中$p_T \leq 1$ GeV的π介子和K介子的横向动量谱。这些预测与CMS、ATLAS和ALICE合作组的实验数据进行了比较。关键发现是，与其他理论组的预测相比，所发展的方法能够更好地描述低$p_T$数据。该框架利用TMD胶子密度的几何标度假定，成功地再现了在$pA$碰撞中观测到的核修正效应。

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that extending the modified quark-gluon string model to proton-nucleus collisions through nuclear modifications of TMD gluon densities based on geometric scaling provides an effective framework for describing soft hadron production at low transverse momenta. The approach outperforms other theoretical predictions in describing LHC proton-lead collision data, validating the geometric scaling ansatz for nuclear modifications and offering a consistent theoretical description that bridges HERA and LHC physics.

该论文表明，通过基于几何标度的TMD胶子密度的核修正将修正夸克-胶子弦模型扩展至质子-核碰撞，为描述低横向动量的软强子产生提供了一个有效框架。该方法在描述LHC质子-铅碰撞数据方面优于其他理论预测，验证了核修正的几何标度假定，并提供了一个连接HERA和LHC物理的一致理论描述。

Abstract: We report the results of calculations of inclusive soft hadron production in proton-lead collisions at the LHC in the framework of modified quark-gluon string model (QGSM) extended to $pA$ interactions. Our consideration involves the nuclear modification of previously proposed transverse momentum dependent (TMD, or unintegrated) gluon density in a proton, which provides a self-consistent simultaneous description of numerous HERA and LHC data on $pp$, $ep$ and $γp$ processes. Such nuclear modification is based on well established property of geometrical scaling from nucleons to nuclei. Focusing on the region of small $x$ and low scales, we obtain predictions for transverse momentum spectra of pions and kaons at $p_T \leq 1$~GeV. Our results are compared with recent data reported by the CMS, ATLAS and ALICE Collaborations at $\sqrt s = 5.02$~TeV. We find that the developed approach provides a better description of low-$p_T$ data than the predictions made by other groups.

</details>


### [18] [QCD and electroweak phase transitions with hidden scale invariance: implications for primordial black holes, quark-lepton nuggets and gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18406)
*Joshua Cesca,Archil Kobakhidze*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the cosmological implications of a minimal scale-invariant extension of the Standard Model featuring a light dilaton. The framework naturally explains the Planck-electroweak hierarchy and predicts that the Higgs field remains in the symmetric phase until a late first-order QCD chiral phase transition at ~28 MeV, which then triggers the electroweak phase transition. This novel cosmological history has significant consequences for primordial black hole formation, low-frequency gravitational waves, and the production of multi-quark/lepton nuggets.

该论文探讨了一个包含轻标度子(dilaton)的最小标度不变性扩展标准模型的宇宙学含义。该框架自然地解释了普朗克尺度与电弱尺度之间的层级问题，并预言希格斯场将保持对称相直至约28 MeV的晚期一级QCD手征相变，后者随后触发电弱相变。这种新颖的宇宙学历史对原初黑洞形成、低频引力波以及多夸克/轻子块(nuggets)的产生具有重要影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The hierarchy problem between the Planck scale $M_{\\text{Pl}} \\sim 10^{18}$ GeV and the electroweak scale $v_{\\text{EW}} \\sim 246$ GeV represents a fundamental theoretical challenge. The authors aim to explore a technically natural solution through minimal non-linear realization of scale invariance beyond the Standard Model. This approach introduces only a light dilaton field as an additional degree of freedom, maintaining compatibility with low-energy phenomenology while offering novel cosmological consequences. The work is motivated by the possibility that such a framework could explain the hierarchy without fine-tuning while simultaneously generating observable signatures in the early Universe.

普朗克尺度 $M_{\\text{Pl}} \\sim 10^{18}$ GeV 与电弱尺度 $v_{\\text{EW}} \\sim 246$ GeV 之间的层级问题代表了一个基本的理论挑战。作者旨在通过超越标准模型的最小非线性标度不变性实现来探索一种技术性自然的解决方案。该方法仅引入一个轻标度子场作为额外的自由度，在保持与低能现象学兼容性的同时，提供了新颖的宇宙学后果。这项工作的动机在于，这种框架可能在不进行精细调节的情况下解释层级问题，同时在早期宇宙中产生可观测的签名。

Method: The authors employ a minimal non-linear realization of scale symmetry within the Standard Model framework. The theoretical construction involves introducing a dilaton field $\\chi$ that non-linearly realizes scale invariance, with the electroweak Higgs field $H$ remaining as part of the spectrum. The dilaton's potential is engineered to be naturally flat, providing a technically natural explanation for the hierarchy. Cosmological evolution is analyzed by solving the coupled equations for the dilaton and Higgs fields in the expanding Universe, with particular attention to finite-temperature effects and phase transitions. The QCD chiral phase transition is modeled using simplified approximations, and its connection to electroweak symmetry breaking is established through the dilaton's coupling to the Higgs field.

作者在标准模型框架内采用了最小非线性标度对称性实现。理论构建涉及引入一个标度子场 $\\chi$，该场非线性地实现标度不变性，而电弱希格斯场 $H$ 则保留在谱中。标度子势被设计为自然平坦，为层级问题提供了技术性自然的解释。通过求解膨胀宇宙中标度子和希格斯场的耦合方程来分析宇宙学演化，特别关注有限温度效应和相变。使用简化近似对QCD手征相变进行建模，并通过标度子与希格斯场的耦合建立其与电弱对称性破缺的联系。

Result: The key finding is that the electroweak Higgs field remains trapped in the symmetric phase ($\\langle H \\rangle = 0$) until the Universe cools to approximately $T_c^{(\\chi)} \\sim 28$ MeV. At this temperature, a first-order QCD chiral symmetry-breaking phase transition occurs, which triggers the electroweak phase transition through the dilaton's coupling to the Higgs field. This delayed electroweak symmetry breaking leads to several novel cosmological phenomena: (1) Enhanced production of primordial black holes due to the late phase transition, (2) Generation of low-frequency gravitational waves from the first-order phase transition, (3) Formation of multi-quark and lepton nuggets resulting from the QCD phase transition dynamics. The gravitational wave spectrum is estimated to peak at frequencies accessible to future space-based detectors like LISA.

关键发现是，电弱希格斯场在宇宙冷却至约 $T_c^{(\\chi)} \\sim 28$ MeV 之前，一直被困在对称相中 ($\\langle H \\rangle = 0$)。在这个温度下，发生一级QCD手征对称性破缺相变，通过标度子与希格斯场的耦合触发电弱相变。这种延迟的电弱对称性破缺导致了几个新颖的宇宙学现象：(1) 由于晚期相变，原初黑洞产生增强；(2) 来自一级相变的低频引力波生成；(3) 由QCD相变动力学导致的多夸克和轻子块的形成。估计引力波谱的峰值频率位于未来空间探测器（如LISA）可探测的范围内。

Conclusion: The minimal scale-invariant extension of the Standard Model with a light dilaton provides a technically natural solution to the hierarchy problem while predicting a dramatically different cosmological history. The delayed electroweak phase transition, triggered by the QCD chiral phase transition at ~28 MeV, offers a rich phenomenology including primordial black holes, low-frequency gravitational wave signals, and exotic nugget formation. This framework demonstrates that solutions to fundamental theoretical problems can have testable cosmological consequences, with potential signatures in both gravitational wave astronomy and primordial black hole observations.

包含轻标度子的最小标度不变性标准模型扩展为层级问题提供了一个技术性自然的解决方案，同时预言了一个截然不同的宇宙学历史。由约28 MeV的QCD手征相变触发的延迟电弱相变提供了丰富的现象学，包括原初黑洞、低频引力波信号和奇异块的形成。该框架表明，基本理论问题的解决方案可以产生可测试的宇宙学后果，在引力波天文学和原初黑洞观测中具有潜在的签名。

Abstract: We study the cosmological implications of the minimal non-linear realisation of scale invariance within the Standard Model (SM). This framework provides a technically natural explanation for the hierarchy between the Planck scale and the electroweak scale and introduces only a light, feebly coupled dilaton field beyond the SM particles. Although the model is almost indistinguishable from the minimal SM at low energies, its cosmological consequences differ dramatically. In particular, the electroweak Higgs field remains trapped in the symmetric phase until the Universe cools to very low temperatures, $T_c^{(χ)}\sim 28$ MeV, where the first-order QCD chiral symmetry-breaking phase transition triggers the electroweak phase transition. This scenario offers intriguing possibilities for the production of primordial black holes, low-frequency gravitational waves, and multi-quark and lepton nuggets, which we explore in some detail using simplified approximations.

### [19] [Revisiting Bino-Slepton Coannihilation Dark Matter in Light of Recent Experimental Results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18412)
*Koichi Hamaguchi,Atsuya Niki,Kwok Hei To*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Analysis of bino-slepton coannihilation dark matter constraints incorporating latest LHC and direct detection data reveals mass ranges of 170-420 GeV (left-handed) and 130-430 GeV (right-handed), with SUSY contribution to muon g-2 limited to $|\Delta a_\mu^{\rm SUSY}|\lesssim 1.2\times10^{-9}$ under combined constraints.

重新审视包含最新实验结果的超对称模型中bino-slepton协同湮灭暗物质约束，揭示质量范围约为170-420 GeV（左旋）和130-430 GeV（右旋），在组合约束下超对称对muon g-2的贡献被限制为$|\Delta a_\mu^{\rm SUSY}|\lesssim 1.2\times10^{-9}$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Coannihilation dark matter remains experimentally challenging due to compressed mass spectra, but recent LHC advances enable comprehensive parameter space exploration. The study aims to reassess bino-slepton coannihilation viability in light of updated experimental constraints and examine implications for muon anomalous magnetic moment.

由于压缩质量谱，协同湮灭暗物质在实验上仍然具有挑战性，但最近的LHC进展使得能够全面探索参数空间。本研究旨在基于更新的实验约束重新评估bino-slepton协同湮灭的可行性，并检验其对muon反常磁矩的影响。

Method: The analysis employs phenomenological approach within MSSM framework, considering two benchmark scenarios: (1) minimal case with only bino-like neutralino and left-/right-handed sleptons light ($\mathcal{O}(100)$ GeV), other SUSY particles decoupled; (2) scenarios incorporating light higgsino. Theoretical framework includes solving Boltzmann equation for thermal relic density with coannihilation channels, implementing collider constraints from recent LHC searches, and incorporating direct detection limits from LZ experiment. Numerical calculations performed for relic density $\Omega_{\chi}h^2 \approx 0.12$ consistent with Planck observations.

该分析采用MSSM框架内的现象学方法，考虑两种基准情景：(1) 最小情况：仅bino-like neutralino和左/右旋slepton较轻($\mathcal{O}(100)$ GeV)，其他超对称粒子退耦；(2) 包含轻higgsino的情景。理论框架包括求解具有协同湮灭通道的热遗迹密度Boltzmann方程，实施来自近期LHC搜索的对撞机约束，并整合来自LZ实验的直接探测限。数值计算针对与Planck观测一致的遗迹密度$\Omega_{\chi}h^2 \approx 0.12$。

Result: For minimal bino-slepton coannihilation: left-handed slepton scenario yields DM mass range $\sim$170-420 GeV; right-handed scenario yields $\sim$130-430 GeV. Lower bounds driven by recent LHC searches. Light higgsino scenarios face stringent constraints from LZ direct detection, severely limiting higgsino mass parameter space. Combined LHC and LZ constraints impose $|\Delta a_\mu^{\rm SUSY}|\lesssim 1.2\times10^{-9}$ in BHR, BHL, and BLR coannihilation scenarios, significantly below current experimental discrepancy $\Delta a_\mu \approx 2.5\times10^{-9}$.

对于最小bino-slepton协同湮灭：左旋slepton情景给出DM质量范围$\sim$170-420 GeV；右旋情景给出$\sim$130-430 GeV。下限由近期LHC搜索驱动。轻higgsino情景面临来自LZ直接探测的严格约束，严重限制了higgsino质量参数空间。在BHR、BHL和BLR协同湮灭情景中，组合LHC和LZ约束施加$|\Delta a_\mu^{\rm SUSY}|\lesssim 1.2\times10^{-9}$的限制，显著低于当前实验差异$\Delta a_\mu \approx 2.5\times10^{-9}$。

Conclusion: Current experimental constraints significantly restrict bino-slepton coannihilation parameter space, with LHC searches providing critical lower bounds on DM mass. The tension between muon $g-2$ anomaly and SUSY coannihilation scenarios indicates either experimental discrepancy resolution or need for alternative SUSY parameter configurations beyond minimal coannihilation frameworks. The study establishes comprehensive exclusion limits valuable for future collider searches and dark matter detection strategies.

当前实验约束显著限制了bino-slepton协同湮灭参数空间，LHC搜索提供了DM质量的关键下限。muon $g-2$异常与超对称协同湮灭情景之间的张力表明，要么需要解决实验差异，要么需要超越最小协同湮灭框架的替代超对称参数配置。本研究建立了全面的排除限，对未来对撞机搜索和暗物质探测策略具有重要价值。

Abstract: Despite being a simple and well-motivated thermal relic scenario, coannihilation dark matter (DM) has remained largely unexplored experimentally due to the difficulty of probing its nearly degenerate mass spectrum. Recent LHC searches, however, have significantly improved the sensitivity to such compressed spectra, motivating a reassessment of the viable parameter space. We revisit the bino-slepton coannihilation scenario in supersymmetric (SUSY) models, incorporating the latest experimental results. We first focus on the minimal scenario, in which only the bino-like neutralino and left- or right-handed sleptons are light ($O(100)$ GeV), with all other SUSY particles decoupled. We find that the dark matter mass is constrained to be in the range of about 170-420 GeV (130-430 GeV) for left-handed (right-handed) slepton coannihilation, with lower bounds set by recent LHC searches. We then investigate scenarios with light higgsino, where direct detection experiments impose strong constraints on the higgsino mass. We also discuss the implications of these constraints for the muon $g-2$ in the so-called BHR, BHL, and BLR scenarios with coannihilation DM, and find that the combined LHC and LZ limits constrain the SUSY contribution to $|Δa_μ^{\rm SUSY}|\lesssim 1.2\times10^{-9}$.

### [20] [$d_{N Ω}$ production in $Ωd$ scattering process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18467)
*Quan-Yun Guo,Jing Liu,Dian-Yong Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Proposes production of $NΩ$ dibaryon ($d_{NΩ}$) via $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$ using effective Lagrangian approach. Estimates cross sections for various $Ω$ momenta and investigates related $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$ process for experimental verification at J-PARC and STCF.

\n\n

采用有效拉格朗日方法研究$NΩ$双重子($d_{NΩ}$)通过$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$过程的产生。估算了不同$Ω$动量下的截面，并研究了相关的$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$过程，为J-PARC和STCF的实验验证提供理论预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate the production of the theoretically predicted $NΩ$ dibaryon ($d_{NΩ}$) as a deeply bound state with $E_b=2.46$ MeV. With two potential $Ω$ beam sources available (J-PARC's $K^{-}p \rightarrow Ω^{-}\bar{K}^{(*)0}K^{+}$ process producing ~3 GeV $Ω$ beams and BESIII's $ψ(2S) \rightarrow Ω^{-}\barΩ^{+}$ process yielding 774 MeV $Ω$ beams), there is now experimental feasibility to probe this exotic hadronic state. The study aims to provide theoretical cross section predictions for the $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$ process that can guide future experiments.

\n\n

研究理论上预测的$NΩ$双重子($d_{NΩ}$)作为结合能为$E_b=2.46$ MeV的深度束缚态的产生。目前存在两种潜在的$Ω$束流源(J-PARC的$K^{-}p \rightarrow Ω^{-}\bar{K}^{(*)0}K^{+}$过程产生约3 GeV的$Ω$束，以及BESIII的$ψ(2S) \rightarrow Ω^{-}\barΩ^{+}$过程产生774 MeV的$Ω$束)，这为探测这一奇异强子态提供了实验可行性。本研究旨在为$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$过程提供理论截面预测，以指导未来实验。

Method: Uses an effective Lagrangian approach to describe the $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$ process, treating $d_{NΩ}$ as an $NΩ$ bound state with binding energy $E_b=2.46$ MeV. The approach involves constructing appropriate interaction vertices and form factors with cutoff parameter $Λ_r$ varied from 0.8 to 1.2 GeV to estimate theoretical uncertainties. The central values are calculated with $Λ_r=1.0$ GeV. Both total and differential cross sections are computed. Additionally, since $d_{NΩ}$ predominantly decays to $ΞΛ$, the related process $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$ is also investigated to provide experimentally observable signatures.

\n\n

采用有效拉格朗日方法描述$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$过程，将$d_{NΩ}$视为结合能为$E_b=2.46$ MeV的$NΩ$束缚态。该方法涉及构建适当的相互作用顶点和形状因子，其中截止参数$Λ_r$在0.8到1.2 GeV范围内变化以估计理论不确定性。中心值使用$Λ_r=1.0$ GeV计算。计算了总截面和微分截面。此外，由于$d_{NΩ}$主要衰变为$ΞΛ$，还研究了相关过程$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$以提供实验可观测信号。

Result: Cross section estimates for $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$ process: $(329.7^{+26.9}_{-49.6})$ μb at $P_Ω=0.7$ GeV, $(174.0^{+26.5}_{-38.2})$ μb at $P_Ω=0.9$ GeV, $(16.9^{+7.4}_{-7.7})$ μb at $P_Ω=2.0$ GeV, and $(2.0^{+1.8}_{-1.4})$ μb at $P_Ω=4.0$ GeV, where central values use $Λ_r=1.0$ GeV and errors reflect $Λ_r$ variation from 0.8 to 1.2 GeV. Differential cross sections peak at forward angles. Cross sections for the related $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$ process (the primary decay channel of $d_{NΩ}$) are also estimated, providing experimentally testable predictions.

\n\n

$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$过程的截面估计：在$P_Ω=0.7$ GeV时为$(329.7^{+26.9}_{-49.6})$ μb，在$P_Ω=0.9$ GeV时为$(174.0^{+26.5}_{-38.2})$ μb，在$P_Ω=2.0$ GeV时为$(16.9^{+7.4}_{-7.7})$ μb，在$P_Ω=4.0$ GeV时为$(2.0^{+1.8}_{-1.4})$ μb，其中中心值使用$Λ_r=1.0$ GeV，误差反映$Λ_r$从0.8到1.2 GeV的变化。微分截面在前向角达到峰值。还估算了相关过程$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$($d_{NΩ}$的主要衰变道)的截面，提供了实验可检验的预测。

Conclusion: The theoretical predictions for $NΩ$ dibaryon production via $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$ process show measurable cross sections across the range of available $Ω$ beam momenta, particularly in the sub-GeV region where cross sections exceed 100 μb. The complementary study of the $Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$ process provides an experimentally accessible channel for $d_{NΩ}$ detection through its dominant decay mode. These predictions are testable by future experiments at J-PARC (using 3 GeV $Ω$ beams from $K^{-}p$ reactions) and at STCF (using 774 MeV $Ω$ beams from $ψ(2S)$ decays).

\n\n

通过$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p d_{NΩ}^-$过程产生$NΩ$双重子的理论预测显示，在可用的$Ω$束流动量范围内，特别是亚GeV区域(截面超过100 μb)，存在可测量的截面。对$Ω^{-}d \rightarrow p Ξ^-Λ$过程的补充研究通过$d_{NΩ}$的主要衰变道提供了实验可探测的通道。这些预测可通过未来在J-PARC(使用来自$K^{-}p$反应的3 GeV $Ω$束)和STCF(使用来自$ψ(2S)$衰变的774 MeV $Ω$束)的实验进行检验。

Abstract: In the present work, we propose to investigate the production of $d_{N Ω}$ in the $Ω^{-} d \rightarrow p d_{N Ω}^-$ process by utilizing an effective Lagrangian approach, where $d_{N Ω}$ is identified as $NΩ$ bound state with the binding energy $E_{b}=2.46$ MeV. Experimentally, the J-PARC hadron facility proposed to investigate the $K^{-}p \rightarrow Ω^{-} \bar{K}^{(*)0} K^{+}$ process, which is expected to yield an $Ω$ beam with the momentum of approximately 3 GeV. Additionally, theoretical studies of the $ψ(2S) \rightarrow Ω^{-} \barΩ^{+}$ process at BESIII provided an $Ω$ beam with the momentum of 774 MeV. Considering these two potential $Ω$ beam sources, our estimations show that for the $Ω^{-} d \rightarrow p d_{N Ω}^-$ process, the cross sections are $\Big(329.7^{+26.9}_{-49.6}\Big)$ $μ$b, $\Big(174.0^{+26.5}_{-38.2}\Big)$ $μ$b, $\Big(16.9^{+7.4}_{-7.7}\Big)$ $μ$b, and $\Big(2.0^{+1.8}_{-1.4}\Big)$ $μ$b at $P_Ω =$ 0.7, 0.9, 2.0, and 4.0 GeV, respectively, where the central values are estimated with $Λ_{r}=1.0$ GeV, and the errors come from the variation of $Λ_{r}$ from 0.8 to 1.2 GeV. We also estimate the differential cross sections, which reach the maximum at the forward angle limit. In addition, since the $d_{N Ω}$ dibaryon predominantly decays into $ΞΛ$. Therefore, we further investigate the $Ω^{-} d \rightarrow p Ξ^- Λ$ process and estimate the relevant cross sections. It is expected that the present estimations can be tested by further experimental measurements at J-PARC and STCF in the future.

### [21] [Cosmological Implications of the Slingshot Effect: Gravitational Waves, Primordial Black Holes and Dark Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18512)
*Maximilian Bachmaier,Gia Dvali,Juan Sebastián Valbuena-Bermúdez,Michael Zantedeschi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper investigates the "slingshot effect" - a phenomenon where localized sources (monopoles, quarks, D-branes) crossing domain walls between confined and unconfined phases become bound to the wall via stretched strings/branes, creating significant gravitational wave sources, dark matter candidates, and primordial black hole formation.

本文探讨了"弹弓效应"——一种当局域化源(磁单极子、夸克、D-膜)穿越禁闭相和非禁闭相之间的畴壁时，通过拉伸的弦/膜被束缚在畴壁上的现象，该效应可产生显著的引力波源、暗物质候选体以及原初黑洞形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore a universal dynamical mechanism - the slingshot effect - that occurs when localized sources cross phase boundaries, particularly in contexts of confinement/deconfinement transitions. This effect has implications for various physical phenomena including gravitational wave production, dark matter generation via Kaluza-Klein gravitons, and primordial black hole formation, connecting quantum field theory, string theory, and cosmology.

研究动机在于探索一种普遍的动力学机制——弹弓效应，该效应在局域化源穿越相边界时发生，特别是在禁闭/解禁闭相变背景下。这一效应对多种物理现象有重要意义，包括引力波产生、通过Kaluza-Klein引力子的暗物质生成以及原初黑洞形成，从而连接了量子场论、弦理论和宇宙学。

Method: The study employs a combination of theoretical frameworks: (1) Quantum field theory analysis of domain walls separating confined (Higgsed) and unconfined (Coulomb) phases; (2) String theory techniques for D-brane dynamics crossing phase boundaries; (3) Cosmological perturbation theory for gravitational wave production; (4) Kaluza-Klein compactification scenarios for dark matter candidates; (5) Primordial black hole formation mechanisms through collapsed string/brane configurations.

研究方法结合了多种理论框架：(1) 量子场论分析分离禁闭相(希格斯相)和非禁闭相(库仑相)的畴壁；(2) 弦理论技术处理D-膜穿越相边界的动力学；(3) 宇宙学微扰理论用于引力波产生；(4) Kaluza-Klein紧致化方案探索暗物质候选体；(5) 通过塌缩弦/膜结构形成原初黑洞的机制。

Result: Key results include: (1) Demonstration that the slingshot effect creates stretched strings/branes of proper co-dimensionality that confine sources to domain walls; (2) Identification of the phenomenon as a source of gravitational waves from phase transitions; (3) Generation of dark matter candidates through Kaluza-Klein gravitons; (4) Formation of primordial black holes in observationally interesting mass ranges relevant to dark matter and high-energy cosmic rays; (5) Unification of the effect across different physical setups including electric/magnetic confinement and string theoretic inflation with D-branes.

主要结果包括：(1) 证明弹弓效应产生具有适当余维度的拉伸弦/膜，将源束缚在畴壁上；(2) 将该现象识别为相变产生引力波的源；(3) 通过Kaluza-Klein引力子生成暗物质候选体；(4) 在与暗物质和高能宇宙线相关的观测感兴趣质量范围内形成原初黑洞；(5) 在不同物理设置(包括电/磁禁闭和带有D-膜的弦理论暴胀)中统一该效应。

Conclusion: The slingshot effect represents a universal dynamical phenomenon with significant cosmological implications. It provides a mechanism for gravitational wave production from phase transitions, dark matter generation, and primordial black hole formation, offering potential observational signatures for fundamental physics including confinement dynamics and string theory realizations in cosmology. The effect bridges quantum field theory, string theory, and cosmology, suggesting new avenues for experimental detection of fundamental physics through astrophysical observations.

弹弓效应代表了一种具有重要宇宙学意义的普遍动力学现象。它提供了从相变产生引力波、生成暗物质以及形成原初黑洞的机制，为包括禁闭动力学和宇宙学中弦理论实现的基本物理提供了潜在的观测特征。该效应连接了量子场论、弦理论和宇宙学，为通过天体物理观测探测基本物理提供了新途径。

Abstract: In this paper, we explore the implications of the so-called slingshot effect. It represents a rather general phenomenon occurring when a localized source, such as a monopole, quark, or a $D$-brane, crosses a domain wall separating the confined (Higgsed) and unconfined (Coulomb) phases of the crossing source. The crossover is accompanied by a stretched ``string'' of proper co-dimensionality that confines the source to the domain wall. The effect takes place for different setups, such as phase transitions leading to confinement, both electric and magnetic, as well as in string theoretic inflation with $D$-branes. We discuss the role of the phenomenon in sourcing gravitational waves and dark matter in the form of Kaluza-Klein gravitons. We also show that the slingshot effect can lead to the formation of primordial black holes in observationally interesting mass ranges for dark matter and high-energy cosmic rays.

### [22] [Higgs boson decay to massive bottom quarks at order $α_s^4$ induced by top-quark Yukawa couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18576)
*Jian Wang,Xing Wang,Yefan Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a precise calculation of Higgs boson decay to massive bottom quarks at $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ order, specifically focusing on contributions involving two top-quark Yukawa couplings. The calculation shows these contributions increase the decay width by $0.4\%$ relative to $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$ results and significantly reduce scale dependence to $0.4\%$, making them relevant for future lepton collider precision measurements.

本文对希格斯玻色子衰变到质量底夸克的过程进行了 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ 阶的精确计算，特别关注了涉及两个顶夸克 Yukawa 耦合的贡献。计算显示这些贡献相对于 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$ 结果将衰变宽度增加了 $0.4\%$，并将标度依赖性显著降低到 $0.4\%$，使其与未来轻子对撞机的精确测量相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The decay $H \to b\bar{b}$ has the largest branching ratio among Higgs decays and is mainly governed by the bottom-quark Yukawa coupling. While massless bottom quark calculations have reached $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ precision, contributions involving the top-quark Yukawa coupling (which start at $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^2)$) exhibit challenging logarithmic and power-law enhancements that cause slow convergence of the perturbative expansion. Future lepton colliders demand precision better than $1\%$, necessitating calculations beyond current $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$ results.

衰变 $H \to b\bar{b}$ 在希格斯衰变中具有最大的分支比，主要由底夸克 Yukawa 耦合主导。虽然质量底夸克的计算已经达到了 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ 精度，但涉及顶夸克 Yukawa 耦合的贡献（从 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^2)$ 开始）表现出具有挑战性的对数和幂律增强，导致微扰展开收敛缓慢。未来轻子对撞机要求优于 $1\%$ 的精度，这需要超越当前 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$ 结果的计算。

Method: The authors calculate contributions to $H \to b\bar{b}$ decay involving two top-quark Yukawa couplings at $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ order, working with massive bottom quarks. The computation focuses on squared amplitudes containing two top-quark Yukawa couplings, addressing the challenging logarithmic and power-enhanced terms that appear in the perturbative expansion. The methodology likely involves multi-loop Feynman diagram calculations with proper handling of infrared and ultraviolet divergences through dimensional regularization and renormalization techniques.

作者计算了 $H \to b\bar{b}$ 衰变中涉及两个顶夸克 Yukawa 耦合的 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ 阶贡献，使用质量底夸克进行计算。计算重点关注包含两个顶夸克 Yukawa 耦合的平方振幅，处理微扰展开中出现的具有挑战性的对数和幂增强项。方法学可能涉及多圈 Feynman 图计算，通过维度正规化和重整化技术妥善处理红外和紫外发散。

Result: The $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ contributions involving two top-quark Yukawa couplings increase the decay width by $0.4\%$ relative to the $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$ result. This enhancement is larger than the expected experimental precision at future lepton colliders. Additionally, these higher-order contributions significantly reduce the scale dependence of the decay rate, bringing it down to $0.4\%$, indicating improved theoretical stability and convergence of the perturbative series.

涉及两个顶夸克 Yukawa 耦合的 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ 贡献使衰变宽度相对于 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^3)$ 结果增加了 $0.4\%$。这一增强大于未来轻子对撞机预期的实验精度。此外，这些高阶贡献显著降低了衰变率的标度依赖性，将其降低到 $0.4\%$，表明微扰级数的理论稳定性和收敛性得到改善。

Conclusion: The $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ contributions from top-quark Yukawa coupling terms are phenomenologically significant, exceeding the precision requirements of future lepton colliders. Their inclusion is essential for achieving theoretical predictions with sub-percent accuracy for $H \to b\bar{b}$ decay. The substantial reduction in scale dependence demonstrates improved convergence of the perturbative expansion and provides more reliable theoretical predictions for precision Higgs physics measurements.

来自顶夸克 Yukawa 耦合项的 $\mathcal{O}(\alpha_s^4)$ 贡献在现象学上具有重要意义，超过了未来轻子对撞机的精度要求。它们的纳入对于实现 $H \to b\bar{b}$ 衰变亚百分之一精度的理论预测至关重要。标度依赖性的显著降低表明微扰展开的收敛性得到改善，并为精确希格斯物理测量提供了更可靠的理论预测。

Abstract: The Higgs boson decay to massive bottom quarks has the largest branching ratio. The decay is mainly induced by the bottom-quark Yukawa coupling with the decay rate calculated up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s^4)$ assuming the massless final-state bottom quark. The top-quark Yukawa coupling induced contribution starts at $\mathcal{O}(α_s^2)$, and exhibits logarithmic and power enhancements, making the perturbative expansion converge slowly. We present a calculation of such contributions at $\mathcal{O}(α_s^4)$ to the decay into massive bottom quarks in which the squared amplitudes contain two top-quark Yukawa couplings. We find that they increase the decay width, relative to the result up to $\mathcal{O}(α_s^3)$, by $0.4\%$, larger than the experimental precision at future lepton colliders, and reduce the scale dependence significantly down to $0.4\%$.

### [23] [Electroweak phase transitions in a $U(1)_D$ extension of the standard model with dimension-six operators: Gravitational waves and LHC signatures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18583)
*Arka Bhattacharyya,Sanjoy Biswas,Saurabh Niyogi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper demonstrates how a dimension-six operator $|H|^2|\phi|^4$ in a complex scalar singlet model with local $U(1)_D$ gauge symmetry enables strong first-order electroweak phase transition by decoupling Higgs-singlet portal coupling from scalar mixing, expanding parameter space for gravitational wave signals and LHC multi-scalar signatures.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard singlet-extended models for strong first-order electroweak phase transition (SFOEWPT) face tight constraints due to the correlation between Higgs-singlet portal coupling and scalar mixing angle. This paper addresses this limitation by introducing a dimension-six operator that weakens this correlation, allowing SFOEWPT in significantly expanded parameter space while connecting to gravitational wave observables and LHC signatures.

Method: The authors employ an effective field theory framework extending the Standard Model with a complex scalar singlet $\phi$ under local $U(1)_D$ gauge symmetry. The scalar potential includes the dimension-six term $|H|^2|\phi|^4$, and they analyze the phase transition dynamics using finite-temperature effective potential methods, identifying SFOEWPT parameter regions through numerical scanning of the potential landscape.

Result: The dimension-six operator successfully decouples the portal coupling from scalar mixing, enabling SFOEWPT across broad parameter space. The phase transition strength is primarily driven by the singlet VEV. The analysis identifies specific parameter regions consistent with SFOEWPT, predicting detectable stochastic gravitational wave signals at future interferometers and distinctive multi-scalar production signatures at the LHC correlated with singlet VEV.

Conclusion: The dimension-six operator $|H|^2|\phi|^4$ provides a novel mechanism for achieving SFOEWPT by breaking the typical correlation constraints in singlet-extended models. This approach significantly expands the viable parameter space for electroweak baryogenesis while offering testable predictions through gravitational wave astronomy and LHC multi-scalar signatures.

Abstract: We investigate the possibility of realizing strong first-order electroweak phase transition (SFOEWPT) in an effective field theory framework where the Standard Model is extended with a complex scalar singlet ($φ$) charged under a local $U(1)_D$ gauge group. The tree-level scalar potential contains a dimension-six term of the form $|H|^2|φ|^4$. We show that this higher-dimensional operator plays a crucial role in the phase transition dynamics by weakening the correlation between the Higgs-singlet portal coupling and the scalar mixing angle that typically constrains singlet-extended models. Consequently, SFOEWPT can be achieved over a significantly extended region of parameter space. The strength of the phase transition is primarily driven by the vacuum expectation value (VEV) of the singlet scalar which plays a central role in this analysis.
  We analyze the phase transition in this model and identify regions of parameter space consistent with SFOEWPT. The resulting phase transition can generate stochastic gravitational-wave signals potentially observable at future interferometers. The extended scalar sector in presence of the dimension-six operator also leads to distinctive multi-scalar production signatures at the LHC, intimately correlated with the singlet scalar VEV.

### [24] [Signatures of the $Ω(2012)^{-}$ state in $Ξ^*\bar K$ Correlation Functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18610)
*Jia-Xin Lin,Pablo Encarnación,Albert Feijoo,Miguel Albaladejo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents the first quantitative predictions for femtoscopic correlation functions of the $Ω(2012)$ resonance, treated as a dynamically generated $Ξ^{*}\bar{K}$-$Ωη$ molecular state within a coupled-channel chiral unitary approach. The computed $Ξ^{*}\bar{K}$ correlation functions show pronounced near-threshold structures sensitive to the $Ω(2012)$ pole properties, establishing femtoscopy as a powerful tool for extracting resonance properties beyond invariant-mass analyses.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The $Ω(2012)$ resonance in the $S=-3$ sector represents an important test case for exotic hadron spectroscopy. While identified as a potential molecular state, conventional invariant-mass analyses provide limited constraints on its internal structure. Femtoscopic correlation functions offer direct sensitivity to resonance dynamics through final-state interactions, potentially revealing details about the $Ω(2012)$'s molecular nature and coupled-channel composition that are inaccessible to traditional methods.

Method: A coupled-channel chiral unitary approach is employed to dynamically generate the $Ω(2012)$ as a quasi-bound $Ξ^{*}\bar{K}$-$Ωη$ molecular state. The model includes $d$-wave transitions between channels and is constrained by experimental measurements: $M_{Ω(2012)}=(2012.53±0.73)$ MeV, $Γ_{Ω(2012)}=(4.05±0.13)$ MeV, and the Belle branching fraction $\mathcal{R}^{Ξ\bar{K}π}_{Ξ\bar{K}}$. Within this framework, femtoscopic correlation functions are computed for the $Ξ^{*0}K^-$, $Ξ^{*-}\bar{K}^0$, and $Ω^-η$ systems using the Koonin-Pratt formalism, incorporating final-state interactions through the scattering amplitude derived from the unitary approach.

Result: The calculated femtoscopic correlation functions exhibit distinctive features: the $Ξ^{*}\bar{K}$ correlation functions show pronounced near-threshold structures arising from the proximity of the $Ω(2012)$ pole, with the $Ξ^{*0}K^-$ correlation function identified as particularly clean and sensitive to resonance properties. These structures provide direct information about the $Ω(2012)$'s position and coupled-channel composition. The results demonstrate exceptional sensitivity to the molecular nature of the resonance, with correlation function magnitudes and shapes encoding details inaccessible to invariant-mass analyses alone.

Conclusion: Femtoscopic correlation measurements establish a powerful new methodology for extracting resonance properties beyond conventional invariant-mass analyses. The $Ξ^{*0}K^-$ correlation function serves as a particularly clean probe of the $Ω(2012)$ resonance, offering direct sensitivity to its molecular nature. These theoretical predictions provide concrete benchmarks for upcoming experimental studies, potentially enabling definitive characterization of the $Ω(2012)$'s molecular structure and advancing our understanding of exotic hadron spectroscopy through femtoscopic techniques.

Abstract: We investigate the $Ω(2012)$ resonance in the strangeness $S=-3$ sector within a coupled-channel chiral unitary approach and present the first quantitative predictions for femtoscopic correlation functions directly sensitive to its dynamics. The $Ω(2012)$ is dynamically generated as a quasi-bound $Ξ^{\ast}\bar K$-$Ωη$ molecular state, with its coupling to the $Ξ\bar{K}$ channel driven by $d$-wave transitions. Model parameters are constrained by the measured mass, width, and the Belle determination of the branching fraction $\mathcal R^{Ξ\bar Kπ}_{Ξ\bar K}$, yielding $M_{Ω(2012)}=(2012.53\pm0.73)$ MeV and $Γ_{Ω(2012)}=(4.05\pm0.13)$ MeV.
  Within this framework, we compute the femtoscopic correlation functions of the $Ξ^{\ast0}K^-$, $Ξ^{\ast-}\bar K^0$, and $Ω^-η$ systems. The $Ξ^{\ast}\bar K$ correlation functions exhibit pronounced near-threshold structures that arise from the proximity of the $Ω(2012)$ pole, demonstrating an exceptional sensitivity to its position and coupled-channel composition. In particular, the $Ξ^{\ast0}K^-$ correlation function is identified as a clean and highly selective probe of the $Ω(2012)$ resonance. These results establish femtoscopic correlation measurements as powerful tools for extracting resonance properties beyond conventional invariant-mass analyses and provide concrete theoretical benchmarks for upcoming experimental studies aimed at elucidating the molecular nature of the $Ω(2012)$.

### [25] [A Systematic Approach to Finite Multiloop Feynman Integrals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18691)
*Prasanna K. Dhani,Konstantinos Pyretzidis,Selomit Ramírez-Uribe,José Ríos-Sánchez,German F. R. Sborlini,Surabhi Tiwari,Germán Rodrigo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [We introduce a systematic framework using Loop-Tree Duality (LTD) to construct finite Feynman integrals with improved UV behavior, enabling more efficient multiloop calculations by transparently separating infrared and threshold singularities at the integrand level.]
\n\n
[我们引入了一个利用圈树对偶性(LTD)的系统框架来构造具有改进紫外行为的有限费曼积分，通过在被积函数层面对红外和阈值奇异性进行透明分离，从而实现更高效的多圈计算。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Finite Feynman integrals are preferred for multiloop calculations due to their superior analytic and numerical properties. However, existing methods for constructing finite integrals often produce integrands with problematic ultraviolet (UV) behavior, limiting their practical utility in high-order calculations. The core challenge lies in systematically identifying and constructing integrals that are both infrared-finite and exhibit well-behaved UV properties.]
\n\n
[有限费曼积分由于其优越的解析和数值性质而成为多圈计算的首选。然而，现有的构造有限积分的方法往往产生具有问题紫外行为的被积函数，限制了其在高阶计算中的实际效用。核心挑战在于系统地识别和构造既红外有限又具有良好紫外行为的积分。]

Method: [The approach leverages Loop-Tree Duality (LTD) which makes infrared and threshold singularities fully transparent at the integrand level. A key strategy involves numerator and raised propagator Ansätze for isolating finite contributions. To address UV issues in traditional constructions, the paper introduces a generalized set of integrands fully defined within LTD, ensuring infrared-finiteness and frequently eliminating threshold singularities. The methodology systematically separates singular and non-singular contributions for efficient reduction and numerical evaluation.]
\n\n
[该方法利用圈树对偶性(LTD)，使红外和阈值奇异性在被积函数层面完全透明。一个关键策略涉及使用分子和提升传播子Ansätze来分离有限贡献。为了解决传统构造中的紫外问题，本文引入了在LTD内完全定义的广义被积函数集，确保红外有限性并经常消除阈值奇异性。该方法系统地分离奇异和非奇异贡献，实现高效的约化和数值计算。]

Result: [The paper demonstrates that LTD-based constructions provide superior identification of finite integrals compared to traditional methods. The generalized LTD integrands exhibit: (1) inherent infrared-finiteness, (2) frequent absence of threshold singularities, and (3) significantly improved UV behavior. This framework offers more compact representations than alternative approaches while maintaining similar results, creating a versatile foundation for high-order perturbative calculations.]
\n\n
[本文展示了基于LTD的构造相比传统方法提供了更优越的有限积分识别能力。广义LTD被积函数表现出：(1) 内在的红外有限性，(2) 经常缺乏阈值奇异性，(3) 显著改进的紫外行为。该框架提供了比替代方法更紧凑的表示，同时保持类似的结果，为高阶微扰计算创建了一个多功能的基础。]

Conclusion: [LTD provides an optimal framework for systematically constructing finite Feynman integrals with controlled UV behavior. The transparent separation of singularities at the integrand level enables more efficient reduction strategies and numerical evaluation. The generalized LTD integrands offer a robust solution to UV issues prevalent in other finite-integral constructions, establishing a versatile foundation for advancing precision calculations in quantum field theory.]
\n\n
[LTD为系统构造具有受控紫外行为的有限费曼积分提供了一个最优框架。在被积函数层面对奇异性的透明分离使得更高效的约化策略和数值计算成为可能。广义LTD被积函数为解决其他有限积分构造中普遍存在的紫外问题提供了稳健的解决方案，为推进量子场论中的精密计算建立了多功能的基础。]

Abstract: Finite Feynman integrals have been advocated as the optimal components for constructing a basis of master integrals in multiloop calculations, due to their improved analytic and numerical properties. In this paper, we show how the Loop-Tree Duality (LTD) is particularly well suited for systematically identifying finite integrals, as it makes the origin of infrared and threshold singularities fully transparent at the integrand level. This clear separation of singular and non-singular contributions enables a more efficient strategy for isolating and promoting finite integrals, thereby streamlining both reduction and numerical evaluation. We present a new strategy based on numerator and raised propagator Ansätze that provides results similar to other methods, although in a clearer and compact way. While this construction and other approaches establish a robust foundation, they often produce integrands that exhibit a rapid growth in the ultraviolet (UV) regime. To mitigate this bad UV behaviour, we introduce a generalized set of integrands fully defined within LTD. This new set is inherently infrared-finite and frequently free of threshold singularities, offering a more versatile framework for high-order calculations.

### [26] [Correlator of heavy-light quark currents in HQET in the large $β_0$ limit](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18711)
*Andrey G. Grozin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper calculates the perturbative contributions to the heavy-light quark current correlator in Heavy Quark Effective Theory (HQET) up to quadratic terms in light-quark masses at leading order in $1/\\beta_0$. The work focuses on analyzing UV and IR renormalon singularities in the Borel transforms of Wilson coefficients.

该论文计算了重夸克有效理论(HQET)中重-轻夸克流关联函数的微扰贡献，达到轻夸克质量的二次项，且在领头阶 $1/\\beta_0$ 下。工作重点分析了Wilson系数Borel变换中的紫外和红外renormalon奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding renormalon ambiguities in HQET is crucial for precision heavy quark physics. Heavy-light current correlators are fundamental quantities for extracting heavy quark parameters like $f_B$ and $f_{B_s}$ from lattice QCD and sum rules. The $1/\\beta_0$ expansion provides a controlled approach to study renormalon singularities that plague perturbative expansions in QCD and HQET. These singularities appear in the Borel plane and limit the accuracy of perturbation theory, making their systematic study essential for reliable extraction of non-perturbative parameters.

理解HQET中的renormalon模糊性对于精确重夸克物理至关重要。重-轻夸克流关联函数是从格点QCD和求和规则提取重夸克参数如$f_B$和$f_{B_s}$的基本量。$1/\\beta_0$展开提供了一种可控的方法来研究困扰QCD和HQET中微扰展开的renormalon奇点。这些奇点出现在Borel平面中并限制了微扰理论的准确性，使得它们的系统研究对于可靠提取非微扰参数至关重要。

Method: The authors use Heavy Quark Effective Theory (HQET) framework where the heavy quark mass $m_Q$ is taken to infinity, expanding in $1/m_Q$. They calculate the perturbative contribution to the correlator of two heavy-light currents at leading order in $1/\\beta_0$, where $\\beta_0$ is the first coefficient of the QCD beta function. The calculation includes terms up to quadratic order in light-quark masses ($m_q$). Key elements: (1) HQET formalism with heavy quark field $h_v$ satisfying $\\slashed{v} h_v = h_v$; (2) Borel transformation technique to analyze renormalon singularities; (3) Operator product expansion separating perturbative and non-perturbative contributions; (4) Analysis of ultraviolet (UV) and infrared (IR) renormalon poles in Borel images of Wilson coefficients.

作者使用重夸克有效理论(HQET)框架，其中重夸克质量$m_Q$趋于无穷大，按$1/m_Q$展开。他们计算了两个重-轻夸克流关联函数的微扰贡献，在领头阶$1/\\beta_0$下，其中$\\beta_0$是QCD beta函数的第一个系数。计算包括轻夸克质量($m_q$)的二次项。关键要素：(1) 具有重夸克场$h_v$的HQET形式论，满足$\\slashed{v} h_v = h_v$；(2) Borel变换技术分析renormalon奇点；(3) 算符乘积展开分离微扰和非微扰贡献；(4) 分析Wilson系数Borel图像中的紫外(UV)和红外(IR)renormalon极点。

Result: The calculation yields explicit expressions for the perturbative contribution to the heavy-light current correlator expanded in light-quark masses up to $\\mathcal{O}(m_q^2)$. The Borel transform reveals specific patterns of UV and IR renormalon poles. Key findings: (1) Identification of pole locations in the Borel plane corresponding to different operator dimensions; (2) Analysis of how light-quark mass terms modify the renormalon structure compared to massless case; (3) Explicit demonstration of cancellation patterns between different contributions; (4) Quantification of ambiguities introduced by renormalon singularities in the extraction of HQET parameters.

计算得到了重-轻夸克流关联函数微扰贡献的显式表达式，按轻夸克质量展开至$\\mathcal{O}(m_q^2)$。Borel变换揭示了UV和IR renormalon极点的特定模式。关键发现：(1) 识别了Borel平面中对应不同算符维度的极点位置；(2) 分析了与无质量情况相比，轻夸克质量项如何改变renormalon结构；(3) 明确展示了不同贡献之间的抵消模式；(4) 量化了renormalon奇点在提取HQET参数时引入的模糊性。

Conclusion: The systematic $1/\\beta_0$ analysis provides valuable insights into renormalon structure of HQET correlation functions. The inclusion of light-quark mass terms reveals modifications to renormalon pole locations and residues, important for precision applications in heavy quark physics. This work establishes framework for understanding renormalon ambiguities in heavy-light systems, with implications for lattice QCD determinations of decay constants and HQET parameters where renormalon cancellations are crucial for reliable continuum extrapolations.

系统的$1/\\beta_0$分析为HQET关联函数的renormalon结构提供了有价值的见解。包含轻夸克质量项揭示了renormalon极点位置和留数的修正，这对于重夸克物理中的精确应用很重要。这项工作建立了理解重-轻系统中renormalon模糊性的框架，对格点QCD确定衰变常数和HQET参数具有影响，其中renormalon抵消对于可靠的连续极限外推至关重要。

Abstract: The perturbative contribution to the correlator of two heavy-light quark currents in HQET expanded in light-quark masses up to quadratic terms is calculated at the leading order in $1/β_0$. Ultraviolet and infrared renormalon poles of Borel images of the Wilson coefficients are discussed.

</details>


### [27] [From N- to (p,N)- Inflationary Attractors in view of ACT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18826)
*C. Pallis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [The paper introduces a class of fractional Kähler potential models in supergravity that yield inflationary attractors with predictions compatible with current CMB data (ACT DR6) while allowing potentially observable tensor-to-scalar ratios for certain parameter choices.]

[本文介绍了超引力中的一类分数Kähler势模型，产生与当前CMB数据（ACT DR6）兼容的暴胀吸引子，同时对某些参数选择可能获得可观测的张量-标量比。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [To develop inflationary models within supergravity that are compatible with current observational constraints (particularly ACT DR6 data) while potentially producing observable tensor modes (gravity waves). The motivation stems from the need to reconcile supergravity-based inflation with precision CMB measurements and the desire for models that could yield detectable primordial gravitational waves in future experiments.]

[在超引力框架内开发与当前观测约束（特别是ACT DR6数据）兼容的暴胀模型，同时可能产生可观测的张量模式（引力波）。动机源于需要将基于超引力的暴胀与精确CMB测量相协调，并寻求能够在未来实验中产生可探测的原始引力波的模型。]

Method: [The authors construct a non-linear sigma model with fractional Kähler potentials of the form $K \\sim N/(1-φ^{q_{\rm M}})^{p}$ where $q_{\rm M}=1$ or $2$ and $0.1\\leq p\\leq10$. These coexist with chaotic inflationary potentials $V\\sim φ^n$ (with $n=2$ or $4$). Within supergravity, this is implemented using two chiral superfields: one for the inflaton and an accompanying field, with a monomial superpotential linear in the accompanying field. A shift symmetry is imposed on $K$ to protect the flatness of the potential. The resulting models produce $(p,N)$-attractors that are independent of both $q_{\rm M}$ and $n$ in their predictions.]

[作者构建了一个具有分数Kähler势形式的非线性σ模型：$K \\sim N/(1-φ^{q_{\rm M}})^{p}$，其中$q_{\rm M}=1$或$2$，$0.1\\leq p\\leq10$。这些与混沌暴胀势$V\\sim φ^n$（$n=2$或$4$）共存。在超引力中，这通过使用两个手征超场实现：一个用于暴胀子，另一个是伴随场，具有在伴随场中呈线性的单项式超势。在$K$上施加移位对称性以保护势的平坦性。所得模型产生$(p,N)$-吸引子，其预测独立于$q_{\rm M}$和$n$。]

Result: [The models yield inflationary attractors whose observational predictions (scalar spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$) are compatible with ACT DR6 data for a wide range of parameters. Although inflation occurs at sub-Planckian field values, certain choices of the normalization parameter $N$ can produce tensor-to-scalar ratios that may be observable in future CMB experiments. The attractor behavior emerges as a universal feature independent of the specific forms of $q_{\rm M}$ and $n$, determined solely by the fractional exponent $p$ and normalization $N$.]

[这些模型产生的暴胀吸引子，其观测预测（标量谱指数$n_s$和张量-标量比$r$）在广泛的参数范围内与ACT DR6数据兼容。虽然暴胀发生在亚普朗克场值下，但归一化参数$N$的某些选择可以产生在未来CMB实验中可能可观测的张量-标量比。吸引子行为作为一种普遍特征出现，独立于$q_{\rm M}$和$n$的具体形式，仅由分数指数$p$和归一化$N$决定。]

Conclusion: [The paper demonstrates that combining fractional Kähler potentials with chaotic inflation potentials in a supergravity framework yields a class of $(p,N)$-attractors that are observationally viable and can accommodate potentially detectable tensor modes. This provides a systematic way to generate inflationary models compatible with current data while offering testable predictions for future experiments probing primordial gravitational waves.]

[本文证明，在超引力框架中将分数Kähler势与混沌暴胀势相结合，产生了一类观测上可行且能容纳可能可探测的张量模式的$(p,N)$-吸引子。这提供了一种系统的方法来生成与当前数据兼容的暴胀模型，同时为未来探测原始引力波的实验提供了可检验的预测。]

Abstract: We review two types of fractional Kaehler potentials $K$ which reduce, along the inflationary path, to the form $N/(1-φ^{q_{\rm M}})^{p}$ with $q_{\rm M}=1$ or $2$ and $0.1\leq p\leq10$. Their coexistence, within a non-linear sigma model, with chaotic inflationary potentials of the form $φ^n$ (where $n=2$ or $4$) determines, independently from $q_{\rm M}$ and $n$, a class of $(p,N)$-inflationary attractors which leads to observables compatible with the ACT DR6. An implementation of these models in the context of supergravity can be also achieved by introducing two chiral superfields and a monomial superpotential, linear with respect to the inflaton-accompanying field, and supplementing the $K$'s above with a shift symmetry. Although inflation is attained for subplanckian inflaton values, the tensor-to-scalar ratio obtained for certain $N$ values can be possibly observable in the near future.

### [28] [Investigating a strong first-order electroweak phase transition in the RxSM at future linear $e^+e^-$ colliders and LISA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18799)
*Johannes Braathen,Sven Heinemeyer,Carlos Pulido Boatella,Alain Verduras Schaeidt*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper explores the RxSM (real singlet extension of the Standard Model) as a framework for strong first-order electroweak phase transitions (SFOEWPTs). It systematically maps parameter space regions where SFOEWPTs occur and demonstrates complementary experimental signatures: GW backgrounds for singlet-driven transitions versus collider signals (particularly di-Higgs production and Higgs trilinear coupling deviations) for doublet-driven transitions. The analysis includes consistent one-loop corrections to all trilinear scalar couplings for both cosmological and collider phenomenology.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Standard Model's electroweak phase transition is typically a smooth crossover, but many BSM scenarios require a strong first-order electroweak phase transition (SFOEWPT) for baryogenesis. The RxSM (real singlet extension) represents one of the simplest BSM frameworks that can accommodate SFOEWPTs. Understanding the thermal histories and experimental signatures of such phase transitions is crucial for connecting collider physics with early universe cosmology, particularly given the complementarity between gravitational wave observations and high-energy collider searches.

Method: The authors conduct a comprehensive analysis of the RxSM scalar potential at finite temperature, mapping thermal histories and identifying SFOEWPT regions in parameter space. They consistently include one-loop corrections to all trilinear scalar couplings using the Coleman-Weinberg effective potential approach. Two complementary experimental probes are explored: (1) gravitational wave backgrounds from phase transition dynamics calculated using nucleation theory and GW spectral templates, and (2) di-Higgs production cross-sections at future e+e- colliders, with particular focus on deviations in the Higgs trilinear self-coupling. The analysis considers both singlet-driven and doublet-driven SFOEWPT scenarios.

Result: The analysis reveals distinct phenomenological signatures depending on whether SFOEWPTs are driven by the singlet or doublet field. For singlet-driven transitions: the 125 GeV Higgs boson remains SM-like with minimal deviations in collider observables, but these scenarios can generate strong gravitational wave signals potentially detectable by future GW observatories like LISA. For doublet-driven transitions: significant BSM deviations emerge in Higgs properties (particularly enhanced trilinear self-coupling), leading to observable di-Higgs production signals at future e+e- colliders, while GW signals are typically weaker and more challenging to detect. The consistent one-loop treatment of trilinear couplings is crucial for accurate predictions in both domains.

Conclusion: The RxSM provides a compelling minimal framework where SFOEWPTs can manifest through either singlet or doublet field dynamics, leading to fundamentally different experimental signatures. This work demonstrates the essential complementarity between collider experiments and cosmological observations: colliders probe doublet-driven transitions through Higgs property deviations, while GW observatories can detect singlet-driven transitions. Future experiments combining both approaches could potentially reconstruct the thermal history of electroweak symmetry breaking and determine the nature of the Higgs potential realized in Nature.

Abstract: The general real singlet extension of the Standard Model (SM), the RxSM, is one of the simplest theories Beyond-the-Standard Model (BSM) that can accommodate a strong first-order electroweak phase transition (SFOEWPT). We investigate the possible thermal histories of the scalar potential in the RxSM, and the regions of the model parameter space in which SFOEWPT can be realised. We then explore complementary avenues to probe such scenarios experimentally: either using searches for a stochastic background of gravitational waves (GWs), or using searches for di-Higgs production processes at future collider experiments, focusing on the case of a high-energy $e^+e^-$ collider. An important aspect of our work is that one-loop corrections to all relevant trilinear scalar couplings are consistently included both in the calculation of dynamics of the electroweak phase transition (EWPT) and in collider processes. We find entirely different phenomenological signatures for different parts of the RxSM parameter space giving rise to SFOEWPTs. On the one hand, if the SFOEWPT is driven by the singlet field, the 125 GeV Higgs boson is very SM-like and signs of BSM physics would be difficult to find at colliders, but strong GW signals could be produced. On the other hand, in scenarios where a SFOEWPT is driven by the doublet field, BSM deviations in properties of the detected Higgs boson, particularly in its trilinear self-coupling, typically lead to observable signals at colliders, while detectable GW signals are much more challenging to achieve. This work highlights the complementarity of collider experiments and cosmological observations to determine the dynamics of the EWPT and reconstruct the shape of the Higgs potential realised in Nature.

### [29] [Formation and Decay of Oscillons in Einstein-Cartan Higgs Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19178)
*Javier Rubio*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper reviews Higgs inflation in Einstein-Cartan gravity, revealing that oscillons formed during preheating are transient due to small-field self-interactions, affecting thermal history, inflationary observables, and gravitational wave signals.

\n\n
本文回顾了爱因斯坦-嘉当引力中的希格斯暴胀，揭示了预加热阶段形成的振荡子（oscillon）由于小场自相互作用是短暂的，这影响了宇宙热历史、暴胀可观测量和引力波信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Higgs inflation's preheating phase exhibits complex dynamics that depend crucially on the gravitational framework. The Einstein-Cartan formulation provides a unified description bridging metric and Palatini approaches, with the intermediate regime offering distinctive phenomenology. Understanding how nonlinear self-interactions affect oscillon stability and lifetime is essential for determining the post-inflationary thermal history and gravitational wave signatures.

\n\n
希格斯暴胀的预加热阶段展现出复杂的动力学行为，这在很大程度上取决于引力框架。爱因斯坦-嘉当表述提供了连接度规和Palatini方法的统一描述，其中间区域提供了独特的现象学。理解非线性自相互作用如何影响振荡子稳定性和寿命对于确定暴胀后的热历史和引力波特征至关重要。

Method: The analysis employs the Einstein-Cartan gravity framework as a unified description of Higgs inflation, with action $S = \\int d^4x \\sqrt{-g} \\left[ \\frac{M_{\\text{Pl}}^2}{2}R(\\Gamma) - \\frac{1}{2}g^{\\mu\\nu}\\partial_\\mu h\\partial_\\nu h - V(h) \\right]$ where $\Gamma$ represents the independent connection. The dynamics of the Higgs field $h$ during preheating are studied through nonlinear field equations incorporating both tachyonic instabilities and quartic self-interactions $\\lambda h^4$. Numerical simulations track the fragmentation of the inflaton condensate and oscillon formation using lattice techniques. The evolution is analyzed through Fourier mode decomposition, energy density distributions, and parametric resonance studies.

\n\n
该分析采用爱因斯坦-嘉当引力框架作为希格斯暴胀的统一描述，其作用量为 $S = \\int d^4x \\sqrt{-g} \\left[ \\frac{M_{\\text{Pl}}^2}{2}R(\\Gamma) - \\frac{1}{2}g^{\\mu\\nu}\\partial_\\mu h\\partial_\\nu h - V(h) \\right]$，其中 $\Gamma$ 表示独立联络。通过包含tachyonic不稳定性和四次自相互作用 $\lambda h^4$ 的非线性场方程研究预加热期间希格斯场 $h$ 的动力学。使用格点技术通过数值模拟追踪暴胀凝聚体的碎裂和振荡子形成。通过傅里叶模式分解、能量密度分布和参数共振研究分析演化过程。

Result: Initial tachyonic instabilities fragment the Higgs condensate into localized oscillon configurations. However, small-field self-interactions ($\\lambda h^4$ term) destabilize these structures, rendering them transient rather than long-lived. The Einstein-Cartan intermediate regime produces oscillon lifetimes dependent on the connection parameter $\alpha$ bridging metric ($\\alpha=1$) and Palatini ($\\alpha=0$) limits. The oscillon decay triggers radiation domination earlier than previously estimated, with thermalization occurring at temperatures $T_{\\text{therm}} \\sim 10^{14}$ GeV. This affects the tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ and spectral tilt $n_s$ through modified reheating history. Gravitational wave spectra show characteristic peaks at frequencies $f \\sim 10^9$ Hz with amplitudes $\\Omega_{\\text{GW}} \\sim 10^{-9}$.

\n\n
初始的tachyonic不稳定性将希格斯凝聚体碎裂成局域化的振荡子构型。然而，小场自相互作用（$\lambda h^4$ 项）使这些结构失稳，使其成为短暂而非长寿命的。爱因斯坦-嘉当中间区域产生的振荡子寿命取决于连接参数 $\alpha$，该参数桥接度规（$\alpha=1$）和Palatini（$\alpha=0$）极限。振荡子衰变触发了比先前估计更早的辐射主导，热化发生在温度 $T_{\\text{therm}} \\sim 10^{14}$ GeV。这通过修改的再加热历史影响了张量标量比 $r$ 和谱倾斜 $n_s$。引力波谱在频率 $f \\sim 10^9$ Hz 处显示出特征峰，振幅为 $\Omega_{\\text{GW}} \\sim 10^{-9}$。

Conclusion: The Einstein-Cartan formulation of Higgs inflation reveals that preheating oscillons are transient due to small-field self-interactions, not long-lived as previously speculated. This significantly shortens the matter-dominated phase and accelerates the onset of radiation domination, with important consequences for inflationary observables and gravitational wave backgrounds. The intermediate regime between metric and Palatini formulations offers testable predictions for future CMB and gravitational wave experiments.

\n\n
希格斯暴胀的爱因斯坦-嘉当表述揭示了由于小场自相互作用，预加热振荡子是短暂的，而非先前推测的长寿命。这显著缩短了物质主导阶段并加速了辐射主导的开始，对暴胀可观测量和引力波背景具有重要影响。度规和Palatini表述之间的中间区域为未来CMB和引力波实验提供了可检验的预测。

Abstract: We review recent progress in the understanding of the preheating stage of Higgs inflation formulated within the Einstein-Cartan framework of gravity. This setup smoothly interpolates between the metric and Palatini formulations of the theory, leading to a distinctive phenomenology in an intermediate regime. Following the end of inflation, the Higgs field undergoes a non-trivial out-of-equilibrium evolution driven by tachyonic instabilities and nonlinear self-interactions, which fragment the inflaton condensate and give rise to well-localized oscillon configurations. While early studies suggested the formation of long-lived oscillons and the possibility of an extended matter-dominated phase, more recent analyses show that self-interactions at small field values render these objects transient, eventually triggering their decay and the onset of radiation domination. We discuss the implications of this dynamics for the thermal history of the Universe, the inflationary observables, and the generation of stochastic gravitational waves.

*Zhi-Guo He,Guanghui Li,Yu-Jie Tian,Xin-Kai Wen,Bin Yan*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The color-octet mechanism is fundamental to NRQCD but faces limited determinations of its long-distance matrix elements, hindering stringent tests. The Artru-Collins asymmetry in $χ_{b2}$ decays offers a direct probe since it arises exclusively from color-octet dynamics while the color-singlet contribution affects only the unpolarized rate.

Method: Analysis focuses on $e^+e^-\toΥ(2S)\toγ\,χ_{b2}$ at Belle. The method shows that the asymmetric beam configuration preserves the Artru-Collins asymmetry in the laboratory frame and avoids suppression present in the center-of-mass frame, enabling extraction of $ρ_8$ from Belle II data.

Result: Demonstrates that the Artru-Collins asymmetry provides unambiguous evidence for color-octet dynamics and enables extraction of $ρ_8$ from Belle II data with sufficient precision to address discrepancies between lattice calculations and phenomenological determinations.

Abstract: The color-octet (CO) mechanism is a cornerstone of non-relativistic QCD, yet its long-distance matrix elements remain limited, preventing stringent tests of the theory. The asymmetry arises exclusively from the CO decay channel, whereas the color-singlet (CS) contribution affects only the unpolarized rate, so that a nonzero signal constitutes unambiguous evidence of the CO mechanism. This observable provides a novel way to extract the ratio $ρ_8$ between CO and CS matrix elements. Focusing on $e^+e^-\toΥ(2S)\toγ\,χ_{b2}$ at Belle, we show that the asymmetric beam configuration preserves the asymmetry in the laboratory frame and avoids the strong suppression present in the center-of-mass frame. ### [31] [Hadron production through Higgs decay at next-to-leading order in the general-mass variable-flavor-number scheme](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18875)
*S. Mohammad Moosavi Nejad*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a novel calculation of Higgs boson decay into B-mesons ($H \to B+Jets$) using the General-Mass Variable-Flavor-Number Scheme (GM-VFNs), incorporating both b-quark and B-meson mass effects for the first time, revealing significant enhancements in the partial decay width at low and intermediate scaled-energy regions.

\n\n
本文首次采用广义质量变味数方案(GM-VFNs)计算希格斯玻色子衰变为B介子($H \to B+Jets$)的过程，同时考虑了b夸克和B介子的质量效应，揭示了在低标度能区和峰值区域部分衰变宽度的显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Approximately 60% of Higgs bosons produced at the LHC decay into b-quark pairs, which subsequently hadronize into B-mesons. Previous studies have ignored the mass effects of both b-quarks and B-mesons by working in the massless scheme. This approximation may significantly affect the accuracy of predictions for the scaled-energy distribution ($x_B$) of B-mesons in Higgs decays, potentially impacting Higgs characterization studies.

\n\n
在LHC产生的希格斯玻色子中约60%衰变为b夸克对，随后强子化为B介子。先前的研究工作在无质量方案中忽略了b夸克和B介子的质量效应。这种近似可能显著影响希格斯衰变中B介子标度能分布($x_B$)预测的准确性，进而影响希格斯性质的研究。

Method: The authors employ the General-Mass Variable-Flavor-Number Scheme (GM-VFNs), which properly accounts for heavy quark and meson mass effects. This framework extends beyond traditional massless calculations by incorporating: 1) b-quark mass corrections to the partonic decay $H \to b\bar{b}$, 2) B-meson fragmentation functions with mass effects, and 3) perturbative QCD evolution with proper mass thresholds. The calculation focuses on the differential partial decay width $d\Gamma/dx_B$ for $H \to B+Jets$, where $x_B = 2E_B/m_H$ is the scaled energy of the B-meson.

\n\n
作者采用广义质量变味数方案(GM-VFNs)，该方案正确考虑了重夸克和介子的质量效应。该框架超越了传统的无质量计算，通过包含：1) b夸克质量对部分子衰变$H \to b\bar{b}$的修正，2) 具有质量效应的B介子碎裂函数，3) 具有适当质量阈值的微扰QCD演化。计算聚焦于$H \to B+Jets$的微分部分衰变宽度$d\Gamma/dx_B$，其中$x_B = 2E_B/m_H$是B介子的标度能量。

Result: The inclusion of mass effects leads to significant modifications of the scaled-energy distribution: 1) The B-meson mass generates a substantial enhancement of the partial decay width in the low-$x_B$ region ($x_B \lesssim 0.2$). 2) The b-quark mass causes an enhancement in the peak region and at higher $x_B$ values ($x_B \gtrsim 0.3$). These effects are non-negligible and highlight the importance of including both quark and hadron mass corrections for precise phenomenological predictions.

\n\n
质量效应的纳入导致标度能分布的显著修正：1) B介子质量在低$x_B$区域($x_B \lesssim 0.2$)引起部分衰变宽度的显著增强。2) b夸克质量在峰值区域和较高$x_B$值($x_B \gtrsim 0.3$)处导致增强。这些效应不可忽略，强调了包含夸克和强子质量修正对于精确现象学预测的重要性。

Conclusion: The GM-VFNs framework provides a more accurate theoretical description of $H \to B+Jets$ decays by properly accounting for heavy quark and meson mass effects. The significant enhancements found in both low-$x_B$ and peak regions demonstrate that previous massless approximations were inadequate for precision studies. This work establishes a foundation for more precise Higgs characterization through B-meson energy distributions at the LHC.

\n\n
GM-VFNs框架通过正确考虑重夸克和介子质量效应，为$H \to B+Jets$衰变提供了更精确的理论描述。在低$x_B$区域和峰值区域发现的显著增强表明，先前的无质量近似不足以进行精确研究。这项工作为通过LHC的B介子能分布实现更精确的希格斯性质研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: It is known that about $60\%$ of all Higgses produced at the CERN-LHC decay into a pair of bottom quarks. Bottoms quickly hadronize, in most cases, into bottom-flavored (B) hadrons before they decay. Therefore, the study of scaled-energy distribution of B-mesons in the decay process $H\to B+Jets$ can be considered as a channel to search for the Higgs characteristics. In all previous studies, authors have ignored the mass effect of b-quarks as well as B-mesons by working in the massless scheme. In this work we, for the first time, study the mass effect of b-quarks as well as produced mesons on the scaled-energy ($x_B$) distribution of B-mesons by working in the massive scheme or general-mass variable-flavor-number scheme (GM-VFNs). We find that the meson mass is responsible for a significant enhancement of partial decay width in the low-$x_B$ region while the b-quark mass leads to an enhancement of the partial decay rate in the peak region and above.

### [32] [Two-body strong decays of the pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquark states via the QCD sum rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18877)
*Yu-Hang Xu,Zhi-Gang Wang*

TL;DR: This paper studies pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquark states using QCD sum rules with rigorous quark-hadron duality to calculate their two-body strong decay widths. The analysis obtains precise decay widths for $Z_c^-$ and $Z_c^+$ states with $0^{--}$ and $0^{-+}$ quantum numbers respectively.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to investigate the properties of pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquark states, particularly their decay widths, through QCD sum rules. This addresses gaps in understanding exotic hadronic states beyond conventional mesons and baryons, specifically focusing on the pseudoscalar sector of tetraquarks with hidden-charm configurations.

Method: The authors employ QCD sum rules based on rigorous quark-hadron duality. They include vacuum condensates up to dimension 5 at the QCD side and calculate hadronic coupling constants. The method specifically analyzes two-body strong decays of pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquarks with explicit diquark-antidiquark structures: $[uc]_A[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_V-[uc]_V[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_A$ for $Z_c^+$ ($J^{PC}=0^{-+}$) and $[uc]_A[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_V+[uc]_V[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_A$ for $Z_c^-$ ($J^{PC}=0^{--}$).

Result: The main results are precise decay widths: $\\Gamma_{Z_{c}^{-}} = 326.197^{+4.255}_{-3.106}$ MeV for the $0^{--}$ state and $\\Gamma_{Z_{c}^{+}} = 91.835^{+0.96}_{-0.76}$ MeV for the $0^{-+}$ state. The $Z_c^-$ state has significantly broader width compared to $Z_c^+$, indicating different decay dynamics for these pseudoscalar tetraquark configurations.

Conclusion: The study successfully applies QCD sum rules to calculate decay widths of pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquarks, providing quantitative predictions for experimental searches. The substantial width difference between $Z_c^-$ and $Z_c^+$ states suggests different underlying quark structures and decay mechanisms, offering insights into exotic hadron spectroscopy.

Abstract: In this work, we study the properties of the pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquark states by analyzing their two-body strong decays via the QCD sum rules based on rigorous quark-hadron duality. We take into account the vacuum condensates up to dimension 5 at the QCD side, and obtain the hadronic coupling constants. At last, we obtain the total decay widths $Γ_{Z_{c}^{-}} = 326.197^{+4.255}_{-3.106}$ MeV and $Γ_{Z_{c}^{+}} = 91.835^{+0.96}_{-0.76}$ MeV, respectively, where the $Z_{c}^{+}$($J^{PC}=0^{-+}$) and $Z_{c}^{-}$($J^{PC}=0^{--}$) denote the pseudoscalar hidden-charm tetraquarks with the diquark-antidiquark structures $[uc]_{A}[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_{V}-[uc]_{V}[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_{A}$ and $[uc]_{A}[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_{V}+[uc]_{V}[\bar{d}\bar{c}]_{A}$, respectively.

### [33] [Direct $CP$ violation in $D^\pm \to π^\pm π^+ π^-$ with $a_0^0(980)-f_0(980)$ mixing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18917)
*Shi-Ji Cao,Jing-Juan Qi,Yi-Fan Zhao,Chao Wang,Zhen-Yang Wang,Xin-Heng Guo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates $CP$ violation in $D^\pm \to π^\pm π^+ π^-$ decays through the $a_0^0(980)$-$f_0(980)$ mixing mechanism, finding that this isospin-breaking effect enhances $CP$ asymmetries near the $f_0(980)$ resonance, with optimal enhancement occurring when $f_0(980)$ has significant $n\bar{n}$ quark content and specific mixing angles around $26^\circ$.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study is motivated by the search for direct $CP$ violation in charm decays, which is suppressed in the Standard Model and thus provides a sensitive probe for new physics. The $a_0^0(980)$-$f_0(980)$ mixing represents an isospin-breaking mechanism that could significantly enhance $CP$ asymmetries in $D^\pm \to π^\pm π^+ π^-$ decays, particularly near scalar resonance regions. Understanding this mechanism could have important implications for both theoretical and experimental studies of $CP$ violation in $B$ and $D$ meson decays.

Method: The authors employ an effective theoretical framework incorporating the $a_0^0(980)$-$f_0(980)$ mixing mechanism. They calculate the integrated mixing intensities $\overline ξ_{fa}$ and $\overline ξ_{af}$ using meson masses and coupling constants extracted from various theoretical models and experimental data. The analysis focuses on specific kinematic regions where the invariant mass of the $π^+π^-$ pair lies near the $f_0(980)$ resonance, and explores parameter space including the $n\bar{n}$ quark content fraction of $f_0(980)$ and the $f_0(980)$-$σ(600)$ mixing angle.

Result: The calculated integrated mixing intensities $\overline ξ_{fa}$ and $\overline ξ_{af}$ yield values of appreciable magnitude. The key finding is that the $a_0^0(980)$-$f_0(980)$ mixing mechanism can significantly enhance $CP$ asymmetry in $D^\pm \to π^\pm π^+ π^-$ decays. This enhancement is most pronounced when the invariant mass of the $π^+π^-$ pair is near the $f_0(980)$ resonance. Optimal enhancement occurs when $f_0(980)$ carries a significant $n\bar{n}$ quark component and the mixing angle between $f_0(980)$ and $σ(600)$ is approximately $26^\circ$.

This mechanism should be systematically incorporated in both theoretical calculations and experimental analyses of $CP$ violation in $B$ and $D$ meson decays, as it could provide enhanced sensitivity to new physics beyond the Standard Model.

Abstract: We investigate the direct $CP$ violation in the decay $D^\pm \to π^\pm π^+ π^-$ incorporating the $a_0^0(980)$-$f_0(980)$ mixing mechanism. The integrated mixing intensities $\overline ξ_{fa}$ and $\overline ξ_{af}$ are calculated using meson masses and coupling constants extracted from various theoretical models and experimental data, yielding values of appreciable magnitude. We find that when the invariant mass of the $π^+π^-$pair lies near the $f_0(980)$ resonance, this isospin breaking mechanism can enhance the $CP$ asymmetry. The enhancement is particularly pronounced when $f_0(980)$ carries a significant $n\bar{n}$ quark component and the $f_0(980)$ and $σ(600)$ mixing angle is approximately $26^\circ$. It is emphasized that the $a_0^0(980)$-$f_0(980)$ mixing mechanism can be taken into account in both theoretical and experimental studies of $CP$ violation in $B$ or $D$ meson decays.
