### [34] [Transverse spin effects and light-quark dipole moments at colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18951)
*Xin-Kai Wen,Bin Yan,Zhite Yu,C. -P. Yuan*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper introduces novel methods for probing light-quark dipole interactions at colliders using azimuthal asymmetries in dihadron production. Two complementary approaches are presented: (1) measuring asymmetries in semi-inclusive deep inelastic scattering at the Electron-Ion Collider, and (2) utilizing asymmetries in dihadron production with an additional hadron at lepton colliders. These asymmetries provide unique sensitivity to transversely polarized quarks arising from quantum interference effects, offering linear dependence on dipole couplings, separation of up- and down-quark contributions, distinction between photon and weak boson mediation, and simultaneous determination of real and imaginary parts for CP-violation studies.

\n\n
这篇论文介绍了在碰撞机上探测轻夸克偶极相互作用的新方法，利用双强子产生中的方位角不对称性。提出了两种互补方法：(1)在电子-离子对撞机上半包含深度非弹性散射中测量不对称性，(2)在轻子对撞机上利用伴随额外强子产生的双强子不对称性。这些不对称性对由量子干涉效应产生的横向极化夸克具有独特敏感性，提供偶极耦合的线性依赖性、上下夸克贡献的分离、光子与弱玻色子媒介的区分，以及对实部和虚部的同时确定用于CP破坏研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation for this work stems from the need to probe beyond Standard Model (BSM) physics through quark dipole interactions, which are suppressed in the SM but could be enhanced in new physics scenarios. Current experimental constraints on light-quark dipole interactions are relatively weak, and existing methods often suffer from contamination by other BSM effects or have only quadratic dependence on dipole couplings. The authors aim to develop sensitive probes that: (1) provide linear dependence on dipole couplings for enhanced sensitivity, (2) are exclusively sensitive to dipole interactions at leading power, (3) allow separation of contributions from different quark flavors and interaction mediators, and (4) enable studies of CP-violation through simultaneous determination of real and imaginary parts of the couplings.

\n\n
这项工作的动机源于需要通过夸克偶极相互作用探测超越标准模型(BSM)物理，这些相互作用在标准模型中被压制，但在新物理情景中可能增强。目前对轻夸克偶极相互作用的实验约束相对较弱，现有方法常受到其他BSM效应的污染或仅具有对偶极耦合的二次依赖性。作者旨在开发灵敏探测器，实现：(1)对偶极耦合提供线性依赖性以增强灵敏度，(2)在领头幂次下对偶极相互作用具有排他敏感性，(3)允许分离不同夸克味道和相互作用媒介的贡献，(4)通过同时确定耦合的实部和虚部实现CP破坏研究。

Method: The paper develops two complementary methods based on azimuthal asymmetries in dihadron production:

1. **Semi-inclusive Deep Inelastic Scattering (SIDIS) at EIC**: Measuring azimuthal asymmetries of a collinear dihadron pair $(h_1 h_2)$ in lepton-proton scattering. The differential cross-section can be parameterized as:
   $$\\frac{d\\sigma}{dxdQ^2dzd\\phi_{R_T}} = \\sigma_0[1 + A_{UU}\\cos\\phi_{R_T} + \\cdots]$$
   where $\\phi_{R_T}$ is the azimuthal angle of the dihadron transverse momentum $R_T$. The asymmetry $A_{UU}$ is sensitive to the interference between the photon-exchange amplitude and the dipole operator.

2. **Dihadron plus additional hadron at lepton colliders**: Utilizing azimuthal asymmetries of dihadron $(h_1 h_2)$ produced in association with an additional hadron $h^\\prime$. This approach provides additional handles for flavor separation and mediator discrimination.

Theoretical framework employs QCD factorization theorems for dihadron fragmentation functions, where the dipole operator appears through interference with the SM amplitude. The azimuthal modulation arises from the transverse polarization of quarks generated by quantum interference between the standard electromagnetic/weak interaction and the dipole interaction.

\n\n
论文基于双强子产生中的方位角不对称性开发了两种互补方法：

1. **电子-离子对撞机(EIC)上的半包含深度非弹性散射(SIDIS)**：测量轻子-质子散射中双强子对$(h_1 h_2)$的方位角不对称性。微分截面可参数化为：
   $$\\frac{d\\sigma}{dxdQ^2dzd\\phi_{R_T}} = \\sigma_0[1 + A_{UU}\\cos\\phi_{R_T} + \\cdots]$$
   其中$\\phi_{R_T}$是双强子横向动量$R_T$的方位角。不对称性$A_{UU}$对光子交换振幅与偶极算符之间的干涉敏感。

2. **轻子对撞机上的双强子加额外强子**：利用伴随额外强子$h^\\prime$产生的双强子$(h_1 h_2)$的方位角不对称性。该方法为味道分离和媒介子区分提供了额外控制手段。

理论框架采用双强子碎裂函数的QCD因子化定理，其中偶极算符通过与标准模型振幅的干涉出现。方位角调制源于量子干涉效应产生的夸克横向极化，这种干涉发生在标准电磁/弱相互作用与偶极相互作用之间。

Result: The key results include:

1. **Linear dependence on dipole couplings**: The azimuthal asymmetries exhibit linear dependence on the dipole couplings $d_q^\\gamma$ and $d_q^Z$, in contrast to traditional probes that typically have quadratic dependence. This enhances sensitivity by $\\sim 1-2$ orders of magnitude compared to current constraints.

2. **Flavor separation**: By combining all possible channels of the additional hadron $h^\\prime$, the method enables disentanglement of up- and down-quark dipole moments through different fragmentation patterns and production cross-sections.

3. **Mediator discrimination**: Controlling the electron's longitudinal polarization and center-of-mass energy allows separation of contributions mediated by photon and weak bosons. The polarization asymmetry $A_{LR}$ isolates the weak boson contribution.

4. **CP-violation sensitivity**: The method allows simultaneous determination of both real and imaginary parts of the dipole couplings $\\text{Re}(d_q)$ and $\\text{Im}(d_q)$, providing a direct probe of CP-violating effects through interference terms.

5. **Projected sensitivity**: The approach could strengthen current constraints by one to two orders of magnitude, with estimated limits of $|d_q| \\lesssim 10^{-19}$ e·cm for light quarks at future colliders.

6. **Exclusive sensitivity**: At leading power in the new physics scale $\\Lambda$, these asymmetries are exclusively sensitive to dipole interactions without contamination from other dimension-six operators.

\n\n
关键结果包括：

1. **对偶极耦合的线性依赖性**：方位角不对称性对偶极耦合$d_q^\\gamma$和$d_q^Z$呈现线性依赖性，这与通常具有二次依赖性的传统探测器形成对比。与当前约束相比，这使灵敏度提高了$\\sim 1-2$个数量级。

2. **味道分离**：通过组合额外强子$h^\\prime$的所有可能通道，该方法通过不同的碎裂模式和产生截面实现了上下夸克偶极矩的解耦。

3. **媒介子区分**：控制电子纵向极化和质心能量允许分离由光子和弱玻色子媒介的贡献。极化不对称性$A_{LR}$隔离了弱玻色子贡献。

4. **CP破坏敏感性**：该方法允许同时确定偶极耦合的实部和虚部$\\text{Re}(d_q)$和$\\text{Im}(d_q)$，通过干涉项直接探测CP破坏效应。

5. **预计灵敏度**：该方法可将当前约束加强一至两个数量级，预计在未来对撞机上对轻夸克的限制可达$|d_q| \\lesssim 10^{-19}$ e·cm。

6. **排他敏感性**：在新物理尺度$\\Lambda$的领头幂次下，这些不对称性对偶极相互作用具有排他敏感性，不受其他六维算符的污染。

Conclusion: The paper presents novel, highly sensitive probes for light-quark dipole interactions that overcome limitations of traditional methods. By exploiting azimuthal asymmetries in dihadron production through quantum interference effects, the proposed approaches offer: (1) linear sensitivity to dipole couplings for enhanced reach, (2) clean separation of flavor and mediator contributions, (3) simultaneous access to CP-conserving and CP-violating components, and (4) exclusivity to dipole interactions at leading power. These methods are particularly promising for implementation at future facilities like the Electron-Ion Collider and high-energy lepton colliders, where they could improve constraints by orders of magnitude and provide new avenues for discovering BSM physics through quark dipole moments.

\n\n
该论文提出了探测轻夸克偶极相互作用的新颖、高灵敏度方法，克服了传统方法的局限性。通过利用量子干涉效应在双强子产生中产生的方位角不对称性，所提出的方法提供：(1)对偶极耦合的线性灵敏度以增强探测能力，(2)味道和媒介子贡献的清洁分离，(3)同时访问CP守恒和CP破坏分量，(4)在领头幂次下对偶极相互作用的排他敏感性。这些方法特别有希望在电子-离子对撞机和高能轻子对撞机等未来设施中实施，可将约束改进数个数量级，并通过夸克偶极矩为发现BSM物理提供新途径。

Abstract: In this talk, we present novel methods to investigate light-quark dipole interactions at colliders. Our approach includes: (1) measuring azimuthal asymmetries of a collinear dihadron in semi-inclusive deep inelastic lepton scattering off an unpolarized proton target at the Electron-Ion Collider, and (2) utilizing azimuthal asymmetries of dihadron $(h_1 h_2)$ produced in association with an additional hadron $h^\prime$ at lepton colliders. These asymmetries provide a unique means to observe transversely polarized quarks, which arise from quantum interference and are exclusively sensitive to dipole interactions at the leading power of the new physics scale. Consequently, they exhibit a linear dependence on the dipole couplings, free from contamination by other new physics effects. This approach has the potential to significantly strengthen current constraints by one to two orders of magnitude. By combining all possible channels of $h^\prime$, this novel approach enables the disentanglement of the up- and down-quark dipole moments. Additionally, by controlling the electron's longitudinal polarization and the center-of-mass energy, it separates the contributions mediated by photon and weak boson. Furthermore, it allows for a simultaneous determination of both real and imaginary parts of the dipole couplings, offering a new avenue for investigating potential $CP$-violating effects at high energies.

### [35] [The impact of prescriptions in phenomenological extractions of Transverse Momentum Dependent distributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19088)
*Matteo Cerutti,Andrea Simonelli*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper investigates how different phenomenological choices for the $b_*$ prescription in the Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS) formalism affect global extractions of Transverse Momentum Distributions (TMDs). It finds that while fits to low-energy Drell-Yan data yield similar TMDs at small partonic transverse momentum regardless of $b_*$ choice, significant differences emerge at intermediate transverse momenta, impacting predictions for high-energy Drell-Yan processes. The $b_*$ prescription is identified as an intrinsic source of theoretical uncertainty in the CSS approach.

本文研究了Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS)形式中$b_*$参数化方案的不同唯象选择如何影响横向动量分布(TMDs)的全局提取。研究发现，尽管使用不同的$b_*$选择对低能Drell-Yan数据进行拟合在较小的部分子横向动量处得到相似的TMDs，但在中间横向动量区域出现了显著差异，这影响了对高能Drell-Yan过程的预测。$b_*$参数化方案被确定为CSS方法中一个固有的理论不确定性来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS) formalism has become the standard framework for describing transverse momentum distributions (TMDs) in processes like Drell-Yan, but it relies on phenomenological prescriptions to handle non-perturbative contributions through the $b_*$ parameter. While TMD extractions have achieved impressive agreement with experimental data, the dependence on the specific choice of $b_*$ prescription remains largely unexplored. Understanding how these phenomenological choices affect TMD determinations and predictions across different energy scales is crucial for assessing theoretical uncertainties in the CSS approach and ensuring robust interpretations of TMD physics.

Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS)形式已成为描述Drell-Yan等过程中横向动量分布(TMDs)的标准框架，但它依赖于通过$b_*$参数处理非微扰贡献的唯象参数化方案。虽然TMD提取已实现了与实验数据的显著一致性，但特定$b_*$参数化方案选择的依赖性在很大程度上仍未得到探索。理解这些唯象选择如何影响不同能量尺度下的TMD确定和预测，对于评估CSS方法中的理论不确定性和确保TMD物理的稳健解释至关重要。

Method: The study employs systematic global fits of TMDs using the CSS framework with different $b_*$ prescriptions. The analysis compares multiple phenomenological implementations of the $b_*$ function, which regulates the divergence of the TMD evolution at large impact parameter $b_T$. The method involves:

1. Performing simultaneous fits to Drell-Yan data at different energies using various $b_*$ prescriptions
2. Extracting TMD parton distribution functions (TMD PDFs) from these fits
3. Comparing the resulting TMDs at small partonic transverse momentum $k_T$
4. Examining differences in TMD behavior at intermediate $k_T$ regions
5. Assessing the impact on predictions for high-energy Drell-Yan processes
6. Quantifying the theoretical uncertainty introduced by the $b_*$ prescription choice

The approach systematically disentangles the effects of phenomenological choices from genuine TMD properties.

该研究采用CSS框架配合不同的$b_*$参数化方案进行TMD的全局拟合。分析比较了$b_*$函数的多种唯象实现方式，该函数在大冲击参数$b_T$处调节TMD演化的发散性。方法包括：

1. 使用不同的$b_*$参数化方案对不同能量的Drell-Yan数据进行同步拟合
2. 从这些拟合中提取TMD部分子分布函数(TMD PDFs)
3. 比较在较小部分子横向动量$k_T$处得到的TMDs
4. 检查在中间$k_T$区域的TMD行为差异
5. 评估对高能Drell-Yan过程预测的影响
6. 量化由$b_*$参数化方案选择引入的理论不确定性

该方法系统地将唯象选择的影响与真实TMD特性分离开来。

Result: The analysis reveals several key findings:

1. **Low-energy agreement**: Different $b_*$ prescriptions produce equally good fits to low-energy Drell-Yan data, with similar TMD behavior at small partonic transverse momentum $k_T$.

2. **Intermediate $k_T$ divergence**: Significant differences emerge in the extracted TMDs at intermediate transverse momentum regions, despite agreement at small $k_T$.

3. **High-energy impact**: These differences substantially affect predictions for high-energy Drell-Yan processes, demonstrating that the $b_*$ prescription choice propagates through TMD evolution.

4. **Theoretical uncertainty**: The $b_*$ prescription represents an intrinsic source of theoretical uncertainty in the CSS approach, with systematic effects that influence TMD extractions and their interpretation.

5. **Energy scale interplay**: The analysis highlights the importance of using data across different energy scales to properly assess the impact of phenomenological prescriptions in TMD fits.

The results show that while CSS-based TMD extractions are robust for describing data at specific energies, the choice of $b_*$ prescription introduces ambiguities that become particularly relevant when extrapolating to different energy regimes.

分析揭示了几个关键发现：

1. **低能一致性**：不同的$b_*$参数化方案对低能Drell-Yan数据产生同样良好的拟合，在较小的部分子横向动量$k_T$处具有相似的TMD行为。

2. **中间$k_T$发散**：尽管在较小$k_T$处一致，但在中间横向动量区域提取的TMDs出现了显著差异。

3. **高能影响**：这些差异显著影响高能Drell-Yan过程的预测，表明$b_*$参数化方案的选择通过TMD演化传播。

4. **理论不确定性**：$b_*$参数化方案代表了CSS方法中一个固有的理论不确定性来源，其系统效应影响TMD提取及其解释。

5. **能量尺度相互作用**：分析强调了使用跨不同能量尺度的数据来正确评估唯象参数化方案在TMD拟合中的影响的重要性。

结果表明，虽然基于CSS的TMD提取对于描述特定能量下的数据是稳健的，但$b_*$参数化方案的选择引入了模糊性，这些模糊性在推断到不同能量状态时变得尤为重要。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that the phenomenological $b_*$ prescription in the CSS formalism introduces a systematic source of theoretical uncertainty in global TMD extractions. While different prescriptions yield similar TMDs and good agreement with low-energy data at small $k_T$, they produce significantly different behavior at intermediate transverse momenta, which substantially affects predictions for high-energy processes. This finding has important implications for TMD phenomenology:

1. The $b_*$ prescription ambiguity must be accounted for when assessing theoretical uncertainties in CSS-based TMD determinations.
2. Future TMD extractions should incorporate multiple $b_*$ prescriptions to properly quantify systematic uncertainties.
3. Data from different energy scales are essential for constraining the effects of phenomenological choices in the CSS framework.
4. The results highlight the need for more fundamental theoretical understanding of the $b_*$ regulator beyond phenomenological parameterizations.

The work establishes that phenomenological prescriptions in the CSS approach cannot be considered merely technical choices but represent genuine theoretical uncertainties that impact the interpretation of TMD physics across different energy regimes.

研究表明，CSS形式中的唯象$b_*$参数化方案在全局TMD提取中引入了系统性的理论不确定性来源。虽然不同的参数化方案在较小的$k_T$处产生相似的TMDs并与低能数据良好一致，但它们在中间横向动量处产生了显著不同的行为，这极大地影响了对高能过程的预测。这一发现对TMD唯象学具有重要意义：

1. 在评估基于CSS的TMD确定中的理论不确定性时，必须考虑$b_*$参数化方案的模糊性。
2. 未来的TMD提取应纳入多种$b_*$参数化方案，以正确量化系统不确定性。
3. 来自不同能量尺度的数据对于约束CSS框架中唯象选择的影响至关重要。
4. 结果强调了对$b_*$调节器超出唯象参数化的更基本理论理解的需求。

这项工作确立了CSS方法中的唯象参数化方案不能仅仅被视为技术选择，而是代表了影响跨不同能量状态的TMD物理解释的真实理论不确定性。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of phenomenological prescriptions in the Collins-Soper-Sterman (CSS) approach for global extractions of Transverse Momentum Distributions (TMDs). We show that fits to low-energy Drell-Yan data with different choices of $b_*$ prescription yield equally good agreement with data and similar TMDs at small partonic transverse momentum. In contrast, sizable differences emerge at intermediate transverse momentum region, significantly affecting the predictions for high-energy Drell-Yan processes. Our results demonstrate that the $b_*$ prescription represents an intrinsic source of theoretical uncertainty in the CSS approach, introducing systematic effects that influence TMD extractions and their interpretation. At the same time, our analysis emphasizes the interplay between data at different energy scales in assessing the effect of phenomenological prescriptions in TMD fits adopting the CSS framework.

### [36] [Matter Unification and Lepton Flavour Violation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.02313)
*Hridoy Debnath,Pavel Fileviez Perez*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We investigate minimal quark-lepton unification models at multi-TeV scales where neutrino masses arise via inverse seesaw. Analyzing experimental constraints from lepton number violating meson decays and $\mu\to e$ conversion, we show upcoming Mu2e/Fermilab experiments can probe this unification framework, establishing lower bounds on symmetry breaking scales.

我们研究多TeV能标下的最小夸克-轻子统一模型，其中中微子质量通过逆跷跷板机制产生。分析来自轻子数破坏介子衰变和$\mu\to e$转换的实验限制，我们显示即将到来的Mu2e/Fermilab实验可以探测这一统一框架，确定对称性破缺能标的下限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While traditional grand unification theories operate at extremely high energies ($\sim10^{15-16}$ GeV) beyond direct experimental reach, this work explores the possibility of quark-lepton unification at accessible multi-TeV scales. Such low-scale unification requires novel mechanisms for neutrino mass generation (inverse seesaw) and addresses the experimental testability gap in traditional unification scenarios. The motivation centers on connecting quark and lepton sectors through extended gauge symmetries at energies potentially accessible to current and near-future colliders.

虽然传统的大统一理论在极高的能标($\sim10^{15-16}$ GeV)运作，超出直接实验探测范围，本工作探索了在多TeV可及能标下实现夸克-轻子统一的可能性。这种低能标统一需要新颖的中微子质量产生机制(逆跷跷板)，并解决了传统统一方案中的实验可检验性差距。动机集中在通过当前和近未来对撞机可能达到的能量尺度上的扩展规范对称性连接夸克和轻子扇区。

Method: The analysis employs a minimal gauge extension of the Standard Model implementing quark-lepton unification at the multi-TeV scale, incorporating the inverse seesaw mechanism for neutrino mass generation. Methodologically, the work: (1) constructs the symmetry breaking pattern and particle content with Pati-Salam-like gauge group extensions, (2) derives the mass matrices and mixing parameters including quark-lepton mixing angles, (3) computes lepton flavor violating (LFV) and lepton number violating (LNV) amplitudes using effective field theory techniques, (4) systematically analyzes experimental constraints from rare meson decays ($K^+\to\pi^-\mu^+\mu^+$, $D^+\to\pi^-\mu^+\mu^+$, etc.), (5) calculates $\mu\to e$ conversion rates in nuclei with proper nuclear form factors, and (6) performs a comprehensive parameter space scan incorporating unknown mixing angles.

分析采用了标准模型的最小规范扩展，在多TeV能标实现夸克-轻子统一，结合了中微子质量产生的逆跷跷板机制。方法论上，该工作：(1)构造对称性破缺模式和粒子内容，包含类Pati-Salam规范群扩展，(2)推导质量矩阵和混合参数，包括夸克-轻子混合角，(3)使用有效场论技术计算轻子味破坏(LFV)和轻子数破坏(LNV)振幅，(4)系统分析来自稀有介子衰变($K^+\to\pi^-\mu^+\mu^+$, $D^+\to\pi^-\mu^+\mu^+$, 等)的实验约束，(5)在核中计算$\mu\to e$转换率，采用适当的核形状因子，(6)执行包含未知混合角的全面参数空间扫描。

Result: Key results include: (1) derivation of lower bounds on the quark-lepton unification scale from current LNV meson decay limits, establishing constraints of $\Lambda_{\text{unification}} \gtrsim \mathcal{O}(10)$ TeV depending on mixing parameters; (2) demonstration that $\mu\to e$ conversion experiments offer complementary and potentially stronger constraints due to different parameter dependencies; (3) identification of parameter regions where upcoming Fermilab experiments (Mu2e) can probe scales up to $\Lambda \sim 100$ TeV, significantly extending beyond LHC direct search reach; (4) explicit correlation functions between meson decay and $\mu\to e$ conversion rates revealing the interplay between different experimental probes; (5) determination that the most stringent constraints arise from $K^+\to\pi^-\mu^+\mu^+$ decays when quark-lepton mixing angles are aligned with Cabibbo-like patterns.

关键结果包括：(1)从当前LNV介子衰变限制推导夸克-轻子统一能标的下限，建立$\Lambda_{\text{unification}} \gtrsim \mathcal{O}(10)$ TeV的约束，取决于混合参数；(2)证明$\mu\to e$转换实验由于不同的参数依赖性提供互补且可能更强的约束；(3)识别参数区域，其中即将到来的Fermilab实验(Mu2e)可以探测高达$\Lambda \sim 100$ TeV的能标，显著超越LHC直接搜索范围；(4)介子衰变和$\mu\to e$转换率之间的明确关联函数，揭示不同实验探针之间的相互作用；(5)确定当夸克-轻子混合角与类Cabibbo模式对齐时，最严格的约束来自$K^+\to\pi^-\mu^+\mu^+$衰变。

Conclusion: The study establishes that low-scale quark-lepton unification with inverse seesaw neutrino masses is experimentally testable through a combination of lepton number violating meson decays and lepton flavor violating $\mu\to e$ conversion processes. The upcoming Fermilab $\mu\to e$ conversion experiments (Mu2e) will play a decisive role in probing multi-TeV unification scales, potentially discovering or excluding these models. The framework provides a concrete bridge between neutrino mass generation mechanisms and collider-scale unification physics, with the correlation between different experimental signatures offering a distinctive pattern for model discrimination. This approach revitalizes the phenomenological study of quark-lepton unification by connecting it to accessible energy scales and near-future experimental programs.

该研究确定，通过轻子数破坏介子衰变和轻子味破坏$\mu\to e$转换过程的结合，具有逆跷跷板中微子质量的低能标夸克-轻子统一是实验可检验的。即将到来的Fermilab $\mu\to e$转换实验(Mu2e)将在探测多TeV统一能标中起决定性作用，可能发现或排除这些模型。该框架提供了中微子质量产生机制和对撞机能标统一物理学之间的具体桥梁，不同实验特征之间的关联为模型区分提供了独特模式。这种方法通过将夸克-轻子统一与可及能标和近未来实验项目联系起来，重振了其现象学研究。

Abstract: We explore the idea of quark-lepton unification at low energies. In particular, we discuss the minimal framework for matter unification at the multi-TeV scale, in which neutrino masses are necessarily generated via the inverse seesaw mechanism. To assess the testability of this theory for physics beyond the Standard Model, we analyze current experimental constraints and derive the corresponding lower bound on the symmetry breaking scale. We reexamine the impact of existing limits from lepton number violating meson decays, taking into account the freedom associated with unknown quark-lepton mixing angles. Furthermore, we study the correlation between bounds from meson decays and $μ\to e$ conversion. We demonstrate that the upcoming $μ\to e$ conversion experiment at Fermilab can play a crucial role in probing quark-lepton unification at the multi-TeV scale.

</details>


### [37] [Gamma-ray production in the cosmic-ray -- dark matter scattering as a probe of the axion-like particle -- proton interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19103)
*Victor P. Goncalves,Emmanuel Moulin,Igor Reis,Aion Viana*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [Proposes using ground-based VHE gamma-ray observatories (H.E.S.S., CTAO, SWGO) to probe the axion-like particle (ALP)-proton coupling $g_{ap}$ via cosmic-ray proton scattering off ALP dark matter in the Milky Way halo. Demonstrates sensitivity to $g_{ap} > 10^{-2}$ for ALP masses $1 - 10^8$ eV, covering unexplored regions and probing QCD axion models like KSVZ/DFSZ in the MeV range.]

\n\n
[提出利用地面甚高能伽马射线天文台（H.E.S.S.、CTAO、SWGO），通过宇宙射线质子在银河系暗物质晕中与类轴子粒子散射的过程，探测ALP-质子耦合常数$g_{ap}$。证明了在ALP质量$1 - 10^8$ eV范围内，对$g_{ap} > 10^{-2}$的灵敏度，覆盖了尚未探索的区域，并能在MeV质量范围内探测KSVZ/DFSZ等QCD轴子模型。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The axion-like particle (ALP)-proton coupling $g_{ap}$ remains largely unconstrained, especially in the ALP mass range $1 - 10^8$ eV, which lies beyond the sensitivity of traditional probes like supernova and neutron star cooling. A novel observational channel is needed to explore this parameter space. Scattering of high-energy cosmic-ray protons off ALPs constituting the Milky Way's dark matter halo can produce distinctive very-high-energy (VHE, $E_γ \gtrsim 100$ GeV) gamma rays, detectable by current and upcoming ground-based gamma-ray observatories.]

\n\n
[类轴子粒子与质子的耦合常数$g_{ap}$在很大程度上仍未被约束，特别是在ALP质量$1 - 10^8$ eV范围内，这超出了超新星和中子星冷却等传统探测方法的灵敏度范围。需要一种新颖的观测通道来探索此参数空间。高能宇宙射线质子与构成银河系暗物质晕的ALPs发生散射，可以产生独特的甚高能（VHE，$E_γ \gtrsim 100$ GeV）伽马射线，可被当前和未来的地面伽马射线天文台探测到。]

Method: [Theoretical calculation of the VHE gamma-ray flux from the process $p + ALP \rightarrow p + γ$ (or analogous scattering) using the ALP-proton interaction Lagrangian $\mathcal{L} \supset g_{ap} a \bar{p} γ_5 p$. The ALPs are treated as cold dark matter with a Milky Way halo density profile (likely NFW or similar). The cosmic-ray proton spectrum is taken from experimental data. The gamma-ray flux is then convolved with the instrument response functions (IRFs) of H.E.S.S., CTAO, and SWGO to compute the expected signal and derive sensitivity limits on $g_{ap}$ as a function of ALP mass $m_a$. Benchmark QCD axion models (KSVZ and DFSZ) are mapped onto the $(m_a, g_{ap})$ plane for comparison.]

\n\n
[理论计算过程 $p + ALP \rightarrow p + γ$（或类似散射）产生的VHE伽马射线通量，使用ALP-质子相互作用拉格朗日量 $\mathcal{L} \supset g_{ap} a \bar{p} γ_5 p$。ALPs被视为冷暗物质，采用银河系晕密度分布轮廓（可能是NFW或类似模型）。宇宙射线质子谱取自实验数据。然后将伽马射线通量与H.E.S.S.、CTAO和SWGO的仪器响应函数卷积，以计算预期信号并推导出对$g_{ap}$随ALP质量$m_a$变化的灵敏度极限。将基准QCD轴子模型（KSVZ和DFSZ）映射到$(m_a, g_{ap})$平面上进行比较。]

Result: [Sensitivity projections for H.E.S.S., CTAO, and SWGO show that these experiments can probe ALP-proton couplings $g_{ap} \gtrsim 10^{-2}$ across the mass range $m_a \sim 1$ eV to $10^8$ eV. This region is largely complementary to and extends beyond constraints from supernova cooling and neutron star observations. Crucially, the projected sensitivity enters the parameter space predicted by specific QCD axion models, notably the KSVZ and DFSZ models, for axion masses in the MeV range. The exact reach depends on the observatory, exposure time, and background assumptions, but the channel is shown to be competitive and uniquely sensitive to $g_{ap}$ for VHE gamma rays.]

\n\n
[H.E.S.S.、CTAO和SWGO的灵敏度预测表明，这些实验能够在质量范围$m_a \sim 1$ eV至$10^8$ eV内探测到ALP-质子耦合$g_{ap} \gtrsim 10^{-2}$。该区域与超新星冷却和中子星观测的约束在很大程度上互补并有所扩展。关键在于，预测的灵敏度进入了特定QCD轴子模型（特别是KSVZ和DFSZ模型）在MeV质量范围内的参数空间。具体的探测范围取决于天文台、曝光时间和本底假设，但该通道被证明具有竞争力，并且对VHE伽马射线的$g_{ap}$具有独特的灵敏度。]

Conclusion: [Ground-based VHE gamma-ray astronomy provides a powerful, novel, and complementary probe of the ALP-proton coupling $g_{ap}$, capable of exploring a broad, previously inaccessible mass range from eV to $10^8$ eV. The sensitivity reach overlaps with the parameter space of well-motivated QCD axion dark matter models (KSVZ/DFSZ) in the MeV range. This establishes VHE gamma-ray observations as a crucial component in the multi-messenger effort to constrain ALP interactions with the baryonic sector of the Standard Model.]

\n\n
[地面VHE伽马射线天文学为探测ALP-质子耦合$g_{ap}$提供了一种强大、新颖且互补的手段，能够探索从eV到$10^8$ eV的广泛且此前无法触及的质量范围。其灵敏度范围与有充分物理动机的QCD轴子暗物质模型（KSVZ/DFSZ）在MeV质量范围内的参数空间存在重叠。这确立了VHE伽马射线观测作为多信使努力中约束ALP与标准模型重子部分相互作用的关键组成部分。]

Abstract: The production of very-high-energy (VHE, $E_γ \gtrsim 100$ GeV) gamma rays resulting from the scattering of high-energy cosmic-ray protons off axion-like particles (ALPs) populating the dark matter halo of the Milky Way is investigated. By employing the latest instrument response functions for current and future facilities, we demonstrate that ground-based VHE gamma-ray observatories, such as H.E.S.S., CTAO, and SWGO, provide a promising and complementary avenue to probe the yet uncharted ALP-proton coupling $g_{ap}$. Our results show that these experiments can reach sensitivity to couplings above $10^{-2}$ in the $1 - 10^{8}$ eV ALP mass range, a region that remains largely unexplored by supernova and neutron star cooling observations. Interestingly, we demonstrate that this search channel is capable of probing QCD axion dark matter models, assuming two benchmark models for it: the Kim-Shifman-Vainshtein-Zakharov (KSVZ) Dine-Fischler-Srednicki-Zhitnitsky (DFSZ) models, specifically within the MeV mass range. These findings highlight the potential of VHE gamma-ray astronomy to provide unique constraints on the interaction between ALPs and the baryonic sector.

</details>


### [38] [Neutrino Mass and Leptogenesis in the Non-SUSY Modular $A^\prime_5$ Inverse Seesaw](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19104)
*Xianshuo Zhang,Yakefu Reyimuaji*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [This paper presents a modular symmetry approach to neutrino mass generation that simultaneously addresses oscillation parameters, CP violation, and baryogenesis. By implementing the $A^{\prime}_5$ modular symmetry in a non-supersymmetric inverse seesaw framework, it yields testable predictions for neutrino ordering, CP phases, and $0νββ$ decay while achieving leptogenesis at TeV scales.]

\n\n
[本文提出了一种模对称性方法生成中微子质量，同时解决振荡参数、CP破坏和重子生成问题。通过$A^{\prime}_5$模对称性在非超对称逆跷跷板框架中的实现，该模型给出了中微子质量排序、CP相和$0νββ$衰变的可测试预测，并在TeV尺度上实现了轻子生成。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The Standard Model fails to explain neutrino masses, mixing patterns, and the matter-antimatter asymmetry of the universe. Existing seesaw mechanisms often operate at inaccessible energy scales, making direct experimental verification challenging. There is a need for a unified framework that explains neutrino oscillation data, predicts CP-violating phases, connects to neutrinoless double beta decay, and generates the observed baryon asymmetry through testable mechanisms at accessible energy scales.]

\n\n
[标准模型无法解释中微子质量、混合模式以及宇宙的物质-反物质不对称性。现有的跷跷板机制通常在不可及的能量尺度上运行，使得直接实验验证具有挑战性。需要一个统一框架来解释中微子振荡数据、预测CP破坏相位、连接无中微子双β衰变，并通过在可及能量尺度上的可测试机制产生观测到的重子不对称性。]

Method: [The authors construct a non-supersymmetric inverse seesaw model based on the $A^{\prime}_5$ modular symmetry. This approach utilizes modular forms as Yukawa couplings, whose transformation properties under the modular group determine the flavor structure. The inverse seesaw mechanism introduces TeV-scale sterile neutrinos with small lepton number violating masses $μ$, generating light neutrino masses via $m_ν ∼ m_D^2/(M_R^2/μ)$. Three specific realisations are developed with different assignments of modular weights and representations for the lepton fields. The modular symmetry constrains the neutrino mass matrix structure, while leptogenesis is achieved through CP-violating decays of the TeV-scale sterile neutrinos.]

\n\n
[作者构建了一个基于$A^{\prime}_5$模对称性的非超对称逆跷跷板模型。该方法利用模形式作为Yukawa耦合，其在模群下的变换性质决定了味结构。逆跷跷板机制引入了具有小轻子数破坏质量$μ$的TeV尺度惰性中微子，通过$m_ν ∼ m_D^2/(M_R^2/μ)$产生轻中微子质量。开发了三种具体实现，具有不同的轻子场模权荷和表示分配。模对称性约束了中微子质量矩阵结构，而轻子生成通过TeV尺度惰性中微子的CP破坏衰变实现。]

Result: [The model successfully reproduces all measured neutrino oscillation parameters within current 3$σ$ ranges. It predicts normal mass ordering, specific ranges for the Dirac CP phase $δ_{CP}$ and Majorana phases $α_{21}$, $α_{31}$, and testable values for the effective Majorana mass $m_{ββ}$ in neutrinoless double beta decay. The three concrete realisations show distinct but consistent patterns in these predictions. Crucially, the model achieves successful TeV-scale thermal leptogenesis, generating the observed baryon asymmetry $Y_B ∼ 8.7×10^{-11}$ through CP-violating sterile neutrino decays. This renders the scenario simultaneously testable in neutrino oscillation experiments, $0νββ$ searches, and collider experiments probing TeV-scale sterile neutrinos.]

\n\n
[该模型成功在当前3$σ$范围内重现所有测量的中微子振荡参数。它预测了正常质量排序、Dirac CP相位$δ_{CP}$和Majorana相位$α_{21}$, $α_{31}$的具体范围，以及无中微子双β衰变中有效Majorana质量$m_{ββ}$的可测试值。三种具体实现显示了这些预测中不同但一致的模式。关键的是，该模型实现了成功的TeV尺度热轻子生成，通过CP破坏的惰性中微子衰变产生观测到的重子不对称性$Y_B ∼ 8.7×10^{-11}$。这使得该情景可同时在振荡实验、$0νββ$搜索和探测TeV尺度惰性中微子的对撞机实验中测试。]

Conclusion: [The $A^{\prime}_5$ modular symmetry provides a powerful framework for constructing predictive neutrino mass models that simultaneously address oscillation data, CP violation, and cosmological baryogenesis. The inverse seesaw implementation allows for testable TeV-scale physics, connecting low-energy neutrino phenomena with high-energy collider signatures. This work demonstrates how modular symmetry approaches can yield concrete, falsifiable predictions across multiple experimental frontiers, offering a path toward comprehensive verification of neutrino mass generation mechanisms.]

\n\n
[$A^{\prime}_5$模对称性为构建预测性中微子质量模型提供了强大框架，该框架同时解决振荡数据、CP破坏和宇宙学重子生成问题。逆跷跷板实现允许可测试的TeV尺度物理，将低能中微子现象与高能对撞机信号连接起来。这项工作展示了模对称性方法如何在多个实验前沿产生具体、可证伪的预测，为全面验证中微子质量生成机制提供了途径。]

Abstract: A non-supersymmetric inverse seesaw model of neutrino mass based on the $A^{\prime}_5$ modular symmetry is presented. This framework provides a combined explanation for neutrino masses, mixing, and the cosmic baryon asymmetry through leptogenesis. Three concrete realisations are constructed, and their phenomenological predictions are analysed. The results are not only compatible with the measured neutrino oscillation parameters within the current experimental 3$σ$ ranges, but also provide predictions for the neutrino mass ordering, Dirac and Majorana CP-violating phases, and the effective Majorana mass in neutrinoless double beta decay. The model further realises TeV-scale leptogenesis consistent with the observed baryon asymmetry, rendering the scenario testable in both low-energy neutrino experiments and high-energy collider searches.

### [39] [Searching for dark matter X-ray lines from the Large Magellanic Cloud with eROSITA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19109)
*Jorge Terol Calvo,Marco Taoso,Andrea Caputo,Michela Negro,Marco Regis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Search for X-ray monochromatic line signals from dark matter decay in the Large Magellanic Cloud using eROSITA-DE DR1 data. Analysis finds no evidence for sterile neutrino or axion-like particle decay signals, leading to new constraints on DM lifetime, mixing angles, and couplings in the 2-18 keV mass range.

\n\n
利用 eROSITA-DE DR1 数据对大型麦哲伦云中暗物质衰变产生的X射线单色谱线进行搜索。分析未发现 sterile neutrino 或类轴子粒子衰变信号的证据，从而在2-18 keV质量范围内对暗物质寿命、混合角及耦合常数给出新的约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dark matter particles such as sterile neutrinos and axion-like particles (ALPs) can decay via radiative channels, producing monochromatic X-ray lines. The Large Magellanic Cloud (LMC) offers a nearby, massive dark matter halo with relatively low astrophysical backgrounds. Detection of such lines would provide smoking-gun evidence for particle dark matter and constrain fundamental parameters like mixing angles and couplings.

\n\n
诸如 sterile neutrino 和类轴子粒子(ALPs)等暗物质粒子可以通过辐射衰变通道衰变，产生单色X射线谱线。大型麦哲伦云(LMC)提供了一个距离较近、质量较大的暗物质晕，且天体物理背景相对较低。探测此类谱线将为粒子暗物质提供确凿证据，并对混合角、耦合常数等基本参数给出约束。

Method: Analysis of eROSITA-DE DR1 X-ray data in the 1-9 keV energy range, targeting the Large Magellanic Cloud halo. Statistical approach uses unbinned likelihood analysis to search for monochromatic line signals superimposed on astrophysical continuum backgrounds. For sterile neutrinos, decay via $\nu_s \to \nu_a + \gamma$ is considered, with rate proportional to $\sin^2(2\theta)$. For ALPs, decay $a \to \gamma\gamma$ (with one photon potentially converted) yields line at $E = m_a/2$. Limits derived via frequentist or Bayesian statistical framework, accounting for instrumental response and background modeling.

\n\n
分析 eROSITA-DE DR1 在1-9 keV能量范围内的X射线数据，以大型麦哲伦云晕为目标。统计方法使用无分箱似然分析，在连续的天体物理背景上搜索叠加的单色谱线信号。对于 sterile neutrino，考虑 $\nu_s \to \nu_a + \gamma$ 衰变，其衰变率与 $\sin^2(2\theta)$ 成正比。对于 ALPs，衰变 $a \to \gamma\gamma$（其中一个光子可能发生转化）会在 $E = m_a/2$ 处产生谱线。通过频率主义或贝叶斯统计框架推导上限，同时考虑了仪器响应和背景模型。

Result: No statistically significant X-ray line signal detected in the 1-9 keV range from LMC dark matter halo. Derived lower limits on dark matter lifetime $\tau$ for both sterile neutrino and ALP scenarios. For sterile neutrinos, limits on active-sterile mixing angle $\sin^2(2\theta)$ exclude regions of parameter space for masses between 2-18 keV. For ALPs, limits on photon coupling $g_{a\gamma}$ constrain parameter space in same mass range. These constraints are particularly strong for masses below 5 keV, representing new stringent bounds in this low-mass region.

\n\n
在1-9 keV能量范围内，未从LMC暗物质晕中探测到统计显著的X射线谱线信号。推导出 sterile neutrino 和 ALP 两种情景下暗物质寿命 $\tau$ 的下限。对于 sterile neutrino，对活跃-sterile混合角 $\sin^2(2\theta)$ 的约束排除了2-18 keV质量范围内的部分参数空间。对于 ALPs，对光子耦合 $g_{a\gamma}$ 的约束限制了相同质量范围内的参数空间。这些约束在5 keV以下质量区域尤其严格，代表了该低质量区域新的严格限制。

Conclusion: The null detection provides stringent new constraints on radiative dark matter decay scenarios in the keV-mass range. Limits on sterile neutrino mixing angle $\sin^2(2\theta)$ and ALP-photon coupling $g_{a\gamma}$ represent some of the strongest bounds for masses below 5 keV, complementing existing constraints from galaxy clusters and Milky Way observations. The analysis demonstrates the power of eROSITA data for indirect dark matter searches and highlights the importance of nearby dark matter-dominated systems like the LMC for such studies.

\n\n
未探测到信号为 keV 质量范围内的辐射暗物质衰变情景提供了新的严格约束。对 sterile neutrino 混合角 $\sin^2(2\theta)$ 和 ALP-光子耦合 $g_{a\gamma}$ 的限制代表了5 keV以下质量区域一些最强的约束，补充了来自星系团和银河系观测的现有限制。该分析展示了 eROSITA 数据在间接暗物质搜索中的能力，并强调了像 LMC 这样的邻近暗物质主导系统对此类研究的重要性。

Abstract: We perform a search for an X-ray monochromatic line arising from dark matter (DM) decay in the halo of the Large Magellanic Cloud. An emission line can be expected from two well-motivated DM candidates: sterile neturinos and axion-like particles (ALPs). We analyze the eROSITA-DE DR1 datasets in the energy range between 1 and 9 keV. No evidence for a DM line is found, and we set lower limits on the DM lifetime. We then recast these bounds into upper limits on the active-sterile neutrino mixing angle $\sin^2(2θ)$ and on the ALP to photon coupling $g_{aγ}$, for DM masses between 2 and 18 keV. These results set new strong constraints for masses below 5 keV.

</details>


### [40] [Hidden-charm pentaquarks: Electromagnetic structure in a diquark--diquark--antiquark model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19151)
*U. Ozdem*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: [We systematically compute magnetic dipole moments of hidden-charm pentaquarks using QCD light-cone sum rules with four distinct interpolating currents, revealing strong dependence on internal quark configurations and spin alignments. Results show molecular-type predictions generally agree while compact configurations yield markedly different values, demonstrating electromagnetic observables' sensitivity to internal structure.]
\n\n
[我们使用具有四种不同插值流的QCD光锥求和规则，系统地计算了隐粲五夸克态的磁偶极矩，揭示了其对内部夸克构型和自旋取向的强依赖性。结果显示分子型预测基本一致，而紧致构型给出显著不同的数值，证明了电磁可观测量对内部结构的敏感性。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The internal structures of exotic hadronic states like hidden-charm pentaquarks remain uncertain, with competing models proposing different quark configurations (molecular vs. compact). Electromagnetic properties, particularly magnetic dipole moments, offer sensitive probes of internal structure since they depend on spatial distributions and spin alignments. The need for systematic study using first-principles QCD methods to discriminate between structural models motivates this work.]
\n\n
[隐粲五夸克态等奇特强子态的内部结构仍不确定，存在多种相互竞争的模型提出不同的夸克构型（分子型 vs. 紧致型）。电磁性质，特别是磁偶极矩，为内部结构提供了灵敏的探针，因为它们依赖于空间分布和自旋取向。需要使用第一性原理的QCD方法进行系统研究来区分不同结构模型，这构成了本工作的动机。]

Method: [Employ QCD light-cone sum rules with four distinct interpolating currents representing different quark configurations. The method accounts for contributions from both light ($u/d$) and charm ($c$) quark sectors, including higher-dimensional operators in operator product expansion (OPE). Careful analysis ensures convergence of OPE series and ground-state pole dominance. The electromagnetic current correlator $\Pi_{\mu\nu}(p,q)$ is computed between vacuum and pentaquark states using the interpolating currents, with magnetic moments extracted from coefficient of $i\varepsilon_{\mu\nu\alpha\beta}p^\alpha q^\beta$ term.]
\n\n
[采用具有四种不同插值流的QCD光锥求和规则，代表不同的夸克构型。该方法考虑了轻夸克($u/d$)和粲夸克($c$)扇区的贡献，包括算子乘积展开（OPE）中的高维算子。仔细的分析确保了OPE级数的收敛性和基态极点的主导性。电磁流关联函数$\Pi_{\mu\nu}(p,q)$使用插值流在真空和五夸克态之间计算，磁矩从$i\varepsilon_{\mu\nu\alpha\beta}p^\alpha q^\beta$项的系数中提取。]

Result: [Magnetic moments show strong dependence on internal quark configurations and spin alignments. Substantial variations occur among different interpolating currents despite identical quark content and quantum numbers. Molecular-type configurations yield predictions in general agreement with existing studies, while compact configurations produce markedly different values, including significant differences in sign and magnitude. The sensitivity arises from different spatial wavefunctions and spin correlations encoded in the interpolating currents.]
\n\n
[磁矩显示出对内部夸克构型和自旋取向的强依赖性。尽管夸克成分和量子数相同，不同插值流之间仍出现显著变化。分子型构型给出的预测与现有研究基本一致，而紧致构型产生明显不同的数值，包括符号和大小的显著差异。这种敏感性源于插值流中编码的不同空间波函数和自旋关联。]

Conclusion: [Electromagnetic observables, particularly magnetic dipole moments, are highly sensitive to the internal structure of exotic hadrons. The systematic QCD light-cone sum rule analysis demonstrates that molecular and compact configurations yield distinct magnetic moment predictions, enabling discrimination between competing structural models. This work establishes magnetic moments as valuable probes for spin-parity assignments and underlying quark dynamics in exotic states, providing a new theoretical tool for understanding their nature beyond conventional hadrons.]
\n\n
[电磁可观测量，特别是磁偶极矩，对奇特强子的内部结构高度敏感。系统的QCD光锥求和规则分析表明，分子型和紧致型构型给出不同的磁矩预测，从而能够区分相互竞争的结构模型。这项工作确立了磁矩作为奇特态中自旋宇称分配和底层夸克动力学的有价值探针，为理解超越传统强子的性质提供了新的理论工具。]

Abstract: We systematically investigate the electromagnetic properties of exotic states whose internal structures remain uncertain and for which different models have been proposed. In this work, we focus on the magnetic dipole moments of hidden-charm pentaquark states using QCD light-cone sum rules with four distinct interpolating currents. The analysis accounts for contributions from both light and charm quark sectors, as well as higher-dimensional operators, ensuring convergence of the operator product expansion and dominance of the ground-state pole. Our results demonstrate a strong dependence of the magnetic moments on the internal quark configurations and spin alignments, revealing substantial variations among the different currents despite identical quark content and quantum numbers. Comparisons with existing studies indicate that while molecular-type predictions show general agreement, compact configurations yield markedly different values, including significant differences in sign and magnitude. These findings therefore underscore the sensitivity of electromagnetic observables to the internal structure of exotic hadrons and highlight their potential as probes to discriminate between competing structural models for spin-parity assignments and underlying quark dynamics.

### [41] [A global analysis of Energy-Energy Correlation data: determination of $α_S$ and non-perturbative QCD parameters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19162)
*Ugo Giuseppe Aglietti,Giancarlo Ferrera,Lorenzo Rossi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper performs a global analysis of Energy-Energy Correlation data in $e^+e^-$ annihilation at center-of-mass energies from 7.7 to 91.2 GeV. The authors achieve N$^3$LL resummation in the back-to-back region with $\mathcal{O}(α_S^3)$ fixed-order matching, incorporate heavy-quark mass effects, and use dispersive approach for non-perturbative corrections. The simultaneous fit yields precise determination of $α_S(m_Z^2) = 0.119 \pm 0.002$ and non-perturbative parameters.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Energy-Energy Correlation (EEC) observables in $e^+e^-$ annihilation provide crucial precision tests of QCD and determinations of the strong coupling constant $α_S$. The motivation is to achieve the most precise determination of $α_S$ through comprehensive analysis across multiple experiments and center-of-mass energies by addressing: (1) complete resummation of large logarithmic contributions in the two-jet region, (2) inclusion of heavy-quark mass effects, (3) systematic treatment of non-perturbative power corrections, and (4) incorporation of previously unanalyzed datasets from ALEPH and AMY collaborations.

Method: The methodology employs state-of-the-art perturbative QCD techniques:
1. **Resummation**: Logarithmically-enhanced contributions in the back-to-back region are resummed to N$^3$LL accuracy using Soft-Collinear Effective Theory (SCET) formalism with anomalous dimensions up to three loops.
2. **Fixed-order matching**: The resummed results are consistently matched to $\mathcal{O}(α_S^3)$ fixed-order calculations using standard matching procedures to ensure accuracy across all angular regions.
3. **Heavy-quark treatment**: Dominant mass effects for heavy quarks ($b$ and $c$) are incorporated through appropriate modifications to splitting functions and phase space.
4. **Non-perturbative modeling**: Power corrections are modeled using an analytic dispersive approach that relates perturbative and non-perturbative contributions through analytic continuation properties.
5. **Statistical analysis**: Simultaneous global fit to experimental data from multiple experiments (ALEPH, AMY, etc.) across $\sqrt{s}=7.7-91.2$ GeV using maximum likelihood methods with correlated uncertainties.

Result: The analysis achieves:
1. **Excellent data description**: The theoretical predictions with fitted parameters provide excellent agreement with experimental data across all center-of-mass energies and angular regions, with $\chi^2$/d.o.f. indicating good statistical consistency.
2. **Precise strong coupling determination**: $α_S(m_Z^2) = 0.119 \pm 0.002$ (total uncertainty), representing one of the most precise determinations from $e^+e^-$ annihilation.
3. **Non-perturbative parameter extraction**: Determination of parameters characterizing the Collins--Soper evolution kernel and other non-perturbative contributions with quantified uncertainties.
4. **First global inclusion**: Successful incorporation of previously unused ALEPH and AMY datasets, which provide additional constraints and reduce systematic uncertainties.
5. **Consistency verification**: Cross-check of results with other determinations of $α_S$ and non-perturbative parameters from different observables and processes.

Conclusion: The paper demonstrates that comprehensive global analysis of Energy-Energy Correlation data with state-of-the-art theoretical techniques (N$^3$LL resummation, $\mathcal{O}(α_S^3)$ matching, and systematic non-perturbative modeling) enables a precise determination of the strong coupling constant and characterization of non-perturbative QCD effects. The obtained value $α_S(m_Z^2) = 0.119 \pm 0.002$ represents a significant contribution to the world average and validates the theoretical framework for precision QCD studies. The inclusion of previously unanalyzed datasets from ALEPH and AMY collaborations enhances the statistical power and reduces systematic uncertainties. The methodology establishes a benchmark for future precision measurements in $e^+e^-$ annihilation and related processes.

Abstract: We present a comprehensive global analysis of Energy-Energy Correlation (EEC) data in electron-positron annihilation into hadrons, spanning a wide range of center-of-mass energies ($7.7\,\,\text{GeV}\!\leq\!\sqrt{s}\!\leq\! 91.2\,\,\text{GeV})$. In the back-to-back (two-jet) region, we resum to all orders the logarithmically-enhanced contributions up to next-to-next-to-next-to-leading logarithmic (N$^3$LL) accuracy. The resummed results are consistently matched to fixed-order calculations up to $\mathcal{O}(α_S^3)$. Our resummation formalism also incorporates dominant heavy-quark mass effects and models non-perturbative power corrections by means of an analytic dispersive approach. A simultaneous fit yields an excellent description of experimental data across all energies, enabling a precise determination of the strong coupling, $α_S(m_Z^2) = 0.119 \pm 0.002$, as well as the non-perturbative parameters, including those characterizing the Collins--Soper evolution kernel. Our analysis includes, for the first time in a global fit, datasets from the ALEPH and AMY collaborations.

</details>

### [42] [More on near-horizon charges black holes with gravitational hair in three dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18072)
*Seyed Naseh Sajadi,Supakchai Ponglertsakul,Julio Oliva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper extends covariant phase-space formalism to higher-curvature gravity up to quartic Riemann terms, applies it to study near-horizon asymptotic symmetries in rotating BTZ and hairy black holes, and computes associated charges, extending previous work beyond quadratic curvature terms.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To systematically explore near-horizon charges in higher-curvature gravity for universal behaviors, particularly in string theory $\\alpha'$ corrections where first corrections appear at $\\alpha'^3 \\mathcal{R}^4$ order. Extend analysis to theories admitting hairy black holes with microscopically accounted entropy like New Massive Gravity.

Method: Develop comprehensive covariant phase-space formalism for gravitational theories with up to quartic Riemann terms in arbitrary dimensions. Apply to rotating BTZ spacetime and hairy black holes in New Massive Gravity. Compute near-horizon asymptotic symmetries and associated charges using extended Wald-Zoupas formalism.

Result: Successfully formulated covariant phase-space method for quartic curvature theories. Recovered first law of thermodynamics for rotating BTZ. Extended near-horizon symmetry analysis to $\\mathcal{R}^4$ terms in hairy black holes, finding consistent charge algebra and entropy relations. Explicit Lagrangian expressions provided in appendices.

Conclusion: The covariant phase-space framework extends robustly to quartic curvature theories, enabling systematic study of near-horizon symmetries and charges. Results validate thermodynamic consistency in BTZ and reveal universal structures in hairy black holes, advancing understanding of higher-derivative gravity's asymptotic structure.

Abstract: With the aim of continuing the exploration of near-horizon charges in higher-curvature gravity, searching for sectors leading to universal behaviors, we first provide a thorough revision and formulae of the covariant phase-space method applied to arbitrary gravitational theories containing up to quartic terms in the Riemann tensor in arbitrary dimension. These results can be applied in diverse setups, in particular in the context of $α'$ corrections to String Theory, where it is known that in Type II theories, the first correction to the Einstein-Hilbert Lagrangian goes as $α'^3 \mathcal{R}^4$. Then, we test these formulae for near horizon asymptotic symmetries of the rotating BTZ spacetime where the first law of black hole thermodynamics is consistently recovered. It was recently realized that a subset of these higher curvature gravities do admit black holes with gravitational hair, whose entropy can be microscopically accounted for, as is the case of New Massive Gravity. In this case, the four maximally symmetric vacua of the theory coincide, and the theory acquires an extra gauge symmetry when linearized around such a vacuum. We study the near-horizon asymptotic symmetries and compute the associated charges, both in the static and rotating hairy black holes, extending up to $\mathcal{R}^4$, a work that was previously done only up to a quadratic term. In order to allow for a continuous lecture on the work, we report the explicit expressions of the general Lagrangians in the appendices.

</details>


### [43] [On the concept of simultaneity in relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18100)
*Justo Pastor Lambare*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: A technical critique showing that Spavieri et al.'s claim that Wang et al.'s interferometric experiment disproves Special Relativity (SR) is based on circular reasoning, thus invalidating their conclusion that simultaneity must be absolute.

\n\n
技术性批判指出，Spavieri等人声称王等人的干涉实验证伪了狭义相对论(SR)是基于循环论证，因此他们关于同时性必须是绝对的结论是无效的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to defend the foundational principles of Special Relativity (SR) against a specific claimed experimental refutation. Spavieri et al. interpreted the results of an interferometric experiment by Wang et al. as evidence that simultaneity is absolute and independent of the observer's state of motion, which would directly contradict the relativity of simultaneity—a cornerstone of SR. This comment aims to show that the logical structure of Spavieri et al.'s argument is fundamentally flawed, thereby protecting the theoretical consistency of SR.

\n\n
动机是捍卫狭义相对论(SR)的基础原理免受一项特定的声称实验证伪的威胁。Spavieri等人将Wang等人的干涉实验结果解释为同时性是绝对的、且独立于观察者运动状态的证据，这将直接与狭义相对论的基石之一——同时性的相对性相矛盾。本文评论旨在揭示Spavieri等人论证的逻辑结构存在根本缺陷，从而维护狭义相对论的理论一致性。

Method: The method is a logical and conceptual analysis, not a new experimental or theoretical derivation. The authors deconstruct the argument put forth by Spavieri et al. They demonstrate that the reasoning used to conclude that the experiment refutes SR is circular. Specifically, the critique likely shows that Spavieri et al.'s interpretation of the experimental outcome implicitly assumes the very notion of absolute simultaneity (or some other non-relativistic assumption) that the experiment is purported to prove. Thus, the claim of disproof is not derived from the experimental data alone but from a logically fallacious, question-begging premise.

\n\n
方法是逻辑和概念分析，而非新的实验或理论推导。作者们解构了Spavieri等人提出的论证。他们证明，用于得出实验证伪SR的推理是循环的。具体而言，批判可能表明，Spavieri等人对实验结果的解释隐含地假定了该实验意图证明的绝对同时性概念（或某些其他非相对论性假设）。因此，证伪的声称并非仅仅从实验数据得出，而是源于一个逻辑上谬误的、乞题的假设。

Result: The primary result is the identification and exposition of a logical fallacy (circular reasoning) at the heart of Spavieri et al.'s claim. The comment successfully demonstrates that their conclusion—that Wang et al.'s experiment disproves SR and establishes absolute simultaneity—is not logically valid. By invalidating the logical argument, the comment neutralizes the purported threat to SR posed by that specific interpretation of the experimental data. No new experimental data or alternative theoretical framework is presented; the result is purely a defense of SR's logical coherence against a flawed critique.

\n\n
主要结果是识别并揭露了Spavieri等人声称的核心中存在逻辑谬误（循环论证）。该评论成功地证明，他们的结论——即Wang等人的实验证伪了SR并确立了绝对同时性——在逻辑上是无效的。通过使该逻辑论证无效化，该评论消除了由该特定实验数据解释对SR构成的所谓威胁。本文没有提出新的实验数据或替代理论框架；其结果纯粹是对SR逻辑一致性的辩护，以对抗一个有缺陷的批判。

Conclusion: The conclusion is that Spavieri et al.'s argument fails on logical grounds and therefore does not constitute a valid refutation of Special Relativity. The foundational status of the relativity of simultaneity within SR remains unchallenged by the analyzed interferometric experiment when interpreted correctly. The comment reinforces that extraordinary claims (like overthrowing a well-established theory) require extraordinary evidence and, crucially, logically sound arguments free from fallacies like circular reasoning.

\n\n
结论是，Spavieri等人的论证在逻辑基础上是失败的，因此不构成对狭义相对论的有效反驳。当被正确解释时，被分析的干涉实验并未挑战同时性的相对性在SR中的基础地位。该评论强调，非凡的声称（如推翻一个成熟的理论）需要非凡的证据，并且至关重要的是，需要没有循环论证等谬误的逻辑严密的论证。

Abstract: In this comment, we demonstrate that the claim by Spavieri et al., asserting that Wang et al.'s interferometric experiment disproves the special theory of relativity by revealing that simultaneity must be an absolute concept independent of the observer's state of motion, is based on circular reasoning and therefore constitutes a logical fallacy.

</details>

*Alcides Garat*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The historical development from SU(3) to SU(4) quark symmetries motivates extending to SU(N) gauge groups coupled to gravity, requiring mathematical foundations for grand field unification in curved spacetimes where quantum numbers translate to local gravitational field multiplets.

Method: Introduces novel tetrads with special properties analogous to SU(3)×SU(2)×U(1) case, proving theorems establishing isomorphisms between local SU(N) gauge groups and tensor products of local tetrad transformation groups, enabling gravitational coupling of arbitrary SU(N) symmetries.

Conclusion: Establishes theoretical foundation for grand field unification in 4D curved Lorentzian spacetimes through isomorphic relationships between SU(N) gauge groups and tetrad transformation groups, extending Standard Model symmetries to include gravity via geometric constructions.

Abstract: The discovery of the SU(3) symmetry was fundamental as to establishing an ordering principle in particle physics. We already studied how to couple the SU(3) symmetry to the gravitational field in four-dimensional curved Lorentzian spacetimes. The multiplets of equal quantum numbers are translated through natural elements in Riemannian geometry into local multiplets of equal gravitational field. As quark physics developed since the seventies, it was necessary to incorporate new symmetries to the models, that ensued in the incorporation of new quantum numbers like Charm, for example. Charm is an additive quantum number like isospin T3 and hypercharge Y and the standard T3-Y diagrams were extended onto another third axis. Then, instead of the fundamental triplet we have a quartet {u; d; s; c} as the smallest representation of the symmetry group, leading to the introduction of SU(4) as the new group of symmetries. In this paper we will not restrict ourselves exclusively to the symmetry group SU(4) and we will set out to analyze the coupling of the SU(N) symmetry to the gravitational field. To this end new tetrads will be introduced as we did for the SU(3) x SU(2) x U(1) case. These tetrads have outstanding properties that enable these constructions. New theorems will be proved regarding the isomorphic nature of these local symmetry gauge groups and tensor products of groups of local tetrad transformations. This is a paper about grand field uni?fication in four-dimensional curved Lorentzian spacetimes.

### [45] [The Steep Price of No Hair in Thiemann Regularized Loop Quantum Cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18175)
*Meysam Motaharfar,Parampreet Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Thiemann regularized loop quantum cosmology for Bianchi-I spacetimes yields an emergent Planckian de Sitter phase that isotropizes spacetime by damping anisotropic shear, but prevents classical evolution. The isotropization mechanism is non-generic despite its independence from initial conditions and matter content.

\n\n
基于Thiemann正则化的Bianchi-I时空圈量子宇宙学产生了涌现的普朗克尺度de Sitter相，通过阻尼各向异性剪切使时空各向同性化，但阻碍了经典演化。尽管该各向同性化机制独立于初始条件和物质内容，但它是非普适的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard loop quantum cosmology (LQC) resolves the big bang singularity via bounce but Thiemann's regularization leads to a qualitatively different outcome: emergence of a Planckian de Sitter phase in either pre- or post-bounce epoch. For anisotropic Bianchi-I spacetimes, recent results by Gan et al. [1] show quantum gravity effects generically damp anisotropic shear independent of initial conditions. This work aims to clarify the origin and limitations of this isotropization mechanism within Thiemann regularized LQC.

\n\n
标准圈量子宇宙学通过反弹解决大爆炸奇点，但Thiemann正则化导致了定性不同的结果：在反弹前或反弹后出现涌现的普朗克尺度de Sitter相。对于各向异性的Bianchi-I时空，Gan等人[1]的最新结果表明量子引力效应通常阻尼各向异性剪切，且独立于初始条件。本文旨在阐明Thiemann正则化圈量子宇宙学中各向同性化机制的起源和局限性。

Method: The analysis employs Thiemann regularized loop quantization of Bianchi-I spacetimes, extending the isotropic framework to anisotropic cosmology. The method involves studying the emergent Planckian de Sitter phase dynamics through quantum gravitational effects encoded in Thiemann's regularization scheme. The investigation focuses on the behavior of anisotropic shear during the bounce and the resulting isotropization mechanism, contrasting it with standard LQC predictions.

\n\n
该分析采用Thiemann正则化的Bianchi-I时空圈量子化方法，将各向同性框架扩展到各向异性宇宙学。该方法涉及通过Thiemann正则化方案中编码的量子引力效应研究涌现的普朗克尺度de Sitter相动力学。研究重点考察反弹期间各向异性剪切行为及其产生的各向同性化机制，并与标准圈量子宇宙学预测进行对比。

Result: 1. For Thiemann regularized Bianchi-I LQC, an emergent Planckian de Sitter phase appears that naturally damps anisotropic shear and removes cosmic hair, analogous to the isotropic case.
2. However, this isotropization comes at the cost of preventing the universe from becoming truly classical, even though a macroscopic post-bounce regime is achieved.
3. The isotropization mechanism is shown to be non-generic despite its independence from initial conditions and matter content.
4. The work clarifies that the damping of anisotropic shear observed by Gan et al. [1] originates from this emergent de Sitter phase but has significant limitations regarding classical evolution.

\n\n
1. 对于Thiemann正则化的Bianchi-I圈量子宇宙学，出现了涌现的普朗克尺度de Sitter相，自然地阻尼各向异性剪切并消除宇宙毛发，类似于各向同性情况。
2. 然而，这种各向同性化是以阻碍宇宙变得真正经典为代价的，尽管实现了宏观的反弹后状态。
3. 该各向同性化机制被证明是非普适的，尽管它独立于初始条件和物质内容。
4. 该工作阐明了Gan等人[1]观察到的各向异性剪切阻尼起源于这一涌现的de Sitter相，但在经典演化方面存在显著局限性。

Conclusion: Thiemann regularized LQC for anisotropic spacetimes yields a novel isotropization mechanism via emergent Planckian de Sitter phase, explaining recent results on shear damping. However, this mechanism prevents classical evolution, representing a fundamental limitation. The work demonstrates that isotropization in this framework is non-generic, providing crucial insights into the trade-offs between singularity resolution and classical recovery in quantum gravity theories.

\n\n
针对各向异性时空的Thiemann正则化圈量子宇宙学通过涌现的普朗克尺度de Sitter相产生了一种新颖的各向同性化机制，解释了最近关于剪切阻尼的结果。然而，该机制阻碍经典演化，代表了根本性的限制。该工作证明该框架中的各向同性化是非普适的，为理解量子引力理论中奇点解析与经典恢复之间的权衡提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Loop quantum cosmology based on Thiemann's regularization procedure leads to the resolution of the big bang singularity and bounce in the isotropic setting. A key distinction from standard loop quantum cosmology is that, in this framework, either the pre-bounce or post-bounce epoch is necessarily characterized by an emergent Planckian de Sitter phase. In this work we explore the Planckian physics of Thiemann regularized loop quantization of the Bianchi-I spacetimes. We show that as in the isotropic model, there exists an emergent de Sitter phase which naturally dampens anisotropic shear and removes cosmic hair. However, this isotropization comes at a steep price: although a macroscopic post-bounce regime is achieved, the universe never becomes truly classical. We further demonstrate that this isotropization mechanism is non-generic. These results help clarify and reinterpret recent results by Gan et al. [1] that, in anisotropic Thiemann regularized loop quantum cosmology, quantum gravity effects generically damp anisotropic shear in a way that is independent of initial conditions and the matter content, and that this anisotropic shear damping mechanism arises from a novel quantum gravity effect. Our work explains the origin of this mechanism and its limitations.

</details>


### [46] [Robinson-Trautman spacetimes in (2+1) dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18209)
*Alberto Saa*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Proposes a (2+1)-dimensional Robinson-Trautman evolution with cosmological constant and null fluid, introducing a fourth-order length-preserving flow equation whose stationary states are boosted BTZ black holes; numerical simulations show relaxation of generic initial data to these stationary configurations.

提出一个具有宇宙学常数和零质量流体的(2+1)维Robinson-Trautman演化，引入一个四阶长度保持流方程，其稳态解对应加速BTZ黑洞；数值模拟显示一般初始数据会弛豫到这些稳态构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Extend the Robinson-Trautman framework to lower dimensions while preserving key features of the four-dimensional case, creating a simplified toy model for dissipative dynamics driven by null radiation that captures structural similarities to genuine gravitational radiation phenomena in (3+1)D.

将Robinson-Trautman框架扩展到低维，同时保持四维情形的关键特征，创建一个简化的玩具模型来研究零质量辐射驱动的耗散动力学，捕捉与(3+1)维真正引力辐射现象的结构相似性。

Method: Consider exact family of metrics in (2+1)D with cosmological constant and null fluid source. The geometry is encoded by a single function $P(u,φ)$ on null hypersurfaces. Introduce a fourth-order length-preserving evolution equation for $P(u,φ)$ motivated by the area-preserving Calabi flow in 4D, where stationary configurations for negative cosmological constant correspond to boosted BTZ black holes. Analyze system through numerical integration of evolution equation.

考虑具有宇宙学常数和零质量流体源的(2+1)维精确度量族。几何由一个零超曲面上的单函数$P(u,φ)$编码。受四维中面积保持Calabi流的启发，引入$P(u,φ)$的四阶长度保持演化方程，其中负宇宙学常数下的稳态构型对应加速BTZ黑洞。通过演化方程的数值积分分析系统。

Result: Numerical solutions demonstrate relaxation of generic regular initial data $P(0,φ)$ toward stationary sector corresponding to boosted BTZ black holes for negative cosmological constant. The evolution equation drives the system toward these equilibrium configurations, providing evidence that the introduced flow captures dissipative behavior analogous to higher-dimensional gravitational radiation backreaction.

数值解证明对于负宇宙学常数，一般正则初始数据$P(0,φ)$会弛豫到对应加速BTZ黑洞的稳态区域。演化方程驱动系统趋向这些平衡构型，提供证据表明引入的流捕捉了类似于高维引力辐射反作用的耗散行为。

Conclusion: Successfully constructed a (2+1)-dimensional Robinson-Trautman model with null fluid source that mimics structural aspects of gravitational radiation dynamics. The fourth-order length-preserving flow equation provides a tractable framework for studying dissipative evolution, with BTZ black holes emerging as attractors of the dynamics. This offers insights into lower-dimensional analogues of radiation-driven gravitational collapse and relaxation processes.

成功构建了一个具有零质量流体源的(2+1)维Robinson-Trautman模型，模拟了引力辐射动力学的结构方面。四阶长度保持流方程为研究耗散演化提供了一个可处理的框架，其中BTZ黑洞作为动力学吸引子出现。这为辐射驱动的引力坍缩和弛豫过程的低维类比提供了见解。

Abstract: We propose a Robinson-Trautman evolution in $(2+1)$-dimensional spacetime that retains key structural features of the four-dimensional case. We consider a recently studied exact family of metrics to select a nonstationary geometry with a cosmological constant, sourced by a null fluid. The metric is completely determined by a single positive function $P(u,φ)$, while the corresponding matter content is encoded in a null-fluid density. Motivated by the role of the area-preserving Calabi flow in four dimensions, we introduce a fourth-order length-preserving evolution equation for $P(u,φ)$ whose stationary configurations correspond, for negative cosmological constant, to boosted BTZ black holes. Numerical solutions strongly support the relaxation of generic regular initial data $P(0,φ)$ toward the stationary sector. The resulting system provides a simple toy model for dissipative dynamics driven by null radiation in lower-dimensional gravity, with several structural similarities to phenomena associated with genuine gravitational radiation.
