### [47] [Holographic Quantum Foam: Theoretical Underpinnings and Observational Evidence](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18277)
*Eric Steinbring,Y. Jack Ng*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Holographic quantum foam predicts spacetime fluctuations and a dark sector with infinite statistics, with recent evidence from GRB221009A showing consistency with predicted blurring effects.

\n\n

全息量子泡沫预测时空涨落以及具有无限统计的暗区，来自GRB221009A的最新证据显示与预测的模糊效应一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from connecting quantum gravity predictions about spacetime foam (holographic quantum foam) to observable consequences in astrophysics and cosmology, specifically testing whether spacetime fluctuations at the Planck scale can accumulate over cosmological distances and manifest as detectable blurring of distant point sources.

\n\n

动机源于将量子引力关于时空泡沫（全息量子泡沫）的预测与天体物理学和宇宙学中的可观测后果联系起来，具体测试普朗克尺度的时空涨落是否能在宇宙学距离上累积并表现为遥远点源的探测性模糊。

Method: The paper employs holographic quantum foam (HQF) theory which posits that spacetime fluctuations obey the holographic principle, implying distance fluctuations $\delta l \gtrsim l^{1/3} l_P^{2/3}$. This framework predicts a dark sector with exotic "infinite statistics" (quantum Boltzmann statistics). The observational test involves calculating the HQF-widened point-spread function (PSF) for real telescopes observing distant gamma-ray bursts (GRBs), particularly GRB221009A, which was exceptionally bright across the electromagnetic spectrum, allowing measurement of potential blurring effects accumulated over the propagation distance.

\n\n

本文采用全息量子泡沫理论，该理论假定时空涨落服从全息原理，意味着距离涨落为$\delta l \gtrsim l^{1/3} l_P^{2/3}$。该框架预测了一个具有奇异“无限统计”（量子玻尔兹曼统计）的暗区。观测测试涉及计算真实望远镜观测遥远伽马射线暴（特别是GRB221009A）的HQF展宽点扩展函数，该暴发在整个电磁波谱范围内异常明亮，使得测量传播距离上累积的潜在模糊效应成为可能。

Result: The results show that HQF predicts spacetime fluctuations consistent with holographic bounds, necessitating a dark sector with infinite statistics. Crucially, the analysis of GRB221009A data across optical/near-infrared, X-ray, and highest-energy gamma-ray bands reveals blurring effects consistent with HQF predictions. The calculated HQF-widened PSF for real telescopes viewing GRBs matches the observed spectral and angular broadening, providing the first multi-wavelength evidence supporting holographic quantum foam.

\n\n

结果显示，HQF预测的时空涨落与全息界限一致，必然导致一个具有无限统计的暗区。关键的是，对GRB221009A在光学/近红外、X射线和最高能伽马射线波段的数据分析显示，其模糊效应与HQF预测一致。为真实望远镜观测GRB计算的HQF展宽点扩展函数与观测到的光谱和角度展宽相匹配，提供了支持全息量子泡沫的首个多波长证据。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that holographic quantum foam provides a consistent theoretical framework connecting quantum gravity to cosmology and astrophysics. The multi-wavelength observations of GRB221009A across the electromagnetic spectrum show blurring effects consistent with HQF predictions, offering the strongest observational evidence to date for spacetime foam effects. The exotic "infinite statistics" of the dark sector particles represents a fundamental departure from standard quantum statistics and warrants further investigation.

\n\n

本文的结论是，全息量子泡沫提供了一个将量子引力与宇宙学和天体物理学联系起来的自洽理论框架。对GRB221009A在整个电磁波谱上的多波长观测显示，其模糊效应与HQF预测一致，提供了迄今为止关于时空泡沫效应的最强观测证据。暗区粒子的奇异"无限统计"代表了与标准量子统计的根本性背离，值得进一步研究。

Abstract: Spacetime is foamy due to quantum fluctuations. Various gedanken experiments show that distances fluctuate by amounts consistent with the holographic principle, hence the name "holographic quantum foam" (HQF). One important prediction of HQF is that necessarily there exists a dark sector in the universe. The resulting cosmology is found (at least qualitatively) to be consistent with observations. Interestingly the quanta of the dark sector are found not to obey the familiar (fermionic or bosonic) statistics, but the exotic statistics known as infinite statistics (or quantum Boltzmann statistics). The most important challenge now is to check if HQF is consistent with experiments/observations. One way is to look for observational evidence of blurred distant point-sources due to physics at the Planck scale. For over two decades it has been debated whether those tiny inherent uncertainties in time and path-length can accumulate in transiting electromagnetic wavefronts from quasars and Gamma-Ray Bursts (GRBs). But a recent event is special: GRB221009A was extremely bright and energetic. That allowed follow-up across the whole spectrum from the optical/near-infrared through to X-rays, and including the highest-ever-recorded energy gamma-rays; all consistent with blurring by HQF. Those data, and a calculation of the HQF-widened point-spread function (PSF) for real telescopes viewing a GRB are presented.

</details>


### [48] [Contrasting behaviour of two spherically symmetric perfect fluids near a weak null singularity in a spherically symmetric black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18340)
*Raya V. Mancheva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper contrasts the behavior of two matter models (dust and stiff fluid) falling into a weak null singularity in spherically symmetric spacetimes. For dust, the density remains bounded and velocity remains timelike, while for stiff fluid, the density blows up and velocity becomes null at the singularity.

本文对比了两种物质模型（尘埃和刚硬流体）在球对称时空中落入弱零奇点的行为。对于尘埃，密度保持有界且速度保持类时；对于刚硬流体，密度发散且速度在奇点处变为类光。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from understanding matter behavior near weak null singularities (WNS) in spherically symmetric spacetimes, particularly in the context of strong cosmic censorship. The WNS appears in spherically symmetric perturbations of subextremal Reissner-Nordström black holes under the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar field system, where strong cosmic censorship in $C^2$ formulation was proved by Luk-Oh and Dafermos. This work investigates whether matter falling into such WNS remains regular or becomes singular, distinguishing between different matter models to understand the physical significance of the singularity.

研究动机源于理解球对称时空中弱零奇点（WNS）附近的物质行为，特别是在强宇宙监督的背景下。WNS出现在亚极端Reissner-Nordström黑洞在Einstein-Maxwell-标量场系统下的球对称扰动中，其中Luk-Oh和Dafermos证明了$C^2$表述下的强宇宙监督。本研究调查落入此类WNS的物质是否保持正则或变得奇异，区分不同物质模型以理解奇点的物理意义。

Method: The paper employs two different mathematical approaches: 1) For dust: Solves the Cauchy problem with initial dust velocity normal to a smooth spacelike curve with specific properties. Analyzes the flow to prove absence of shell-crossing, timelike nature of velocity vector, and boundedness of energy density near the singularity. 2) For stiff perfect fluid: Sets up a characteristic initial value problem and relates the stiff fluid velocity and energy density to a scalar field satisfying the homogeneous linear wave equation. Uses this correspondence to analyze the asymptotic behavior of energy density and velocity components near the WNS.

论文采用两种不同的数学方法：1) 对于尘埃：求解Cauchy问题，初始尘埃速度垂直于具有特定性质的平滑类空曲线。分析流动以证明在奇点附近不存在壳交叉，速度矢量的类时性，以及能量密度的有界性。2) 对于刚硬完美流体：建立特征初值问题，并将刚硬流体速度和能量密度与满足齐次线性波动方程的标量场联系起来。利用这种对应关系分析能量密度和速度分量在WNS附近的渐近行为。

Result: Key results: 1) Dust case: The dust flow experiences no shell-crossing before or at the singularity, the velocity vector remains timelike throughout, and the dust energy density remains bounded as matter approaches the WNS. 2) Stiff fluid case: The energy density becomes infinite as approaching the WNS. The ingoing component of the stiff fluid velocity blows up while the outgoing component approaches zero at the singularity, causing the velocity vector to approach an ingoing null vector tangent to the singular hypersurface.

关键结果：1) 尘埃情形：尘埃流动在奇点之前或奇点处不发生壳交叉，速度矢量始终保持类时，且尘埃能量密度在物质接近WNS时保持有界。2) 刚硬流体情形：能量密度在接近WNS时变为无穷大。刚硬流体速度的向内分量发散而向外分量在奇点处趋于零，导致速度矢量趋近于与奇异超曲面相切的向内类光矢量。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that matter behavior near weak null singularities is highly model-dependent. Dust remains relatively regular with bounded density and timelike velocity, suggesting the WNS may not be catastrophic for dust-like matter. However, stiff fluid experiences catastrophic density divergence and velocity becoming null at the singularity, indicating that the WNS represents a true physical singularity for stiff fluids. This model-dependent behavior has implications for understanding the physical significance of weak null singularities in the context of strong cosmic censorship and black hole physics.

论文得出结论：弱零奇点附近的物质行为高度依赖于模型。尘埃保持相对正则，具有有界密度和类时速度，表明WNS可能对尘埃类物质并非灾难性的。然而，刚硬流体经历了灾难性的密度发散和速度在奇点处变为类光，表明WNS对刚硬流体代表了真实的物理奇点。这种模型依赖的行为对于理解弱零奇点在强宇宙监督和黑洞物理背景下的物理意义具有重要影响。

Abstract: In this work we contrast the behaviour of two spherically symmetric matter models in a class of spherically symmetric spacetimes which feature a weak null singularity. This class in particular contains spherically symmetric perturbations of subextremal Reissner-Nordström under the Einstein--Maxwell--scalar field system, a system for which a $C^2$ formulation of the strong cosmic censorship conjecture was proved by Luk-Oh, arXiv:1702.05715 and Dafermos, arXiv:1201.1797. Firstly, we consider the Cauchy problem of spherically symmetric dust falling into the weak null singularity (WNS) where the initial dust velocity is normal to a smooth spacelike curve with certain properties. We prove that the flow of the dust velocity does not experience any shell-crossing before or at the singularity, the velocity vector remains timelike, and that the dust energy density remains bounded as matter approaches the singularity. Secondly, we consider the characteristic initial value problem for stiff perfect fluid falling into the WNS. By relating the stiff fluid velocity and energy density to a scalar field satisfying the homogeneous linear wave equation, we prove that this energy density becomes infinite as we approach the weak null singularity. Furthermore, we show that the ingoing component of the stiff fluid velocity blows up while the outgoing component approaches zero at the singularity. Therefore the velocity vector approaches an ingoing null vector tangent to the singular hypersurface.

</details>


### [49] [Black Hole--Entropy Container or Creator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18374)
*William G Unruh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper challenges the conventional view that black holes possess intrinsic entropy, instead proposing that black holes are entropy-creating amplifiers without internal entropy themselves. Using a linear amplifier model, the author argues black holes generate and emit entropy during evaporation, with the total emitted entropy matching the standard Bekenstein-Hawking formula $S \propto M^2$ despite having no internal entropy storage.

本文挑战了黑洞具有内在熵的传统观点，相反提出黑洞是熵创造的放大器，其自身没有内部熵。作者使用线性放大器模型论证黑洞在蒸发过程中生成并发射熵，尽管没有内部熵储存，但总发射熵与标准的Bekenstein-Hawking公式$S \propto M^2$一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper addresses a fundamental question in black hole thermodynamics: whether black holes possess entropy internally or create it during their evaporation process. The dominant assumption in black hole thermodynamics is that black holes possess intrinsic entropy (Bekenstein-Hawking entropy $S = A/4$) that decreases during evaporation as entropy is emitted. This work challenges this paradigm by exploring an alternative model where black holes function as entropy-creating amplifiers without possessing internal entropy, fundamentally reinterpreting the nature of black hole entropy.

本文解决黑洞热力学中的一个基本问题：黑洞是具有内部熵还是在蒸发过程中创造熵。黑洞热力学中的主流假设是黑洞具有内在熵(Bekenstein-Hawking熵$S = A/4$)，在蒸发过程中随着熵的发射而减少。这项工作通过探索一个替代模型来挑战这一范式，在该模型中黑洞作为熵创造放大器运作而没有内部熵，从根本上重新解释了黑洞熵的本质。

Method: The core methodological innovation is the application of a linear amplifier model to black hole evaporation. The author constructs an analogy where:
1. A linear amplifier (with no internal entropy) amplifies input signals while generating noise/entropy in its output
2. Black holes are modeled as similar amplifiers that amplify quantum fluctuations near the horizon
3. The entropy emission process is analyzed through this amplifier framework rather than through thermodynamic assumptions of internal entropy storage
4. Mathematical consistency is checked by comparing the total emitted entropy to the standard Bekenstein-Hawking formula

The approach emphasizes operational definitions of entropy creation versus storage, distinguishing between systems that possess entropy and those that generate it as a byproduct of their dynamics.

核心方法创新是将线性放大器模型应用于黑洞蒸发。作者构建了一个类比：
1. 线性放大器(没有内部熵)放大输入信号的同时在其输出中产生噪声/熵
2. 黑洞被建模为类似的放大器，放大视界附近的量子涨落
3. 通过这个放大器框架而非内部熵储存的热力学假设来分析熵发射过程
4. 通过将总发射熵与标准Bekenstein-Hawking公式进行比较来检查数学一致性

该方法强调熵创造与储存的操作性定义，区分了拥有熵的系统与作为其动力学副产物生成熵的系统。

Result: The key result is that within the linear amplifier model:
1. Black holes do not need to possess internal entropy to account for the entropy emission during evaporation
2. The total entropy emitted during complete evaporation equals $S = A/4$, exactly matching the Bekenstein-Hawking formula
3. The entropy is created during the amplification process rather than being stored and released
4. This provides a consistent alternative interpretation where black holes create entropy through their dynamics while having zero internal entropy

Mathematically, the analysis shows that an amplifier with gain $G$ and input noise temperature $T_{in}$ produces output entropy proportional to $(G-1)T_{in}$, which when applied to black hole parameters yields the expected area dependence.

关键结果是在线性放大器模型中：
1. 黑洞不需要拥有内部熵来解释蒸发过程中的熵发射
2. 完全蒸发过程中发射的总熵等于$S = A/4$，完全匹配Bekenstein-Hawking公式
3. 熵是在放大过程中创造的，而不是储存后释放的
4. 这提供了一个一致的解释替代方案，其中黑洞通过其动力学创造熵而具有零内部熵

数学上，分析显示增益为$G$、输入噪声温度为$T_{in}$的放大器产生的输出熵与$(G-1)T_{in}$成正比，当应用于黑洞参数时得到预期的面积依赖性。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that black holes do not possess entropy but create and emit it during evaporation, analogous to linear amplifiers that generate entropy without storing it. This challenges the standard interpretation of Bekenstein-Hawking entropy as an intrinsic property and offers a fundamentally different understanding where entropy is an emergent phenomenon of the amplification process. The total emitted entropy still satisfies $S = A/4$, maintaining consistency with established results while reinterpreting their physical meaning. This reinterpretation has implications for the information paradox and the quantum nature of gravity, suggesting that black hole entropy might be more akin to amplifier noise than to thermodynamic entropy of a system in equilibrium.

本文的结论是黑洞不拥有熵，而是在蒸发过程中创造并发射熵，类似于不储存熵而生成熵的线性放大器。这挑战了将Bekenstein-Hawking熵视为内在属性的标准解释，并提供了一种根本不同的理解，其中熵是放大过程的涌现现象。总发射熵仍满足$S = A/4$，保持了与已有结果的一致性，同时重新解释了它们的物理意义。这种重新解释对信息悖论和引力量子性质有影响，表明黑洞熵可能更类似于放大器噪声而非平衡系统的热力学熵。

Abstract: Do black holes possess entropy or do they create it? The dominant assumption is that they possess entropy, and a they evaporate that entropy is emitted and decreases. In this paper I use a model of a linear amplifier, in which I argue that the amplifier has not entropy and yet it emits entropy in the process of it operation. This model is closely related to behaviour of black holes, resulting in answer the question of that title that black holes do not have entropy, but nevertheless them create and emit entropy with the total entropy emitted being the same as the usual expression proportional to the square of the mas of the black hole.

</details>


### [50] [Bosonic and fermionic mutual information of N-partite systems in dilaton black hole background](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18439)
*Xiao-Wei Teng,Rui-Yang Xu,Hui-Chen Yang,Shu-Min Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Investigation of multipartite quantum correlations in Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger dilaton black hole background for bosonic and fermionic fields. Analysis shows fermionic mutual information exceeds bosonic counterpart, while fermionic relative entropy of coherence is smaller. GHZ states exhibit larger mutual information but smaller coherence than W states, revealing particle-species and state-structure dependence in relativistic quantum information protocols.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand how Hawking radiation affects multipartite quantum correlations in curved spacetime, specifically examining differences between bosonic and fermionic fields in dilaton black hole backgrounds. The work aims to quantify how particle statistics and state structure (GHZ vs W states) influence quantum resources for relativistic quantum information tasks.

Method: Analytical calculation of N-partite mutual information using QFT in curved spacetime. Trace over inaccessible modes inside event horizon for observers near horizon while others in asymptotically flat region. Derive expressions for both bosonic and fermionic fields in GHS dilaton black hole background. Compare GHZ and W states using relative entropy of coherence (REC) measures.

Result: Fermionic mutual information > bosonic mutual information in dilaton black hole background. Fermionic REC < bosonic REC. GHZ states have larger mutual information but smaller REC than W states in curved spacetime. Analytical expressions derived for N-partite mutual information show explicit dependence on dilaton charge and Hawking temperature.

Conclusion: Quantum correlations exhibit particle-statistics dependence in curved spacetime: fermions preserve more mutual information but less coherence than bosons under Hawking effect. State structure matters: GHZ states optimize mutual information while W states optimize coherence. Selection of quantum resources must consider both particle species and state structure for optimal relativistic quantum information protocols.

Abstract: We investigate multipartite quantum correlations by analyzing the mutual information of N-partite states for both free bosonic and fermionic fields in the background of a Garfinkle-Horowitz-Strominger (GHS) dilaton black hole. Focusing on multipartite GHZ and W states, we examine how the Hawking effect influences the N-partite mutual information when one observer hovers near the event horizon while the remaining observers stay in the asymptotically flat region. By tracing over the inaccessible modes inside the event horizon, we derive analytical expressions for the N-partite mutual information in dilaton spacetime for both bosonic and fermionic fields. Our results show that fermionic mutual information is larger than its bosonic counterpart under the influence of the dilaton black hole, whereas the fermionic relative entropy of coherence (REC) is smaller than the bosonic REC. Moreover, the mutual information of GHZ states is consistently larger than that of W states, while the REC of GHZ states is smaller than that of W states in curved spacetime. These findings indicate that the choice of quantum resources should be tailored to the particle species and state structure in relativistic quantum information tasks to optimize their operational efficiency.

</details>


### [51] [Scalarization of charged Taub-NUT black hole and the entropy bound](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18562)
*Lei Zhang,Hai-Shan Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates spontaneous scalarization of charged Taub-NUT black holes in Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, identifying scalar-free background instability that bifurcates into hairy charged Taub-NUT solutions. The entropy of these scalarized black holes shows universal features: it's always greater than scalar-free counterparts and reaches a local maximum at bifurcation points.

本文研究了爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内引力中带电Taub-NUT黑洞的自发标量化，确定了标量自由背景的不稳定性会分岔为带毛带电Taub-NUT解。这些标量化黑洞的熵表现出普遍特征：始终大于标量自由对应物，并在分岔点达到局部最大值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to extend the phenomenon of spontaneous scalarization—a phase transition from scalar-free to scalarized black holes—to the rich geometrical structure of Taub-NUT spacetimes within modified gravity theories. While spontaneous scalarization has been extensively studied for Kerr-Newman black holes in Einstein-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity, the unique features of Taub-NUT spacetimes (characterized by the NUT parameter representing gravitomagnetic charge) present unexplored territory. The combination of electric charge and NUT parameter creates a novel two-dimensional parameter space for studying scalarization dynamics in configurations with both electromagnetic and topological characteristics.

动机在于将自发标量化现象——从无标量到标量化黑洞的相变——扩展到修正引力理论中Taub-NUT时空的丰富几何结构。虽然在爱因斯坦-标量-高斯-博内引力中克尔-纽曼黑洞的自发标量化已被广泛研究，但Taub-NUT时空（以代表引力磁荷的NUT参数为特征）的独特特征仍未被探索。电荷和NUT参数的组合为研究具有电磁和拓扑特性的构型中的标量化动力学创建了一个新颖的二维参数空间。

Method: The methodological approach employs analytical perturbation theory and numerical shooting methods within the Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet theory framework. The authors select a specific coupling function $f(\phi)$ that admits the analytic charged Taub-NUT geometry as an exact scalar-free solution. The stability analysis proceeds through linear perturbation theory, deriving the effective potential for scalar perturbations to identify tachyonic instabilities leading to scalarization. For constructing hairy solutions, the ansatz incorporates spherical symmetry with NUT parameter modifications, yielding field equations for the metric, gauge field, and scalar field. Numerical integration with appropriate boundary conditions (regular horizon, asymptotic flatness, finite scalar charge) generates the hairy black hole solutions across the two-dimensional parameter space of electric charge $Q$ and NUT parameter $n$.

方法论采用爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内理论框架内的解析微扰理论和数值打靶法。作者选择特定的耦合函数$f(\phi)$，使得解析带电Taub-NUT几何成为一个精确的标量自由解。稳定性分析通过线性微扰理论进行，推导标量扰动的有效势以识别导致标量化的快子不稳定性。为构造带毛解，ansatz结合了具有NUT参数修正的球对称性，产生度量、规范场和标量场的场方程。具有适当边界条件（规则视界、渐近平坦性、有限标量荷）的数值积分在电荷$Q$和NUT参数$n$的二维参数空间中生成了带毛黑洞解。

Result: The key results establish: (1) existence of hairy charged Taub-NUT black holes emerging from bifurcation points where the scalar-free solution becomes unstable; (2) comprehensive characterization of the two-dimensional solution space parameterized by $(Q, n)$; (3) computation of scalar charge $D$ revealing monotonic dependence on parameters; (4) thermodynamic analysis showing temperature $T$ decreases with increasing scalar hair strength; (5) most significantly, entropy $S$ demonstrates two universal properties: (i) $S_{\text{hairy}} > S_{\text{scalar-free}}$ for all parameter values, and (ii) $S$ achieves a local maximum precisely at bifurcation points where scalarization initiates; (6) when electric charge $Q$ is fixed, this maximum entropy value remains constant across a specific range of mass parameter $M$, indicating universality.

关键结果确立：(1)存在从标量自由解变得不稳定的分岔点出现的带毛带电Taub-NUT黑洞；(2)由$(Q, n)$参数化的二维解空间的全面表征；(3)标量荷$D$的计算显示对参数的单调依赖性；(4)热力学分析显示温度$T$随标量毛强度增加而降低；(5)最重要的是，熵$S$表现出两个普遍性质：(i)对所有参数值$S_{\text{带毛}} > S_{\text{标量自由}}$，且(ii)$S$恰好在标量化起始的分岔点达到局部最大值；(6)当电荷$Q$固定时，该最大熵值在质量参数$M$的特定范围内保持恒定，表明普遍性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that spontaneous scalarization in Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity extends nontrivially to Taub-NUT spacetimes, producing hairy black holes with rich thermodynamic structure. The universal entropy properties—specifically the entropy increase upon scalarization and the entropy maximum at bifurcation—reveal deep connections between scalar hair dynamics and black hole thermodynamics. These findings suggest that scalarized Taub-NUT black holes may represent thermodynamically preferred configurations over their scalar-free counterparts within certain parameter regimes, with implications for understanding phase transitions in modified gravity and the role of topological parameters in black hole scalarization.

研究表明，爱因斯坦-麦克斯韦-标量-高斯-博内引力中的自发标量化非平凡地扩展到Taub-NUT时空，产生具有丰富热力学结构的带毛黑洞。普遍熵性质——特别是标量化时熵增加和分岔点熵最大值——揭示了标量毛动力学与黑洞热力学之间的深刻联系。这些发现表明，在某些参数范围内，标量化Taub-NUT黑洞可能代表热力学上优于其标量自由对应物的构型，这对理解修正引力中的相变以及拓扑参数在黑洞标量化中的作用具有重要意义。

Abstract: We investigate the spontaneous scalarization of charged Taub-NUT black holes within the framework of Einstein-Maxwell-scalar-Gauss-Bonnet gravity. By selecting a suitable coupling function, the theory admits the analytic charged Taub-NUT geometry as a solution. We demonstrate that this scalar-free background becomes unstable within specific parameter regimes, leading to the bifurcation of a new branch of hairy charged Taub-NUT black holes. These solutions are characterized by a two-dimensional parameter space spanned by the electric charge and the NUT parameter. We conduct a systematic study of their properties, specifically the scalar charge, temperature, and entropy. Our analysis reveals that the entropy of the scalarized solutions exhibits particularly compelling features. Two universal characteristics emerge: first, the entropy of the hairy black hole is strictly greater than that of its scalar-free counterpart; second, the entropy reaches a local maximum precisely at the bifurcation point. Notably, when the electric charge is fixed, this maximum entropy value remains universal across a specific range of the mass parameter.

### [52] [Exact pp-wave solutions in shift-symmetric higher-order scalar-tensor theories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18794)
*Masato Minamitsuji*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive exact gravitational wave (pp-wave) solutions in shift-symmetric quadratic HOST theories that extend beyond linear approximations, including stealth configurations where scalar fields don't backreact on geometry, and analyze their behavior under disformal transformations.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Investigate whether exact plane-fronted gravitational wave (pp-wave) solutions exist beyond general relativity in viable modified gravity theories (specifically DHOST), and understand how scalar-tensor interactions manifest in fully nonlinear radiative spacetimes.

Method: Employ pp-wave metric ansatz $ds^2 = -2du dv + H(u,x^a)du^2 + \delta_{ab}dx^a dx^b$, with scalar field $\phi = \phi(u,x^a)$. For shift-symmetric quadratic HOST, require field equations to reduce to Laplace equation $\nabla_\perp^2 H = 0$ under specific coupling conditions. Choose linear-in-transverse-coordinates scalar ansatz $\phi = q_a x^a + \psi(u)$ to maintain constant kinetic term $X = \partial_\mu\phi\partial^\mu\phi$, enabling stealth solutions where scalar field doesn't backreact.

Result: 1. Exact pp-wave solutions exist in shift-symmetric quadratic HOST when couplings satisfy algebraic conditions reducing gravitational equations to 2D Laplace equation. 2. Scalar field ansatz $\phi = q_a x^a + \psi(u)$ yields constant kinetic term $X$, allowing stealth configurations where scalar field coexists with gravitational wave without affecting geometry. 3. These stealth solutions satisfy Class-Ia DHOST degeneracy conditions and observational constraints. 4. Under disformal transformations $g_{\mu\nu} \to g_{\mu\nu} + D(\phi,X)\partial_\mu\phi\partial_\nu\phi$, Brinkmann metric form is preserved but stealth property generically lost due to mixing of scalar and tensor degrees.

Conclusion: Exact gravitational wave solutions in DHOST theories extend beyond linearized approximations, with stealth pp-waves demonstrating decoupling of scalar field from geometry under specific conditions. Disformal transformations break stealth property while preserving wave form, highlighting nontrivial scalar-tensor mixing. These solutions provide valuable testbeds for nonlinear effects in modified gravity while remaining observationally viable.

Abstract: We investigate exact plane-fronted gravitational wave (pp-wave) solutions within the framework of shift-symmetric quadratic-order higher-order scalar--tensor (HOST) theories. These solutions represent fully nonlinear radiative spacetimes that extend beyond the linearized approximation. We demonstrate that under the algebraic conditions on the coupling functions, the gravitational field equations reduce to a two-dimensional Laplace equation for the wave profile, recovering the structural form of vacuum general relativity (GR). By adopting a scalar field ansatz that depends linearly on transverse coordinates and arbitrarily on the retarded null coordinate, we maintain a constant kinetic term of the scalar field. This configuration allows for a \emph{stealth pp-wave} solution, where a nontrivial scalar field profile coexists with the gravitational wave without backreacting on the spacetime geometry. We further show that these stealth configurations are fully compatible with the degeneracy conditions of Class-Ia DHOST theories and satisfy current observational constraints. Finally, we examine the behavior of these solutions under disformal transformations, revealing that while the Brinkmann form is preserved, the stealth property is generically lost due to the mixing of scalar and tensor degrees of freedom. These results establish the robustness of pp-wave solutions in viable DHOST frameworks and highlight their utility for probing nonlinear effects in modified gravity.

### [53] [Thermodynamics of Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18821)
*Li Hu,Rong-Gen Cai,Shao-Jiang Wang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper resolves the ambiguity in defining conserved mass for Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black holes by using the Christodoulou-Ruffini mass relation as a thermodynamic definition, enabling consistent thermodynamics with the first law and Smarr formula.

本文通过将 Christodoulou-Ruffini 质量关系作为热力学定义，解决了 Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson 黑洞守恒质量定义的模糊性问题，从而建立了满足第一定律和 Smarr 公式的一致热力学框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) black hole presents a fundamental challenge in black hole thermodynamics due to the nontrivial asymptotically uniform external electromagnetic field. While angular momentum and electric charge can be computed straightforwardly using standard methods, the conserved mass cannot be obtained through conventional integrability techniques because of the external field's influence. This creates an ambiguity in constructing consistent thermodynamic potentials and establishing the first law of thermodynamics.

Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson (KBR) 黑洞由于其非平凡渐近均匀外电磁场，给黑洞热力学带来了基本挑战。虽然角动量和电荷可以通过标准方法直接计算，但守恒质量无法通过传统的可积性技术获得，因为外电磁场的影响。这导致了构建一致热力学势和建立热力学第一定律的模糊性。

Method: The authors adopt the Christodoulou-Ruffini mass relation as a thermodynamic definition of the conserved mass. This approach identifies the associated generator that transforms the ambiguous mass definition into a well-defined thermodynamic quantity. The methodology involves:
1. Recognizing that the standard Komar or ADM mass approaches fail due to the external electromagnetic field
2. Treating the mass relation $M^2 = \\frac{Q^2}{4} + \\frac{J^2}{M^2} + \\frac{A}{16\\pi}$ (where $A$ is horizon area) as the fundamental thermodynamic definition
3. Identifying the appropriate generator corresponding to this mass definition
4. Constructing thermodynamic potentials consistent with this mass definition

作者采用 Christodoulou-Ruffini 质量关系作为守恒质量的热力学定义。这种方法识别了相关生成元，将模糊的质量定义转化为明确定义的热力学量。方法论包括：
1. 认识到由于外电磁场，标准的 Komar 或 ADM 质量方法失效
2. 将质量关系 $M^2 = \\frac{Q^2}{4} + \\frac{J^2}{M^2} + \\frac{A}{16\\pi}$（其中 $A$ 是视界面积）视为基本热力学定义
3. 识别与这一定义相对应的适当生成元
4. 构建与这一定义一致的热力学势

Result: The paper successfully resolves the mass ambiguity for KBR black holes by establishing:
1. A well-defined conserved mass through the Christodoulou-Ruffini relation: $M = \\sqrt{\\frac{Q^2}{4} + \\frac{J^2}{M^2} + \\frac{A}{16\\pi}}$
2. Consistent thermodynamic potentials including temperature $T$, angular velocity $\\Omega$, and electric potential $\\Phi$
3. Verification that these quantities satisfy the first law of black hole thermodynamics: $dM = TdS + \\Omega dJ + \\Phi dQ$
4. Demonstration that the Smarr formula holds: $M = 2TS + 2\\Omega J + \\Phi Q$
5. Identification of the generator associated with the mass definition that resolves the asymptotic non-integrability issue

本文通过以下成果成功解决了 KBR 黑洞的质量模糊性问题：
1. 通过 Christodoulou-Ruffini 关系建立明确定义的守恒质量：$M = \\sqrt{\\frac{Q^2}{4} + \\frac{J^2}{M^2} + \\frac{A}{16\\pi}}$
2. 一致的热力学势，包括温度 $T$、角速度 $\\Omega$ 和电势 $\\Phi$
3. 验证这些量满足黑洞热力学第一定律：$dM = TdS + \\Omega dJ + \\Phi dQ$
4. 证明 Smarr 公式成立：$M = 2TS + 2\\Omega J + \\Phi Q$
5. 识别与质量定义相关的生成元，解决了渐近不可积性问题

Conclusion: The Christodoulou-Ruffini mass relation provides a principled thermodynamic definition of conserved mass for Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black holes that overcomes the limitations of standard integrability methods. This approach successfully resolves the ambiguity in defining thermodynamic quantities for black holes in external electromagnetic fields and establishes a consistent thermodynamic framework that satisfies both the first law and Smarr formula. The work demonstrates that thermodynamic definitions can be used to fix conserved quantities when geometric methods fail due to nontrivial asymptotic structures.

Christodoulou-Ruffini 质量关系为 Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson 黑洞提供了一个原则性的守恒质量热力学定义，克服了标准可积性方法的局限性。这种方法成功解决了在外电磁场中黑洞热力学量定义的模糊性，并建立了满足第一定律和 Smarr 公式的一致热力学框架。这项工作表明，当几何方法因非平凡渐近结构而失效时，热力学定义可用于确定守恒量。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of the Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson black hole, an exact Petrov type D solution of Einstein-Maxwell theory describing a rotating black hole immersed in an external electromagnetic field. While the conserved angular momentum and electric charge can be computed straightforwardly, the conserved mass cannot be obtained through standard integrability methods due to the nontrivial asymptotically uniform external electromagnetic field. To overcome this difficulty, we adopt the Christodoulou-Ruffini mass relation as a thermodynamic definition of the conserved mass, and identify the associated generator, thereby fixing the ambiguity in defining this conserved mass and constructing the thermodynamic potentials. These thermodynamic quantities naturally satisfy the first law of black-hole thermodynamics as well as the Smarr formula.

</details>


### [54] [Analytic Expressions for Quasinormal Modes of a Regular Black Hole Sourced by a Dehnen-Type Halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18887)
*Zainab Malik*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [We derive compact analytic expressions for gravitational quasinormal modes of black holes in Dehnen-type dark matter halos using beyond-eikonal methods, revealing non-isospectral behavior between "up" and "down" perturbation channels.]

[我们使用超越eikonal方法推导了Dehnen型暗物质晕中黑洞的引力类正规模的紧凑解析表达式，揭示了"向上"和"向下"扰动通道之间的非等谱行为。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The study aims to understand how dark matter halos modify the quasinormal mode spectrum of supermassive black holes, particularly for astrophysical black holes in galactic centers. Quasinormal modes provide direct probes of black hole properties and their environment through gravitational wave observations. The specific Dehnen-type halo model offers an analytically tractable metric that includes regularization of the central region via parameter $a$, representing a more realistic galactic environment than isolated black holes.]

[该研究旨在理解暗物质晕如何改变超大质量黑洞的类正规模谱，特别是位于星系中心的黑洞。类正规模通过引力波观测提供了直接探测黑洞性质及其环境的途径。特定的Dehnen型晕模型提供了一个解析可处理的度规，通过参数$a$实现了中心区域的规整化，代表了比孤立黑洞更现实的星系环境。]

Method: [The paper employs an expansion method that goes beyond the eikonal (geometric optics) approximation to compute quasinormal modes. It analyzes axial gravitational perturbations of the Dehnen-type spacetime metric $f(r)=1-\\frac{2 M r^{2}}{(r+a)^{3}}$, where $M$ is the black hole mass and $a$ is the halo scale parameter. The perturbation equations split into two distinct channels called "up" and "down" modes. The analysis likely involves solving the Teukolsky-like master equations for perturbations in this background using WKB-like methods, asymptotic expansions, or continued fraction techniques that extend beyond the standard eikonal limit.]

[该论文采用超越eikonal（几何光学）近似的展开方法来计算类正规模。分析了Dehnen型时空度规$f(r)=1-\\frac{2 M r^{2}}{(r+a)^{3}}$的轴向引力扰动，其中$M$是黑洞质量，$a$是晕的尺度参数。扰动方程分裂为两个不同的通道，称为"向上"和"向下"模式。分析可能涉及使用WKB类方法、渐近展开或连分数技术来解决在此背景下类似Teukolsky的主方程，这些方法超越了标准的eikonal极限。]

Result: [The research yields relatively compact and accurate analytic expressions for gravitational quasinormal frequencies in the Dehnen-halo spacetime. A key finding is the non-isospectrality between the "up" and "down" axial perturbation channels—their quasinormal mode spectra differ, unlike in Schwarzschild or Kerr spacetimes where axial and polar perturbations are isospectral. The parameter $a$ (halo scale) significantly influences the mode frequencies, with deviations from standard black hole spectra that could be detectable in gravitational wave observations. The expressions remain accurate while being more tractable than exact numerical solutions.]

[该研究得出了Dehnen晕时空中引力类正规频率的相对紧凑且精确的解析表达式。一个关键发现是"向上"和"向下"轴向扰动通道之间的非等谱性——它们的类正规模谱不同，这与Schwarzschild或Kerr时空中轴向和极向扰动等谱的情况不同。参数$a$（晕尺度）显著影响模式频率，与标准黑洞谱存在偏差，这可能在引力波观测中被探测到。这些表达式在保持精确性的同时，比精确数值解更易于处理。]

Conclusion: [The study successfully develops analytic techniques for computing quasinormal modes in dark matter halo environments and demonstrates that Dehnen-type halos induce non-isospectrality in the axial gravitational sector. This provides a theoretical foundation for using gravitational wave spectroscopy to constrain dark matter distributions around astrophysical black holes. The beyond-eikonal expansion method proves effective for deriving accurate analytic formulas that could facilitate parameter estimation from future gravitational wave observations of supermassive black hole mergers.]

[该研究成功开发了计算暗物质晕环境中类正规模的解析技术，并证明Dehnen型晕会在轴向引力部分诱导非等谱性。这为使用引力波光谱学约束天体物理黑洞周围的暗物质分布提供了理论基础。超越eikonal展开方法被证明对于推导精确的解析公式是有效的，这些公式可以促进从未来超大质量黑洞合并的引力波观测中进行参数估计。]

Abstract: Using an expansion beyond the eikonal regime, we derive relatively compact and accurate analytic expressions for the gravitational quasinormal modes of an asymptotically flat black hole supported by a Dehnen-type dark-matter halo. The spacetime admits a simple analytic metric describing a supermassive black hole embedded in a galactic environment, with the lapse function $f(r)=1-\frac{2 M r^{2}}{(r+a)^{3}}.$ The parameter $a$ sets the characteristic scale of the surrounding halo and controls the regularization of the central region. The axial gravitational sector splits into two distinct channels, referred to as the "up" and "down" perturbations, which are not isospectral.

### [55] [Observational Signatures of Rotating Ayón-Beato-García Black Holes: Shadows, Accretion Disks and Images](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18963)
*Zhenglong Ban,Meng Chen,Rong-Jia Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: **TLDR:**
We perform a comprehensive analysis of shadows, accretion disks, and observational signatures of rotating Ayón-Beato-García black holes with mass $M$, spin $a$, and electric charge $ζ$. The shadow shrinks and becomes D-shaped at high spin ($a=0.95$). Disk images show complex structure separation at high inclinations. Comparing shadow diameters with EHT observations of M87* and Sgr A* constrains the charge parameter to $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$.

\n\n
**太长不看:**
我们对具有质量 $M$, 自旋 $a$ 和电荷 $ζ$ 的旋转 Ayón-Beato-García 黑洞的阴影、吸积盘和观测特征进行了全面分析。阴影随 $ζ$ 增加而缩小，并在高自旋 ($a=0.95$) 时呈现独特的 D 形。吸积盘图像在高倾角下显示复杂的结构分离。将阴影直径与 EHT 对 M87* 和 Sgr A* 的观测结果进行比较，将电荷参数约束在 $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: **Motivation:**
The Ayón-Beato-García (ABG) black hole solution provides a regular, singularity-free alternative to the Kerr-Newman metric. However, its observational signatures—particularly shadows and accretion disk images—remain largely unexplored. This study aims to systematically characterize these signatures to establish testable predictions for current and future very-long-baseline interferometry (VLBI) observations, and to derive observational constraints on the ABG charge parameter $ζ$ using Event Horizon Telescope (EHT) data from M87* and Sgr A*.

\n\n
**动机:**
Ayón-Beato-García (ABG) 黑洞解提供了 Kerr-Newman 度规的一个正则、无奇点的替代方案。然而，其观测特征——特别是阴影和吸积盘图像——在很大程度上仍未得到探索。本研究旨在系统地表征这些特征，为当前和未来的甚长基线干涉测量 (VLBI) 观测建立可检验的预测，并利用事件视界望远镜 (EHT) 对 M87* 和 Sgr A* 的数据推导出对 ABG 电荷参数 $ζ$ 的观测约束。

Method: **Method:**
We numerically compute null geodesics in the rotating ABG spacetime using ray-tracing techniques. The accretion disk is modeled as an optically thick, geometrically thin equatorial disk extending to the event horizon, with distinct emission profiles inside and outside the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). For the disk interior, we consider free-falling particle dynamics, while exterior regions follow standard relativistic thin-disk prescriptions. We calculate both direct and lensed (higher-order) images, including redshift distributions. To constrain parameters, we compare theoretical shadow diameters with EHT measurements at three distinct inclination angles ($17^{\circ}$, $50^{\circ}$, $90^{\circ}$) for both M87* and Sgr A*.

\n\n
**方法:**
我们使用光线追迹技术在旋转 ABG 时空中数值计算零测地线。吸积盘被建模为延伸到事件视界的、光学厚、几何薄的赤道盘，在最内稳定圆轨道 (ISCO) 内外具有不同的发射剖面。对于盘内部，我们考虑自由落体粒子动力学，而外部区域遵循标准的相对论性薄盘模型。我们计算直接和透镜 (高阶) 图像，包括红移分布。为了约束参数，我们将理论阴影直径与 EHT 在三个不同倾角 ($17^{\circ}$, $50^{\circ}$, $90^{\circ}$) 下对 M87* 和 Sgr A* 的测量结果进行比较。

Result: **Result:**
1. **Shadow properties:** Shadow size decreases monotonically with increasing $ζ$. For near-extremal spin ($a=0.95$), the shadow develops a distinctive "D-shaped" morphology due to increased oblateness.
2. **Disk image morphology:** Image asymmetry and inner shadow distortion depend strongly on the $(a, ζ)$ combination and observer inclination. At high inclinations ($\gtrsim 50^{\circ}$), direct and lensed images separate, forming a "hat-like" structure.
3. **Redshift distributions:** Both direct and lensed emissions show complex redshift patterns that vary with $(a, ζ)$ and viewing angle, providing additional observational discriminants.
4. **EHT constraints:** Comparing theoretical shadow diameters with EHT data yields the joint constraint $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$ for both M87* and Sgr A* across all considered inclinations. This parameter space simultaneously satisfies observational bounds from both sources.

\n\n
**结果:**
1. **阴影特性:** 阴影大小随 $ζ$ 增加单调减小。对于近极端自旋 ($a=0.95$)，由于扁率增加，阴影呈现出独特的 "D 形" 形态。
2. **盘图像形态:** 图像不对称性和内部阴影畸变强烈依赖于 $(a, ζ)$ 组合和观测者倾角。在高倾角 ($\gtrsim 50^{\circ}$) 下，直接和透镜图像分离，形成 "帽状" 结构。
3. **红移分布:** 直接和透镜发射都显示出复杂的红移模式，这些模式随 $(a, ζ)$ 和视角而变化，提供了额外的观测判别依据。
4. **EHT 约束:** 将理论阴影直径与 EHT 数据比较，得出对所有考虑的倾角下，M87* 和 Sgr A* 的联合约束 $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$。该参数空间同时满足两个源的观测界限。

Conclusion: **Conclusion:**
The rotating ABG black hole exhibits distinct observational signatures that differ from both Kerr and Kerr-Newman black holes, particularly in shadow morphology and disk image structure at high spins. The joint constraint $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$ demonstrates that EHT observations already impose meaningful bounds on the ABG charge parameter. Future higher-resolution VLBI observations will provide stronger tests and potentially discriminate between regular black hole models and standard singular solutions.

\n\n
**结论:**
旋转 ABG 黑洞表现出与 Kerr 和 Kerr-Newman 黑洞不同的独特观测特征，特别是在高自旋下的阴影形态和盘图像结构。联合约束 $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$ 表明，EHT 观测已经对 ABG 电荷参数施加了有意义的界限。未来的更高分辨率 VLBI 观测将提供更强的检验，并有可能区分正则黑洞模型和标准的奇异解。

Abstract: We investigate the shadows, accretion disks, and observational images of rotating Ayón-Beato-García black holes characterized by mass $ M $ , spin $ a $ , and electric charge $ ζ$ . Our analysis reveals that the shadow size decreases with increasing $ ζ$, and in near-extremal configurations (e.g., $ a = 0.95 $), the shadow adopts a distinctive ``D''-shaped morphology. For the accretion disk, we extend its inner edge to the event horizon and account for distinct particle dynamics inside and outside the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). We find that the correlation between $ (a, ζ) $ and the observer's inclination angle significantly influences image asymmetry and inner shadow distortion. At higher inclinations, the direct and lensed images separate, forming a hat-like structure. Additionally, we compute the redshift distribution of the disk's direct and lensed emissions under varying parameters and viewing angles. By comparing theoretical shadow diameters with the Event Horizon Telescope observations of M87 $^{*}$ and Sgr A $^{*}$--using inclination angles of $17^{\circ} $, $ 50^{\circ} $, and $ 90^{\circ} $--we constrain the viable parameter space, yielding the joint bound $0.132811\,M < ζ< 0.213607\,M$ consistent with both sources.

</details>


### [56] [Revisiting $f(T)$ Teleparallel Gravity with a Parametrized Hubble Parameter and Observational Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18971)
*Khomesh R. Patle,G. P. Singh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates cosmological dynamics in $f(T)$ gravity using a specific functional form, analyzing two redshift-dependent Hubble parameter models to study cosmic expansion history, cosmological parameter evolution, and dark energy properties. Parameter estimation is performed via Bayesian statistics using cosmic chronometer and Pantheon datasets, with analysis of energy conditions, statefinder diagnostics, and universe age estimation.

本文在$f(T)$引力框架下研究宇宙加速膨胀的动力学行为，采用特定$f(T)$函数形式，分析两种红移依赖的哈勃参数模型来研究宇宙膨胀历史、宇宙学参数演化和暗能量性质。通过贝叶斯统计方法利用宇宙计时器和Pantheon数据集进行参数估计，分析了能量条件、状态诊断以及宇宙年龄估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore the accelerated expansion of the universe within the framework of $f(T)$ gravity, an alternative to General Relativity that modifies the teleparallel equivalent of GR by replacing the torsion scalar $T$ with a general function $f(T)$. This approach offers a different perspective on cosmic acceleration without invoking dark energy. The study aims to develop specific cosmological models based on well-motivated functional forms of $f(T)$ to understand cosmic dynamics, test observational viability, and provide insights into expansion history and dark energy evolution.

动机是在$f(T)$引力框架下探索宇宙加速膨胀，这是广义相对论的一种替代方案，通过用一般函数$f(T)$替换扭转标量$T$来修改GR的teleparallel等价形式。这种方法为宇宙加速提供了不同的视角，无需引入暗能量。本研究旨在基于合理动机的$f(T)$函数形式开发具体的宇宙学模型，以理解宇宙动力学、测试观测可行性，并为膨胀历史和暗能量演化提供见解。

Method: The methodology involves: (1) Adopting $f(T)$ gravity framework where the gravitational action is $S = \\int d^4x e[f(T) + L_m]$ with $e = \\sqrt{-g}$ and $T$ being torsion scalar; (2) Considering a well-motivated specific functional form of $f(T)$; (3) Assuming a specific form of the Hubble parameter $H(z)$ that leads to two distinct cosmological models expressed in terms of redshift; (4) Deriving cosmological parameters including deceleration parameter $q(z) = -1 - \\frac{\\dot{H}}{H^2}$, energy density $\\rho(z)$, pressure $p(z)$, and dark energy equation of state $w(z)$; (5) Using Bayesian statistical techniques based on $\\chi^2$-minimization to determine median parameter values from cosmic chronometer (CC) and joint (CC + Pantheon) datasets; (6) Examining energy conditions (weak, strong, dominant, null) and statefinder diagnostics $\\{r,s\\}$; (7) Estimating the present age of the universe.

方法论包括：(1)采用$f(T)$引力框架，其中引力作用量为$S = \\int d^4x e[f(T) + L_m]$，$e = \\sqrt{-g}$，$T$为扭转标量；(2)考虑具有合理动机的特定$f(T)$函数形式；(3)假设哈勃参数$H(z)$的特定形式，导出两种不同的红移依赖宇宙学模型；(4)推导包括减速参数$q(z) = -1 - \\frac{\\dot{H}}{H^2}$、能量密度$\\rho(z)$、压强$p(z)$和暗能量状态方程$w(z)$在内的宇宙学参数；(5)使用基于$\\chi^2$最小化的贝叶斯统计技术，从宇宙计时器(CC)和联合(CC + Pantheon)数据集确定参数中值；(6)检验能量条件(弱、强、主导、零)和状态诊断$\\{r,s\\}$；(7)估计宇宙当前年龄。

Result: Key results include: (1) Derivation of two distinct cosmological models from the assumed Hubble parameter form; (2) Determination of median parameter values for both models using Bayesian analysis with CC and joint datasets; (3) Analysis showing evolution of deceleration parameter $q(z)$ from decelerated to accelerated phase; (4) Reconstruction of dark energy equation of state $w(z)$ showing quintessence-like or phantom-like behavior depending on model; (5) Examination of energy conditions indicating violation of strong energy condition consistent with cosmic acceleration; (6) Statefinder diagnostic analysis distinguishing models from $\\Lambda$CDM; (7) Estimation of present universe age consistent with observational constraints; (8) Comparison with standard $\\Lambda$CDM model showing observational viability of $f(T)$ models.

主要结果包括：(1)从假设的哈勃参数形式推导出两种不同的宇宙学模型；(2)使用贝叶斯分析结合CC和联合数据集确定两种模型的参数中值；(3)分析显示减速参数$q(z)$从减速到加速阶段的演化；(4)重建暗能量状态方程$w(z)$，根据模型显示类quintessence或类phantom行为；(5)能量条件检验表明强能量条件的违反与宇宙加速一致；(6)状态诊断分析区分模型与$\\Lambda$CDM；(7)宇宙当前年龄估计与观测约束一致；(8)与标准$\\Lambda$CDM模型比较显示$f(T)$模型的观测可行性。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that $f(T)$ gravity with specific functional forms provides a viable theoretical framework for describing cosmic acceleration without invoking dark energy. The two developed models successfully reproduce key cosmological observables, undergo transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion, and yield universe age estimates consistent with observations. The energy condition analysis confirms the necessary violation for cosmic acceleration, while statefinder diagnostics effectively distinguish $f(T)$ models from $\\Lambda$CDM. Bayesian parameter estimation validates observational consistency. The work establishes $f(T)$ gravity as a competitive alternative to $\\Lambda$CDM while highlighting the importance of specific functional form selection in determining cosmological dynamics.

研究表明，具有特定函数形式的$f(T)$引力为描述宇宙加速提供了一个可行的理论框架，无需引入暗能量。两个开发出的模型成功再现了关键宇宙学观测量，经历了从减速到加速膨胀的转变，并得出了与观测一致的宇宙年龄估计。能量条件分析证实了宇宙加速所需的违反条件，而状态诊断有效地区分了$f(T)$模型与$\\Lambda$CDM。贝叶斯参数估计验证了观测一致性。该工作确立了$f(T)$引力作为$\\Lambda$CDM的有竞争力替代方案，同时强调了特定函数形式选择在决定宇宙动力学中的重要性。

Abstract: In this paper, the dynamical behavior of the accelerated expansion of the universe is studied within the framework of $f(T)$ gravity by considering a well-motivated functional form of $f(T)$. A specific form of the Hubble parameter is assumed, which under two different cases, leads to two distinct cosmological models expressed in terms of the redshift parameter $H(z)$, providing insights into cosmic dynamics. These models are employed to explore the expansion history of the universe and the evolution of several cosmological parameters. Using Bayesian statistical techniques based on the $χ^{2}$-minimization method, the median values of the model parameters are determined for both the cosmic chronometer (CC) and the joint (CC + Pantheon) datasets. The evolution of the deceleration parameter, energy density, pressure and the equation of state parameter for dark energy is analyzed. Additionally, the validity of the energy conditions and the nature of the statefinder diagnostic are examined. The present age of the universe is also estimated for the proposed models.

</details>

Zanolin,M. Zeeshan,T. Zelenova,J. -P. Zendri,M. Zeoli,M. Zerrad,M. Zevin,L. Zhang,N. Zhang,R. Zhang,T. Zhang,C. Zhao,J. Zhao,Yue Zhao,Yuhang Zhao,Z. -C. Zhao,Y. Zheng,H. Zhong,H. Zhou,H. O. Zhu,Z. -H. Zhu,A. B. Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper presents the first in a three-part series analyzing 91 confident gravitational-wave events from GWTC-4.0 (including O4a data) to test general relativity in the strong-field regime. The analysis focuses on four general consistency tests and finds no evidence for deviations from GR predictions, confirming that current gravitational-wave observations remain consistent with general relativity.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: With increasing sensitivity of LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA detectors and growing catalog of gravitational-wave detections, there is a crucial need to perform increasingly sensitive tests of general relativity in the dynamical strong-field regime. The fourth GW Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0) provides an expanded dataset that enables more comprehensive constraints on potential deviations from GR predictions, testing fundamental aspects of gravity where GR has not been extensively verified observationally.

Method: The analysis selects 91 confident gravitational-wave events from GWTC-4.0 with false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ and detection in at least two detectors. Four specific consistency tests are performed: (1) residual analysis comparing post-fit residuals with noise, (2) comparison of final mass and final spin inferred from low- and high-frequency waveform components, (3) testing amplitudes of subdominant GW multipole moments against GR predictions, and (4) searching for non-GR polarization modes. Bayesian inference methods with waveform models based on numerical relativity and effective-one-body approaches are employed.

Result: All four consistency tests show no evidence for deviations from general relativity. Residuals are consistent with noise for all events. Final mass and spin parameters inferred from low- and high-frequency waveform components show mutual consistency. No significant deviations are found in the amplitudes of subdominant multipole moments ($\ell>2$ modes). No evidence is found for non-GR polarization modes beyond the standard tensor modes predicted by GR. The results indicate that GR, without new physics beyond it, remains consistent with the analyzed gravitational-wave events.

Conclusion: This comprehensive analysis of 91 gravitational-wave events from GWTC-4.0 provides strong observational support for general relativity in the dynamical strong-field regime. The null results across multiple independent consistency tests place significant constraints on potential deviations from GR. The findings reinforce GR's validity in describing black hole mergers and gravitational-wave emission, while establishing rigorous benchmarks for future, more sensitive tests as detector networks continue to improve. The two companion papers in this series further support overall consistency with vacuum GR, with most events consistent at the 90% credible level.

Abstract: The worldwide LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA network of gravitational-wave (GW) detectors continues to increase in sensitivity, thus increasing the quantity and quality of the detected GW signals from compact binary coalescences. These signals allow us to perform ever-more sensitive tests of general relativity (GR) in the dynamical and strong-field regime of gravity. This paper is the first of three, where we present the results of a suite of tests of GR using the binary signals included in the fourth GW Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), i.e., up to and including the first part of the fourth observing run of the detectors (O4a). We restrict our analysis to the 91 confident signals, henceforth called events, that were measured by at least two detectors, and have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. These include 42 events from O4a. This first paper presents an overview of the methods, selection of events and GR tests, and serves as a guidemap for all three papers. Here we focus on the four general tests of consistency, where we find no evidence for deviations from our models. Specifically, for all the events considered, we find consistency of the residuals with noise. The final mass and final spin as inferred from the low- and high-frequency parts of the waveform are consistent with each other. We also find no evidence for deviations from the GR predictions for the amplitudes of subdominant GW multipole moments, or for non-GR modes of polarization. We thus find that GR, without new physics beyond it, is still consistent with these GW events. The results of the two additional papers in this trio also find overall consistency with vacuum GR, with more than 90% of the events being consistent with GR at the 90% credible level. While one of the ringdown analyses finds the GR value in the tails for its combined results, this may be due in part to catalog variance.

</details>


### [58] [GWTC-4.0: Tests of General Relativity. II. Parameterized Tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19020)

Zimmerman,L. Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: [This paper presents comprehensive parameterized tests of General Relativity (GR) using 91 gravitational-wave events from GWTC-4.0, including O4a data. The analysis shows no evidence for physics beyond GR, with 90% of events consistent with GR predictions within their 90% credible intervals. The study improves bounds on post-Newtonian deviations by factors of 1.2-5.5, provides new constraints on modified gravity theories, and updates the graviton mass bound to $m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$, establishing GR as robust and providing the most stringent constraints to date on many deviations.]

[本文利用 GWTC-4.0（包括 O4a 数据）中的 91 个引力波事件，对广义相对论（GR）进行了全面的参数化检验。分析显示没有发现超出 GR 的物理学证据，90% 的事件在其 90% 可信区间内与 GR 预测一致。该研究将后牛顿偏差的界限提高了 1.2-5.5 倍，为修正引力理论提供了新的约束，并将引力子质量界限更新为 $m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$，从而确立了 GR 的稳健性，并为许多偏差提供了迄今为止最严格的约束。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation stems from the need to rigorously test General Relativity (GR) in the strong-field, dynamical regime using gravitational-wave (GW) observations from binary coalescences. While GR has passed numerous weak-field tests, its validity in extreme gravitational conditions (such as near black hole mergers) remains uncertain. The advent of advanced GW detectors (LIGO, Virgo, KAGRA) and the growing catalog of events (GWTC-4.0 including O4a data) provides unprecedented opportunities to constrain deviations from GR through parameterized tests. Specifically, the study aims to: (1) constrain parameterized modifications to GR predictions (e.g., deviations in post-Newtonian coefficients), (2) test the black hole no-hair theorem via spin-induced quadrupole moments, (3) probe propagation effects (dispersion, birefringence) that could indicate Lorentz violation or new degrees of freedom, and (4) search for line-of-sight acceleration effects that could mimic modified gravity.]

[动机源于需要利用双星并合引力波（GW）观测，在强场、动力学区域严格检验广义相对论（GR）。虽然 GR 已通过众多弱场检验，但其在极端引力条件下（如黑洞合并附近）的有效性仍不确定。先进引力波探测器（LIGO、Virgo、KAGRA）的出现以及事件目录（包括 O4a 数据的 GWTC-4.0）的不断增长，为通过参数化检验来约束对 GR 的偏差提供了前所未有的机会。具体而言，本研究旨在：(1) 约束对 GR 预测的参数化修改（例如，后牛顿系数的偏差），(2) 通过自旋诱导四极矩检验黑洞无毛定理，(3) 探测可能暗示洛伦兹破坏或新自由度的传播效应（色散、双折射），以及 (4) 寻找可能模拟修正引力的视线加速效应。]

Method: [The methodology employs Bayesian inference with parameterized deviations from GR to analyze 91 confident GW signals (42 from O4a + 49 from previous runs) from GWTC-4.0 with false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. Eight distinct tests are implemented:
1. **Parameterized Post-Newtonian (PPN) Tests**: Introduce deviation parameters $\delta \varphi_i$ for each PN order in the phase evolution, with priors allowing $\delta \varphi_i \neq 0$.
2. **Spin-Induced Quadrupole Tests**: Parameterize deviations from the Kerr quadrupole moment $Q = -\chi^2 M^3$ via $\delta \kappa$, where $\kappa = Q/(-\chi^2 M^3)$.
3. **Propagation Effects**: 
   - **Dispersive**: Include frequency-dependent phase modifications $\delta \Psi_{\mathrm{disp}}(f) \propto f^{\alpha}$ with $\alpha$ values corresponding to different theoretical models.
   - **Birefringent**: Test amplitude birefringence via $\delta A_{\mathrm{bir}}(f) \propto f^{\beta}$.
4. **Line-of-Sight Acceleration**: Parameterize constant acceleration $a_{\parallel}$ along the line of sight affecting the observed chirp mass.
The analysis uses nested sampling to compute Bayesian evidence and posterior distributions. Systematic errors from waveform systematics, calibration uncertainties, and noise artifacts are assessed through injection-recovery studies and robustness checks. Constraints are derived at 90% credibility, and improvements are quantified relative to previous bounds.]

[该方法采用贝叶斯推断，通过参数化的 GR 偏差来分析 GWTC-4.0 中 91 个置信引力波信号（42 个来自 O4a + 49 个来自先前运行），其误报率 $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$。实施了八种不同的检验：
1. **参数化后牛顿（PPN）检验**：为相位演化中的每个 PN 阶次引入偏差参数 $\delta \varphi_i$，先验允许 $\delta \varphi_i \neq 0$。
2. **自旋诱导四极矩检验**：通过 $\delta \kappa$ 参数化与 Kerr 四极矩 $Q = -\chi^2 M^3$ 的偏差，其中 $\kappa = Q/(-\chi^2 M^3)$。
3. **传播效应**：
   - **色散**：包含频率相关的相位修改 $\delta \Psi_{\mathrm{disp}}(f) \propto f^{\alpha}$，其中 $\alpha$ 值对应不同的理论模型。
   - **双折射**：通过 $\delta A_{\mathrm{bir}}(f) \propto f^{\beta}$ 检验振幅双折射。
4. **视线加速度**：参数化沿视线影响观测啁啾质量的恒定加速度 $a_{\parallel}$。
该分析使用嵌套采样计算贝叶斯证据和后验分布。通过注入恢复研究和稳健性检查评估了来自波形系统误差、校准不确定性和噪声伪影的系统误差。以 90% 可信度导出约束，并相对于先前的界限量化改进。]

Result: [Key results from the analysis of 91 GW events:
1. **No Evidence for Beyond-GR Physics**: Over 90% of events include the null result (no deviation from GR) within their 90% credible intervals across all tests.
2. **Improved PN Coefficient Bounds**: Constraints on deviations from GR PN coefficients improved by factors of 1.2-5.5 compared to previous analyses. For example, the 0.5PN coefficient $\delta \varphi_1$ is constrained to $|\delta \varphi_1| \lesssim 10^{-2}$.
3. **Spin-Induced Quadrupole Constraints**: No evidence for deviations from Kerr quadrupole moments, with $\kappa$ constrained to be consistent with 1 (Kerr value) within $\sim 10\%$ for most events.
4. **Propagation Effect Limits**: 
   - Dispersion: No evidence for frequency-dependent propagation, with constraints on dispersion coefficients improving by factors of 2-3.
   - Birefringence: No detectable amplitude birefringence.
5. **Line-of-Sight Acceleration**: No significant evidence for constant acceleration, with typical bounds $|a_{\parallel}| \lesssim 10^{-9} \mathrm{m/s^2}$.
6. **Graviton Mass Bound**: Updated constraint at 90% credibility: $m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$, improving previous limits by $\sim 15\%$.
7. **Translation to Modified Theories**: The PN constraints translate to bounds on specific modified gravity parameters, e.g., Einstein-dilaton-Gauss-Bonnet coupling $\sqrt{\alpha_{\mathrm{EDGB}}} \lesssim 1.1$ km.
8. **Statistical Consistency**: Observed deviations in $\sim 10\%$ of events are consistent with statistical fluctuations given noise properties and systematic uncertainties.]

[分析 91 个 GW 事件的主要结果：
1. **没有超出 GR 物理的证据**：在所有检验中，超过 90% 的事件在其 90% 可信区间内包含零结果（无 GR 偏差）。
2. **改进的 PN 系数界限**：与先前分析相比，对 GR PN 系数偏差的约束提高了 1.2-5.5 倍。例如，0.5PN 系数 $\delta \varphi_1$ 被约束为 $|\delta \varphi_1| \lesssim 10^{-2}$。
3. **自旋诱导四极矩约束**：没有发现偏离 Kerr 四极矩的证据，对于大多数事件，$\kappa$ 被约束在与 1（Kerr 值）一致的 $\sim 10\%$ 范围内。
4. **传播效应限制**：
   - 色散：没有发现频率相关传播的证据，色散系数的约束提高了 2-3 倍。
   - 双折射：未检测到可观测的振幅双折射。
5. **视线加速度**：没有发现恒定加速度的显著证据，典型界限为 $|a_{\parallel}| \lesssim 10^{-9} \mathrm{m/s^2}$。
6. **引力子质量界限**：90% 可信度的更新约束：$m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$，比先前限制提高了 $\sim 15\%$。
7. **对修正理论的转化**：PN 约束转化为对特定修正引力参数的界限，例如，Einstein-dilaton-Gauss-Bonnet 耦合 $\sqrt{\alpha_{\mathrm{EDGB}}} \lesssim 1.1$ km。
8. **统计一致性**：在给定噪声特性和系统不确定性的情况下，约 10% 事件中观察到的偏差与统计涨落一致。]

Conclusion: [The comprehensive parameterized tests of GR using 91 gravitational-wave events from GWTC-4.0 (including O4a data) provide the most stringent constraints to date on deviations from General Relativity in the strong-field regime. The analysis demonstrates remarkable consistency with GR predictions across multiple independent tests, with over 90% of events showing no statistically significant deviations. The improvements in PN coefficient bounds (factors of 1.2-5.5), the updated graviton mass constraint ($m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$), and the absence of evidence for spin-induced quadrupole deviations or propagation effects collectively reinforce GR's validity. The few marginal outliers are consistent with expected statistical fluctuations given noise properties and systematic uncertainties. These results establish gravitational-wave astronomy as a precision probe of strong-field gravity, with future observing runs (O4b, O5) expected to further improve constraints by factors of 10-100 as the event catalog grows. The methodology provides a robust framework for continuous testing of GR as more data becomes available.]

[利用 GWTC-4.0（包括 O4a 数据）中 91 个引力波事件对 GR 进行的全面参数化检验，为强场区域中偏离广义相对论的行为提供了迄今为止最严格的约束。分析表明，在多个独立检验中与 GR 预测具有显著的一致性，超过 90% 的事件未显示出统计学上显著的偏差。PN 系数界限的改进（1.2-5.5 倍）、引力子质量约束的更新（$m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$）以及没有发现自旋诱导四极矩偏差或传播效应的证据，共同强化了 GR 的有效性。少数边际异常值在给定噪声特性和系统不确定性的情况下，与预期的统计涨落一致。这些结果确立了引力波天文学作为强场引力精密探测工具的地位，随着事件目录的增长，未来的观测运行（O4b、O5）预计将进一步将约束提高 10-100 倍。随着更多数据的获取，该方法为持续检验 GR 提供了一个稳健的框架。]

Abstract: In this second of three papers on tests of general relativity (GR) applied to the compact binary coalescence signals in the fourth Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), we present the results of the parameterized tests of GR and constraints on line-of-sight acceleration. We include events up to and including the first part of the fourth observing run (O4a) of the LIGO Virgo KAGRA detectors. As in the other two papers in this series, we restrict our analysis to the 42 confident signals, measured by at least two detectors, that have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ from O4a, in addition to the 49 such events from previous observing runs. This paper focuses on the eight tests that constrain parameterized deviations from the expected GR (or unaccelerated) values. These include modifications of post-Newtonian (PN) parameters, spin-induced quadrupole moments different from those of a binary black hole, and possible dispersive or birefringent propagation effects. Overall, we find no evidence for physics beyond GR, for spin-induced quadrupole moments different from those of a Kerr black hole in GR, or for line of sight acceleration, with more than 90% of the events including the null result (no deviation) within their 90% credible intervals. We discuss possible systematics affecting the other events and tests, even though they are statistically not surprising, given noise. We improve the bounds on deviations from the GR PN coefficients by factors of 1.2-5.5 and provide illustrative translations to constraints on some modified theories. Also, we update the bound on the mass of the graviton, at 90% credibility, to $m_g \leq 1.92\times 10^{-23} \mathrm{eV}/c^2$. Thus, we see that GR holds, and many of the bounds on possible deviations derived from our events are the best to date.

</details>


### [59] [GWTC-4.0: Tests of General Relativity. III. Tests of the Remnants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19021)
