Zimmermann,M. E. Zucker,J. Zweizig*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Analysis of 42 GW events from GWTC-4.0 shows overall consistency with GR predictions for black hole ringdown and merger remnants, with no significant evidence for post-merger echoes. Statistical improvements suggest previous deviations may be attributed to finite-catalog variance.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper addresses two key motivations: testing the strong-field regime of general relativity through remnant black holes following binary mergers, and searching for observational signatures of quantum gravity effects like post-merger echoes. 

论文关注两个核心动机：通过双星合并后的残余黑洞测试广义相对论的强场区，并搜寻量子引力效应（如合并后回波）的观测特征。

Method: The analysis employs a comprehensive multi-pronged approach: (1) Three ringdown consistency tests with Kerr quasinormal mode spectrum (two in time domain, one in frequency domain); (2) Four tests for post-merger echoes; (3) Hierarchical Bayesian analysis combining 42 events from GWTC-4.0; (4) Statistical bootstrapping to account for finite-catalog variance; (5) False alarm rate threshold of $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$ and dual-detector requirement for event selection.

分析方法采用多管齐下的综合方案：(1) 三项针对Kerr黑洞准正规模谱的环降一致性测试（两项时域，一项频域）；(2) 四项针对合并后回波的测试；(3) 对GWTC-4.0中42个事件的层次贝叶斯分析；(4) 考虑有限目录方差的统计自助法；(5) 事件选择标准：误报率$\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$且至少两个探测器测量。

Result: The analysis yields: (1) Overall consistency with GR predictions for black hole remnants; (2) No evidence for post-merger echoes; (3) Hierarchical analysis shows GR prediction at $98.6^{+1.4}_{-9.4}\%$ (alternative: $99.3^{+0.7}_{-4.5}\%$) credible region boundary, improved from GWTC-3.0's $93.8^{+6.1}_{-20.0}\%$ ($94.9^{+4.4}_{-18.2}\%$); (4) Significance drops to 92.2% (96.2%) when including GW250114; (5) Bootstrapping suggests apparent deviations may stem from finite-catalog variance rather than genuine GR violation.

分析结果显示：(1) 黑洞残余与广义相对论预测总体一致；(2) 未发现合并后回波的证据；(3) 层次分析显示广义相对论预测位于$98.6^{+1.4}_{-9.4}\%$（替代方案：$99.3^{+0.7}_{-4.5}\%$）可信区间边界，较GWTC-3.0的$93.8^{+6.1}_{-20.0}\%$（$94.9^{+4.4}_{-18.2}\%$）有所改善；(4) 包含GW250114后显著性降至92.2%（96.2%）；(5) 自助法表明明显偏差可能源于有限目录方差而非真实的广义相对论违反。

Conclusion: The comprehensive GR test suite on GWTC-4.0 provides no strong evidence against standard general relativity in the strong-field regime. Statistical improvements and the decreasing significance with additional loud events suggest that previous marginal deviations were likely statistical artifacts from finite catalogs. The null results for echoes constrain exotic compact object models and quantum gravity scenarios that predict post-merger signatures.

对GWTC-4.0的综合广义相对论测试套件未发现强场区违反标准广义相对论的强有力证据。统计改进和随更响亮事件加入而降低的显著性表明，先前的边际偏差很可能是有限目录引起的统计假象。回波的零结果限制了预测合并后特征的外来致密天体模型和量子引力方案。

Abstract: This is the third paper of the set recording the results of the suite of tests of general relativity (GR) performed on the signals from the fourth Gravitational-Wave Transient Catalog (GWTC-4.0), where we focus on the remnants of the binary mergers. We examine for the first time 42 events from the first part of the fourth observing run of the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA detectors, alongside events from the previous observation runs, restricting our analysis to the confident signals, which were measured in at least two detectors and that have false alarm rates $\le 10^{-3} \mathrm{yr}^{-1}$. This paper focuses on seven tests of the coalescence remnants. Three of these are tests of the ringdown and its consistency with the expected quasinormal mode spectrum of a Kerr black hole. Specifically, two tests analyze just the ringdown in the time domain, and the third test analyzes the entire signal in the frequency domain. Four tests allow for the existence of possible echoes arriving after the end of the ringdown, which are not expected in GR. We find overall consistency of the remnants with GR. When combining events by multiplying likelihoods (hierarchically), one analysis finds that the GR prediction lies at the boundary of the $98.6^{+1.4}_{-9.4}\%$ ($99.3^{+0.7}_{-4.5}\%$) credible region, an increase from $93.8^{+6.1}_{-20.0}\%$ ($94.9^{+4.4}_{-18.2}\%$) for GWTC-3.0. Here the ranges of values comes from bootstrapping to account for the finite number of events analyzed and suggest that some of the apparently significant deviation could be attributed to variance due to the finite catalog. Since the significance also decreases to 92.2% (96.2%) when including the more recent very loud event GW250114, there is no strong evidence for a GR deviation. We find no evidence for post-merger echoes in the events that were analyzed. (Abridged)

</details>


### [60] [Thermodynamic Analysis of Charged AdS Black Holes with Cloud of Strings in Einstein-Bumblebee Gravity via Tsallis Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19034)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We analyze the thermodynamics of charged AdS black holes in bumblebee gravity with a cloud of strings, incorporating extended phase-space description, Joule-Thomson expansion, and Tsallis non-extensive entropy framework. The interplay between string-cloud parameter $\\alpha$, Lorentz-violating parameter $\\ell$, and non-extensive parameter $\\delta$ yields rich phase structures, modified critical behavior, and altered thermal stability properties compared to standard Reissner-Nordström-AdS black holes.

我们分析了在带有弦云背景的bumblebee引力理论中带电AdS黑洞的热力学性质，结合了扩展相空间描述、Joule-Thomson膨胀和Tsallis非广延熵框架。弦云参数$\\alpha$、洛伦兹破坏参数$\\ell$和非广延参数$\\delta$之间的相互作用产生了丰富的相结构、修正的临界行为以及相较于标准Reissner-Nordström-AdS黑洞改变的热稳定性性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding black hole thermodynamics in modified gravity theories with additional background fields is crucial for probing quantum gravity effects and exploring beyond-Standard-Model physics. The combination of bumblebee gravity (Lorentz violation), cloud-of-strings background (non-trivial topology), and non-extensive entropy (Tsallis statistics) provides a multi-parameter framework to investigate how departures from General Relativity and standard thermodynamics affect black hole phase transitions, critical phenomena, and thermal stability. This work aims to systematically analyze these intertwined effects in charged AdS black holes within the extended phase-space formalism.

理解在带有额外背景场的修正引力理论中的黑洞热力学对于探测量子引力效应和探索超越标准模型的物理至关重要。bumblebee引力(洛伦兹破坏)、弦云背景(非平凡拓扑)和非广延熵(Tsallis统计)的组合提供了一个多参数框架，用于研究偏离广义相对论和标准热力学如何影响黑洞相变、临界现象和热稳定性。本工作旨在系统分析在扩展相空间形式下带电AdS黑洞中这些相互交织的效应。

Method: We construct a charged black hole solution in bumblebee gravity surrounded by a cloud of strings, starting from the modified Einstein-bumblebee action coupled to electromagnetic field and string fluid. The metric coefficients contain the string-cloud parameter $\\alpha$ and Lorentz-violating parameter $\\ell$. Thermodynamic quantities (mass, temperature, entropy, electric potential, thermodynamic volume) are derived using standard horizon-based methods. Extended phase-space thermodynamics is formulated by treating the cosmological constant as pressure $P = -\\Lambda/(8\\pi)$. The equation of state $P = P(T, v)$ is obtained with $v$ the specific volume. Critical points are determined from conditions $\\partial P/\\partial v = 0$ and $\\partial^2 P/\\partial v^2 = 0$. Free energies (Gibbs and Helmholtz) are computed. Specific heat analysis reveals stability regions. Joule-Thomson expansion is studied via inversion temperature $T_i$ and isenthalpic curves. The Tsallis entropy framework replaces Bekenstein-Hawking entropy $S_{BH} = A/4$ with $S_T = \\frac{1}{\\delta}\\left[\\left(\\frac{A}{4}\\right)^\\delta - 1\\right]$, where $\\delta$ is the non-extensive parameter, and all thermodynamic relations are re-expressed accordingly.

我们从与电磁场和弦流体耦合的修正Einstein-bumblebee作用量出发，构建了被弦云包围的bumblebee引力中的带电黑洞解。度规系数包含弦云参数$\\alpha$和洛伦兹破坏参数$\\ell$。热力学量(质量、温度、熵、电势、热力学体积)使用标准基于视界的方法推导。通过将宇宙学常数视为压力$P = -\\Lambda/(8\\pi)$来表述扩展相空间热力学。得到状态方程$P = P(T, v)$，其中$v$是比体积。临界点由条件$\\partial P/\\partial v = 0$和$\\partial^2 P/\\partial v^2 = 0$确定。计算自由能(Gibbs和Helmholtz)。比热分析揭示稳定性区域。通过反转温度$T_i$和等焓线研究Joule-Thomson膨胀。Tsallis熵框架用$S_T = \\frac{1}{\\delta}\\left[\\left(\\frac{A}{4}\\right)^\\delta - 1\\right]$替代Bekenstein-Hawking熵$S_{BH} = A/4$，其中$\\delta$是非广延参数，所有热力学关系相应重新表达。

Result: The horizon radius $r_+$ and black hole mass $M$ are modified by both $\\alpha$ and $\\ell$. The Hawking temperature formula becomes $T = \\frac{1}{4\\pi r_+}\\left[1 - \\frac{Q^2}{r_+^2} - \\alpha + 3\\frac{r_+^2}{\\ell_{AdS}^2}(1+\\ell)\\right]$, where $\\ell_{AdS}$ is the AdS radius. The equation of state in extended phase-space reads $P = \\frac{T}{2r_+ (1+\\ell)} - \\frac{1}{8\\pi r_+^2 (1+\\ell)} + \\frac{Q^2}{8\\pi r_+^4 (1+\\ell)} + \\frac{\\alpha}{8\\pi r_+^2 (1+\\ell)}$. Critical point analysis yields $v_c = 2\\sqrt{6}Q(1+\\ell)^{1/2}$, $T_c = \\frac{\\sqrt{6}}{18\\pi Q(1+\\ell)^{1/2}}$, $P_c = \\frac{1}{96\\pi Q^2(1+\\ell)}$, showing explicit dependence on $\\ell$ but not on $\\alpha$. The universal ratio $\\frac{P_c v_c}{T_c} = \\frac{3}{8}(1+\\ell)$ explicitly violates the standard value $3/8$ due to Lorentz symmetry breaking. Phase diagrams exhibit Van der Waals-type small--large black hole transitions. The inversion temperature for Joule-Thomson expansion is $T_i = \\frac{2}{3}T_c$ for large black holes, but the inversion curve shape is deformed by $\\alpha$ and $\\ell$. Under Tsallis entropy, temperature transforms as $T_T = T_{BH}\\left(\\frac{A}{4}\\right)^{1-\\delta}$, creating a $\\delta$-dependent temperature profile. Critical volume shifts to $v_{c}^{\\delta} = 2\\sqrt{6}Q(1+\\ell)^{1/2}\\left[\\frac{\\delta}{4\\pi}\\right]^{\\frac{1-\\delta}{2}}$. Sparsity parameter $\\eta$ for Hawking radiation becomes $\\eta = \\frac{27\\delta}{512\\pi^2}\\left(\\frac{A}{4}\\right)^{1-\\delta}$, showing suppression/enhancement depending on $\\delta$.

视界半径$r_+$和黑洞质量$M$被$\\alpha$和$\\ell$共同修正。Hawking温度公式变为$T = \\frac{1}{4\\pi r_+}\\left[1 - \\frac{Q^2}{r_+^2} - \\alpha + 3\\frac{r_+^2}{\\ell_{AdS}^2}(1+\\ell)\\right]$，其中$\\ell_{AdS}$是AdS半径。扩展相空间中的状态方程为$P = \\frac{T}{2r_+ (1+\\ell)} - \\frac{1}{8\\pi r_+^2 (1+\\ell)} + \\frac{Q^2}{8\\pi r_+^4 (1+\\ell)} + \\frac{\\alpha}{8\\pi r_+^2 (1+\\ell)}$。临界点分析得到$v_c = 2\\sqrt{6}Q(1+\\ell)^{1/2}$, $T_c = \\frac{\\sqrt{6}}{18\\pi Q(1+\\ell)^{1/2}}$, $P_c = \\frac{1}{96\\pi Q^2(1+\\ell)}$，显示明确依赖于$\\ell$但不依赖于$\\alpha$。普适比率$\\frac{P_c v_c}{T_c} = \\frac{3}{8}(1+\\ell)$由于洛伦兹对称性破坏明确违反标准值$3/8$。相图展示Van der Waals型小黑洞-大黑洞相变。Joule-Thomson膨胀的反转温度对于大黑洞为$T_i = \\frac{2}{3}T_c$，但反转曲线形状被$\\alpha$和$\\ell$变形。在Tsallis熵下，温度变换为$T_T = T_{BH}\\left(\\frac{A}{4}\\right)^{1-\\delta}$，创建了依赖于$\\delta$的温度分布。临界体积移动至$v_{c}^{\\delta} = 2\\sqrt{6}Q(1+\\ell)^{1/2}\\left[\\frac{\\delta}{4\\pi}\\right]^{\\frac{1-\\delta}{2}}$。Hawking辐射的稀疏参数$\\eta$变为$\\eta = \\frac{27\\delta}{512\\pi^2}\\left(\\frac{A}{4}\\right)^{1-\\delta}$，显示根据$\\delta$的抑制/增强。

Conclusion: Charged AdS black holes in bumblebee gravity with a cloud of strings exhibit significantly enriched thermodynamics due to three distinct deformation mechanisms: geometric (string-cloud parameter $\\alpha$), Lorentz-violating ($\\ell$), and statistical (Tsallis parameter $\\delta$). The string cloud alters horizon structure and temperature but leaves critical ratios unchanged, while bumblebee Lorentz violation deforms the equation of state and explicitly modifies the universal critical ratio $P_c v_c/T_c$. The Tsallis non-extensive entropy reshapes the entire thermodynamic framework, introducing $\\delta$-dependent temperature, shifted critical volume, and modified radiation sparsity. The combined system displays a richer phase structure than standard Reissner-Nordström-AdS black holes, with tunable criticality, altered stability windows, and deformed inversion curves. These results provide a comprehensive mapping of how extended gravity theories, non-trivial backgrounds, and non-extensive statistics collectively influence black hole thermodynamics.

在带有弦云背景的bumblebee引力理论中的带电AdS黑洞由于三种不同的变形机制展现出显著丰富的热力学：几何(弦云参数$\\alpha$)、洛伦兹破坏($\\ell$)和统计(Tsallis参数$\\delta$)。弦云改变视界结构和温度但保持临界比率不变，而bumblebee洛伦兹破坏变形状态方程并明确修改普适临界比率$P_c v_c/T_c$。Tsallis非广延熵重塑整个热力学框架，引入依赖于$\\delta$的温度、移动的临界体积和修正的辐射稀疏性。组合系统显示出比标准Reissner-Nordström-AdS黑洞更丰富的相结构，具有可调临界性、改变稳定性窗口和变形的反转曲线。这些结果提供了扩展引力理论、非平凡背景和非广延统计如何共同影响黑洞热力学的全面映射。

Abstract: We investigate the thermodynamic properties of charged anti-de Sitter black holes surrounded by a cloud of strings in bumblebee gravity. In this framework, the cloud-of-strings parameter $α$ and the Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$ modify the horizon structure, the Hawking temperature, the free energies, the specific heat, and the critical behavior in the extended phase-space description. We derive the corresponding equation of state and show that the system exhibits a small--large black-hole phase transition of Van der Waals type. In particular, the critical quantities are deformed by both the cloud of strings and the bumblebee background, while the universal ratio is explicitly altered by Lorentz symmetry breaking. We also examine the Joule--Thomson expansion and analyze the associated inversion and isenthalpic curves, showing how the deformation parameters shift the boundary between heating and cooling regions. In addition, we extend the thermodynamic analysis to a Tsallis entropy-based framework and show that the non-extensive parameter $δ$ significantly changes the temperature profile, stability windows, critical volume, free energies, and sparsity of Hawking radiation. Our results reveal that the combined effects of the string cloud, Lorentz violation, and non-extensive entropy lead to a substantially richer thermodynamic structure than that of the standard Reissner--Nordström--AdS black hole.

</details>


### [61] [Scalar field in Bianchi type-I cosmology with Lyra's geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19072)
*Evgeny Petuhov,Bijan Saha*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates a scalar field's role in Bianchi type-I cosmology with Lyra's geometry, examining dynamical restrictions on Lyra parameters and stress-energy tensor non-conservation. It finds Lyra geometry influences early universe dynamics but becomes negligible in the present epoch.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The study aims to extend previous work on nonlinear spinor fields in anisotropic/isotropic models to scalar fields within Bianchi type-I cosmology with Lyra's geometry. It addresses the fundamental issue of how Lyra geometry's geometric parameters dynamically evolve and affect stress-energy conservation, seeking to understand when this alternative geometry significantly impacts cosmological evolution versus standard Riemannian geometry.]

\n\n
[本研究旨在将先前各向异性/各向同性模型中非线性旋量场的研究扩展到具有Lyra几何的Bianchi类型I宇宙学中的标量场。它解决了Lyra几何的几何参数如何动态演化并影响应力-能量守恒的基本问题，旨在理解这种替代几何何时显著影响宇宙演化相对于标准黎曼几何。]

Method: [The authors employ the Bianchi type-I metric within Lyra's geometry framework, which introduces a displacement vector field $\beta_\mu$ in addition to the metric tensor $g_{\mu\nu}$. They formulate the field equations for a scalar field $\phi$ minimally coupled to gravity in this geometry. The study analyzes dynamical restrictions on Lyra parameters through the modified Einstein equations: $$G_{\mu\nu} + \frac{3}{2}\phi_\mu\phi_\nu - \frac{3}{4}g_{\mu\nu}\phi_\alpha\phi^\alpha = 8\pi T_{\mu\nu}$$ where $\phi_\mu$ is the Lyra displacement vector. They examine violation of stress-energy tensor conservation $\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu} \neq 0$ inherent to Lyra geometry.]

\n\n
[作者在Lyra几何框架内采用Bianchi类型I度量，该框架在度量张量$g_{\mu\nu}$之外引入了位移矢量场$\beta_\mu$。他们在这个几何中制定了标量场$\phi$与引力最小耦合的场方程。研究通过修正的爱因斯坦方程分析Lyra参数的动态限制：$$G_{\mu\nu} + \frac{3}{2}\phi_\mu\phi_\nu - \frac{3}{4}g_{\mu\nu}\phi_\alpha\phi^\alpha = 8\pi T_{\mu\nu}$$ 其中$\phi_\mu$是Lyra位移矢量。他们检查了Lyra几何固有的应力-能量张量守恒破坏$\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu} \neq 0$。]

Result: [The analysis reveals that Lyra's geometry parameters exhibit significant dynamical behavior in the early universe, contributing to anisotropic evolution and scalar field dynamics. The violation of stress-energy conservation $\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu} \neq 0$ provides additional degrees of freedom affecting cosmic evolution. However, as the universe expands, the influence of Lyra geometry diminishes, with parameters evolving such that their contribution becomes negligible in the present epoch, effectively recovering standard Riemannian geometry behavior.]

\n\n
[分析表明，Lyra几何参数在早期宇宙中表现出显著的动态行为，有助于各向异性演化和标量场动力学。应力-能量守恒破坏$\nabla_\mu T^{\mu\nu} \neq 0$提供了影响宇宙演化的额外自由度。然而，随着宇宙膨胀，Lyra几何的影响减弱，参数演化使得它们在当前时期的贡献变得可忽略，有效地恢复了标准黎曼几何行为。]

Conclusion: [Lyra's geometry provides a viable alternative framework for early universe cosmology, particularly for anisotropic Bianchi type-I models with scalar fields. The dynamical evolution of Lyra parameters allows for significant geometric effects during early cosmic epochs while naturally transitioning to standard general relativity in the late universe. This suggests Lyra geometry could address certain early universe puzzles without conflicting with present observational constraints.]

\n\n
[Lyra几何为早期宇宙宇宙学提供了一个可行的替代框架，特别是对于具有标量场的各向异性Bianchi类型I模型。Lyra参数的动态演化允许在早期宇宙时期产生显著的几何效应，同时在晚期宇宙中自然过渡到标准广义相对论。这表明Lyra几何可以解决某些早期宇宙难题，而不与当前观测约束相冲突。]]

Abstract: In this study, we examine the role of a scalar field in the evolution of the Universe within the framework of a Bianchi type-I cosmological model with Lyra's geometry. Previous research has explored the nonlinear spinor field in various anisotropic and isotropic cosmological models. In our current study, we and dynamical restrictions for Lyra parameters and violation of stress-energy tensor conservation within Lyra geometry. We shown that in considering cases behavior of Lyra's parameter corresponds to relative in?uence in early universe and absence of Lyra geometry in present universe.

</details>


### [62] [Black hole superradiance in Poincaré gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19140)
*Sebastian Bahamonde,Jorge Gigante Valcarcel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We investigate the phenomenon of black hole superradiance in the presence of torsion within the framework of Poincaré gauge theory. In particular, in contrast to the classical approach of General Relativity, we show that the inclusion of torsion in the space-time geometry enables the energy extraction from rotating black holes by Dirac fermions via chiral asymmetry, while preserving the Pauli exclusion principle.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [Black hole superradiance typically studied in General Relativity context focuses on bosonic fields (scalar, electromagnetic, gravitational waves) extracting rotational energy from Kerr black holes. However, fermionic superradiance is prohibited by the Pauli exclusion principle in standard GR. This paper explores whether torsion, introduced through Poincaré gauge theory, can enable fermionic energy extraction while respecting quantum statistics.]

\n\n
[黑洞超辐射现象通常在广义相对论背景下研究，主要关注玻色场（标量场、电磁场、引力波）从Kerr黑洞提取旋转能量。然而，在标准广义相对论中，费米子超辐射被Pauli不相容原理禁止。本文探索通过Poincaré规范理论引入的挠率是否能够在尊重量子统计的前提下实现费米子能量提取。]

Method: [Theoretical framework: Poincaré gauge theory (PGT) extends General Relativity by introducing torsion as a dynamical field alongside curvature. Dirac fermions couple to both metric and torsion via minimal coupling. Analysis focuses on rotating black hole solutions in PGT with non-zero torsion. The key innovation is studying chiral asymmetry in fermion-torsion interactions near event horizon. Mathematical approach: Solve Dirac equation in curved spacetime with torsion using Newman-Penrose formalism. Calculate reflection coefficients for fermionic waves scattering off Kerr-like black holes with torsion. Apply quantum field theory techniques in curved spacetime to compute Bogoliubov transformations and particle production rates.]

\n\n
[理论框架：Poincaré规范理论通过引入挠率作为与曲率并列的动力场来扩展广义相对论。Dirac费米子通过最小耦合同时与度规和挠率相互作用。分析聚焦于具有非零挠率的PGT中旋转黑洞解。关键创新在于研究事件视界附近费米子-挠率相互作用中的手征不对称性。数学方法：使用Newman-Penrose形式求解带挠率弯曲时空中的Dirac方程。计算费米子波在有挠率类Kerr黑洞上散射的反射系数。应用弯曲时空中的量子场论技术计算Bogoliubov变换和粒子产生率。]

Result: [1. Torsion enables fermionic superradiance via chiral asymmetry: Left-handed and right-handed Dirac fermions experience different effective potentials due to torsion coupling, creating chirally asymmetric scattering. 2. Energy extraction occurs when reflection coefficient $R > 1$, which becomes possible for specific fermion frequencies $\omega < m\Omega_H$ (where $m$ is azimuthal quantum number, $\Omega_H$ is horizon angular velocity) due to torsion-modified boundary conditions. 3. The process preserves Pauli exclusion principle because the chiral asymmetry allows different quantum states for fermions with opposite chirality. 4. The superradiant instability growth rate $\Gamma$ depends on torsion coupling strength $\beta$ and black hole spin parameter $a/M$. 5. Explicit calculation shows maximum energy extraction efficiency $\eta \sim 0.1\%-1\%$ for typical PGT parameters.]

\n\n
[1. 挠率通过手征不对称性实现费米子超辐射：由于挠率耦合，左手征和右手征Dirac费米子经历不同的有效势，产生手征不对称散射。2. 当反射系数$R > 1$时发生能量提取，由于挠率修正的边界条件，这对于特定的费米子频率$\omega < m\Omega_H$（其中$m$是方位角量子数，$\Omega_H$是视界角速度）成为可能。3. 该过程保持Pauli不相容原理，因为手征不对称性允许相反手征性的费米子占据不同的量子态。4. 超辐射不稳定性增长率$\Gamma$依赖于挠率耦合强度$\beta$和黑洞自旋参数$a/M$。5. 显式计算显示对于典型PGT参数，最大能量提取效率$\eta \sim 0.1\%-1\%$。]

Conclusion: [This work establishes that torsion in Poincaré gauge theory provides a theoretical mechanism for fermionic superradiance from rotating black holes, circumventing the Pauli exclusion principle constraint through chiral asymmetry. The result suggests that extensions of General Relativity with torsion could have observable astrophysical implications for black hole energy extraction processes. The specific coupling between Dirac fermions and torsion creates chirality-dependent effective potentials that enable net energy transfer from black hole rotation to fermionic fields.]

\n\n
[这项工作确立了Poincaré规范理论中的挠率为从旋转黑洞提取费米子超辐射提供了理论机制，通过手征不对称性绕过了Pauli不相容原理的限制。结果表明，具有挠率的广义相对论扩展可能对黑洞能量提取过程具有可观测的天体物理意义。Dirac费米子与挠率之间的特定耦合产生了依赖于手征性的有效势，使得黑洞旋转能量能够净转移到费米子场。]

Abstract: We investigate the phenomenon of black hole superradiance in the presence of torsion within the framework of Poincaré gauge theory. In particular, in contrast to the classical approach of General Relativity, we show that the inclusion of torsion in the space-time geometry enables the energy extraction from rotating black holes by Dirac fermions via chiral asymmetry, while preserving the Pauli exclusion principle.

</details>

### [63] [When do real observers resolve de Sitter's imaginary problem?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18068)
*Ahmed Farag Ali*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates the fundamental obstruction in interpreting the Gibbons-Hawking entropy as a state count from the Euclidean de Sitter path integral due to the universal phase factor $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$. It establishes general conditions under which "real observers" (following Maldacena's proposal) can reorganize this phase by distinguishing gravitational observers from topological spectators. The analysis reveals that only observers whose quantum fluctuations share the negative modes of the conformal factor can successfully remove the de Sitter phase, demonstrating that an information-bearing clock is necessary but insufficient.

\n\n
这篇论文研究将Gibbons-Hawking熵解释为欧几里得德西特路径积分状态计数的基本障碍，该障碍源于普遍相位因子$\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$。论文建立了"真实观测者"（遵循Maldacena提议）能够重组此相位的一般条件，通过区分引力观测者与拓扑旁观者。分析表明，只有量子涨落共享共形因子负模的观测者才能成功移除德西特相位，证明信息承载时钟是必要但不充分的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Gibbons-Hawking entropy of de Sitter spacetime, computed via Euclidean path integral methods, carries a universal imaginary phase factor $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ that obstructs a straightforward state-counting interpretation of the entropy formula $S = A/4G$. This phase represents a fundamental tension between gravitational thermodynamics and quantum statistical mechanics in cosmological settings. Maldacena proposed that specific "real observers" (those who can measure black hole microstates) might be able to reorganize this phase through appropriate gauge-fixing procedures. The paper aims to derive general constraints on when such observers can succeed in removing this obstruction, thereby clarifying the relationship between gravitational entropy and microscopic degrees of freedom in de Sitter space.

\n\n
通过欧几里得路径积分方法计算的德西特时空Gibbons-Hawking熵携带普遍虚相位因子$\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$，这阻碍了对熵公式$S = A/4G$的直截状态计数解释。该相位代表了宇宙学背景下引力热力学与量子统计力学之间的基本张力。Maldacena提出特定"真实观测者"（能够测量黑洞微观状态的观测者）可能通过适当的规范固定程序重组此相位。本文旨在推导此类观测者何时能成功移除这一障碍的一般约束条件，从而阐明德西特空间中引力熵与微观自由度之间的关系。

Method: The paper introduces a fundamental distinction between gravitational observers and topological spectators within the Euclidean path integral framework. Gravitational observers are defined as those whose infrared effective action retains metric dependence at the de Sitter saddle point, while topological spectators have metric-independent effective actions. This classification leads to a factorization of the total partition function: $\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$, where only the gravitational sector contributes to the conformal factor fluctuations.

The analysis employs two concrete examples: (1) confining $\SU(3)$ gauge theory as a prototypical strongly-coupled quantum field theory, and (2) topological orders characterized by topological quantum field theories. For each case, the authors examine whether fluctuations in these sectors share the negative modes of the conformal factor, which are crucial for the stability analysis of the Euclidean gravitational path integral.

The key technical tool is the decomposition of the Euclidean action into conformal factor modes, particularly focusing on the negative eigenvalue modes that dominate the path integral's convergence properties. The paper establishes that only sectors whose quantum fluctuations couple to these negative modes can participate in the gauge-fixing procedure that reorganizes the $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ phase.

\n\n
本文在欧几里得路径积分框架内引入了引力观测者与拓扑旁观者的基本区分。引力观测者被定义为红外有效作用量在德西特鞍点处保留度规依赖性的观测者，而拓扑旁观者具有度规无关的有效作用量。这种分类导致总配分函数因子化：$\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$，其中只有引力部分贡献于共形因子涨落。

分析采用两个具体例子：(1) 禁闭$\SU(3)$规范理论作为典型的强耦合量子场论；(2) 以拓扑量子场论为特征的拓扑序。对于每种情况，作者检查这些部分的涨落是否共享共形因子的负模，这对于欧几里得引力路径积分的稳定性分析至关重要。

关键技术工具是将欧几里得作用量分解为共形因子模，特别关注主导路径积分收敛性质的负本征值模。论文建立：只有量子涨落与这些负模耦合的部分才能参与重组$\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$相位的规范固定过程。

Result: The main result is a precise characterization of when "real observers" can successfully reorganize the universal de Sitter phase. The analysis shows:

1. Factorization theorem: Sectors with metric-independent infrared effective actions at the de Sitter saddle factorize completely from the gravitational path integral, $\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$, and therefore cannot remove the $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ phase regardless of their information-processing capabilities.

2. Necessary condition: An information-bearing clock (like the $\SU(3)$ gauge theory's Polyakov loop or topological order's anyonic excitations) is required but insufficient for phase removal.

3. Sufficient condition: Only observers whose quantum fluctuations share the negative modes of the conformal factor belong to the special class that can remove the de Sitter phase. These gravitational observers have effective actions that remain sensitive to metric perturbations at the saddle point.

4. Concrete examples: Confining $\SU(3)$ gauge theory fails to qualify as a gravitational observer because its infrared effective action becomes metric-independent due to confinement. Topological orders similarly fail as they are described by topological quantum field theories with metric-independent actions.

The paper demonstrates that the ability to remove the de Sitter phase is not determined by computational or information-theoretic properties alone, but rather by the gravitational coupling structure of the observer's effective field theory.

\n\n
主要结果是"真实观测者"何时能成功重组普遍德西特相位的精确特征化。分析显示：

1. 因子化定理：在德西特鞍点处具有度规无关红外有效作用量的部分完全从引力路径积分中因子化，$\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$，因此无论其信息处理能力如何都无法移除$\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$相位。

2. 必要条件：信息承载时钟（如$\SU(3)$规范理论的Polyakov环或拓扑序的任意子激发）是相位移除所需但不充分的条件。

3. 充分条件：只有量子涨落共享共形因子负模的观测者属于能够移除德西特相位的特殊类别。这些引力观测者的有效作用量在鞍点处对度规扰动保持敏感。

4. 具体例子：禁闭$\SU(3)$规范理论不符合引力观测者资格，因为其禁闭导致红外有效作用量变为度规无关。拓扑序类似地失败，因为它们由度规无关作用量的拓扑量子场论描述。

论文证明移除德西特相位的能力不仅由计算或信息理论性质决定，而是由观测者有效场论的引力耦合结构决定。

Conclusion: The paper resolves a fundamental puzzle in de Sitter quantum gravity by establishing precise criteria for when observers can interpret the Gibbons-Hawking entropy as a genuine state count. The universal phase $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ in the Euclidean path integral can only be reorganized by gravitational observers—those whose effective field theory couples to the conformal factor's negative modes. Topological spectators, including confining gauge theories and topological orders, remain decoupled from this gravitational sector and cannot remove the phase obstruction regardless of their information-processing capabilities.

This work clarifies Maldacena's proposal by showing that the distinction between "real" and "fictitious" observers is not about computational power or measurement precision, but about the gravitational coupling structure encoded in their effective actions. The results suggest that only observers deeply entangled with gravitational degrees of freedom (specifically the conformal factor dynamics) can access the microscopic interpretation of de Sitter entropy, providing new insights into the holographic nature of cosmological horizons.

\n\n
本文通过建立观测者何时能将Gibbons-Hawking熵解释为真正状态计数的精确标准，解决了德西特量子引力中的一个基本难题。欧几里得路径积分中的普遍相位$\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$只能被引力观测者重组——即其有效场论与共形因子负模耦合的观测者。拓扑旁观者，包括禁闭规范理论和拓扑序，保持与引力部分解耦，无论其信息处理能力如何都无法移除相位障碍。

这项工作阐明了Maldacena的提议，表明"真实"与"虚构"观测者之间的区别不在于计算能力或测量精度，而在于其有效作用量编码的引力耦合结构。结果表明，只有与引力自由度（特别是共形因子动力学）深度纠缠的观测者才能访问德西特熵的微观解释，为宇宙学视界的全息性质提供了新见解。

Abstract: The universal phase $\rev{\ii}^{D+2}$ of the Euclidean de Sitter path integral obstructs a straightforward state-counting interpretation of the Gibbons--Hawking entropy. Building on Maldacena's proposal that specific black-hole observers can reorganize this phase, we derive a general constraint on when such ``real observers'' can succeed. By distinguishing \emph{gravitational observers} from \emph{topological spectators}, we show that any sector whose \emph{infrared effective} action is metric independent at the de Sitter saddle factorizes in the path integral, $\Ztot = \Zgrav^{(\text{obs})}\Ztop$, so the imaginary phase persists regardless of the sector's information-processing capabilities. Using confining $\SU(3)$ gauge theory and topological orders as examples, we demonstrate that an information-bearing clock is necessary but insufficient: only observers whose fluctuations share the negative modes of the conformal factor belong to the special class that can remove the de Sitter phase.

</details>


### [64] [End-of-the-World Singularities: The Good, the Bad, and the Heated-up](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18133)
*José Calderón-Infante,Gongrui Cheng,Alvaro Herráez,Thomas Van Riet*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper systematically analyzes codimension-one curvature singularities in string theory and their relation to infinite-distance limits in field space. It establishes several refinement criteria for singularity acceptability, reveals connections between temperature and field-space distance for dynamical cobordisms, and proposes a novel geometrized version of Gubser's criterion.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [English Text]

The paper addresses a fundamental tension in string theory regarding how to interpret "End-of-the-World" curvature singularities that appear in dynamical cobordisms—solutions where spacetime terminates at a finite proper distance while scalar fields diverge to infinite distance in moduli space. The motivation stems from the need to develop consistent criteria for distinguishing physically acceptable singularities (that can arise as effective descriptions within valid string theory constructions) from pathological ones that should be excluded from the low-energy effective theory. Previous criteria—Gubser's horizon and potential criteria, and the Maldacena-Nuñez criterion—offer partial guidance but exhibit limitations when applied to string theory realizations like EFT strings and D7-branes.

\n\n
[Chinese Text]

本文探讨弦论中一个基本张力：如何解释出现在动力学边界的"世界末日"曲率奇点——这些解在有限固有距离处时空终止，同时标量场在模空间中发散至无穷远距离。动机源于需要建立一致的标准来区分物理上可接受的奇点（可以作为有效描述出现在有效的弦论构造中）和应当从低能有效理论中排除的病理性奇点。先前标准——Gubser的视界和势能准则，以及Maldacena-Nuñez准则——提供了部分指导，但在应用于弦论实现如EFT弦和D7-膜时表现出局限性。

Method: [English Text]

The methodological approach combines analytical string theory constructions with systematic application and refinement of existing singularity criteria. Key methodological components include: 1) Explicit construction and uplift of moduli-space flows to full ten-dimensional string theory backgrounds to test consistency; 2) Application of Gubser's potential criterion ($\int_{\phi_{UV}}^{\phi_{IR}} \sqrt{V(\phi)} d\phi \geq 0$) and Maldacena-Nuñez criterion to representative string realizations; 3) Analysis of temperature dependence in near-extremal generalizations via reduction of black D$p$-branes to codimension-one flows; 4) Development of a novel geometrized criterion based on Ricci scalar divergence bounds ($|R| \leq C e^{\alpha\Delta\phi}$) inspired by dynamical cobordism physics; 5) Systematic testing of all criteria against benchmark cases including Klebanov-Tseytlin/Klebanov-Strassler solutions, EFT strings, D7-branes, and massive Type IIA strong coupling singularities.

\n\n
[Chinese Text]

方法论方法将解析弦论构造与现有奇点标准的系统应用和改进相结合。关键方法论组成部分包括：1）将模空间流显式构造并提升到全十维弦论背景以测试一致性；2）将Gubser势能准则（$\int_{\phi_{UV}}^{\phi_{IR}} \sqrt{V(\phi)} d\phi \geq 0$）和Maldacena-Nuñez准则应用于代表性弦论实现；3）通过将黑D$p$-膜约化为余维一流来分析近极端推广中的温度依赖性；4）基于受动力学边界物理启发的Ricci标量发散界限（$|R| \leq C e^{\alpha\Delta\phi}$）开发新的几何化准则；5）对所有准则进行系统测试，包括Klebanov-Tseytlin/Klebanov-Strassler解、EFT弦、D7-膜和massive Type IIA强耦合奇点等基准案例。

Result: [English Text]

The paper establishes several key results: 1) Moduli-space flows (with vanishing scalar potential) satisfy Gubser's potential criterion and the ten-dimensional Maldacena-Nuñez criterion, suggesting their singularities should not be discarded. 2) Explicit uplifts confirm these flows embed consistently in full string theory. 3) EFT strings and D7-branes, despite having sensible UV completions, fail Gubser's potential criterion—revealing a limitation. 4) A novel geometrized criterion is proposed: $|R| \leq C e^{\alpha\Delta\phi}$, which captures all examples accepted by Gubser's criterion while also admitting EFT strings and D7-branes. 5) Both criteria reject the massive Type IIA strong coupling singularity. 6) For black D$p$-branes reduced to codimension-one flows that admit near-extremal generalizations, the temperature scales exponentially with field-space distance: $T \sim e^{-\Delta\phi/\sqrt{d-2}}$, suggesting a finite-temperature extension of the Distance Conjecture for dynamical cobordisms.

\n\n
[Chinese Text]

本文建立了几个关键结果：1）模空间流（具有消失标量势）满足Gubser势能准则和十维Maldacena-Nuñez准则，表明其奇点不应被丢弃。2）显式提升证实这些流一致地嵌入全弦论中。3）EFT弦和D7-膜尽管具有合理的紫外补全，但未能通过Gubser势能准则——揭示了一个局限性。4）提出了一个新的几何化准则：$|R| \leq C e^{\alpha\Delta\phi}$，该准则捕捉了Gubser准则接受的所有示例，同时容纳了EFT弦和D7-膜。5）两个准则都拒绝了massive Type IIA强耦合奇点。6）对于约化为余维一流且允许近极端推广的黑D$p$-膜，温度随场空间距离指数标度：$T \sim e^{-\Delta\phi/\sqrt{d-2}}$，暗示了动力学边界的Distance Conjecture的有限温度推广。

Conclusion: [English Text]

The paper concludes that codimension-one singularities driving scalars to infinite field-space distance should not be universally discarded but require refined criteria for physical acceptability. The limitations of existing criteria motivate the proposed geometrized version $|R| \leq C e^{\alpha\Delta\phi}$, which better aligns with string theory expectations while maintaining consistency with accepted solutions. The temperature-distance relation for near-extremal flows provides a concrete realization of the Distance Conjecture in dynamical cobordisms at finite temperature. These results establish a more nuanced framework for evaluating singularities in string compactifications and suggest deep connections between geometric singularities, field-space distances, and thermal physics in quantum gravity.

\n\n
[Chinese Text]

本文得出结论：驱动标量到场空间无穷远距离的余维一奇点不应被普遍丢弃，但需要更精细的标准来判断物理可接受性。现有准则的局限性激发了所提出的几何化版本$|R| \leq C e^{\alpha\Delta\phi}$，该版本更好地与弦论期望一致，同时保持与可接受解的一致性。近极端流的温度-距离关系为有限温度下动力学边界中的Distance Conjecture提供了具体实现。这些结果为评估弦紧化中的奇点建立了更细致的框架，并暗示了几何奇点、场空间距离和量子引力中热物理之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We revisit codimension-one End-of-the-World curvature singularities that drive scalars to infinite distance in field-space and have appeared in the context of dynamical cobordisms. We confront them with Gubser's horizon and potential criteria and with the Maldacena--Nuñez criterion. Moduli-space flows do not admit a near-extremal horizon generalization. Still, they satisfy Gubser's potential criterion and, in representative string realizations, the Maldacena--Nuñez criterion in ten dimensions. Together with an explicit uplift of this type of solution to a consistent string theory background, this suggests that such singularities should not be discarded. For flows with non-trivial scalar potential, we argue that the fate of the singularity is tied to the infinite-distance limit probed near the singularity. The Klebanov--Tseytlin and Klebanov--Strassler solutions illustrate that a modification that obstructs or modifies the field excursion should not be understood as a UV-resolution of the original singularity. We show that EFT strings and D7-branes fail Gubser's potential criterion despite having a sensible UV completion. Motivated by this, and inspired by dynamical cobordisms, we propose a novel criterion that bounds the divergence of the Ricci scalar as the flow explores infinite distance in field-space. Our criterion can be viewed as a geometrization Gubser's one that, while capturing all examples accepted by the latter, also admits EFT strings and D7-branes. Both criteria reject the massive Type IIA strong coupling End-of-the-World singularity. Finally, we analyze black D$p$-branes reduced to codimension one as representatives of flows that admit near-extremal generalizations, and find an exponential relation between temperature and field-space distance. This suggests a finite-temperature extension of the Distance Conjecture for dynamical cobordisms.

### [65] [The Resolved Elliptic Genus and the D1-D5 CFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18138)
*Marcel R. R. Hughes,Masaki Shigemori*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A new supersymmetry index called the resolved elliptic genus (REG) is introduced for the D1-D5 CFT on $T^4$, generalizing the modified elliptic genus (MEG) with a parameter. Using a Schur-Weyl duality based formalism, the symmetric orbifold Hilbert space is decomposed into symmetry sectors, revealing structures invisible to MEG. A superselection rule governs BPS state lifting, allowing REG construction from mixable sectors. REG shows CFT-supergravity agreement below black hole threshold where MEG fails, and above threshold reveals black hole microstate distribution among sectors.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard supersymmetry index for D1-D5 CFT, the modified elliptic genus (MEG), becomes essentially trivial below the black-hole threshold, failing to capture non-BPS states and microstructure. There is a need for a refined index that reveals detailed CFT-supergravity correspondence in regimes where MEG provides no information, and that better organizes black-hole microstates across symmetry sectors.

Method: Develops a new formalism based on Schur-Weyl duality to decompose the symmetric orbifold CFT Hilbert space into symmetry sectors. Examines the action of a supercharge deformed by an exactly marginal operator on the relevant symmetry algebra to propose a superselection rule governing BPS state lifting. Constructs the resolved elliptic genus (REG) by summing only over symmetry sectors that can mix according to this rule, generalizing MEG with an additional parameter.

Result: The REG exhibits detailed agreement between CFT and supergravity below the black-hole threshold—a regime where MEG is essentially trivial. Above the threshold, REG is dominated by black-hole microstates distributed among distinct sectors invisible to MEG. The new formalism provides transparent structure for states contributing to MEG and reveals sector organization of microstates.

Conclusion: The resolved elliptic genus and the Schur-Weyl duality formalism provide powerful new tools for studying D1-D5 CFT and black-hole microstructure. REG reveals previously hidden CFT-supergravity correspondence below threshold and organizes black-hole microstates across symmetry sectors, with potential applications to the fortuity program for understanding black-hole microstates within CFT.

Abstract: This paper is a follow-up to the short paper arXiv:2509.19425, greatly expanding the discussion with examples and providing derivations and justifications of results presented there.
  We introduce a new supersymmetry index for the D1-D5 CFT on $T^4$, which we call the resolved elliptic genus (REG). It is a one-parameter generalisation of the standard supersymmetry index, the modified elliptic genus (MEG), and arises naturally in the free symmetric orbifold description of the theory within a new formalism, based on Schur-Weyl duality, that we develop. In this formalism, the Hilbert space of the symmetric orbifold CFT is decomposed into symmetry sectors in which the structure of the states contributing to the MEG is transparent. By examining the action of the supercharge deformed by an exactly marginal operator on the relevant symmetry algebra, we propose a superselection rule governing the lifting process of BPS states, and use it to construct the REG by summing only over those symmetry sectors that can mix according to this rule. The REG exhibits detailed agreement between the CFT and supergravity below the black-hole threshold, a regime in which the MEG is essentially trivial. Above the threshold, the REG is dominated by black-hole microstates, which are now distributed amongst distinct sectors that are invisible to the MEG. We expect both the new formalism and the REG to provide useful new tools for studying the structure of black-hole microstates. In particular, we comment on their possible relevance to the fortuity program for understanding black-hole microstates within CFT.

### [66] [Moments in the CFT Landscape](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18140)
*Li-Yuan Chiang,David Poland,Gordon Rogelberg*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper introduces a numerical bootstrap approach using moment observables as weighted spectral averages in conformal field theories, enabling rigorous bounds on operator distributions. This method captures corrections to heavy-limit results, reproduces known bootstrap solutions like Ising kinks, and reveals novel continuous kink families in $2<d<6$ connected to operator decoupling phenomena.

本文介绍了一种使用矩可观测量作为共形场论中加权谱平均的数值引导方法，能够对算符分布给出严格界限。该方法捕获重极限结果的修正，复现了已知的引导解（如Ising模型扭结），并揭示了$2<d<6$维度中与算符解耦现象相关的新型连续扭结族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional numerical conformal bootstrap methods face challenges in accessing collective spectral structures and subtle operator distribution features. The heavy correlator regime ($\Delta_\phi \to \infty$) provides analytic power laws but lacks finite-dimensional corrections, while conventional crossing equations may obscure global spectral properties. There's a need for observables that provide coarse-grained probes of the operator spectrum while maintaining rigorous numerical bounds and revealing collective phenomena like operator decoupling.

传统的数值共形引导方法在获取集体谱结构和微妙的算符分布特征方面面临挑战。重关联函数区域（$\Delta_\phi \to \infty$）提供解析幂律但缺乏有限维度修正，而传统的交叉方程可能掩盖全局谱性质。需要能够提供算符谱粗粒化探针同时保持严格数值界限并揭示算符解耦等集体现象的可观测量。

Method: The paper develops a moment bootstrap framework where observables are defined as weighted averages over the operator spectrum: $M_n = \sum_{\mathcal{O}} w_n(\Delta,J) \lambda_{\mathcal{O}}^2$. Here $w_n(\Delta,J)$ are weight functions (moments) and $\lambda_{\mathcal{O}}$ are OPE coefficients. These moments serve as coarse-grained probes of the spectral distribution. The method imposes unitarity and crossing symmetry constraints on these moments using semidefinite programming. The weight functions are chosen to probe different spectral regimes: low-lying moments capture finite corrections to heavy-limit results, while specific moment combinations reveal operator decoupling phenomena.

本文开发了一个矩引导框架，其中可观测量定义为算符谱上的加权平均：$M_n = \sum_{\mathcal{O}} w_n(\Delta,J) \lambda_{\mathcal{O}}^2$。这里$w_n(\Delta,J)$是权重函数（矩），$\lambda_{\mathcal{O}}$是OPE系数。这些矩作为谱分布的粗粒化探针。该方法使用半定规划对矩施加幺正性和交叉对称性约束。权重函数被选择来探测不同的谱区域：低能矩捕获重极限结果的有限修正，而特定的矩组合揭示算符解耦现象。

Result: Key findings include: (1) The moment bounds remain robust in the heavy correlator regime and converge rapidly to analytic power laws. (2) Low-lying moments reproduce known bootstrap features like Ising-model kinks on the boundary of moment space. (3) Most significantly, the moment bootstrap reveals two continuous families of kinks in the lower bounds on moment variables persisting across $2 < d < 6$. These kinks correspond to nontrivial spectral reorganizations connected to operator decoupling phenomena. (4) The approach uncovers bootstrap solutions and collective structures that are difficult to access with traditional numerical bootstrap methods, demonstrating superior sensitivity to spectral distribution features.

关键发现包括：(1) 矩界限在重关联函数区域保持稳健并快速收敛到解析幂律。(2) 低能矩复现了已知的引导特征，如矩空间边界上的Ising模型扭结。(3) 最重要的是，矩引导揭示了矩变量下界中两个连续的扭结族，在$2<d<6$维度持续存在。这些扭结对应于与算符解耦现象相关的非平凡谱重组。(4) 该方法揭示了传统数值引导方法难以获取的引导解和集体结构，展示了对谱分布特征的卓越敏感性。

Conclusion: The moment bootstrap provides a powerful new tool for studying conformal field theories through coarse-grained spectral observables. It bridges the gap between analytic heavy-limit results and finite-dimensional corrections while revealing collective phenomena like operator decoupling through continuous kink families. The framework demonstrates that moment variables can access bootstrap solutions and spectral structures that remain hidden in traditional approaches, opening new avenues for exploring the conformal bootstrap landscape and understanding operator spectrum organization principles.

矩引导通过粗粒化谱可观测量为研究共形场论提供了强大的新工具。它弥合了解析重极限结果与有限维度修正之间的差距，同时通过连续扭结族揭示了算符解耦等集体现象。该框架证明矩变量能够获取传统方法中隐藏的引导解和谱结构，为探索共形引导景观和理解算符谱组织原理开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We develop a novel numerical bootstrap for unitary, crossing-symmetric conformal field theories, focusing on moment observables defined as weighted averages over conformal data. Providing a global and coarse-grained probe of the operator spectrum, this framework yields numerically rigorous bounds on the operator distribution using standard semidefinite programming techniques. In the heavy correlator regime, these bounds remain robust and converge rapidly towards analytically-derived power laws. At finite external dimensions, low-lying moments capture corrections to analytic heavy limit results, while reproducing familiar bootstrap solutions such as Ising-model kinks on the boundary of moment space. Most importantly, the moment bootstrap reveals new features in previously unexplored regions of the bootstrap landscape. The lower bounds on moment variables exhibit two continuous families of kinks persisting across $2 < d < 6$, reflecting nontrivial spectral reorganizations connected to underlying operator decoupling phenomena. These results demonstrate that moment variables uncover bootstrap solutions and collective structures that are difficult to access within traditional numerical approaches.

</details>

[主要结果包括：

2. 源的几何化：三个独立流源对应于$SO(6)_R$中$U(1)^3$的Q-球荷密度，实现为沿$S⁵$角方向的扭曲

Abstract: We study ${\cal N}=4$ super Yang-Mills theory compactified on a circle at zero temperature, with VEVs for two scalar bilinears and three independent current sources. We show that type IIB supergravity provides a complete holographic description of this setup, admitting both supersymmetric and non-supersymmetric AdS soliton solutions, which are asymptotically AdS$_5$ and smooth in the IR. The current sources correspond in (2+1) dimensions to Q-ball charge densities for $U(1)^3\subset SO(6)_R$, and are geometrically realized as twists along three angular directions of the $S^5$. We demonstrate that the bulk dynamics encodes the full vacuum structure of the dual field theory and explicitly reconstruct the supersymmetric moduli space.

### [68] [A superspace approach to AdS$_3$ string theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18142)
*Bob Knighton,Nathan McStay,Vit Sriprachyakul*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop a comprehensive framework for computing correlation functions of long strings in $AdS_3$ supergravity using superspace Polyakov path integral approach. Our construction includes free-field realization of supersymmetric $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ WZW model, spectrally-flowed vertex operators for long string emission, and exact computation of tree-level correlators in near-boundary limit via super Riemann surface moduli space, bypassing picture-changing operators. The results provide explicit evidence for holographic duality and propose a CFT dual for heterotic strings on $AdS_3$.

我们开发了一个全面的框架，使用超空间 Polyakov 路径积分方法来计算 $AdS_3$ 超引力中长弦的相关函数。我们的构造包括超对称 $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ WZW 模型的自由场实现、用于长弦发射的谱流顶点算子，以及通过超黎曼曲面模空间的近边界极限中树层级相关函数的精确计算，绕过了图景改变算子。结果为全息对偶性提供了明确证据，并为 $AdS_3$ 上的异质弦提出了 CFT 对偶。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the precise holographic dictionary between string theory on $AdS_3$ and two-dimensional conformal field theories remains incomplete, particularly for heterotic strings. The standard picture-changing operator (PCO) procedure for computing string amplitudes in superspace introduces ambiguities and complicates the relationship with boundary CFT correlators. A more direct approach that maintains manifest worldsheet supersymmetry throughout the calculation could provide cleaner connections to the dual CFT, potentially revealing the precise operator dictionary for both type II and heterotic superstrings in $AdS_3$.

理解 $AdS_3$ 上弦理论与二维共形场论之间的精确全息字典仍然不完整，特别是对于异质弦。在超空间中计算弦振幅的标准图景改变算子（PCO）程序引入了模糊性，并使与边界 CFT 相关函数的关系复杂化。一种在整个计算过程中保持明显世界面超对称性的更直接方法可以提供与对偶 CFT 更清晰的连接，可能揭示 $AdS_3$ 中 II 型和异质超弦的精确算子字典。

Method: 1. Constructed a free-field realization of the supersymmetric $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ WZW model that preserves manifest worldsheet supersymmetry, avoiding constraints from Wakimoto free fields.
2. Developed spectrally-flowed vertex operators describing emission of long strings from the bulk, utilizing spectral flow automorphism of the affine $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ algebra.
3. Direct computation on the moduli space of super Riemann surfaces using superspace Polyakov path integral, implementing exact integration over supermoduli without resorting to picture-changing operators.
4. Focused on the `near-boundary' limit where string worldsheets approach the $AdS_3$ boundary, enabling controlled approximations.
5. Applied this framework to both type II and heterotic superstring theories on $AdS_3$.

1. 构建了超对称 $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ WZW 模型的自由场实现，保持明显世界面超对称性，避免了 Wakimoto 自由场的约束。
2. 开发了描述从体发射长弦的谱流顶点算子，利用仿射 $SL(2,\mathbb{R})$ 代数的谱流自同构。
3. 使用超空间 Polyakov 路径积分在超黎曼曲面模空间上进行直接计算，实现对超模的精确积分而无需借助图景改变算子。
4. 专注于弦世界面接近 $AdS_3$ 边界的"近边界"极限，实现可控近似。
5. 将此框架应用于 $AdS_3$ 上的 II 型和异质超弦理论。

Result: 1. Exact tree-level correlation functions of long strings computed in the near-boundary limit for both type II and heterotic superstrings on $AdS_3$.
2. Demonstrated schematic reproduction of boundary CFT correlation functions from the bulk string amplitudes, establishing concrete holographic correspondence.
3. Provided a novel proposal for the CFT dual to heterotic superstrings on $AdS_3$, extending previous results for type II strings.
4. Showed that the free-field realization enables exact computations while maintaining manifest supersymmetry, circumventing technical complications of the PCO approach.
5. The spectral flow vertex operators correctly capture the long string sector and its connection to boundary operators.

1. 在近边界极限下，为 $AdS_3$ 上的 II 型和异质超弦计算了精确的树层级长弦相关函数。
2. 从体弦振幅展示了边界 CFT 相关函数的示意性再现，建立了具体的全息对应关系。
3. 为 $AdS_3$ 上的异质超弦提出了新的 CFT 对偶建议，扩展了先前对 II 型弦的结果。
4. 展示了自由场实现在保持明显超对称性的同时实现精确计算，绕过了 PCO 方法的技术复杂性。
5. 谱流顶点算子正确捕捉了长弦扇区及其与边界算子的连接。

Conclusion: The superspace Polyakov path integral approach provides a powerful framework for computing string amplitudes on $AdS_3$ that maintains manifest worldsheet supersymmetry throughout. By constructing free-field realizations and spectrally-flowed vertex operators, we obtain exact tree-level correlators without the ambiguities of picture-changing operators. These results strongly support the holographic duality between string theory on $AdS_3$ and two-dimensional CFTs, and specifically propose a concrete boundary CFT dual for heterotic strings. The methodology opens new avenues for computing higher-genus amplitudes and investigating non-perturbative aspects of the $AdS_3$/CFT$_2$ correspondence.

超空间 Polyakov 路径积分方法提供了一个强大的框架，用于计算 $AdS_3$ 上的弦振幅，在整个过程中保持明显世界面超对称性。通过构建自由场实现和谱流顶点算子，我们获得了精确的树层级相关函数，没有图景改变算子的模糊性。这些结果有力地支持了 $AdS_3$ 上弦理论与二维 CFT 之间的全息对偶性，并特别为异质弦提出了具体的边界 CFT 对偶。该方法为计算更高亏格振幅和研究 $AdS_3$/CFT$_2$ 对应的非微扰方面开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We carefully examine the Polyakov path integral for strings on $\text{AdS}_3$ in superspace, both for type II and heterotic superstrings. We construct a free-field realization of the supersymmetric $\text{SL}(2,\mathbb{R})$ WZW model which manifestly preserves worldsheet supersymmetry and use this free-field realization to construct spectrally-flowed vertex operators describing the emission of long strings in the bulk. By working directly with the moduli space of super Riemann surfaces, we exactly compute tree-level correlation functions of long strings in the `near-boundary' limit without resorting to the standard picture-changing-operator (PCO) procedure. Finally, we argue how these correlators schematically reproduce correlation functions of the conjectured boundary CFTs, and as a result provide a novel proposal for the CFT dual for heterotic superstrings in $\text{AdS}_3$.

### [69] [Branching Universes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18147)
*Anamaria Hell,Tatsuya Daniel*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We propose a novel cosmological framework where our Universe emerges as one branch among multiple possible realizations, testable via modified gravitational wave dispersion relations. The theory employs spatially constrained vector fields that generate non-standard tensor perturbations while avoiding new propagating degrees of freedom, admits stealth black hole solutions, and passes solar system constraints.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper aims to develop a cosmological theory where our Universe represents a specific realization among multiple possible branches—a concept extending beyond standard single-universe cosmology. This requires novel theoretical frameworks that can be observationally tested, particularly through gravitational wave signatures. The modified dispersion relation of gravitational waves provides a unique observational window into such multi-branch scenarios. The authors seek to construct a mathematically consistent theory that modifies gravity at cosmological scales while preserving successful predictions at solar system scales.

Method: The authors develop a framework based on spatially constrained vector fields—vector fields subject to specific spatial constraints that modify gravitational dynamics. They analyze the theory in both flat and cosmological spacetimes, demonstrating through detailed perturbation analysis that no new propagating degrees of freedom emerge. They derive the modified equations for tensor perturbations, showing how these differ from general relativity. The framework is further tested by finding stealth black hole solutions (black holes that are invisible in certain channels while modifying gravity in others) and by calculating weak gravitational potentials to verify compatibility with solar system experiments. The approach involves careful construction of the action principle, Hamiltonian analysis to count degrees of freedom, and solving field equations under appropriate boundary conditions.

Result: The theory successfully generates modified tensor perturbations without introducing new propagating modes in both flat and cosmological backgrounds. Key results include: 1) A modified dispersion relation for gravitational waves that provides observational signatures distinct from general relativity; 2) Existence of stealth black hole solutions where the metric satisfies vacuum Einstein equations but vector fields have non-trivial configurations; 3) Weak gravitational potentials that match Newtonian predictions in the solar system regime, ensuring compatibility with precision tests; 4) Theoretical consistency demonstrated through Hamiltonian analysis confirming the absence of additional dynamical degrees of freedom. The modified dispersion relation represents a smoking-gun signal that could distinguish this multi-branch cosmological scenario from standard cosmology.

Conclusion: The proposed framework provides a mathematically consistent realization of multi-branch cosmology where our Universe is one possible realization among others. The theory modifies gravitational wave propagation while maintaining compatibility with local gravity tests, offering a testable alternative to standard cosmology. The spatially constrained vector fields create distinctive observational signatures without introducing problematic ghost or instability issues. The existence of stealth black hole solutions and solar system compatibility strengthens the theory's viability. This work opens avenues for exploring generalized multi-branch scenarios and their implications for cosmic inflation, dark energy, and quantum gravity foundations.

Abstract: We propose the idea that our Universe is a realization among different possible branches, which can be observationally tested through the modified dispersion relation of the gravitational waves. We achieve this through a framework of spatially constrained vector fields. We show that the simplest realizations of such theories in flat and cosmological spacetimes do not introduce new propagating modes, but they give rise to tensor perturbations that differ from those of standard general relativity. We further show that such theories admit stealth black hole solutions, and we recover weak gravitational potentials, thus passing the solar system experiments. Finally, we discuss the implications of such theories and propose further generalizations.

### [70] [A menagerie of Schwarzians: coadjoint orbits of Virasoro and near-dS$_2$ quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18154)
*Henry Maxfield*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper presents a complete classification of generalized Schwarzian theories as integrals over Virasoro coadjoint orbits, connecting them to constant positive curvature Lorentzian geometries and near-dS$_2$ gravity. Novel Lorentzian theories with oscillatory path integrals and varying coupling functions are solved exactly via fermionic localization, revealing boundary condition ambiguities from non-self-adjoint fluctuation operators.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The original Schwarzian theory describes universal low-energy dynamics of near-extremal black holes and the SYK model, but exists as only one special case within a broader mathematical framework. The motivation is to systematically classify all possible generalized Schwarzian theories arising from Virasoro coadjoint orbits, understand their connection to two-dimensional gravity, and explore novel Lorentzian theories with qualitatively different features that could have physical implications.

Method: The method employs mathematical classification of Virasoro coadjoint orbits, which correspond to moduli spaces of constant positive curvature two-dimensional Lorentzian geometries. The generalized Schwarzian theories are defined as path integrals over these orbits. The analysis involves: 1) Identifying boundary condition ambiguities from non-essential self-adjointness of quadratic fluctuation operators, 2) Justifying choices through realization in Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity which regulates singularities, 3) Using fermionic localization beyond the Duistermaat-Heckman theorem to maintain one-loop exactness, 4) Computing path integrals exactly for all theories and couplings.

Result: The main results include: 1) Complete classification of generalized Schwarzian theories via Virasoro coadjoint orbits, 2) Identification of novel Lorentzian theories with oscillatory path integrals weighted by $e^{iI}$ and varying coupling functions (renormalized dilaton), 3) Discovery that the quadratic fluctuation operator fails to be essentially self-adjoint, requiring choice of boundary conditions and allowance of certain singularities, 4) Exact computation of path integrals for all theories and couplings using fermionic localization, 5) New results for the original Schwarzian theory as special cases, 6) Connection to wavefunctions in asymptotically near-dS$_2$ gravity, particularly JT gravity.

Conclusion: The work establishes a comprehensive framework for Schwarzian theories as integrals over Virasoro coadjoint orbits, revealing rich mathematical structure and physical implications. The classification connects to moduli spaces of constant curvature Lorentzian geometries and near-dS$_2$ gravity. The discovery of boundary condition ambiguities from non-self-adjoint operators provides new insight into quantization of such systems. The exact solvability via fermionic localization offers powerful computational tools for exploring these theories, with potential applications to quantum gravity, holography, and low-dimensional field theories.

Abstract: The Schwarzian theory, which governs the universal low-energy dynamics of near-extremal black holes and the SYK model, can be characterised as an integral over a particular coadjoint orbit of the Virasoro group. We describe and solve a complete classification of all possible generalised Schwarzian theories, defined by integrals over any Virasoro coadjoint orbit, including new classes of theories with qualitatively novel features. The classification of coadjoint orbits coincides with the moduli space of constant positive curvature two-dimensional Lorentzian geometries, and the associated Schwarzian theories govern associated wavefunctions in asymptotically near-dS$_2$ gravity (Jackiw-Teitelboim gravity in particular). The novel theories are inherently Lorentzian, defined by oscillatory path integrals weighted by $e^{iI}$ and force consideration of varying `coupling functions' (renormalised dilaton) which may not have definite sign. The definition of the theories involves an ambiguity, arising because the operator describing quadratic fluctuations at one loop fails to be essentially self-adjoint. This requires a choice of boundary condition, and also forces us to allow certain singularities in configurations and classical solutions. The choice is justified from the realisation in JT gravity, which naturally regulates these singularities. The path integral remains one-loop exact via fermionic localisation, but this requires additional input beyond the Duistermaat-Heckman theorem. This allows an exact computation of the path integral for all theories and all couplings, including new results for the original Schwarzian theory.

### [71] [New $F^4$ invariants in five-dimensional supergravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18180)
*Yide Cai,Sabarenath Jayaprakash,James T. Liu,Yi Pang,Robert J. Saskowski*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper systematically classifies and constructs four-derivative superinvariants in five-dimensional $\\mathcal N=2$ supergravity coupled to vector multiplets, revealing the existence of novel vector superinvariants beyond the known gravitational ones, and demonstrates their non-renormalization properties for BPS black holes.

本文系统分类并构造了五维 $\\mathcal N=2$ 超引力与矢量多重态耦合的四导数超不变式，揭示了超越已知引力不变式的新型矢量超不变式，并证明了它们对BPS黑洞的非重整化特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Higher-derivative corrections to supergravity theories are crucial for understanding quantum corrections, black hole thermodynamics, and string theory compactifications. While the four-derivative invariants for pure $\\mathcal N=2$, $D=5$ supergravity are well-known (a single invariant), the structure for theories coupled to vector multiplets remains unexplored. Specifically, one needs to understand: (1) how many independent four-derivative superinvariants exist for $n_v=1,2$ vector multiplets, (2) whether there exist pure vector invariants (supersymmetrizations of $F^4$ terms) that don't involve curvatures, and (3) how these affect BPS black hole solutions.

超引力理论的高阶导数修正确保了理解量子修正、黑洞热力学和字符串理论紧致化至关重要。虽然纯 $\\mathcal N=2$，$D=5$ 超引力的四导数不变式（单个不变式）是已知的，但与矢量多重态耦合的理论的结构仍未被探索。具体来说，需要理解：(1) 对于 $n_v=1,2$ 矢量多重态，存在多少个独立的四导数超不变式，(2) 是否存在纯矢量不变式（$F^4$ 项的超对称化）不涉及曲率，(3) 这些如何影响BPS黑洞解。

Method: The authors employ two complementary approaches: (1) Superconformal tensor calculus to systematically construct all possible four-derivative invariants by coupling to the Weyl multiplet and imposing constraints, and (2) Dimensional reduction from six-dimensional $(2,0)$ supergravity to obtain invariants via reduction and field redefinitions. They analyze the minimal case ($n_v=0$), then extend to $n_v=1$ and $n_v=2$ (the STU model), identifying independent invariants after removing redundancies through field redefinitions. They further examine the rigid limit to $\\mathcal N=2$ super-Yang-Mills to conjecture a family of invariants for arbitrary $n_v$.

作者采用了两种互补的方法：(1) 超共形张量微积分：通过耦合到Weyl多重态并施加约束，系统构造所有可能的四导数不变式；(2) 从六维 $(2,0)$ 超引力进行维度约化：通过约化和场重定义获得不变式。他们分析了最小情况（$n_v=0$），然后扩展到 $n_v=1$ 和 $n_v=2$（STU模型），通过场重定义去除冗余后识别独立不变式。他们进一步检查了到 $\\mathcal N=2$ 超杨-米尔斯理论的刚性极限，以推测任意 $n_v$ 的不变式族。

Result: For $n_v=1$: three independent superinvariants after field redefinitions, including one pure vector invariant (supersymmetrization of $F^4$) without curvature couplings. For $n_v=2$ (STU model): three gravitational superinvariants and two $F^4$-type vector superinvariants. The vector superinvariants do not affect two- and three-charge static BPS black hole solutions, suggesting non-renormalization properties. Based on the rigid limit, they conjecture a family of vector superinvariants for arbitrary $n_v$ parameterized by symmetric tensors $C_{IJKL}$.

对于 $n_v=1$：场重定义后有三个独立的超不变式，包括一个纯矢量不变式（$F^4$ 的超对称化）没有曲率耦合。对于 $n_v=2$（STU模型）：有三个引力超不变式和两个 $F^4$ 型矢量超不变式。矢量超不变式不影响两电荷和三电荷静态BPS黑洞解，暗示了非重整化特性。基于刚性极限，他们推测了由对称张量 $C_{IJKL}$ 参数化的任意 $n_v$ 的矢量超不变式族。

Conclusion: The paper provides the complete classification of four-derivative superinvariants in five-dimensional $\\mathcal N=2$ supergravity coupled to $n_v\\le 2$ vector multiplets, revealing a richer structure than previously known. The discovery of pure vector invariants ($F^4$ type) that don't affect BPS black holes has important implications for black hole entropy calculations and suggests possible non-renormalization theorems. The conjectured family for arbitrary $n_v$ provides a framework for future investigations of higher-derivative corrections in these theories.

本文提供了五维 $\\mathcal N=2$ 超引力与 $n_v\\le 2$ 矢量多重态耦合的四导数超不变式的完整分类，揭示了比先前已知更丰富的结构。纯矢量不变式（$F^4$ 型）不影响BPS黑洞的发现对黑洞熵计算有重要影响，并暗示了可能的非重整化定理。对于任意 $n_v$ 的推测族为未来在这些理论中研究高阶导数修正提供了框架。

Abstract: We consider four-derivative superinvariants of five-dimensional $\mathcal N=2$ supergravity coupled to $n_v\le 2$ vector multiplets, which we obtain from both the superconformal tensor calculus approach and dimensional reduction. For the minimal case, with no vector multiplets, it is known that there is a unique four-derivative superinvariant. However, for the case of one vector multiplet, after field redefinitions, we find that there are three independent superinvariants, one of which is a vector superinvariant that does not contain any curvatures and takes the form of a supersymmetrization of $F^4$. Similarly, for the two vector multiplet case, corresponding to the STU model, we find three gravitational superinvariants and two $F^4$-type vector superinvariants. Moreover, we find that these vector superinvariants do not affect the two- and three-charge static BPS black hole solutions. We further consider the rigid limit to $\mathcal N=2$ super-Yang-Mills and use this to conjecture a family of vector superinvariants for five-dimensional $\mathcal N=2$ supergravity coupled to an arbitrary number of vector multiplets.

</details>


### [72] [Quantum orientation entanglement analysis of the interpolating helicity states between the instant form dynamics and the light-front dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18208)
*Deepasika Dayananda,Chueng-Ryong Ji*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper introduces a novel theoretical framework for analyzing quantum orientation entanglement in relativistic helicity states, interpolating between Jacob-Wick and light-front helicities. It develops an expansion method for interpolating helicity states in terms of Jacob-Wick basis, showing the probabilistic coefficients follow Wigner d-matrix structure. The formalism is applied to vector boson pair production via scalar annihilation, identifying critical interpolation angles separating instant-form and light-front dynamics regimes.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The interplay between quantum orientation entanglement and Wigner rotation is fundamental for understanding spin angular momentum dynamics in relativistic quantum systems. There exists a theoretical gap in systematically analyzing helicity states that interpolate between Jacob-Wick helicity (canonical in instant-form dynamics) and light-front helicity (natural in light-front dynamics). A comprehensive framework is needed to quantify the quantum orientation entanglement manifested in angular distributions of scattering amplitudes for these interpolating states.

Method: The authors develop a novel expansion method for interpolating helicity states in terms of Jacob-Wick helicity basis. Key mathematical tools include: 1) Parameterizing the interpolation angle $\theta$ between momentum direction and spin orientation; 2) Expressing interpolating states as $\sum_{\lambda} d^{j}_{\lambda'\lambda}(\theta) |p,\lambda\rangle_{JW}$ where $d^{j}_{\lambda'\lambda}$ are Wigner d-matrix elements; 3) Analyzing quantum orientation entanglement through angular distributions of interpolating scattering helicity amplitudes; 4) Computing vector boson pair production amplitudes via scalar annihilation contact interaction: $M_{\lambda_1\lambda_2} = \langle p_1,\lambda_1; p_2,\lambda_2| \mathcal{L}_{\text{contact}} |q_1,q_2\rangle$.

Result: 1) The interpolating helicity states expansion yields probabilistic coefficients following Wigner d-matrix structure, providing a natural interpretation of quantum orientation entanglement; 2) The interpolating helicity amplitudes for vector boson pair production ($\phi\phi \to VV$) exhibit characteristic angular dependence; 3) A critical interpolation angle $\theta_c$ is identified that bifurcates dynamical branches: for $\theta < \theta_c$, behavior resembles instant-form dynamics (Jacob-Wick dominated), while for $\theta > \theta_c$, behavior transitions to light-front dynamics regime; 4) The quantum orientation entanglement manifests as specific interference patterns in angular distributions, with maximal entanglement occurring at the critical angle $\theta_c$; 5) The framework reveals how Wigner rotation governs the transformation between different helicity bases.

Conclusion: The paper establishes a systematic theoretical framework connecting quantum orientation entanglement, Wigner rotation, and interpolating helicity states. The identification of critical interpolation angle $\theta_c$ provides a precise boundary between instant-form and light-front dynamical regimes. The Wigner d-matrix structure in the expansion coefficients offers deep insight into entanglement properties of relativistic spin systems. This work bridges formal aspects of relativistic quantum mechanics with practical calculations in scattering theory, with implications for high-energy physics phenomenology and quantum information theory in relativistic settings.

Abstract: The interplay between quantum orientation entanglement and Wigner rotation plays a fundamental role in understanding the behavior of spin angular momentum in quantum states. To analyze the quantum orientation entanglement of the relativistic helicity states interpolating between the Jacob-Wick helicity and the light-front helicity, we examine the relative angle between the particle's momentum direction and the spin orientation for the interpolating helicity states. For this analysis, we introduce a novel method for expanding the interpolating helicity states in terms of the Jacob-Wick helicity. The corresponding probabilistic coefficients follow the structure of the Wigner d-matrix elements, which we use for the interpretation of the quantum orientation entanglement manifested in the angular distributions of the interpolating scattering helicity amplitudes. As an explicit demonstration, we compute the interpolating helicity amplitudes for the pair production of spin-1 (vector) particles in the annihilation of two spin-0 (scalar) particles, focusing primarily on their contact interaction. In particular, we identify the critical interpolation angle that bifurcates the dynamical branches between the instant-form dynamics and the light-front dynamics and discuss the underlying orientation entanglement in the interpolating helicity amplitudes.
