### [73] [Type IIB Supergravity Action and Holography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18248)
*Soumya Adhikari,Junho Hong,Chanyoung Joung,Geum Lee*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: [The paper proposes a generalized topological term in the Type IIB supergravity action that ensures a non-vanishing on-shell value for direct holographic comparison of free energies. This resolves the longstanding issue where the conventional pseudo-action vanishes on $AdS_5\times S^5$ backgrounds, and is extended to broader classes including AdS geometries with non-trivial 2-form potentials, validating the approach on solutions like Lunin-Maldacena backgrounds and $AdS_4$ $S$-folds.]

\n\n
[该论文在Type IIB超引力作用量中提出了一个广义的拓扑项，确保了直接全息比较自由能时的非零在线值。这解决了长期以来常规伪作用量在$AdS_5\times S^5$背景上消失的问题，并将其扩展到包括具有非平凡2-形式势的AdS几何在内的更广泛类别，在Lunin-Maldacena背景和$AdS_4$ $S$-folds等解上验证了该方法。]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [In holography, the free energy of CFT$_4$ from $\mathcal{N}=4$ SU$(N)$ SYM is typically computed via the on-shell action of five-dimensional gauged supergravity, not directly from the ten-dimensional Type IIB supergravity. This indirect approach stems from a fundamental issue: the conventional Type IIB pseudo-action vanishes identically when evaluated on the $AdS_5\times S^5$ vacuum, preventing a first-principles holographic comparison. While a recent proposal by Kurlyand and Tseytlin resolved this for a restricted class of backgrounds using the Pasti-Sorokin-Tonin (PST) formulation, there remained a need to extend this solution to more general Type IIB backgrounds including those with non-zero 2-form potentials and different dimensional AdS factors, to establish a robust ten-dimensional framework for direct holographic computations.]

\n\n
[在全息对偶中，CFT$_4$的自由能来自$\mathcal{N}=4$ SU$(N)$ SYM，通常通过五维规范超引力的在线作用量计算，而非直接从十维Type IIB超引力计算。这种间接方法源于一个基本问题：传统Type IIB伪作用量在$AdS_5\times S^5$真空上求值时恒为零，阻碍了第一性原理的全息比较。虽然Kurlyand和Tseytlin最近使用Pasti-Sorokin-Tonin (PST)公式为一类受限背景解决了此问题，但仍需要将此解决方案扩展到更一般的Type IIB背景，包括具有非零2-形式势和不同维度AdS因子的背景，从而建立用于直接全息计算的稳健十维框架。]

Method: [The authors extend the Kurlyand-Tseytlin proposal by introducing a generalized topological correction to the Type IIB supergravity action under milder conditions than the original PST formulation. The correction is designed to yield a non-vanishing on-shell action while preserving the equations of motion. The key mathematical innovation is a systematic construction of this topological term that accommodates: (1) generic AdS$_d$ × $M_{10-d}$ geometries beyond $AdS_5\times S^5$; (2) non-vanishing 2-form potentials (the self-dual 5-form flux remains non-zero as usual). The approach employs differential form language and careful treatment of the self-duality constraint. The method is then applied to compute the on-shell action for specific non-trivial backgrounds: the Lunin-Maldacena $\beta$-deformed background and the $AdS_4$ $S$-fold solution, comparing results with the corresponding lower-dimensional gauged supergravity computations.]

\n\n
[作者通过引入对Type IIB超引力作用量的广义拓扑修正，扩展了Kurlyand-Tseytlin的提议，该修正比原始PST公式的条件更宽松。该修正旨在产生非零的在线作用量，同时保持运动方程。关键的数学创新是该拓扑项的系统构造，其适用于：(1) 超越$AdS_5\times S^5$的通用AdS$_d$ × $M_{10-d}$几何；(2) 非零的2-形式势（自对偶5-形式通量如通常保持非零）。该方法采用微分形式语言并谨慎处理自对偶约束。随后将该方法应用于计算特定非平凡背景的在线作用量：Lunin-Maldacena $\beta$-变形背景和$AdS_4$ $S$-fold解，并将结果与相应的低维规范超引力计算进行比较。]

Result: [The generalized topological correction successfully yields a finite, non-zero on-shell action for the targeted backgrounds, matching the free energy computed from the corresponding lower-dimensional gauged supergravity. Specifically: (1) For the $AdS_5\times S^5$ vacuum, the corrected ten-dimensional action reproduces the known result $F \propto N^2$. (2) For the Lunin-Maldacena $\beta$-deformed background, the computed on-shell action agrees with the five-dimensional gauged supergravity result, confirming the holographic free energy of the $\beta$-deformed $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM. (3) For the $AdS_4$ $S$-fold solution, the ten-dimensional on-shell action matches that obtained from four-dimensional gauged supergravity, validating the holographic dictionary for these non-conformal backgrounds. The correction is shown to be essential; without it, the on-shell action would vanish or be ill-defined.]

\n\n
[广义拓扑修正成功为目标背景产生了有限、非零的在线作用量，与从相应低维规范超引力计算的自由能相匹配。具体而言：(1) 对于$AdS_5\times S^5$真空，修正后的十维作用量重现了已知结果$F \propto N^2$。(2) 对于Lunin-Maldacena $\beta$-变形背景，计算的在线作用量与五维规范超引力结果一致，确认了$\beta$-变形$\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM的全息自由能。(3) 对于$AdS_4$ $S$-fold解，十维在线作用量与四维规范超引力获得的结果匹配，验证了这些非共形背景的全息字典。该修正被证明是必要的；若无此修正，在线作用量将消失或无定义。]

Conclusion: [The work establishes a robust ten-dimensional framework for direct holographic computation of free energies by generalizing the topological term required for consistent evaluation of the Type IIB on-shell action. This resolves the longstanding puzzle of the vanishing pseudo-action and extends the applicability to a wide class of backgrounds including AdS geometries of various dimensions and those with non-vanishing 2-form potentials. The successful matching with lower-dimensional gauged supergravity results for both conformal and non-conformal cases validates the approach and solidifies the foundation for first-principles holographic comparisons entirely within the ten-dimensional Type IIB supergravity. The proposed topological correction should be incorporated as a standard component of the Type IIB action for holographic applications.]

\n\n
[该工作通过推广Type IIB在线作用量一致求值所需的拓扑项，建立了用于直接全息计算自由能的稳健十维框架。这解决了长期存在的伪作用量消失之谜，并将适用性扩展到包括各种维度的AdS几何和具有非零2-形式势的背景在内的广泛类别。对于共形和非共形情况，与低维规范超引力结果的成功匹配验证了该方法，并巩固了完全在十维Type IIB超引力内进行第一性原理全息比较的基础。所提出的拓扑修正应作为Type IIB作用量的标准组成部分，用于全息应用。]

Abstract: In the prototypical AdS$_5$/CFT$_4$ correspondence, the free energy of $\mathcal{N}=4$ SU$(N)$ super Yang-Mills theory is commonly reproduced from the Euclidean on-shell action of five-dimensional gauged supergravity -- a consistent truncation of Type IIB supergravity -- rather than computed directly in ten dimensions. A longstanding obstacle to the latter is that the conventional Type IIB pseudo-action evaluated on the $AdS_5\times S^5$ background vanishes identically, apparently precluding a first-principles holographic comparison. A recent proposal by Kurlyand and Tseytlin, based on the Pasti-Sorokin-Tonin formulation, resolves this issue for a special class of backgrounds including the $AdS_5\times S^5$ vacuum by introducing a topological term required for consistency, yielding a non-vanishing on-shell value in agreement with holography. In this work we extend this refinement to a broader class of Type IIB backgrounds by introducing a generalized topological correction under milder conditions, encompassing AdS geometries of generic dimension and non-vanishing 2-form potentials. We test the proposal on non-trivial solutions such as the Lunin-Maldacena background and the $AdS_4$ $S$-fold solution, and find agreement with the corresponding lower-dimensional gauged supergravity on-shell actions and thereby with the expected holographic observables. Our results place direct holographic comparisons within the ten-dimensional Type IIB framework on firmer ground.

### [74] [Multifield dark energy: Interplay between curved field space and curved spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18341)
*Diego Gallego,J. Bayron Orjuela-Quintana*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: [This paper presents a comprehensive analysis of two-field exponential quintessence models with curved field space in spatially curved FLRW universes. Combining dynamical systems methods with numerical integration and observational constraints, the study shows that mechanisms enabling acceleration on steep potentials are restricted to distinct invariant manifolds and cannot operate simultaneously in the presence of background fluids. The analysis reveals degeneracies between curvature and scalar dynamics, leading to effectively single-field evolution in the observationally viable regime, with a constraint λ≲0.75 on the potential slope from cosmological data.]

While single-field models with exponential potentials require very flat slopes (λ < √2) for cosmic acceleration, multifield configurations with non-geodesic motion might permit acceleration on steeper potentials. Additionally, spatial curvature introduces new dynamical possibilities that could potentially soften acceleration requirements. However, the interplay between curved field space, spatial curvature, and background fluids in a fully cosmological context remains poorly understood, particularly whether these mechanisms can operate simultaneously to enable acceleration on steep potentials while maintaining observational viability.]

\n\n
[在string紧致化中自然出现的指数势quintessence模型通常涉及在弯曲场空间上演化的伸缩子场和轴子场。虽然具有指数势的单场模型需要非常平坦的斜率(λ < √2)才能产生宇宙加速，但具有非测地线运动的多场构型可能允许在更陡峭的势上产生加速。此外，空间曲率引入了新的动力学可能性，可能软化加速要求。然而，弯曲场空间、空间曲率和背景流体在完整宇宙学背景下的相互作用仍知之甚少，特别是这些机制能否同时运作以在陡峭势上实现加速同时保持观测可行性。]

Method: [The analysis employs a comprehensive dynamical systems approach for the minimal two-field exponential system in curved FLRW background with radiation and matter components. The methodology includes: (1) Full dynamical systems classification of fixed points and invariant manifolds in the phase space, identifying scaling solutions, curvature-dominated equilibria, and accelerated expansion regions; (2) Analytical approximations for trajectories in different asymptotic regimes; (3) Numerical integration of the full coupled equations including scalar fields, spatial curvature, and cosmological fluids; (4) Confrontation with current cosmological background data using Planck 2018 distance priors, Pantheon+ supernovae, BAO measurements, and cosmic chronometers to constrain model parameters via Bayesian inference.]

\n\n
[该分析采用综合的动力系统方法研究具有辐射和物质组分的弯曲FLRW背景下的最小两场指数系统。方法包括：(1) 对相空间中的不动点和不变流形进行完整的动力系统分类，识别标度解、曲率主导平衡和加速膨胀区域；(2) 不同渐近机制中轨迹的解析近似；(3) 包含标量场、空间曲率和宇宙学流体的完整耦合方程数值积分；(4) 使用Planck 2018距离先验、Pantheon+超新星、BAO测量和宇宙计时器数据与当前宇宙学背景数据对比，通过贝叶斯推断约束模型参数。]

Result: [Key findings include: (1) In the scalar-dominated limit, non-geodesic trajectories can sustain accelerated expansion on steep potentials, but these exist only in invariant manifolds that exclude background fluids; (2) A scaling-curvature fixed point can soften acceleration requirements in curved universes, but this also belongs to a distinct invariant manifold; (3) No non-geodesic scaling fixed point exists within an open region of parameter space when background fluids are included—the two mechanisms cannot be simultaneously realized; (4) In the observationally viable thawing regime, the axion does not track the background fluid and spatial curvature becomes dynamically subdominant, leading to effectively single-field evolution; (5) A degeneracy exists between curvature effects and scalar-field dynamics that limits their independent impact on late-time cosmology; (6) From current cosmological data, the potential slope is constrained to λ≲0.75 at 95% CL, similar to the single-field bound λ<√2≈1.41.]

\n\n
[关键发现包括：(1) 在标量主导极限下，非测地线轨迹能够在陡峭势上维持加速膨胀，但这些仅存在于排除背景流体的不变流形中；(2) 在弯曲宇宙中，标度-曲率不动点可以软化加速要求，但这同样属于不同的不变流形；(3) 当包含背景流体时，在参数空间的开放区域内不存在非测地线标度不动点——两种机制无法同时实现；(4) 在观测可行的解冻机制中，轴子不追踪背景流体，空间曲率变得动态亚主导，导致实质上单场演化；(5) 曲率效应与标量场动力学之间存在简并性，限制了它们对晚期宇宙学的独立影响；(6) 从当前宇宙学数据得到势斜率约束为λ≲0.75(95%置信水平)，与单场界限λ<√2≈1.41相似。]

Conclusion: [Even in the minimal multifield setup with spatial curvature, sustained late-time acceleration requires a sufficiently flat potential, with observational constraints giving λ≲0.75. The theoretical mechanisms that could in principle allow acceleration on steeper potentials—non-geodesic motion in curved field space and curvature-assisted scaling solutions—are restricted to distinct invariant manifolds and cannot operate simultaneously in the presence of background fluids. This forces the system into an effectively single-field thawing regime where the axion becomes dynamically irrelevant and curvature is subdominant. Consequently, the tension between cosmic acceleration and quantum gravity expectations for steep potentials (λ≳1 in string compactifications) persists within this framework, suggesting that more sophisticated multifield constructions or additional dynamical ingredients may be needed to reconcile steep potentials with observational cosmology.]

\n\n
[即使在包含空间曲率的最小多场设置中，持续的晚期加速仍需要足够平坦的势，观测约束给出λ≲0.75。理论上可能允许在陡峭势上加速的机制——弯曲场空间中的非测地线运动和曲率辅助标度解——被限制在不同的不变流形中，并且在背景流体存在时无法同时运作。这迫使系统进入实质上的单场解冻机制，其中轴子变得动态无关且曲率亚主导。因此，宇宙加速与量子引力对陡峭势的期望(在string紧致化中λ≳1)之间的张力在此框架内仍然存在，表明可能需要更复杂的多场构造或额外的动力学成分来调和陡峭势与观测宇宙学。]

Abstract: Exponential quintessence models motivated by string compactifications naturally involve both a dilatonic scalar and its axionic partner evolving on a curved field space, while spatial curvature enlarges the cosmological phase space and may affect late-time dynamics. We perform a systematic analysis of the minimal two-field exponential system in a curved FLRW background including radiation and matter components, combining a complete dynamical systems classification with analytical approximations and numerical integration. In the scalar-dominated limit, non-geodesic trajectories can sustain accelerated expansion on steep potentials, and in curved universes a scaling-curvature fixed point can in principle soften the requirements for acceleration. However, we show that these mechanisms arise in distinct invariant manifolds and cannot be simultaneously realized in the presence of a background fluid: no non-geodesic scaling fixed point exists within an open region of parameter space. As a consequence, in the observationally viable thawing regime the axion does not track the background fluid and spatial curvature becomes dynamically subdominant, leading to an effectively single-field evolution. We further identify a degeneracy between curvature effects and scalar-field dynamics that limits their independent impact on late-time cosmology. Confronting the model with current cosmological background data (Planck 2018 distance priors, Pantheon+, BAO, and cosmic chronometers), we obtain an upper bound $λ\lesssim 0.75$ (95 percent CL) on the potential slope. Our results demonstrate that even in the minimal multifield setup with spatial curvature, sustained late-time acceleration requires a sufficiently flat potential, so that the tension between cosmic acceleration and quantum gravity expectations persists within this framework.

</details>

Conclusion: While the worldline formalism provides elegant compact representations that encode information from many Feynman diagrams, significant mathematical and computational challenges remain in evaluating the resulting non-standard integrals, particularly for QED applications, requiring development of new algorithms and specialized techniques beyond conventional integration methods.

Abstract: The worldline formalism allows one to obtain compact integral representations combining the information of large numbers of Feynman diagrams. However, their analytic calculation leads to a non-standard integration problem for which existing mathematical algorithms are of little help. Here I will summarize the state-of-the-art of worldline integration focusing on examples from QED in vacuum and in constant external fields.

### [76] [Dark Matter and Strong CP Problem in Type IIA String Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18566)
*Yang Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We construct a Type IIA string theory model on $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2)$ orientifold with intersecting D6-branes that yields a 3-generation MSSM-like spectrum with $\mathcal{N}=1$ SUSY.   <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Two fundamental problems in particle physics/cosmology require UV-complete solutions: 1) Dark matter's nature and origin, and 2) The strong CP problem. String theory offers a framework for both, but constructing realistic, globally consistent models that address both simultaneously has been challenging. The goal is to find such a unified framework within Type IIA compactifications that yields the MSSM spectrum while naturally incorporating axions and solving the strong CP problem.

Method: 1) Compactify Type IIA string theory on a $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2)$ orientifold with intersecting D6-branes (Model A) 2) Ensure global consistency conditions: tadpole cancellation, K-theory constraints, RR flux quantization 3) Embed four-form flux mechanism to dynamically relax the $\theta$-angle 4) Compute relic abundance using Boltzmann equations for multi-component dark matter (axions from string theory moduli and neutralinos from SUSY sector) 5) Explore observational signatures via direct/indirect detection and cosmological probes.

Result: 1) The model yields a 3-generation MSSM-like spectrum with $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetry from intersecting D6-branes 2) Successfully embeds four-form flux mechanism to address strong CP problem by dynamically relaxing $\theta$ to zero 3) Predicts multi-component dark matter: QCD axion from moduli and neutralino from lightest SUSY particle 4) Computed relic abundances satisfy $\Omega_{DM}h^2 \sim 0.12$ via freeze-out and misalignment mechanisms 5) Specific stringy constraints on axion decay constant and neutralino mass emerge from global consistency.

Conclusion: This Type IIA string theory construction on $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2)$ orientifold provides a concrete, globally consistent, UV-complete framework that simultaneously addresses dark matter and the strong CP problem. The model successfully yields the MSSM spectrum while naturally incorporating axions and neutralinos as dark matter candidates, demonstrating string theory's potential to solve fundamental particle physics and cosmological puzzles in a unified manner.

Abstract: We present a study of dark matter and the strong CP problem within a globally consistent framework of Type IIA string theory, compactified on a $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2)$ orientifold with intersecting D6-branes (Model A). This setup naturally gives rise to a 3-generation MSSM-like spectrum with $\mathcal{N}=1$ supersymmetry. Phenomenologically, the model predicts a multi-component dark matter scenario comprising both axions and neutralino. We also explore how to embed the four-form flux mechanism into Type IIA $T^6/(\mathbb{Z}_2 \times \mathbb{Z}_2)$ orientifold string theory model to address the strong CP problem. We compute the relic abundance of these candidates and explore their observational signatures. In conclusion, our analysis provides a concrete unified, UV-complete framework that successfully addresses two of the most important problems in particle physics and cosmology.

### [77] [Subleading soft dressings for QED scattering states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18587)
*Stavros Christodoulou,Nicolaos Toumbas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: **TL;DR:**
The paper demonstrates that Faddeev-Kulish dressed states systematically remove IR divergences in QED scattering by dressing charged particles with coherent photon clouds below an IR scale $E_d$, making amplitudes finite order-by-order. When extended to subleading order in soft expansion, these dressings also suppress tree-level soft-photon emission.

\n\n
**太长不看总结:**
本文论证了Faddeev-Kulish dressed states通过给带电粒子穿上能量低于IR尺度$E_d$的相干光子云，系统地消除了QED散射中的红外发散，使振幅按微扰阶数有限。当软展开扩展到次领头阶时，这些dressing还会抑制树图级软光子发射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: **Motivation:**
The infrared (IR) problem in quantum electrodynamics presents long-standing theoretical challenges: scattering amplitudes involving charged particles suffer from uncancelled IR divergences at each order in perturbation theory when using standard Fock states. The Faddeev-Kulish (FK) dressing provides a promising solution by constructing coherent states that accompany charged particles with soft photon clouds, but the systematic implementation and physical consequences of this approach warrant detailed investigation, particularly regarding momentum/angular momentum dependence and subleading soft behavior.

\n\n
**研究动机:**
量子电动力学中的红外(IR)问题提出了长期的理论挑战：当使用标准Fock态时，涉及带电粒子的散射振幅在每个微扰阶数上都存在未抵消的红外发散。Faddeev-Kulish(FK) dressing通过构建伴随带电粒子的软光子云的相干态提供了一个有前景的解决方案，但这种方法在动量/角动量依赖性和次领头软行为方面的系统性实现和物理后果值得详细研究。

Method: **Method:**
The authors analyze scattering processes of FK dressed states in QED, focusing on explicit processes that clearly display the dependence of soft factors on hard particles' momenta and total angular momenta. The incoming/outgoing charged particles are dressed with coherent clouds of soft photons with energies below characteristic infrared scale $E_d$. The analysis proceeds order-by-order in perturbation theory, examining how virtual soft photon contributions regulated at scale $E_d$ through the dressing. Special attention is given to extending dressings to subleading order in soft-momentum expansion as prescribed by Choi-Akhoury formalism.

\n\n
**方法:**
作者分析了QED中FK dressed states的散射过程，重点关注能够清晰展示软因子对硬粒子动量和总角动量依赖性的显式过程。入射/出射带电粒子被能量低于特征红外尺度$E_d$的软光子相干云所dress。分析按微扰阶数进行，研究了虚拟软光子贡献如何通过dressing在尺度$E_d$处被正规化。特别关注按照Choi-Akhoury形式将dressing扩展到软动量展开的次领头阶。

Result: **Result:**
1. FK dressings systematically remove IR divergences in hard amplitudes order-by-order in perturbation theory, effectively regulating virtual soft photon contributions at scale $E_d$.
2. FK hard amplitudes become equivalent to the infrared-finite part of corresponding Fock-basis amplitudes.
3. The dressings' dependence on hard particles' momenta and total angular momenta is explicitly demonstrated through suitable scattering processes.
4. When dressings are extended to subleading order in soft-momentum expansion (Choi-Akhoury prescription), tree-level soft-photon emission becomes suppressed.
5. The coherent photon clouds accompanying charged particles provide physical regularization without introducing ad hoc IR cutoffs.

\n\n
**结果:**
1. FK dressing按微扰阶数系统地消除了硬振幅中的红外发散，有效地在尺度$E_d$处正规化了虚拟软光子贡献。
2. FK硬振幅变得等价于相应Fock基振幅的红外有限部分。
3. 通过合适的散射过程，明确展示了dressing对硬粒子动量和总角动量的依赖性。
4. 当dressing扩展到软动量展开的次领头阶(Choi-Akhoury方案)时，树图级软光子发射被抑制。
5. 伴随带电粒子的相干光子云提供了物理正规化，无需引入特设的IR截断。

Conclusion: **Conclusion:**
The FK dressed state formalism provides a consistent framework for infrared-safe scattering amplitudes in QED, where dressing charged particles with coherent soft photon clouds naturally regularizes IR divergences. The equivalence between FK amplitudes and infrared-finite parts of Fock amplitudes establishes physical correspondence while avoiding artificial regulators. Extending dressings to subleading order yields further physical consequences, including suppression of tree-level soft emission, suggesting that the FK approach captures essential infrared dynamics beyond leading soft theorems. This work clarifies systematic implementation of the dressing procedure and its observable consequences for scattering processes.

\n\n
**结论:**
FK dressed state形式为QED中的红外安全散射振幅提供了一个一致的框架，其中通过用相干软光子云dressing带电粒子自然地正规化了红外发散。FK振幅与Fock振幅红外有限部分之间的等价性建立了物理对应关系，同时避免了人工正规化子。将dressing扩展到次领头阶产生了进一步的物理后果，包括树图级软发射的抑制，这表明FK方法捕捉到了超越领头软定理的本质红外动力学。这项工作阐明了dressing程序的系统性实现及其对散射过程的可观测后果。

Abstract: We study soft emission in QED during scattering of Faddeev-Kulish dressed states. The incoming and outgoing charged particles are accompanied by coherent clouds of soft photons with energies below a characteristic infrared scale $E_d$. We focus on explicit processes that allow the dependence of the soft factors on the hard particles' momenta and total angular momenta to be displayed clearly. We argue that the dressings remove the infrared divergences in hard amplitudes order by order in perturbation theory, effectively regulating the contributions from virtual soft photons at the scale $E_d$. Essentially, the Faddeev-Kulish hard amplitudes become equivalent to the infrared-finite part of the corresponding Fock-basis amplitudes. Finally, tree-level soft-photon emission is found to be suppressed once the dressings are extended to subleading order in the soft-momentum expansion, as prescribed in recent work by Choi and Akhoury.

### [78] [Comments on the Emergence of 4D Topological Amplitudes in M-Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18681)
*Manuel Artime,Ralph Blumenhagen,Aleksandar Gligovic,Panagiotis Leivadaros*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper extends the M-theoretic Emergence Proposal for 4D N=2 compactifications by resolving two open issues: demonstrating equivalence of regularization schemes between complex structure and Kähler moduli spaces, and extending the regularization technique to one-loop prepotential linear terms.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The M-theoretic Emergence Proposal posits that all terms in low-energy effective actions emerge from integrating out massive states. While recent evidence showed classical cubic terms in the prepotential $F_0$ emerge from summing over Gopakumar/Vafa invariants using novel regularization, two key issues remained unresolved: (1) equivalence of regularization across different moduli spaces, and (2) extension to one-loop prepotential $F_1$ linear terms.

M-理论涌现提案认为低能有效作用量中的所有项都来自积分掉大质量态。尽管近期证据表明预势$F_0$中的经典三次项可通过使用新颖正规化对Gopakumar/Vafa不变量求和而涌现，但两个关键问题仍未解决：(1)不同模空间正则化方案的等价性，(2)对一圈预势$F_1$线性项的扩展。

Method: The authors employ techniques from topological string theory and M-theory compactifications. They use the Gopakumar/Vafa invariants to represent the tower of light states in the M-theory limit. A novel regularization scheme is developed to handle infinite sums over these invariants. The key methodological innovations are: (1) demonstrating equivalence between complex structure moduli space regularization and Kähler moduli space regularization, likely through mirror symmetry arguments, and (2) extending the regularization technique to handle the linear terms in the one-loop prepotential $F_1$, involving more subtle asymptotic behavior analysis of the sums.

作者采用拓扑弦理论和M-理论紧化的技术。他们使用Gopakumar/Vafa不变量来表示M-理论极限下的轻态塔。开发了一种新颖的正则化方案来处理这些不变量的无穷求和。关键方法创新包括：(1)通过镜像对称论证展示复结构模空间正则化与Kähler模空间正则化的等价性，(2)将正则化技术扩展到处理一圈预势$F_1$中的线性项，涉及对求和更微妙的渐近行为分析。

Result: Two main results are achieved: First, the regularization scheme for obtaining classical cubic terms in $F_0$ is shown to be equivalent when performed in complex structure moduli space versus Kähler moduli space, establishing consistency across dual descriptions. Second, the regularization is successfully extended to the linear terms in the one-loop prepotential $F_1$, demonstrating that these terms also emerge from integrating out the infinite tower of light states in the M-theory limit. The results provide stronger evidence for the Emergence Proposal in the context of 4D N=2 supersymmetric compactifications.

取得两个主要结果：首先，获得$F_0$中经典三次项的正则化方案在复结构模空间与Kähler模空间中执行时被证明是等价的，建立了对偶描述间的一致性。其次，正则化成功扩展到一圈预势$F_1$中的线性项，证明这些项也来自积分掉M-理论极限下无穷轻态塔。结果为4D N=2超对称紧化背景下的涌现提案提供了更强证据。

Conclusion: The paper strengthens the M-theoretic Emergence Proposal by resolving two previously open issues. The equivalence of regularization schemes across moduli spaces confirms the robustness of the approach, while extension to $F_1$ linear terms demonstrates the generality of the emergence mechanism. These results suggest that not only classical terms but also quantum corrections in topological string amplitudes can be understood as emergent phenomena from integrating out infinite towers of states, providing deeper insight into how low-energy physics emerges from fundamental M-theory.

本文通过解决两个先前悬而未决的问题加强了M-理论涌现提案。跨模空间正则化方案的等价性确认了方法的稳健性，而对$F_1$线性项的扩展证明了涌现机制的普适性。这些结果表明，不仅经典项，拓扑弦振幅中的量子修正也可以理解为积分掉无穷态塔涌现的现象，为低能物理如何从基本M-理论中涌现提供了更深入的见解。

Abstract: The M-theoretic Emergence Proposal claims that all of the terms in the low-energy action arise from quantum effects. After reviewing the current status of this proposal, we focus on four-dimensional compactifications with $N=2$ supersymmetry, where kinetic terms are encoded in topological string amplitudes, such as the prepotential $F_0$. Evidence for the emergence of such terms was provided recently, where in particular it was shown that the classical cubic term in $F_0$ can be obtained by integrating out the light towers of states in the M-theory limit, using a novel regularization of the infinite sum over Gopakumar/Vafa invariants. We address two issues that were left open. First, we show that the regularization can be equivalently performed in complex structure moduli space and in Kähler moduli space. Second, we extend the proposed regularization to the linear terms in the one-loop prepotential $F_1$.

### [79] [Non-Hermitian Structure and Exceptional Points in Yang-Mills Theory from Analytic Continuation of Nc](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19006)
*Qingjun Jin,Ke Ren,Gang Yang,Rui Yu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We demonstrate that analytic continuation of $N_c$ in Yang-Mills theory reveals non-Hermitian structure with topological Exceptional Points in complex $N_c$-space, connecting PT symmetry breaking to logarithmic CFT behavior.

我们证明，杨-米尔斯理论中$N_c$的解析延拓揭示了具有复$N_c$空间中拓扑奇异点的非厄米结构，将PT对称性破缺与对数CFT行为联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional Yang-Mills theory is studied with integer $N_c$ values in the Hermitian regime. The motivation is to explore the theoretical implications of analytically continuing $N_c$ to complex values, which naturally introduces non-Hermitian structure and could reveal hidden topological features not accessible in the conventional unitary formulation.

传统杨-米尔斯理论在厄米体系中研究整数$N_c$值。动机是探索将$N_c$解析延拓到复数值的理论意义，这自然地引入了非厄米结构，并可能揭示传统幺正表述中无法访问的隐藏拓扑特征。

Method: We analytically continue the number of colors $N_c$ to complex values and examine the spectrum of the dilatation operator $D$ as a function of complex $N_c$. This reveals Exceptional Points (EPs) where eigenvalues and eigenvectors coalesce. We construct the complex $N_c$-space as a Riemann surface with EPs as topological defects, analyze the resulting non-Abelian geometric phases via monodromy transformations, and establish the correspondence between emergent PT symmetry of $D$ and fundamental spacetime PT symmetry of the gauge theory.

我们将颜色数$N_c$解析延拓到复数值，并考察伸缩算子$D$的谱作为复$N_c$的函数。这揭示了特征值和特征向量合并的奇异点(EPs)。我们将复$N_c$空间构造为以EPs作为拓扑缺陷的黎曼曲面，通过单值变换分析由此产生的非阿贝尔几何相位，并建立$D$的涌现PT对称性与规范理论的基本时空PT对称性之间的对应关系。

Result: We identify networks of Exceptional Points in complex $N_c$-space where anomalous dimensions degenerate and operator eigenstates coalesce. These EPs act as topological defects generating non-Abelian geometric phases and enforcing nontrivial monodromies among gauge-invariant operators. Spontaneous breaking of the dilatation operator's emergent PT symmetry corresponds to breaking of fundamental spacetime PT symmetry. Near EPs, non-Hermitian dynamics produces logarithmic scaling in correlation functions, characteristic of logarithmic conformal field theories.

我们在复$N_c$空间中识别了异常维度简并且算子本征态合并的奇异点网络。这些EPs作为拓扑缺陷生成非阿贝尔几何相位，并在规范不变算子之间强制执行非平凡的单值性。伸缩算子的涌现PT对称性自发破缺对应于基本时空PT对称性的破缺。在EPs附近，非厄米动力学在关联函数中产生对数标度行为，这是对数共形场论的特征。

Conclusion: Analytic continuation of $N_c$ reveals that conventional unitary Yang-Mills theory resides within a broader complexified parameter space with rich topological structure governed by Exceptional Points. This establishes a novel connection between non-Hermitian physics and quantum field theory, with implications for logarithmic CFTs, topological phases in gauge theories, and the geometric structure of renormalization group flows.

$N_c$的解析延拓揭示了传统幺正杨-米尔斯理论存在于一个由奇异点支配的、具有丰富拓扑结构的更广泛的复参数空间中。这在非厄米物理学与量子场论之间建立了新颖联系，对对数量形场论、规范理论中的拓扑相位以及重整化群流的几何结构具有重要意义。

Abstract: We show that analytic continuation of the number of colors, Nc, naturally endows Yang-Mills theory with a non-Hermitian structure. By examining the spectrum of the dilatation operator as a function of complex Nc, we identify a network of Exceptional Points (EPs) -- non-Hermitian degeneracies where anomalous dimensions degenerate and operator eigenstates coalesce. We demonstrate that these EPs act as topological defects in complex Nc-space, generating non-Abelian geometric phases and enforcing nontrivial monodromies among gauge-invariant operators. Moreover, we establish a correspondence between the spontaneous breaking of an emergent PT symmetry of the dilatation operator and the fundamental spacetime PT symmetry of the underlying gauge theory. In the vicinity of EPs, the resulting non-Hermitian dynamics produces logarithmic scaling behavior in correlation functions, characteristic of logarithmic conformal field theories. Our results place conventional unitary Yang-Mills theory within a broader complexified parameter space possessing rich topological structure, suggesting a new interface between non-Hermitian physics and quantum field theory.

</details>


### [80] [Unfolded hypermultiplet in harmonic superspace](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19033)
*Nikita Misuna*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We construct an unfolded system for free massless hypermultiplet showing harmonic superspace arises from vielbeinization of unfolded 1-forms associated with R-symmetry. The approach exhibits background universality, systematically yielding harmonic, N=2, N=1 superspace, and component Minkowski formulations from the same unfolded system. We also discuss off-shell extensions and how harmonic contributions appear in the universal unfolded fiber.

我们构建了自由无质量超多重态的展开系统，表明调和超空间源于与 R-对称相关的展开1-形式的"标架化"。该方法展示了背景普适性，从同一展开系统系统性地推导出调和、N=2、N=1超空间以及闵可夫斯基空间的分量表述。我们还讨论了离壳扩展以及调和贡献如何出现在普适展开纤维中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation stems from the need to understand the fundamental connections between different superspace formulations of hypermultiplets and demonstrate the power of the unfolded dynamics approach as a unifying framework. Specifically, harmonic superspace provides a powerful tool for N=2 supersymmetric theories but its origin from more fundamental principles remains unclear. The paper aims to show that harmonic superspace naturally emerges from the vielbeinization procedure applied to unfolded 1-forms associated with R-symmetry, establishing a deeper connection between geometric and algebraic structures.

动机源于需要理解超多重态不同超空间表述之间的基本联系，并展示展开动力学方法作为统一框架的能力。具体而言，调和超空间为N=2超对称理论提供了强大工具，但其来自更基本原理的起源仍不清楚。本文旨在表明调和超空间自然产生于应用于与R-对称相关的展开1-形式的标架化过程，从而建立几何结构与代数结构之间更深层的联系。

Method: The method employs the unfolded dynamics formalism, constructing an unfolded system for a free massless hypermultiplet. Key technical steps include: (1) Formulating the hypermultiplet as an unfolded system using differential forms on an extended manifold; (2) Implementing "vielbeinization" of unfolded 1-forms associated with R-symmetry to derive harmonic superspace; (3) Demonstrating background universality by systematically deducing formulations in different superspaces (harmonic, N=2, N=1) and component Minkowski space from the same unfolded system; (4) Analyzing the relationship between harmonic contributions and the universal unfolded fiber.

方法采用展开动力学形式体系，构建自由无质量超多重态的展开系统。关键技术步骤包括：(1) 使用扩展流形上的微分形式将超多重态表述为展开系统；(2) 对与R-对称相关的展开1-形式实施"标架化"以推导调和超空间；(3) 通过从同一展开系统系统性地推导不同超空间（调和、N=2、N1）和分量闵可夫斯基空间的表述，展示背景普适性；(4) 分析调和贡献与普适展开纤维之间的关系。

Result: The main results are: (1) Explicit construction of an unfolded system describing on-shell free massless hypermultiplet; (2) Demonstration that the standard harmonic superspace formulation naturally arises from vielbeinization of unfolded 1-forms associated with R-symmetry, establishing a direct connection: $\\Omega_{R\\text{-sym}}^{(1)} \\xrightarrow{\\text{vielbeinization}} H^{a\\alpha}$ (harmonic vielbeins); (3) Proof of background universality showing that harmonic superspace, N=2 superspace, N=1 superspace, and component Minkowski formulations are all systematically derived from the same unfolded system; (4) Identification of how harmonic contributions manifest in the universal unfolded fiber structure: $\\mathcal{F}_{\\text{univ}} = \\mathcal{F}_{\\text{dyn}} \\oplus \\mathcal{F}_{\\text{harm}}$; (5) Comments on off-shell extensions and consistency conditions.

主要结果是：(1) 描述在壳自由无质量超多重态的展开系统的显式构建；(2) 证明标准调和超空间表述自然产生于与R-对称相关的展开1-形式的标架化，建立了直接联系：$\\Omega_{R\\text{-sym}}^{(1)} \\xrightarrow{\\text{标架化}} H^{a\\alpha}$（调和标架）；(3) 背景普适性的证明表明调和超空间、N=2超空间、N=1超空间和分量闵可夫斯基空间表述都从同一展开系统系统性地推导得出；(4) 识别调和贡献如何体现在普适展开纤维结构中：$\\mathcal{F}_{\\text{univ}} = \\mathcal{F}_{\\text{dyn}} \\oplus \\mathcal{F}_{\\text{harm}}$；(5) 关于离壳扩展和一致性条件的评论。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that harmonic superspace is not an ad hoc construction but naturally emerges from the vielbeinization of unfolded 1-forms associated with R-symmetry within the unfolded dynamics framework. This demonstrates the background universality of the unfolded approach, where different superspace formulations and component field theories appear as specific "background choices" or "gauge fixings" of the same universal unfolded system. The work provides a deeper understanding of the geometric origin of harmonic superspace and showcases the unifying power of unfolded dynamics as a master framework for supersymmetric field theories.

本文确立了调和超空间并非特设构造，而是在展开动力学框架内自然地产生于与R-对称相关的展开1-形式的标架化。这展示了展开方法的背景普适性，其中不同的超空间表述和分量场论作为同一普适展开系统的特定"背景选择"或"规范固定"出现。这项工作提供了对调和超空间几何起源的更深刻理解，并展示了展开动力学作为超对称场论主框架的统一能力。

Abstract: We construct an unfolded system that describes an on-shell free massless hypermultiplet and show that the standard harmonic superspace formulation of this model naturally arises from the "vielbeinization" of unfolded 1-forms associated to R-symmetry. Moreover, using this system as an example, we demonstrate the phenomenon of background universality of the unfolded dynamics approach: we systematically deduce formulations in harmonic, N=2, and N=1 superspaces, as well as the component formulation in Minkowski space, directly from this unfolded system. We also comment on a putative off-shell extension of the on-shell system we constructed, and show how the harmonic contribution is reflected in the universal unfolded fiber.

### [81] [$S^3$ partition functions and Equivariant CY$_4 $/ CY$_3$ correspondence from Quantum curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19159)
*Kiril Hristov,Naotaka Kubo,Yi Pang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper establishes exact agreement between M2-brane theories' three-sphere partition functions computed via Fermi gas/quantum curves and topological string predictions, confirming equivariant constant maps proposal. It further proposes novel equivariant correspondence between CY4 and C×CY3 geometries based on quantum curve relations, extending TS/ST correspondence.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primary motivation is to test and extend the proposal by [1] that the round three-sphere partition function in M2-brane theories admits an Airy-function representation exactly matching predictions from equivariant constant maps in topological string theory. The work aims to provide affirmative tests for specific toric geometries and establish deeper connections between quantum curves, spectral theory, and holography.

Method: The authors employ Fermi gas formalism and quantum curve techniques to compute the perturbative large-$N$ expansion of the three-sphere partition function. They analyze specific M2-brane theories including flavored SYM, ABJM, and theories with $(p,q)$ 5-brane web descriptions. The quantum curves are derived and compared with topological string predictions, leading to the identification of constraints that establish the proposed equivariant correspondence.

Result: Exact agreement is found between the Airy-function representation of partition functions computed via Fermi gas/quantum curves and topological string predictions based on equivariant constant maps. Affirmative tests are provided for three toric geometries: $\mathbb{C} \times \mathcal{C}$ (conifold), cone over $Q^{1,1,1}$, and $\mathbb{C} \times \mathrm{SPP}$. A novel equivariant correspondence $\mathrm{CY}_4 \leftrightarrow \mathbb{C} \times\mathrm{CY}_3$ is proposed based on relations between quantum curves under specific constraints.

Conclusion: The work confirms the proposal by [1] and establishes the Airy-function representation as exact. The novel equivariant correspondence suggests an extension of the topological string/spectral theory (TS/ST) correspondence, provides insights into the geometric origin of this correspondence, and offers new perspectives on holography duality structure. The quantum curve approach emerges as a powerful tool connecting partition functions, spectral theory, and geometry.

Abstract: We study the perturbative large-$N$ expansion of the round three-sphere partition function in a class of M2-brane theories, including flavored SYM and ABJM theories as well as more general 3d theories admitting dual $(p,q)$ 5-brane web descriptions. Using the Fermi gas formalism and quantum curve techniques, we derive the Airy-function representation of the partition function and find exact agreement with predictions based on equivariant constant maps in topological string theory proposed in [1]. In particular, we provide affirmative tests of this proposal for the toric geometries $\mathbb{C} \times \mathcal{C}$ (the conifold), the cone over the Sasakian space $Q^{1,1,1}$, and $\mathbb{C} \times \mathrm{SPP}$ (the suspended pinch point). Motivated by a recent conjecture in [2], we further propose a novel equivariant correspondence between distinct toric Calabi-Yau manifolds of the form $\mathrm{CY}_4 \leftrightarrow \mathbb{C} \times\mathrm{CY}_3$, arising from relations between the corresponding quantum curves under specific constraints. This correspondence suggests an equivariant extension and points toward a geometric origin of the topological string/spectral theory (TS/ST) correspondence, while offering new insight into the structure of the holography duality.

### [82] [Quasinormal Modes of Extremal Reissner-Nordstrom Black Holes via Seiberg-Witten Quantization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19168)
*Yi-Rong Wang,Peng Yang,Kilar Zhang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: [Non-perturbative calculation of scalar quasinormal mode frequencies for extremal Reissner-Nordström black holes using quantum Seiberg-Witten theory in Nekrasov-Shatashvili limit]

\n\n
[使用 Nekrasov-Shatashvili 极限下的量子 Seiberg-Witten 理论，对极端 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞的标量准正态模频率进行非微扰计算]

[Method maps master equation (double confluent Heun) to quantum SW curve, computes frequencies via quantization condition from NS free energy]

\n\n
[方法将主方程(双汇合 Heun 方程)映射到量子 SW 曲线，通过来自 NS 自由能的量子化条件计算频率]

[Results match numerical benchmarks for massless fields and capture massive quasi-resonances at strict extremal limit]

\n\n
[结果与无质量场的数值基准匹配，并在严格极端极限下捕捉到有质量的准共振行为]


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: [The motivation is to provide an analytical, non-perturbative framework for computing quasinormal mode frequencies of extremal black holes, particularly Reissner-Nordström black holes. Traditional methods for quasinormal mode calculations face difficulties in the extremal limit where separation constants diverge. The paper seeks to leverage the deep connection between black hole perturbation equations and quantum integrable systems/Seiberg-Witten theory to overcome these limitations.]

\n\n
[动机是为计算极端黑洞(特别是 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞)的准正态模频率提供一个分析性的非微扰框架。传统的准正态模计算方法在极端极限下面临困难，其中分离常数发散。该论文旨在利用黑洞扰动方程与量子可积系统/Seiberg-Witten 理论之间的深层联系来克服这些限制。]

Method: [The method establishes a precise mathematical mapping between the scalar perturbation master equation for extremal Reissner-Nordström black holes and quantum Seiberg-Witten theory. The master equation is identified as a double confluent Heun equation. This is mapped to the quantum Seiberg-Witten curve of $\mathcal{N}=2$ $\mathrm{SU(2)}$ gauge theory with $N_f=2$ flavors in the Nekrasov-Shatashvili limit ($\epsilon_1=\hbar$, $\epsilon_2=0$). Quasinormal mode frequencies are computed using the exact quantization condition derived from the Nekrasov-Shatashvili free energy: $\mathcal{F}_{\text{NS}}(a,\hbar) = \lim_{\epsilon_2\to0} \epsilon_2 \log Z(a,\epsilon_1=\hbar,\epsilon_2)$. The quantization condition takes the form: $a_{\text{QNM}} = f(E, \ell, m, M, Q)$ where $E$ is the complex frequency, $\ell,m$ are angular quantum numbers, $M,Q$ are black hole mass and charge.]

\n\n
[方法建立了极端 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞的标量扰动主方程与量子 Seiberg-Witten 理论之间的精确数学映射。主方程被识别为双汇合 Heun 方程。这被映射到 Nekrasov-Shatashvili 极限($\epsilon_1=\hbar$, $\epsilon_2=0$)下具有 $N_f=2$ 风味的 $\mathcal{N}=2$ $\mathrm{SU(2)}$ 规范理论的量子 Seiberg-Witten 曲线。准正态模频率使用从 Nekrasov-Shatashvili 自由能导出的精确量子化条件计算：$\mathcal{F}_{\text{NS}}(a,\hbar) = \lim_{\epsilon_2\to0} \epsilon_2 \log Z(a,\epsilon_1=\hbar,\epsilon_2)$。量子化条件形式为：$a_{\text{QNM}} = f(E, \ell, m, M, Q)$，其中 $E$ 是复频率，$\ell,m$ 是角量子数，$M,Q$ 是黑洞质量和电荷。]

Result: [1. The paper successfully maps the scalar perturbation equation for extremal Reissner-Nordström black holes to the quantum Seiberg-Witten curve, establishing explicit parameter identifications between black hole parameters ($M,Q,\ell,m,E$) and gauge theory parameters ($a,u,\Lambda,\hbar$).

2. Non-perturbative quasinormal mode frequencies are computed analytically via the exact quantization condition from the Nekrasov-Shatashvili free energy. The results show excellent agreement with numerical calculations for massless scalar fields across various angular modes.

3. For massive scalar fields, the method captures the quasi-resonance behavior (long-lived modes with small imaginary parts) that emerges at the strict extremal limit. These quasi-resonances correspond to poles in the transmission amplitude that approach the real axis.

4. The analytical expressions reveal the functional dependence of quasinormal mode frequencies on black hole parameters, angular quantum numbers, and scalar field mass, providing insights into the spectral structure of extremal black holes.]

\n\n
[1. 论文成功地将极端 Reissner-Nordström 黑洞的标量扰动方程映射到量子 Seiberg-Witten 曲线，建立了黑洞参数($M,Q,\ell,m,E$)与规范理论参数($a,u,\Lambda,\hbar$)之间的显式参数对应关系。

2. 通过来自 Nekrasov-Shatashvili 自由能的精确量子化条件，非微扰地解析计算了准正态模频率。结果显示与各种角模式下无质量标量场的数值计算高度一致。

3. 对于有质量标量场，该方法捕捉到了在严格极端极限下出现的准共振行为(具有小虚部的长寿命模式)。这些准共振对应于接近实轴的透射振幅的极点。

4. 解析表达式揭示了准正态模频率对黑洞参数、角量子数和标量场质量的函数依赖关系，为理解极端黑洞的谱结构提供了洞见。]

Conclusion: [The paper demonstrates a powerful application of quantum field theory techniques to black hole physics. By establishing a precise connection between extremal black hole perturbations and $\mathcal{N}=2$ gauge theory in the Nekrasov-Shatashvili limit, it provides an analytical, non-perturbative method for computing quasinormal mode spectra. This approach overcomes limitations of traditional perturbation methods in the extremal regime and reveals the underlying quantum integrable structure of black hole perturbation theory. The agreement with numerical benchmarks validates the mapping, while the capture of massive quasi-resonances showcases the method's ability to probe subtle spectral features. This work suggests deeper connections between black hole spectroscopy and quantum gauge theories that warrant further exploration.]

\n\n
[论文展示了量子场论技术在黑洞物理中的强大应用。通过建立极端黑洞扰动与 Nekrasov-Shatashvili 极限下的 $\mathcal{N}=2$ 规范理论之间的精确联系，它提供了一种解析的、非微扰的计算准正态模谱的方法。这种方法克服了传统扰动方法在极端区域中的限制，并揭示了黑洞扰动理论背后的量子可积结构。与数值基准的一致性验证了该映射的有效性，而对有质量准共振的捕捉展示了该方法探测微妙谱特征的能力。这项工作表明黑洞光谱学与量子规范理论之间存在更深的联系，值得进一步探索。]

Abstract: We study the neutral scalar perturbations of asymptotically flat extremal Reissner-Nordström black holes via the quantum geometry of $\mathcal{N}=2$ $\mathrm{SU(2)}$ gauge theory with $N_f=2$ flavors. The master equation, given by a double confluent Heun equation, is mapped to the quantum Seiberg-Witten curve in the Nekrasov-Shatashvili limit. We compute the quasinormal mode frequencies non-perturbatively using the quantization condition derived from the Nekrasov-Shatashvili free energy. Our analytical results accurately reproduce the numerical benchmarks for massless fields, and capture the quasi-resonance behavior of massive probes at the strict extremal limit.

### [83] [Perturbative approach to the infrared gluon propagator in the maximal Abelian gauge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.19174)
*D. M. van Egmond,L. C. Ferreira,A. D. Pereira,G. Peruzzo,S. P. Sorella*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: This paper investigates whether the mass-deformation approach, successful in Landau gauge, can also describe infrared gluon and ghost propagator behavior in maximal Abelian gauge (MAG). Through one-loop computations for $SU(2)$, they find good agreement between the transverse non-Abelian and diagonal gluon propagators with lattice data in the infrared regime.

本文研究质量变形方法（在Landau规范中成功）是否也能描述极大Abelian规范（MAG）中的红外胶子和鬼传播子行为。通过对$SU(2)$的单圈计算，他们发现横向非Abelian和diagonal胶子传播子在红外区域与格点数据有很好的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The mass-deformation approach in Landau gauge has successfully reproduced lattice results for gauge-fixed correlation functions perturbatively. However, these quantities are gauge-dependent, raising questions about the generality of this prescription for describing infrared behavior of gluon and Faddeev-Popov ghost propagators in different gauges. The maximal Abelian gauge (MAG) is particularly interesting as it cannot be deformed into Landau gauge and has been investigated in gauge-fixed lattice simulations, providing a testbed for the universality of the mass-deformation approach.

Landau规范中的质量变形方法已成功微扰地再现了格点规范固定关联函数的结果。然而，这些量是规范依赖的，引发了对该方法在不同规范中描述胶子和Faddeev-Popov鬼传播子红外行为的普遍性的质疑。极大Abelian规范（MAG）特别有趣，因为它不能变形为Landau规范，且已在格点模拟中被研究，为质量变形方法的普适性提供了测试平台。

Method: The study employs a systematic investigation of the mass-deformation approach in maximal Abelian gauge (MAG). The methodology involves:
1. One-loop perturbative computations of both non-Abelian and diagonal gluon propagators
2. Application of mass-deformation to the MAG framework
3. Numerical fits to available lattice simulation data for $SU(2)$ gauge theory
4. Comparison of transverse components of the non-Abelian gluon propagator and diagonal gluon propagator with lattice results in the infrared region

该方法采用系统研究极大Abelian规范（MAG）中的质量变形方法。方法学包括：
1. 对非Abelian和diagonal胶子传播子进行单圈微扰计算
2. 将质量变形应用于MAG框架
3. 对$SU(2)$规范理论的可用格点模拟数据进行数值拟合
4. 将非Abelian胶子传播子和diagonal胶子传播子的横向分量与红外区域的格点结果进行比较

Result: The key results show:
1. The transverse component of the non-Abelian gluon propagator computed with mass-deformation in MAG exhibits good agreement with lattice data in the infrared regime
2. The diagonal gluon propagator similarly shows good agreement with lattice simulations in the infrared
3. These findings demonstrate that the mass-deformation prescription, while originally developed and validated in Landau gauge, extends effectively to maximal Abelian gauge despite their topological differences
4. The success suggests that certain infrared properties of gluon propagators may be captured by this simple mass-like term across different gauge choices

关键结果显示：
1. 在MAG中使用质量变形计算的非Abelian胶子传播子的横向分量在红外区域与格点数据表现出良好的一致性
2. diagonal胶子传播子同样在红外区域与格点模拟显示出良好的一致性
3. 这些发现表明，尽管存在拓扑差异，但最初在Landau规范中发展和验证的质量变形方法能有效地扩展到极大Abelian规范
4. 这一成功表明，胶子传播子的某些红外特性可以通过这种简单的类质量项在不同规范选择中被捕捉

Conclusion: The mass-deformation approach, which successfully reproduces lattice results in Landau gauge, proves to be generalizable to maximal Abelian gauge (MAG) for describing infrared behavior of gluon propagators. The good agreement between one-loop perturbative computations and lattice data for both transverse non-Abelian and diagonal gluon propagators suggests that this prescription captures essential infrared features that transcend specific gauge choices. This finding enhances our understanding of gauge dependence in non-perturbative QCD and supports the robustness of mass-deformed Yang-Mills theories in describing confinement physics across different gauges.

成功再现Landau规范中格点结果的质量变形方法被证明可推广到极大Abelian规范（MAG）用于描述胶子传播子的红外行为。单圈微扰计算与格点数据对横向非Abelian和diagonal胶子传播子的一致性表明，该方法捕捉了超越特定规范选择的基本红外特征。这一发现增强了我们对非微扰QCD中规范依赖性的理解，并支持质量变形Yang-Mills理论在不同规范中描述禁闭物理的稳健性。

Abstract: The inclusion of a mass-like term for the gluon in Yang-Mills theories quantized in the Landau gauge has proven to be an effective way of reproducing lattice results for gauge-fixed correlation functions within perturbative computations. Since those quantities are gauge dependent, it is natural to question how general this prescription is for describing the infrared behavior of gluon and Faddeev-Popov ghost propagators in different gauges. In this work, we provide a systematic investigation of this issue in the maximal Abelian gauge, which cannot be deformed into the Landau gauge and has been investigated in gauge-fixed lattice simulations. We compute the one-loop non-Abelian and diagonal gluon propagators and perform fits to lattice data in the case of $SU(2)$. Our results show that the transverse component of the non-Abelian gluon propagator as well as the diagonal gluon propagator, are in good agreement with lattice data in the infrared.

</details>
